10th akṣaya: Prajñā

(p. 61) 10th Imperishable: Insight.


de nas tshe daṅ ldan pa śa ra dva ti’i bus byaṅ chub sems dpa’ blo gros mi zad pa la ’di skad ces smras so: - rigs kyi bu, byaṅ chub sems dpa’ rnams kyi bsam gtan mi zad pa ’di ni khyod kyis legs par smras na, rigs kyi bu, byaṅ chub sems dpa’ rnams kyi śes rab mi zad pa la brtsams te, ji ltar byaṅ chub sems dpa’ rnams śes rab mi zad par ’gyur ba khyod spobs par gyis śig!

atha khalv āyuṣmāñ śāradvatīputro ’kṣayamatiṃ bodhisattvam idam avocat: subhāṣitā tvayeyaṃ, kulaputra, bodhisattvānāṃ dhyānākṣayatā; pratibhātu te, kulaputra, bodhisattvānāṃ prajñākṣayatām ārabhya, yathā bodhisattvānāṃ prajñākṣayā bhavet.

Then the venerable Śāradvatīputra addressed himself to the bodhisattva Akṣayamati: – Well spoken by you, son of good family, was this imperishability of the bodhisattvas’ meditation. May you be inspired, son of good family, on the subject of the imperishability of the bodhisattvas’ insight, as to how the insight of the bodhisattvas becomes imperishable.

śes rab mi zad pa la gnas pa’i byaṅ chub sems dpa’ ni chos la mi ñams pa’i byaṅ chub sems dpa’ źes bya ste, de bstan pa’i phyir btsun pa śa ra dva ti’i bu byaṅ chub sems dpa’ rnams kyi śes rab kyaṅ mi zad pa yin te źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs so – "The bodhisattva established in the imperishability of insight is the bodhisattva not forgetting religion (prajñākṣayatāpratiṣṭhito bodhisattvo dharmāpramuṣito bodhisattvaḥ)...".
ṭ. fol. 88a6-7: de mi zad pa yaṅ ’og nas sems can thams cad kyi sems kyi spyod pa ji sñed pa śes rab daṅ ye śes kyi las kyaṅ de sñed do źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs pas bstan te, sems can thams cad kyi sems daṅ spyod pa nam mkha’ bźin mtha’ thug pa med pa la dmigs pas zad mi śes pa’i phyir ro; yaṅ na sñiṅ rje chen po’i rgyu las byuṅ ba daṅ, sems can thams cad kyi phyir bsgrub pa daṅ, śes bya mtha’ med pa’i yul la dmigs pa daṅ, rnam par mi rtog pa’i ye śes kyis zin pa’i phyir śes rab mi zad pa źes bya’o. The imperishability of insight is explained by the fact that its object (ālambana), the thoughts and practices (cittacarita) of all beings, is endless like space, and thus it must itself also be imperishable, quoting Akṣ p. 8324-25 to support this argument. Also, it is imperishable because it has great compassion as its cause (mahākaruṇāhetuka), because it is attained for the sake of all beings, because its range is endless, and because it is "embraced by knowledge beyond thought-constructions (nirvikalpajñānaparigṛhīta)".
ṭ. fol. 88a7-b3: śes rab mi zad pa de yaṅ rnam pa bdun lta ste: śes rab kyi a) rnam pa daṅ, b) ’jug pa daṅ, c) ṅes pa’i tshig daṅ, d) ’bras bu daṅ, e) raṅ bźin daṅ, f) yul daṅ, g) las (94b) rnams so. de las a) rnam pa ni thos pa’i rnam pa brgyad cu rtsa bźis bstan, b) ’jug pa ni tshul bźin yid la byed pa la ’jug pa sum cu rtsa gcig gis bstan, c) ṅes pa’i tshig ni rigs pa’i tshig go źes bya ba la sogs pa’i tshig gi tshar gyis bstan, d) ’bras bu ni tshul bźin źes bya ba ni chos thams cad do źes bya ba la sogs pas bstan, e) raṅ bźin ni ’grogs pa bcu drug daṅ lhan cig mi gnas pas bstan, f) yul ni chos brgyad la mkhas pas bstan, g) las ni gźan yaṅ dge ba daṅ mi dge ba’i chos rnams rab tu śes pa ni śes rab bo źes bya ba ni de la byaṅ chub sems dpas bslab par bya’o źes bya ba yan chad kyis bstan to.
These are the divisions on which our edition is based. An alternative division is, however, given at fol. 88b3-89a1: yaṅ na śes rab mi zad pa de yaṅ 1) śes rab kyi raṅ bźin daṅ, 2) śes rab kyi ’jug pa daṅ, 3) śes rab kyi rgyu daṅ, 4) śes rab de śes rab kyi mi mthun pa’i phyogs daṅ ma ’dres pa daṅ, 5) śes rab kyi yul daṅ, 6) śes rab kyi ṅes pa’i tshig daṅ, 7) śes rab kyi ’bras bu daṅ, 8) bstan pa’i bdag ñid chen po brjod pas bstan to; de la 1) thos pa’i rnam pa brgyad cu rtsa bźi ni śes rab kyi raṅ bźin no, 2) tshul bźin yid la byed pa la ’jug pa sum cu rtsa gñis ni śes rab kyi ’jug pa’o, 3) gźan yaṅ btsun pa śa ra dva ti’i bu tshul bźin źes bya ba ni chos thams cad do źes bya ba la sogs pa ni śes rab kyi rgyu’o, 4) de la śes rab ni ’grogs pa bcu drug daṅ lhan cig mi gnas so źes bya ba la sogs pa ni śes rab de śes rab kyi mi mthun pa’i phyogs daṅ ma ’dres pa’o, 5) phuṅ po la sogs pa chos brgyad ni śes rab kyi yul lo, 6) gźan yaṅ dge ba daṅ mi dge ba’i chos rnams rab tu śes pa źes bya ba la sogs pa ni śes rab kyi ṅes pa’i tshig go, 7) btsun pa śa ra dva ti’i bu de ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’ rnams kyi śes rab mi zad pa ste, śes rab mi zad pa ’dis ye śes mi zad pa thob par ’gyur ro źes bya ba ni śes rab kyi ’bras bu’o, 8) śes rab mi zad pa bstan pa’i chos kyi le’u ’di źes bya ba la sogs pas ni bstan pa’i bdag ñid chen po brjod pa bstan to – 1) Essence of insight (prajñāsvabhāva), 2) entrance into insight (prajñāpraveśa), 3) cause of insight (prajñāhetu), 4) that insight is not mixed up with its contrary (tasyāḥ prajñāyā vipakṣāsaṃsṛṣṭatā), 5) range of insight (prajñāviṣaya), 6) etymology of insight (prajñānirukti), 7) fruit of insight (prajñāphala), 8) praising the greatness of the teaching (nirdeśamahātmyānuśaṃsānirdeśa); 1) corresponds to a), 2) corresponds to b), 3) corresponds to d), 4) corresponds to e), 5) corresponds to f), 6) corresponds to g) except for the last few lines, 7) is p. 8332-34 and 8) p. 8335-37. Item c) is for some reason left out in this scheme, possibly because this paragraph deals with nirukti according to the first scheme, while g) deals with nirukti according to the second.


blo gros mi zad pas smras pa: - btsun pa śa ra dva ti’i bu, byaṅ chub sems dpa’ rnams kyi śes rab kyaṅ mi zad pa yin te. śes rab de’i rnam pa ni ji lta bu, ’jug pa ni ci źe na?

akṣayamatir āha: bodhisattvānāṃ prajñāpi, bhadanta śāradvatīputrākṣayā. tasyāḥ prajñāyāḥ kīdṛśa ākāraḥ, kaḥ praveśaḥ? p. 62

Akṣayamati said: – The bodhisattvas’ insight, reverend Śāradvatīputra, is also imperishable. What is the form [or essence (svabhāva) ] of that insight, what is the entrance into it [or, rather, the understanding of the essential character of moments of existence (dharmalakṣaṇa) through that insight]?

śes rab de’i rnam pa ji lta bu źes bya ba ni śes rab de’i raṅ bźin ji lta bu źes bya ba’i tshig go. ’jug pa ni ci źes bya ba ni śes rab des chos rnams kyi mtshan ñid la ji ltar rtog ces bya ba’i tha tshig ste, ’jug pa’i sgra ni rtog par byed pa la bya’o.


thos pa ni rnam pa’o, tshul bźin yid la byed pa ni ’jug pa’o.

śrutam ākāro yoniśomanasikāraḥ praveśah.

Learning is the form, and thorough mental effort is the entrance to it.


thos pa’i yaṅ rnam pa ni ji lta bu, ’jug pa ni ci źe na?

kīdṛśaś ca śrutākāraḥ, kaḥ praveśaḥ?

So, of what kind then is the form [of insight] consisting in learning, what is the entrance to it,

de skad dris pa daṅ lan du thos pa ni rnam pa’o, tshul bźin yid la byed pa ni ’jug pa’o źes gsuṅs te, thos pa ni śes rab kyi raṅ bźin yin la, tshul bźin yid la byed pa’i sgo nas chos rnams kyi mtshan ñid rtogs par ’gyur bas tshul bźin yid la byed pa ni ’jug pa źes bya’o. yaṅ na, rnam pa ni śes rab kyi raṅ bźin ji lta bu bye brag tu ’byed pa’o, de yaṅ thos pa las śes rab kyi bye brag phyed par ’gyur te, de bas na thos pa’i rnam pa brgyad cu rtsa bźi po de dag las śes rab ’byuṅ ba’i phyir, brgyad cu rtsa bźi po dag ni śes rab kyi bye brag gam rnam graṅs źes bya’o. yaṅ na, śes rab de’i rnam pa ji lta bu źes bya ba ni rgyu ’dri ba’i tshig ste, śes rab de’i rgyu gaṅ yin źes bya ba’i don to. The form (ākāra), namely learning (śruta), is explained as the essence (svabhāva) of prajñā, but alternatively as eighty-four forms of prajñā originating from śruta; and again, alternatively, ākāra is glossed with hetu, "What is the cause of insight?" being the meaning of the question "What is the form of insight?". In the Sanskrit text -ākāraṃ is clearly a bahuvrīhi in apposition to śruta, not withstanding the yaṅ in the Tibetan text p. 622 between thos pa’i and rnam pa.


byaṅ chub sems dpa’ rnams kyi thos pa’i rnam pa ni ci źe na?brgyad cu rtsa bźi ste, ’di lta ste: ’dun pa’i rnam pa daṅ;bsam pa’i rnam pa daṅ;lhag pa’i bsam pa’i rnam pa daṅ;sbyor ba’i rnam pa daṅ;dge ba’i bśes gñen gyi rnam pa daṅ;ṅa rgyal med pa’i rnam pa daṅ;bag yod pa’i rnam pa daṅ;gus par byed pa’i rnam pa daṅ;’thun par ’dzin pa’i rnam pa daṅ;bka’ blo bde ba’i rnam pa daṅ;bsñen bkur byed pa’i rnam pa daṅ;rna ba blags te ñan pa’i rnam pa daṅ;yid la byed pa’i rnam pa daṅ;rnam par mi g-yeṅ ba’i rnam pa daṅ;gnas kyi rnam pa daṅ;rin po cher ’du śes pa’i rnam pa daṅ;sman du ’du śes pa’i rnam pa daṅ;ñon moṅs pa’i nad thams cad źi bar byed pa’i rnam pa daṅ;dran pa’i snod kyi rnam pa daṅ;rtogs pa śes pa’i rnam pa daṅ;blo gros ’dod pa’i rnam pa daṅ;blo la ’jug pa’i rnam pa daṅ;saṅs rgyas kyi chos la mi ṅoms par ñan pa’i rnam pa daṅ;gtoṅ ba spel ba’i rnam pa daṅ;dul źiṅ caṅ śes pa’i rnam pa daṅ;maṅ du thos pa la bsten pa’i rnam pa daṅ;bsti staṅ du byas te dga’ ba myoṅ bar byed pa’i rnam pa daṅ;lus bde ba’i rnam pa daṅ;sems rab tu dga’ ba’i rnam pa daṅ;mi skyo bar ñan pa’i rnam pa daṅ;don ñan pa’i rnam pa daṅ;chos ñan pa’i rnam pa daṅ;nan tan ñan pa’i rnam pa daṅ;gźan gyis bstan pa ñan pa’i rnam pa daṅ;chos ma thos pa ñan pa’i rnam pa daṅ;mṅon par śes pa ñan pa’i rnam pa daṅ;theg pa gźan la ’dod pa med pa’i rnam pa daṅ;pha rol tu phyin pa ñan pa’i rnam pa daṅ;byaṅ chub sems dpa’i sde snod ñan pa’i rnam pa daṅ;bsdu ba’i dṅos po ñan pa’i rnam pa daṅ;thabs mkhas pa ñan pa’i rnam pa daṅ;tshaṅs pa’i gnas ñan pa’i rnam pa daṅ;dran pa daṅ śes bźin ñan pa’i rnam pa daṅ;skye ba la mkhas pa ñan pa’i rnam pa daṅ;mi skye ba la mkhas pa ñan pa’i rnam pa daṅ;mi sdug pa’i rnam pa daṅ;byams pa’i rnam pa daṅ;rten ciṅ ’brel bar ’byuṅ ba’i rnam pa daṅ;mi rtag pa’i rnam pa daṅ;sdug bsṅal ba’i rnam pa daṅ;bdag med pa’i rnam pa daṅ;źi ba’i rnam pa daṅ;stoṅ pa ñid kyi rnam pa daṅ;mtshan ma med pa’i rnam pa daṅ;smon pa med pa’i rnam pa daṅ;mṅon par ’du mi byed pa’i rnam pa daṅ;dge ba mṅon par ’du byed pa’i rnam pa daṅ;bden pas byin gyis brlabs pa’i rnam pa daṅ;chud mi gzon pa’i rnam pa daṅ;raṅ gi kha na las pa’i rnam pa daṅ;raṅ gi sems sruṅ ba’i rnam pa daṅ;brtson ’grus mi gtoṅ ba’i rnam pa daṅ;chos la ṅes par sems pa’i rnam pa daṅ;ñon moṅs pa’i gñen po’i rnam pa daṅ;raṅ gi phyogs sruṅ ba’i rnam pa daṅ;pha rol gyi phyogs daṅ ñon moṅs pa tshar gcod pa’i rnam pa daṅ;nor bdun yaṅ dag par ’du ba’i rnam pa daṅ;dbul ba thams cad tshar gcod pa’i rnam pa daṅ;mdzaṅs pas bsṅags pa’i rnam pa daṅ;mkhas pa mṅon par dga’ ba’i rnam pa daṅ;’phags pas kun śes pa’i rnam pa daṅ;’phags pa ma yin pa dad par byed pa’i rnam pa daṅ;bden pa mthoṅ ba’i rnam pa daṅ;phuṅ po’i skyon rnam par spaṅ ba’i rnam pa daṅ;’dus byas kyi skyon yoṅs su ’jal ba’i rnam pa daṅ;don la rton pa’i rnam pa daṅ;chos la rton pa’i rnam pa daṅ;ye śes la rton pa’i rnam pa daṅ;ṅes pa’i don gyi mdo sde la rton pa’i rnam pa daṅ;sdig pa thams cad mi bya ba’i rnam pa daṅ;bdag daṅ gźan la phan pa’i rnam pa daṅ;legs par byas pa’i las kyi rnam pa daṅ, mi ’gyod pa’i rnam pa daṅ;khyad par du ’gro ba’i rnam pa daṅ;saṅs rgyas kyi chos thams cad ’thob pa’i rnam pa ste;

ko bodhisattvānāṃ śrutākāraḥ?caturaśītis tad yathā chandākāram;āśayākāram;adhyāśayākāraṃ;prayogākāraṃ;kalyāṇamitrākāraṃ;nirmāṇākāram;apramādākāraṃ;gauravākāraṃ;pradakṣiṇākāraṃ;suvacanākāraṃ;paryupāsanākāram;avahitaśrotrākāraṃ;manasikārākāram;avikṣepākāram;avasthānākāraṃ;ratnasaṃjñākāraṃ;bhaiṣajyasaṃjñākāraṃ;kleśavyādhiśamanākāraṃ;smṛtibhājanākāraṃ;gatibodhanākāraṃ;matirocanākāraṃ;buddhipraveśākāram;atṛptabuddhadharmaśravaṇākāraṃ;tyāgavṛṃhaṇākāraṃ;dāntājāneyākāraṃ;bahuśrutasevanākāraṃ;satkṛtyaprītyanubhavanākāraṃ;kāyaudbilyākāraṃ;cittaprahlādanākāram;aparikhedaśravaṇākāram;arthaśravaṇākāraṃ;dharmaśravaṇākāraṃ;pratipattiśravaṇākāraṃ;paradeśanāśravaṇākāram;aśrutaśravaṇākāram;abhijñāśravaṇākāram;ananyayānāspṛhaṇākāraṃ;pāramitāśravaṇākāraṃ;bodhisattvapiṭakaśravaṇākāraṃ;saṃgrahavastuśravaṇākāram;upāyakauśalyaśravaṇākāraṃ;brahmavihāraśravaṇākāraṃ;smṛtisaṃprajanyaśravaṇākāram;utpādakauśalyaśravaṇākāram;anutpādakauśalyaśravaṇākāram;aśubhākāraṃ;maitryākāraṃ;pratītyasamutpādākāraṃ;anityākāraṃ;duḥkhākāram;anātmākāraṃ;śāntākāraṃ;śūnyatākāram;animittākāram;apraṇihitākāram;anabhisaṃskārākāraṃ;kuśalābhisaṃskārākāraṃ;satyādhiṣṭhānākāram;avipraṇāśākāraṃ;svādhīnākāraṃ;svacittārakṣaṇākāraṃ;vīryasyāśraṃsanākāraṃ;dharmanidhyaptyākāraṃ;kleśavipakṣākāraṃ;svapakṣaparirakṣaṇākāraṃ;parapakṣakleśanigrahākāraṃ;saptadhanasamavasaraṇākāraṃ;sarvadāridryopacchedākāraṃ;sarvavidvatpraśastākāraṃ;pāṇḍitābhinandanākāram;āryasaṃmatākāram;anāryaprasādanākāraṃ;satyadarśanākāraṃ;skandhadoṣavivarjanākāraṃ;saṃskṛtadoṣaparitulanākāram;arthapratiśaraṇākāraṃ;dharmapratiśaraṇākāraṃ;jñānapratiśaraṇākāraṃ;nītārthapratiśaraṇākāraṃ;sarvapāpākaraṇākāram;ātmaparahitākāraṃ;sukṛtakarmānanutapyanākāraṃ;viśeṣagamanākāraṃ;sarvabuddhadharmapratilābhākāram.

a) [The essence (svabhāva), form (ākāra) or cause (hetu) of insight (prajñā):] What is the form of learning of the bodhisattvas?It has eighty-four, namely, 1) the form of eagerness;2) the form of intention;3) the form of determination;4) the form of practice;5) the form of spiritual friends;6) the form of no pride;7) the form of no carelessness;8) the form of respect;9) the form of accordance with instruction;10) the form of good speech;11) the form of serving;12) the form of attentive hearing;13) the form of mental effort;14) the form of no divertedness;15) the form of stability;16) the form of having the concept of [learning (śruta), or hearing the true religion (saddharma), as] a jewel;17) the form of having the concept of [learning (śruta) as] a medicine [since learning takes away the three kinds of poison (= rāga, dveṣa, moha) ];18) [and thus it is] the form of appeasement of the sickness of vices;19) the form of vessel of remembrance;20) the form of comprehension through understanding;21) the form of desire for intelligence;22) the form of entering into consciousness;23) the form of never getting tired of listening to the religion of the Buddha;24) the form of increasing renunciation;25) the form of being disciplined and well trained;26) the form of serving those with great learning;27) the form of feeling joy when paying respect;28) the form of feeling well in body;29) the form of happiness in thought;30) the form of indefatigable listening;31) the form of listening to the meaning [which is extinction (nirvāṇa), the fruit of the holy path (āryamārga) ];32) the form of listening to the religious teachings;33) the form of listening to the way of progress [the holy eightfold path (āryâṣṭâṅgamārga), etc.];34) the form of listening to the teachings of others [giving up holding on to one’s own views (svadṛṣṭiparāmarṣa), being thus without conceitedness (nirmāṇa) ];35) the form of listening to what has not been heard before;36) the form of listening to [the teachings on] supernormal powers;37) the form of having no wish for other religious ways;38) the form of listening to [the teachings on] the perfections;39) the form of listening to the collected teachings of the bodhisattvas;40) the form of listening to the [teachings on] ways of attracting beings;41) the form of listening to [teachings on] skill in expedient means;42) the form of listening to [teachings on] pure behaviour;43) the form of listening to [the teachings on] recollection and awareness;44) the form of listening to skill concerning origination;45) the form of listening to skill concerning the unoriginated;46) the form of [meditation on] the ugly;47) the form of friendliness;48) the form of dependent origination [the antidotes of cupidity, aversion and bewilderment (rāgadveṣamohapratipakṣa), which originate from learning (śruta) ];49) the form of impermanence [in the way that all conditioned things are momentary (kṣaṇikaṃ sarve saṃskārāḥ) ];50) the form of suffering;51) the form of egolessness;52) the form of peace;53) the form of emptiness;54) the form of no distinguishing marks;55) the form of nothing to be longed for;56) the form of the unconditioned;57) the form of bringing the good about;58) the form of the magical power of truth;59) the form of non-disappearance [of action and its maturing fruit (karmaphalavipāka) ];60) the form of being self-contained;61) the form of protecting one’s own thoughts [by not doing things not to be done];62) the form of not losing vigour;63) the form of introspection into the moments of existence;64) the form of contrast to vices;65) the form of protecting one’s own position [the position of the bodhisattva, to wit, the pure moments of existence (vaiyavadānikadharma) and the beings belonging to his retinue; (tatparivāraparyāpanna); protecting the position so it will not be attacked by others in the way that it will get into the power of the vices (kleśavaśa) ];66) the form of suppressing the vices and the other positions [of the Evil Ones and the heretics, etc. (māratīrthikâdi) ];67) the form of attaining the seven kinds of [religious] riches;68) [and thus] the form of abolition of all poverty;69) the form of being praised by all the learned;70) the form of being a joy to the wise;(p. 63) 71) the form of being approved by the holy;72) the form of giving faith to the unholy;73) the form of seeing the truth;74) the form of avoiding the imperfections in the parts of the personality;75) the form of considering the imperfections of the conditioned;76) the form of reliance on the meaning;77) the form of reliance on religion;78) the form of reliance on knowledge;79) the form of reliance on explicit meaning;80) the form of not doing any sin;81) the form of doing good both to oneself and the others;82) the form of a good deed [since learning itself is the essence of the good (śrutam eva kuśalasvabhāvaḥ) and thus], also no regret;83) the form of being [gradually] distinguished;[and to conclude] 84) the form of attaining all the qualities of a buddha [as they are all based upon learning (śruta) ].

’di lta ste ’dun pa’i rnam pa daṅ źes bya ba la sogs pas thos pa’i rnam pa brgyad cu rtsa bźi po de dag gaṅ yin pa ston te, ’dun pa ni chos ñan par ’dod pa la bya ste, ñan par ’dod pa las thos pa daṅ śes rab ’byuṅ gi ’dod pa med na mi ’byuṅ bas de’i phyir ’dun pa ni śes rab ’byuṅ ba’i rgyur rig par bya’o. yaṅ na thos pa las ’dun pa’i rnam pa ’byuṅ gi ma thos pa las ma yin pas thos pa ni ’dun pa ’byuṅ ba’i rgyu yin te; ’dun pa daṅ thos pa gñis gcig gi rgyu gcig yin par blta’o. yaṅ na śes rab kyi raṅ bźin ji lta bu źes dris pa na, ’dun pa’i rnam pa źes bya ba ni śes rab de ’dun pa’i raṅ bźin źes bya ba’i don to. de bźin du rnam pa’i sgra ni bsam pa’i rnam pa la sogs pa lhag pa rnams la yaṅ sbyar ro – "Eagerness (chanda) is "the wish to listen to religious teachings (dharmaśravaṇakāma)". (1) From the wish to listen (śravaṇakāma) learning (śruta) and insight (prajñā) arise, without the wish they do not; thus eagerness is to be understood as the cause (hetu) by which insight arises. Or (atha vā), (2) from learning (śruta) eagerness (chanda) arises, from no learning it does not; thus learning is the cause (hetu) by which eagerness (chanda) arises; and thus eagerness and learning (namely insight, prajñā) are the cause of each other (chandaśrutayor itaritarahetutvaṃ draṣṭavyam). Or (atha vā), (3) if asking what the essence (svabhāva) of insight (prajñā) is: "It has the form of eagerness" should be taken in the meaning "that insight has the essence of eagerness" (chandākāram iti sā prajñā chandasvabhāvety arthaḥ). In the following items, the form of intention etc., the word form should be understood accordingly." The alternatives are: 1. chanda cause of śruta and prajñā; chanda cause of prajñā; 2. śruta cause of chanda; chanda and śruta (=prajñā) cause of each other; 3. chanda essence of prajñā.bsam pa’i rnam pa ni goṅ du bsam pa mi zad pa’i skabs su rgya cher bśad pa la bya’o. de yaṅ mdor bsdu na bsam pa rnam pa gñis te, phan par bya ba’i bsam pa daṅ, bde bar bya ba’i bsam pa’o. de la phan par bya ba’i bsam pa ni mi dge ba’i gnas nas bton nas dge ba’i gnas su ’god par ’dod pa gaṅ yin pa’o; bde bar bya ba’i bsam pa ni sems can phoṅs pa daṅ, mgon med pa daṅ, rten med pa rnams la ñon moṅs pa can spaṅs te phan pa’i dṅos po bsgrub par ’dod pa gaṅ yin pa’o. Besides referring to the section on āśaya, this short definition is given by quoting from Bbh p. 1817-21: hitādhyāśayaś ca sukhādhyāśayaś ca. tatra hitādhyāśayaḥ yā akuśalāt sthānād vyutthāpya kuśale sthāne pratiṣṭhāpanakāmatā. sukhādhyāśayo yā vighātinām anāthānām apratisaraṇānāṃ sattvānāṃ kliṣṭavarjitānugrāhakavastūpasaṃharaṇakāmatā. Note that the definition from Bbh is that of adhyāśaya, not that of āśaya as in ṭ, showing the close connection between the two concepts.lhag pa’i bsam pa’i rnam pa ni goṅ du lhag pa’i bsam pa mi zad pa’i skabs su rgya cher bśad pa la bya’o.89b2-90a2 refers to the section on the topic, but gives besides a shorter definition: sbyor ba’i rnam pa ni sbyor ba mi zad pa’i skabs su rgya cher bśad pa la bya’o. de yaṅ mdor bsdus na rnam pa drug ste: 1) phoṅs pa sel ba’i sbyor ba daṅ, 2) mos pa la sbyor ba daṅ, 3) bsgrub pa la sbyor ba daṅ, 4) śes bźin du srid par skye ba la sbyor ba daṅ, 5) tshogs yoṅs su rdzogs par sbyor ba daṅ, 6) dka’ bar spyod pa bzod pa la sbyor ba’o. 1) sems can dṅos po gaṅ gis phoṅs pa de la de gtoṅ ba ni phoṅs pa sel ba la sbyor ba źes bya ste, de yaṅ sbyin pa mi zad pa’i skabs su zas ’dod pa la zas sbyin par byed pa daṅ btuṅ ba ’dod pa la btuṅ ba sbyin par byed pa źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs pa’o. 2) mos pa la sbyor bar byed pa ni gaṅ zag la bdag med pa daṅ chos la bdag med pa’i mtshan ñid de bźin ñid la mos par byed pa’o. 3) sgrub pa la sbyor bar byed pa ni rtag tu gźan gyi don sgrub par byed pa ste, gaṅ sbyor ba mi zad pa’i skabs su dge ba’i rtsa ba la rab tu gzud pa’i phyir sems can byaṅ chub kyi sems ’dzin du ’jug pa’i bsam pa ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i sbyor ba mi zad pa’o źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs pa’o. 4) śes bźin du srid par skye ba la sbyor ba ni las daṅ ñon moṅs pa’i dbaṅ gis khams gsum du skye ba ni ma yin gyi, smon lam gyis śes bźin du ’khor bar skye ba’o. 5) tshogs yoṅs su rdzogs par bya ba la sbyor ba ni bsod nams daṅ ye śes kyi tshogs rdzogs par bya ba’i phyir pha rol tu phyin pa drug la sbyod pa ste, gaṅ goṅ du sbyin pa mi zad pa’i bsam pa ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i sbyor ba mi zad pa ste źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs so. 6) dka’ bar spyod pa bzod pa la sbyor ba ni sems can yoṅs su smin par bya ba daṅ saṅs rgyas kyi chos yoṅs su smin par bya ba’i phyir naṅ gi sdug bsṅal mgo daṅ rkaṅ lag la sogs pa btaṅ ba daṅ, phyi’i sdug bsṅal graṅ ba daṅ tsha ba la sogs pa bzod pa ste, de yaṅ goṅ du btsun pa śa ra dva ti’i bu bźi po ’di dag ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’ rnams kyi sbyor ba mi zad pa ste, bźi gaṅ źe na? byaṅ chub kyi sems kyi sbyor ba mi zad pa daṅ, chos sbyin pa ston pa’i sbyor ba mi zad pa daṅ, sems can yoṅs su smin par byed pa’i sbyor ba mi zad pa la sogs pas bstan to. The six items refer to important loci on the subject supra.dge ba’i bśes gñen gyi rnam pa źes bya ba la 1) bskyod par byed pa daṅ, 2) ’jog par byed pa daṅ, 3) stobs par byed pa daṅ, 4) skyabs dpag tu med par byed pa ni dge ba’i bśes gñen źes bya’o. de la 1) bskyod par byed pa ni srog gcod pa la sogs pa mi dge ba bcu spyod pa las bskyod par byed pa ste, las ṅan pa spoṅ du ’dzud ces bya ba’i don to. 2) ’jog par byed pa ni srog gcod pa las ldog pa la sogs pa dge ba bcu la ’god par byed pa’o. 3) stobs par byed pa ni lha daṅ mi’i bde ba sbyin par byed pa nas bla na med pa’i byaṅ chub kyi ’bras bu’i bar du sbyin pa daṅ ’thob pa byed pa’o. 4) skyabs dpag tu med par byed pa ni mu stegs can la sogs pa’i lta ba ṅan par mi ltuṅ bar skyob pa daṅ, ñan thos la sogs pa’i theg pa dman par mi ltuṅ bar skyob pa daṅ, ’khor ba’i lam ṅan par mi ltuṅ ba skyob pa daṅ, sdug bsṅal gyi gnas ṅan soṅ du mi ltuṅ bar skyob pa’o. chos thos pa las sems can thams cad 1) mi dge ba las bskyod par byed pa daṅ, 2) dge ba la ’jog par byed pa daṅ, 3) ’bras bu stobs par byed pa daṅ, 4) sdug bsṅal dpag tu med pa las skyob par byed pas na dge ba’i bśes gñen gyi rnam pa źes bya’o. No exact counterpart has been found, but cf. Bbh p. 23713ff: tatra katibhir ākāraiḥ samanvāgataṃ bodhisattvasya kalyāṇamitraṃ veditavyam ...ṅa rgyal med pa ni cho rigs daṅ śes ñen la sogs pas mi sñems pa’o.bag yod pa ni bag med pa’i gñen po ste, bag med pa yaṅ gźan las ’byuṅ ba daṅ, bdag las ’byuṅ ba rnam pa gñis yod de; gźan las ’byuṅ ba yaṅ rnam pa gñis te, byur las byuṅ ba daṅ, sems can las byuṅ ba’o: de la byur las byuṅ ba ni tshe rabs sṅa ma’i mi dge ba’i las kyi ’dod chags la sogs pa mi dge ba’i rtsa ba ’byuṅ ba daṅ, srog gcod pa la sogs pa mi dge ba’i las byed pa’o. sems can las byuṅ ba ni ’dod chags daṅ źe sdaṅ skye bar ’gyur ba’i yul ñe bar ’oṅs pas ’dod chags la sogs pa ñon moṅs pa ’byuṅ ba’o. bdag las ’byuṅ ba yaṅ rnam pa gñis te, lus kyi ’du ’dzi las ’byuṅ ba daṅ, log pa’i rnam par rtog pa las ’byuṅ ba’o: de la lus kyi ’du ’dzi las ’byuṅ ba ni bdag ñid khye’u daṅ, bu mo daṅ, ’gro ba bzaṅ mo daṅ, rgyal rigs daṅ, bram ze’i rigs la sogs pa daṅ ’dra bar mos pas ñon moṅs pa ’byuṅ ba’o. log pa’i rnam par rtog pa las ’byuṅ ba ni ’dod pa daṅ ’dun pa daṅ gnod sems la sogs pa la rtog pa’i rgyus ñon moṅs pa ’byuṅ ba ste, thos pa las de dag sṅon ’byuṅ ba yaṅ, spoṅ bar byed la, phyis kyaṅ mi ’byuṅ bar byed pas na bag yod pa’i rnam pa źes bya’o.gus par byed pa ni chos daṅ chos smra ba la brñas pa med pa ste, mdo las: dge sloṅ dag, ri dags kyi rgyal po seṅ ge ni ri boṅ la mchoṅ na yaṅ bsgrims te, mchoṅ gi ma bsgrims par ma yin no. rta daṅ glaṅ po la mchoṅ na yaṅ bsgrims te, mchoṅ gi ma bsgrims par ma yin no źes rgyas par gsuṅs pa bźin du chos daṅ chos smras pa la brñas pa med par byas nas gus par ñan pa’o.’thun par ’dzin pa ni mkhan po daṅ slob dpon la sogs pas ji skad bstan pa bźin du sgrub par byed pa’o.bka’ blo bde ba ni phyir mi ldog pa ñan pa daṅ spyod lam gus pa bstan pa’o.bsñen bkur byed pa ni chos daṅ chos smra ba la ci rigs par phyag ’tshal ba la sogs pa lus daṅ ṅag gis rim gro byed pa’o. yaṅ na bsñen bkur mi byed pa’i gñen po ni bsñen bkur byed pa ste, bsñen bkur med pa ni ñan pa khri mtho la, ’chad pa khri dma’ ba la bźag ciṅ, rkaṅ lag brkyaṅ ba daṅ kha glal ba la sogs pas ṅan ṅon ñan pa ste, thos pa daṅ ldan pa rnams ni chos bla mar byed pa de lta bu med de, de bas na bsñen bkur byed pa’i rnam pa źes bya’o.rna ba blags te ñan pa ni phyi rol du g-yeṅ ba daṅ naṅ du gñid daṅ rmugs pas sems bsdus pa chos ñan pa’i dri ma gñis med par ñan pa ste, mdo las kyaṅ: dge sloṅ dag gñis po ’di dag ni chos ñan pa’i dri ma ste, de khyed rnams kyis spaṅ bar bya’o. gñis gaṅ źe na? sems rgod pa daṅ źum pa’o, źes gsuṅs pa’i phyir ro.yid la byed pa ni ji skad bstan pa bźin du chos ñid phyin ci ma log pa daṅ, dgoṅs pa phyin ci ma log par ’dzin pa ste, de la chos ñid phyin ci ma log par ’dzin pa ni ma rig pa’i rkyen gyis ’du byed la sogs pa ’byuṅ gi rgyu med pa daṅ mi mthun pa’i rgyu las skye bar mi rtog pa’o; dgoṅs pa phyin ci ma log pa ’dzin pa ni tshor ba thams cad sdug bsṅal ba źes gsuṅs pa la, bde ba’i tshor ba daṅ gñis ka ma yin pa’i tshor ba raṅ bźin gyis sdug bsṅal ba ni ma yin gyi, ’gyur ba daṅ ’du byed kyi ’du byed la dgoṅs pa la sogs pa rtogs pa’o.rnam par mi g-yeṅ ba ni g-yeṅ ba rnam pa gsum po raṅ bźin gyis g-yeṅ ba daṅ, phyi rol du g-yeṅ ba daṅ, naṅ du g-yeṅ ba med pa ste, de la raṅ bźin gyis g-yeṅ ba ni chos ñan pa’i tshe mig la sogs pa’i rnam par śes pa rnams rnam pa sna tshogs su rtog pa ’jug pa’o; phyi rol du g-yeṅ ba ni chos ñan pa’i tshe ñan par mi ’dod ciṅ skyo ba skye la gzugs la sogs pa la rtog pa ’byuṅ ba’o; naṅ du g-yeṅ ba ni chos ñan pa’i tshe źum pa’am rgod pa’i dbaṅ du gyur pa’o.gnas ni lus kyi spyod lam mi rgod pa ste, gnas gcig na ’dug ciṅ ñan pa’o.rin po cher ’du śes pa ni thos pa de ñid rin po che daṅ ’dra bar dkon pas ’du śes nas ñan pa la bya’o; yaṅ na dam pa’i chos ñan pa ni phan pa daṅ bde ba’i rgyur ’gyur ba daṅ śin tu dkon pa daṅ, bsgrub dka’ bar ’du śes bskyed nas ñan pa ni rin po cher ’du śes pa’i rnam pa źes bya’o; de la phan pa’i rgyur ’gyur ba ni lha daṅ mi’i bde ba nas mya ṅan las ’das pa’i bar gyi bde ba ’thob pa’i rgyu yin pa’i phyir ro, bde ba’i rgyur ’gyur ba ni mu stegs can gyi dka’ thub bdag ñid ṅal bar byed pa’i mtha’ daṅ ’dod pa la loṅs spyod pa rnams kyi ’dod pa’i bsod nams kyi mtha’ gñis spaṅs pa dbu ma’i lam bde ba la ’jug pa’i rgyu yin pa’i phyir ro; śin tu dkon pa ni de bźin gśegs pa brgya lam na ’jig rten du ’byuṅ źiṅ dam pa’i chos bśad pa yaṅ brgya lam na ’byuṅ ba’i phyir ro; bsgrub par dka’ ba ni de bźin gśegs pa’i gsuṅ rab kyi tshig bźi pa’i tshigs su bcad pa gcig tsam mñan pa yaṅ bsod nams daṅ ye śes kyi tshogs dpag tu med pas bsgrub dgos pa’i phyir ro.sman du ’du śes pa ni thos pas dug gsum gyi nad sel bar ’gyur ba’i phyir te, de bas na ñon moṅs pa’i nad thams cad źi bar byed pa’i rnam pa źes tshig goṅ ma gsal bar bśad do.dran pa’i snod ces bya ba la, dran pa ñid snod yin pas na dran pa’i snod de, dran pa’i sgras ni thos pa’i śes rab la bya’o, snod kyi sgras ni mi brjed pa’i gźi la bya ste, thos pa las yid gźuṅs pa ’byuṅ ste, mi brjed pa’i gźi byed pas na thos pa ni dran pa’i snod kyi rnam pa źes bya’o. rtogs pa śes pa ni bsam pa’i śes rab la bya ste, bsam pa’i śes rab kyaṅ mñam par bźag pa daṅ ma bźag pa’i bye brag gis rnam pa gñis te, de la rtogs pa des śes pas na rtogs pa śes pa źes bya ste, rtogs pa śes pa’i sgras ni mñam par bźag pa’i śes rab la bya’o. blo gros ’dod pa źes bya ba la blo gros kyi sgra ni mñam par bźag pa’i śes rab la bya ste, ’di ltar thos pa daṅ ldan pa blo che ba la dga’ bar ’gyur ba’am, yaṅ na ’dod pa źes bya ba ’bar ba’am gsal ba lta bu la bya ste, thos pa la blo gros gsal bar ’gyur bas na blo gros ’dod pa’i rnam pa źes bya’o. blo bsgoms pa las byuṅ ba’i śes rab la bya la, ’jug pa ni goms par byed pa la bya ste, ’di ltar thos pa las blo la ’dris śiṅ goms pa ’byuṅ ba na thos pa ni blo la ’jug pa’i rnam pa źes bya’o. yaṅ na dran pa de’i snod yin pas na dran pa’i snod de, dran pa źes bya ba ni sṅon ji ltar bzuṅ ba’i chos daṅ don mi brjed pa’o, dran pa de’i snod ni thos pa’i śes rab ste, sṅon thos pa’i gźi las dran pa ’byuṅ gi ma thos pa las ni ma yin pa’i phyir ro. blo de la ’jug pas na blo la ’jug pa ste, blo ni thogs pa daṅ chags pa med pa’i ye śes la bya’o, ’jug pa ni mṅon sum du byed pa ste, thos pa las de bźin rtogs pa’i ye śes mṅon sum du ’gyur pas na thos pa ni blo la ’jug pa’i rnam pa źes bya’o. yaṅ na blo ’dis ’jug pas na blo la ’jug pa ste, blo ni bsgom pa’i śes rab la ’jug pa ni brjod du med pa’i bdag ñid chos bdag med pa rtogs pa la bya ste, bsgom pa’i śes rab kyis de bźin rtogs par ’gyur ba’i phyir ro, de’i rgyu yaṅ thos pa’i śes rab yin te, de bas na skabs ’dir yaṅ thos pa ni blo la ’jug pa’i rnam pa yin par sbyar ro.saṅs rgyas kyi chos ni ñan thos daṅ raṅ saṅs rgyas kyi theg pa daṅ theg pa bla na med pa ste, mi ṅoms par ñan pa ni de dag ñan pa la chog mi śes pa’o.gtoṅ ba ni ji skad du thos pa’i chos rnams ’chad pa’o, spel ba ni gaṅ zag ’ga’ tsam la phyogs gcig tsam du bar ’ga’ ’chad pa ma yin źiṅ, sems can thams cad la phyogs kun tu rtag tu ’chad pa’o. yaṅ na gtoṅ ba spel ba ni sems kyi rgyan daṅ, sems kyi yo byad daṅ, rnal ’byor gyi tshogs daṅ, don gyi mchog thob par bya ba’i phyir kha na ma tho ba med pa’i sbyin pa sbyin par byed pa’o. de la 1) sus sbyin par byed, 2) su la sbyin par byed, 3) ci źig sbyin par byed, 4) cis sbyin par byed, 5) ji ltar sbyin par byed, 6) ci’i phyir sbyin par byed ce na? smras pa: 1) sus sbyin par byed pa ni thos pa daṅ ldan pa gtoṅ ba po’i gaṅ zag gis so. 2) su la sbyin par byed pa ni bźi la ste, sdug bsṅal ba daṅ, phan ’dogs pa daṅ, sdug pa daṅ, khyad par can la sbyin par byed do; de la sdug bsṅal ba ni bza’ ba daṅ bgo ba la sogs pas phoṅs pa mgon daṅ skyabs med pa’i bram ze daṅ tshoṅ pa daṅ gdol ba la sogs pa’o; phan ’dogs pa ni pha ma daṅ sdug bsṅal dpag tu med par źugs pa las ’byin pa’i gaṅ zag rnams so; sdug pa ni smos ’drin gaṅ dag de la byams pa’am gtam ’dres pa daṅ, phebs par smra ba daṅ, ’grogs bśes rnams so. khyad par can ni gaṅ ñon moṅs pa gdul ba la źugs pa’am, ñon moṅs pa btul ba’i ’bras bu la gnas pa rnams so, yaṅ na byaṅ chub sems dpa’i sbyin pa’i gnas ni sems can thams cad de su la sbyin pa ni sems can thams cad la’o. 3) ci źig sbyin pa ni phyi daṅ naṅ gi dṅos po’o. 4) cis sbyin pa ni sems mṅon par ’du byed pa yid kyi las chags med pa daṅ gtoṅ ba’i lus daṅ ṅag gi las kyis so. 5) ji ltar sbyin pa ni ma ’oṅs pa la blta ba daṅ ’bras bu mthoṅ ba’i dad pas sbyin par byed pa daṅ, brñas pa med par raṅ gi lag nas sbyin par byed pa’o. 6) ci’i phyir sbyin pa ni sems can thams cad la sñiṅ rje’i rgyus sbyin pa ste, sbyin pa de lta bu yaṅ sems can thams cad la sñiṅ brtse ba daṅ ldan pa, loṅs spyod thams cad rmi lam daṅ ’dra bar sñiṅ po med par ’dzin pa, gźan gyi don la gtso bor byed pa’i gaṅ zag thos pa daṅ ldan pa rnams la ’byuṅ gi gźan las ma yin pas na thos pa ni gtoṅ ba spel ba’i rnam pa źes bya’o.’dis ni chos daṅ zaṅ ziṅ gi sbyin pa rgya cher byed pa bstan te, dul ba ni gñen po bsgom pa ’phel ba daṅ ldan pas mig la sogs pa’i dbaṅ po rnams yul la mi ’jug pas dul ba daṅ, ’dod chags la sogs pa ñon moṅs pa rnams dul ba ste, de ni rgyu’o. de lta bu dul bas na caṅ śes pa źes bya ste, caṅ śes pa ni lam draṅ po nas ji srid bgrod par bya bar phyin par ’gro ba’i phyir te, ’di ni ’bras bu’o. de la lam draṅ po ni thabs daṅ śes rab zuṅ du ’brel ba daṅ, ’phags pa’i lam yan lag brgyad pa daṅ, ’phags pa’i bden pa bźi la sogs pa’o. bgrod par bya ba ni mya ṅan las ’das pa la bya ste, de lta bu ’phags pa’i lam rgyu daṅ ’bras bu’i mtshan ñid kyaṅ thos pa las byuṅ bas na thos pa ni dul źiṅ caṅ śes pa’i rnam pa źes bya’o.maṅ du thos pa la bsten pa ni maṅ po las rnam pa maṅ du chos gaṅ thog mar dge ba, bar du dge ba, tha mar dge ba, don bzaṅ po, tshig ’bru bzaṅ po, ma ’dres pa, yoṅs su rdzogs pa, yoṅs su dag pa, yoṅs su byaṅ ba źes bya ba la sogs pa’i mdo sde phal cher thos pa la bya’o. de la maṅ po la źes bya ba ni dge ba’i bśes gñen maṅ po la thos pa’o, rnam pa maṅ du źes bya ba ni chos de ñid la lan graṅs maṅ du thos pa ste, de yaṅ thos pa las ’byuṅ gi, ma thos pa las ma yin pas ni thos pa ni maṅ du thos pa la bsten pa’i rnam pa źes bya’o.bsti staṅ du byas te dga’ ba myoṅ bar byed pa źes bya ba la, bsti staṅ du byas pa ni chos daṅ chos smra ba’i gaṅ zag la lus daṅ ṅag daṅ yid kyi bsti staṅ du byas nas ñan pa ste, de ltar bsti staṅ du byas te mñan na dga’ źiṅ yid du ’oṅ ba bzaṅ po daṅ ldan par ’byuṅ bas na thos pa ni bsti staṅ du byas te dga’ ba myoṅ bar byed pa’i rnam pa źes bya’o. de la lus kyi bsti staṅ du byas te, ñan pa ni dus thams cad du lus kyi spyod lam mi mdzes pa mi ston ciṅ ’dud pa daṅ, thal mo sbyar ba la sogs pa byed pa’o. sems kyi gus par byas te ñan pa ni chos daṅ chos smra ba la gnod pa’i bsam pa daṅ, ’phyas gdags pa’i bsam pa daṅ, klan ka’i bsam pa med ciṅ, chos don du gñer ba’i bsam pas bla na med pa’i lam stobs par byed pa’i sñam du bsams nas ñan pa’o. ṅag gis gus par byed de ñan pa ni chos smra ba’i gaṅ zag la nams kyaṅ źer ’debs pa’i tshig mi smra źiṅ rtag tu de’i yon tan brjod par byed pa’o. thos pa las sems ma ’khrugs śiṅ źi gnas kyi mtshan ñid tiṅ ṅe ’dzin thob par ’gyur la, źi gnas daṅ ldan pas mig la sogs pa dbaṅ po’i yul la mi ’jug ciṅ sems rnam par rtog pa maṅ pos g-yen spyo ba med pas sems bde bar ’gyur la sems bde na lus bde bar ’gyur bas lus bde ba’i rnam pa źes bya’o. thos pa las śes rab kyi mtshan ñid lhag mthoṅ thob par ’gyur la, lhag mthoṅ gis the tshom daṅ yid gñis sel bar byed pas sems rab tu dga’ ba’i rnam pa źes bya’o.brtson ’grus kyi skyon gñis so, ha caṅ brtun drags pa daṅ, g-yel ba las phyis chos ñan pa mi ’dod pa’am, ched ’ga’ ñan ched ’ga’ mi ñan pa ni skyo ba ste, de lta bu med pas mi skyo bar ñan pa źes bya’o.don daṅ chos daṅ nan tan ñan pa’i rnam pa gsum gyis thob par bya ba daṅ, bśad par bya ba daṅ, bsgrub par bya ba ñan par rim bźin du bstan to.
de la don ni mya ṅan las ’das pa la bya ste, ’phags pa’i lam gyis bsgrubs pa’i ’bras bu yin pa’i phyir ro.
ṭ then explains the twelvefold structure of the canonical scriptures: chos ni gsuṅ rab kyi yan lag bcu gñis te: 1) mdo’i sde daṅ, 2) dbyaṅs kyis bsñad pa’i sde daṅ, 3) luṅ du bstan pa’i sde daṅ, 4) tshigs su bcad pa’i sde daṅ, 5) ched du brjod pa’i sde daṅ, 6) gleṅ gźi’i sde daṅ, 7) rtogs pa brjod pa’i sde daṅ, 8) de lta bu byuṅ ba’i sde daṅ, 9) skyes pa rabs kyi sde daṅ, 10) śin tu rgyas pa’i sde daṅ, 11) rmad du byuṅ ba’i chos kyi sde daṅ, 12) gtan la phab par bstan pa’i sde dag go. [1) de la mdo sde gaṅ źe na? bcom ldan ’das kyis de daṅ de dag tu gdula ba de daṅ de dag daṅ gdula ba’i spyod pa rnams las brtsams te, phuṅ po daṅ ldan pa’i gtam daṅ, skye mched daṅ ldan pa daṅ, rten ciṅ ’brel bar ’byuṅ ba daṅ ldan pa daṅ, zas daṅ bden pa daṅ khams daṅ ldan pa daṅ, ñan thos daṅ raṅ saṅs rgyas daṅ de bźin gśegs pa daṅ ldan pa daṅ, dran pa ñe bar gźag pa daṅ, yaṅ dag par spoṅ ba daṅ rdzu ’phrul gyi rkaṅ pa daṅ dbaṅ po daṅ stobs daṅ byaṅ chub kyi yan lag daṅ ldan pa daṅ, mi sdug pa daṅ dbugs rdub pa daṅ dbyuṅ ba daṅ bslab pa daṅ śes nas dad pa daṅ ldan pa’i gtam gsuṅs pa gaṅ yin pa dag yaṅ dag par sdud par byed pa rnams kyis yoṅs su bzuṅ nas bstan pa yun riṅ du gnas par bya ba’i don du miṅ daṅ tshig daṅ yi ge’i tshogs mthun pa dag gis ci rigs par rim gyis bkod ciṅ sbyar ba gaṅ yin pa’o. 2) dbyaṅs kyis bsñad pa’i sde ni gaṅ gi tha ma’i mjug tu tshigs su bcad pa mṅon par brjod pa daṅ, bkri ba’i don gyi mdo sde gaṅ yin pa’o. 3) luṅ du bstan pa’i sde ni gaṅ las ñan thos śi ’phos pa daṅ, dus byas pa daṅ, skye ba luṅ ston pa daṅ, ṅes pa’i don gyi mdo sde gaṅ yin pa’o. 4) tshigs su bcad pa’i sde ni rkyaṅ pas bśad pa ma yin pa ste, ’di ltar rtsa ba gñis pa’am, gsum pa’am, bźi pa’am, lṅa pa’am, rtsa ba drug par rtsa bsdebs te bśad pa gaṅ yin pa’o. 5) ched du brjod pa’i sde ni gaṅ zag gi miṅ daṅ rigs yoṅs su ma brjod ma bstan par phyis dam pa’i chos yun riṅ du gnas par bya ba’i phyir bśad pa’o. 6) gleṅ gźi’i sde ni gaṅ zag gi miṅ daṅ rigs yoṅs su brjod ciṅ bstan te bśad pa daṅ, gaṅ daṅ ’dul ba daṅ ldan pa’i byuṅ ba daṅ bcas, gleṅ gźi daṅ bcas pa so sor thar pa’i mdo sde gaṅ yin pa’o. 7) rtogs par brjod pa’i sde ni dpe daṅ bcas par bstan pa ste, dpe des don gyi raṅ bźin de rnam par gsal bar ’gyur ba gaṅ yin pa’o. 8) de lta bu byuṅ ba’i sde ni cuṅ zad sṅon gyi sbyor ba daṅ ldan pa gaṅ yin pa’o. 9) skyes pa rabs kyi sde ni ’das pa’i dus la brten te, bcom ldan ’das kyis ’chi ’pho daṅ skye ba de daṅ de dag tu byaṅ chub sems dpa’i spyod pa daṅ dka’ bar spyod pa bstan pa gaṅ yin pa’o. 10) śin tu rgyas pa’i sde ni gaṅ las bla na med pa yaṅ dag par rdzogs pa’i byaṅ chub daṅ stobs bcu daṅ, sgrib pa med pa’i ye śes yaṅ dag par sgrub pa’i phyir byaṅ chub sems dpa’ rnams kyi lam bstan pa gaṅ yin pa’o. 11) rmad du byuṅ ba’i chos kyi sde ni gaṅ las saṅs rgyas rnams daṅ saṅs rgyas kyi ñan thos rnams kyi thun moṅ daṅ, thun moṅ ma yin pa daṅ, de las gźan khyad par du ’phags pa’i yon tan khyad par can ṅo mtshar rmad du byuṅ bar grags pa dag bstan pa gaṅ yin pa’o. 12) gtan la phab par bstan pa’i sde ni mdo sde ’dren par byed ciṅ, mdo sde rnam par ’chad par byed pa, ma lta bu’i chos mṅon pa thams cad la bya’o. gsuṅ rab yan lag bcu gñis po de dag la mdo sde yaṅ yod, ’dul ba yaṅ yod, chos mṅon pa yaṅ yod de, de la re źig mdo sde daṅ, dbyaṅs kyis bsñad pa’i sde daṅ, luṅ du bstan pa’i sde daṅ, tshigs su bcad pa’i sde daṅ, ched du brjod pa’i sde daṅ, rtogs pa brjod pa’i sde daṅ, de lta bu byuṅ ba’i sde daṅ, skyes pa rabs kyi sde daṅ, śin tu rgyas pa’i sde daṅ, rmad du byuṅ ba’i chos kyi sde gaṅ yin pa ni mdo sde’o. gleṅ gźi’i sde gaṅ yin pa ni ’dul ba’o. gtan la phab par bstan pa’i sde gaṅ yin pa ni chos mṅon pa’o.] de la sde snod gsum pa de dag las mdo sde’i mtshan ñid ni chos rnams mdor bsdus nas ston pa’o. ’dul ba’i mtshan ñid ni chos daṅ don mṅon du byed pa ste, ñon moṅs pa btul na chos daṅ don mṅon du ’gyur ba’i phyir ro. chos mṅon pa’i mtshan ñid ni ṅes pa’i gtam gtan la ’bebs pas chos kyi loṅs spyod la rig par byed pa’o. de dag gi las ni mdo sde’i sde snod kyis the tshom ñe ba’i ñon moṅs pa sel bar byed do, ’dul ba’i sde snod kyis mtha’ gñis la sbyor ba’i ñe ba’i ñon moṅs pa sel bar byed do, chos mṅon pa’i sde snod kyis raṅ gi lta ba mchog tu ’dzin pa’i kun nas ñon moṅs pa sel bar byed pa’o.

arthopasaṃhitānāṃ brahmacaryopasaṃhitānām idam ucyate sūtram] / geyaṃ [katamat /] (6) yasyānte paryavasāne gāthā abhigītā / yac ca sūtraṃ neyārtham [idam ucyate geyaṃ] / vyākaraṇaṃ [katamat |] yasmiṃ chrāvako ’bhyatītakālagata upapattau vyākriyate / yac ca sūtraṃ nītārtham [idam ucyate vyākaraṇaṃ] / gāthā [katamā /] yā na gadyena bhāṣitā / api tu pādopanibandhena dvipadā vā tripadā vā catuṣpadā vā [katamat /] yat pudgalasya nāmagotraṃ parikīrtayitvā uddiśya bhāṣitam / (7B2) yac ca vinayapratisaṃyuktaṃ sotpattikaṃ sanidānaṃ prātimokṣasūtram [idam ucyate nidānaṃ] / avadānaṃ [katamat /] yat [katamat /] yad atītam adhvānam upādāya tatra tatra bhagavataḥ cyutyupapādeṣu bodhisatvacaryā duṣkaracaryā ākhyātā [idam ucyate jātakaṃ] / vaipulyaṃ [katamat /] yatra bodhisatvānāṃ mārgo deśyate anuttarāyai samyaksaṃbodhaye daśabalānāvaraṇajñānasamudāgamāya [idam ucyate vaipulyaṃ] / adbhutā dharmāḥ [katame /] yatra bu(3)ddhānāñ ca buddhaśrāvakāṇāñ ca [bhikṣūṇāñ ca bhikṣūṇīnāñ ca śikṣamāṇānāṃ gāthodānāvadānavṛttakajātakavaipulyādbhutadharmā iti / idaṃ tāvat sūtraṃ / yat punar āha nidānam ity / ayam ucyate vinayaḥ / yat punar āha upadeśā iti / ayam ucyate (5) abhidharmaḥ /
nan tan ’phags pa’i lam yan lag brgyad pa la sogs pa bsgrub par bya ba’i chos rnams la bya’o.
