Knowledge of the undivided essence of these things is the bodhisattva’s skill with the parts of personality (teṣām abhinnasvabhāvajñānaṃ bodhisattvasya skandhakauśalyam).
Cf. Msa. p. 1493-12:
kaḥ punar anityārtho yāvac chāntārthaḥ ity āha /
asadartho vikalpārthaḥ parikalpārtha eva ca/
vikalpopaśamārthaś ca dhīmatāṃ tac catuṣṭayaṃ//
bodhisatvānām asadartho ’nityārthaḥ / yan nityaṃ nāsti tad anityaṃ teṣāṃ yat parikalpitalakṣaṇaṃ / abhūtavikalpārtho duḥkhārtho yat paratantralakṣaṇaṃ / parikalpamātrārtho ’nātmārthaḥ / evaśabdenāvadhāraṇaṃ / parikalpita ātmā nāsti parikalpamātraṃ tv astīti parikalpitalakṣaṇasyābhāvārtho ’nātmārtha ity uktaṃ bhavati / vikalpopaśamārthaḥ śāntārthaḥ pariniṣpannalakṣaṇaṃ nirvāṇaṃ / kṣaṇabhaṅgārtho ’py anityārtho veditavyaḥ paratantralakṣaṇasya /
Cf. also Sūtrālaṃkāravṛttibhāṣya tsi fol. 132a3ff ji ltar na mi rtag pa’i don źes bya ba la sogs pa la .... which commentary on Msa also refers to Akṣ on the topic (cf. introduction, quotations o’, p’, q’ and r’ to Akṣ in Sūtrālaṃkāravṛttibhāṣya). The content of Sūtrālaṃkāravṛttibhāṣya is similar to ṭ, but cannot be regarded as a quotation.


de la byaṅ chub sems dpa’i khams la mkhas pa gaṅ źe na?

tatra katamad bodhisattvasya dhātukauśalyam?

2) What then is the bodhisattva’s skill with the spheres?

phuṅ po la mkhas pa bstan pa’i ’og tu khams la mkhas pa bstan pas na ji ltar bstan pa de bźin du bśad par ’dod nas de la byaṅ chub sems dpa’i khams la mkhas pa gaṅ źe na źes dris so. de la khams kyi don ni mtshan ñid ’dzin pa’i don to; yaṅ na rgyu’i don te, khams daṅ sa bon daṅ rigs ni rgyu’i miṅ gi rnam graṅs te, gaṅ la dmigs nas de bźin gśegs pa’i stobs daṅ mi ’jigs pa la sogs pa ’byuṅ ba’i rgyu ni khams źes bya la; de rtogs pa’i ye śes ni khams la mkhas pa źes bya ba’i phyir ro – "The meaning of sphere is the meaning of holding essential characteristics (tatra dhātvartho lakṣaṇadhāraṇārthaḥ); or, it has the meaning of cause; sphere, seed and type are synonyms of the word cause (atha vā hetvarthaḥ, dhātur bījaṃ gotraṃ hetuparyāyāḥ), depending on which cause the powers and intrepidities of the tathāgata arise (yaṃ hetum ālambya tathāgatabalavaiśāradyādyutpāda iti dhātuḥ). The knowledge which consists in the understanding of that is skill with the spheres (tadadhigamajñānaṃ dhātukauśalyam iti)." Cf. Śbh p. 38514-16.


gaṅ chos kyi dbyiṅs la ’jug pa’i ye śes so.

yad dharmadhātupraveśajñānam.

The knowledge [beyond thought-constructions (nirvikalpajñāna) ] of entering the sphere of total reality [which is the cause that produces the qualities (dharma) of disciples, isolated buddhas and Buddhas, the powers and intrepidities, etc., having the essential characteristic of being the highest meaning (paramārthalakṣaṇa) ].

de la byaṅ chub sems dpa’i khams la mkhas pa gaṅ źe na? gaṅ chos kyi dbyiṅs la ’jug pa’i ye śes so źes bya ba smos te, chos ni ñan thos daṅ raṅ saṅs rgyas daṅ saṅs rgyas kyi chos stobs daṅ mi ’jigs pa la sogs pa’o. chos de dag skyed pa’i rgyu ni chos kyi dbyiṅs źes bya ste, don dam pa stoṅ pa’i mtshan ñid do. chos kyi dbyiṅs de rtogs pa’i ye śes ni chos kyi dbyiṅs la ’jug pa’i ye śes źes bya ste, chos kyi dbyiṅs kyaṅ rnam par mi rtog pa’i ye śes kyis rtogs pas na ye śes kyi sgra ni ’dir rnam par mi rtog pa’i ye śes ñid la bya’o. de ni ’di skad du bstan pa yin te, mig la sogs pa khams so so’i mtshan ñid dmigs pa daṅ rten lta bus khoṅ du chud pa ni khams la mkhas par mi ’gyur gyi, gaṅ chos rnams kyi chos kyi dbyiṅs don dam pa’i mtshan ñid de rnam par mi rtog pa’i ye śes kyis rtogs na khams la mkhas pa yin no źes ston to.


chos kyi dbyiṅs ni sa’i khams yin mod kyi, chos kyi dbyiṅs sra ba’i mtshan ñid ni ma yin no;chos kyi dbyiṅs chu’i khams yin mod kyi, chos kyi dbyiṅs rlan pa’i mtshan ñid ni ma yin no;chos kyi dbyiṅs me’i khams yin mod kyi, chos kyi dbyiṅs yoṅs su smin par byed pa’i mtshan ñid ni ma yin no;chos kyi dbyiṅs rluṅ gi khams yin mod kyi, chos kyi dbyiṅs g-yo ba’i mtshan ñid ni ma yin no.

dharmadhātuḥ pṛthivīdhātur api na tu dharmadhātuḥ kaṭhinalakṣaṇaḥ;dharmadhātur abdhātur api na tu dharmadhātuḥ snehalakṣaṇaḥ;dharmadhātus tejodhātur api na tu dharmadhātuḥ paripācanalakṣaṇaḥ;dharmadhātur vāyudhātur api na tu dharmadhātuḥ samudīraṇalakṣaṇaḥ.

Even though the sphere of total reality is [the same as] the element of earth [since the element of earth is not different from total reality because it is, in the highest meaning (paramārthatas), essentially empty], the sphere of total reality does not have the essential characteristic of hardness [as this only exists in the wrong (viparīta) understanding of the naive (pṛthagjana) ];even though the sphere of total reality is the element of water, the sphere of total reality does not have the essential characteristic of moistness;even though the sphere of total reality is the element of fire, the sphere of total reality does not have the essential characteristic of ripening;even though the sphere of total reality is the element of wind, the sphere of total reality does not have the essential characteristic of motility.

chos kyi dbyiṅs gaṅ yin pa daṅ ji ltar na chos kyi dbyiṅs la ’jug par ’gyur ba bstan pa’i phyir chos kyi dbyiṅs sa’i khams yin mod kyi, chos kyi dbyiṅs sra ba’i mtshan ñid ni ma yin no źes bya ba smos te, don dam par sa’i khams kyaṅ ṅo bo ñid kyis stoṅ pas chos kyi dbyiṅs daṅ tha mi dad pa’i phyir chos kyi dbyiṅs sa’i khams yin no; gal te chos kyi dbyiṅs sa’i khams yin na, sa’i khams sra ba’i mtshan ñid yin pa bźin du chos kyi dbyiṅs kyaṅ sra ba’i mtshan ñid yin nam? sñam pa la chos kyi dbyiṅs sra ba’i mtshan ñid ni ma yin no źes bya ba smos te, sa’i khams ni sa’i raṅ bźin te, de’i raṅ bźin ni raṅ bźin gyis stoṅ pa dben pa yin pas sra ba ni byis pa so so’i skye bo rnams kyis phyin ci log tu rtogs pa ste, de’i mtshan ñid ma yin pas na chos kyi dbyiṅs sra ba’i mtshan ñid ni ma yin no źes gsuṅs so. de bźin du chu’i khams la sogs pa la yaṅ ci rigs par sbyar bar bya’o.
The contents of this section, and the next, are related to the idea of kṛtsnāyatana and the exercise of meditation to see the whole of reality in the particular elements. Cf. Daśa § 42: sarvadhātūn pṛthivīdhātāv adhimucya sarvam api pṛthivīdhātur evaikadhātur bhavati, etc., and further references in Edg. s. v.


chos kyi dbyiṅs mig gi khams yin mod kyi, chos kyi dbyiṅs lta ba’i mtshan ñid ni ma yin no;chos kyi dbyiṅs rna ba’i khams yin mod kyi, chos kyi dbyiṅs ñan pa’i mtshan ñid ni ma yin no;chos kyi dbyiṅs sna’i khams yin mod kyi, chos kyi dbyiṅs snom pa’i mtshan ñid ni ma yin no;chos kyi dbyiṅs lce’i khams yin mod kyi, chos kyi dbyiṅs myaṅ bar byed pa’i mtshan ñid ni ma yin no;chos kyi dbyiṅs lus kyi khams yin mod kyi, chos kyi dbyiṅs nom pa’i mtshan ñid ni ma yin no;chos kyi dbyiṅs yid kyi khams yin mod kyi, chos kyi dbyiṅs rnam par rig pa’i mtshan ñid ni ma yin no.

dharmadhātuś cakṣurdhātur api na tu dharmadhātur darśanalakṣaṇaḥ;dharmadhātuḥ śrotradhātur api na tu dharmadhātuḥ śravaṇalakṣaṇaḥ;dharmadhātur ghrāṇadhātur api na tu dharmadhātur ghrāṇalakṣaṇaḥ;dharmadhātur jihvādhātur api na tu dharmadhātū rasanalakṣaṇaḥ;dharmadhātuḥ kāyadhātur api na tu dharmadhātur āmarśalakṣaṇaḥ;dharmadhātur manodhātur api na tu dharmadhātur vijñaptilakṣaṇaḥ.

Even though the sphere of total reality is the sphere of the eye, the sphere of total reality does not have the essential characteristic of seeing;even though the sphere of total reality is the sphere of the ear, the sphere of total reality does not have the essential characteristic of hearing;even though the sphere of total reality is the sphere of the nose, the sphere of total reality does not have the essential characteristic of smelling;even though the sphere of total reality is the sphere of tongue, the sphere of total reality does not have the essential characteristic of tasting;even though the sphere of total reality is the sphere of body, the sphere of total reality does not have the essential characteristic of touch;even though the sphere of total reality is the sphere of mind, the sphere of total reality does not have the essential characteristic of cognition.




chos kyi dbyiṅs mig gi rnam par śes pa’i khams yin mod kyi, chos kyi dbyiṅs gzugs so sor rnam par rig pa’i mtshan ñid ni ma yin no;chos kyi dbyiṅs rna ba’i rnam par śes pa’i khams yin mod kyi, chos kyi dbyiṅs sgra so sor rnam par rig pa’i mtshan ñid ni ma yin no;chos kyi dbyiṅs sna’i rnam par śes pa’i khams yin mod kyi, chos kyi dbyiṅs dri so sor rnam par rig pa’i mtshan ñid ni ma yin no;chos kyi dbyiṅs lce’i rnam par śes pa’i khams yin mod kyi, chos kyi dbyiṅs ro so sor rnam par rig pa’i mtshan ñid ni ma yin no;chos kyi dbyiṅs lus kyi rnam par śes pa’i khams yin mod kyi, chos kyi dbyiṅs reg bya so sor rnam par rig pa’i mtshan ñid ni ma yin no;chos kyi dbyiṅs yid kyi rnam par śes pa’i khams yin mod kyi, chos kyi dbyiṅs chos so sor rnam par rig pa’i mtshan ñid ni ma yin no.

dharmadhātuś cakṣurvijñānadhātur api na tu dharmadhātū rūpaprativijñaptilakṣaṇaḥ;dharmadhātuḥ śrotravijñānadhātur api na tu dharmadhātuḥ śabdaprativijñaptilakṣaṇaḥ;dharmadhātur ghrāṇavijñānadhātur api na tu dharmadhātur gandhaprativijñaptilakṣaṇaḥ;dharmadhātur jihvāvijñānadhātur api na tu dharmadhātū rasaprativijñaptilakṣaṇaḥ;dharmadhātuḥ kāyavijñānadhātur api na tu dharmadhātuḥ spraṣtavyaprativijñaptilakṣaṇaḥ;dharmadhātur manovijñānadhātur api na tu dharmadhātur dharmaprativijñaptilakṣaṇaḥ.

Even though the sphere of total reality is the sphere of eye-consciousness, the sphere of total reality does not have the essential characteristic of recognition of form;even though the sphere of total reality is the sphere of ear-consciousness, the sphere of total reality does not have the essential characteristic of recognition of sound;even though the sphere of total reality is the sphere of nose-consciousness, the sphere of total reality does not have the essential characteristic of recognition of smell;even though the sphere of total reality is the sphere of tongue-consciousness, the sphere of total reality does not have the essential characteristic of recognition of taste;even though the sphere of total reality is the sphere of body-consciousness, the sphere of total reality does not have the essential characteristic of recognition of tangibles;even (p. 70) though the sphere of total reality is the sphere of mind-consciousness, the sphere of total reality does not have the essential characteristic of recognition of moments of existence.




chos kyi dbyiṅs gzugs kyi khams yin mod kyi, chos kyi dbyiṅs mig gi rnam par śes pas rnam par rig par bya ba’i mtshan ñid ni ma yin no;chos kyi dbyiṅs sgra’i khams yin mod kyi, chos kyi dbyiṅs rna ba’i rnam par śes pas rnam par rig par bya ba’i mtshan ñid ni ma yin no;chos kyi dbyiṅs dri’i khams yin mod kyi, chos kyi dbyiṅs sna’i rnam par śes pas rnam par rig par bya ba’i mtshan ñid ni ma yin no;chos kyi dbyiṅs ro’i khams yin mod kyi, chos kyi dbyiṅs lce’i rnam par śes pas rnam par rig par bya ba’i mtshan ñid ni ma yin no;chos kyi dbyiṅs reg bya’i khams yin mod kyi, chos kyi dbyiṅs lus kyi rnam par śes pas rnam par rig par bya ba’i mtshan ñid ni ma yin no;chos kyi dbyiṅs chos kyi khams yin mod kyi, chos kyi dbyiṅs yid kyi rnam par śes pas rnam par rig par bya ba’i mtshan ñid ni ma yin no.chos kyi dbyiṅs gzugs kyi khams yin mod kyi, chos kyi dbyiṅs gzugs su rnam par rig pa’i mtshan ñid ni ma yin no;chos kyi dbyiṅs sgra’i khams yin mod kyi, chos kyi dbyiṅs sgrar rnam par rig pa’i mtshan ñid ni ma yin no;chos kyi dbyiṅs dri’i khams yin mod kyi, chos kyi dbyiṅs drir rnam par rig pa’i mtshan ñid ni ma yin no;chos kyi dbyiṅs ro’i khams yin mod kyi, chos kyi dbyiṅs ror rnam par rig pa’i mtshan ñid ni ma yin no;chos kyi dbyiṅs reg bya’i khams yin mod kyi, chos kyi dbyiṅs reg byar rnam par rig pa’i mtshan ñid ni ma yin no;chos kyi dbyiṅs chos kyi khams yin mod kyi, chos kyi dbyiṅs chos su rnam par rig pa’i mtshan ñid ni ma yin no.chos kyi dbyiṅs daṅ bdag gi khams, de ni mtshuṅs so;chos kyi dbyiṅs daṅ ’dod pa’i khams daṅ, gzugs kyi khams daṅ, gzugs med pa’i khams, de ni mtshuṅs so;chos kyi dbyiṅs daṅ ’khor ba’i khams daṅ, mya ṅan las ’das pa’i dbyiṅs, de ni mtshuṅs so;chos kyi dbyiṅs daṅ sems can gyi khams daṅ, nam mkha’i khams daṅ, chos thams cad kyi khams, de ni mtshuṅs so.

dharmadhātuḥ rūpadhātur api na tu dharmadhātuḥ cakṣurvijñānavijñeyalakṣaṇaḥ;dharmadhātuḥ śabdadhātur api na tu dharmadhātuḥ śrotravijñānavijñeyalakṣaṇaḥ;dharmadhātur gandhadhātur api na tu dharmadhātur ghrāṇavijñānavijñeyalakṣaṇaḥ;dharmadhātū rasadhātur api na tu dharmadhātur jihvāvijñānavijñeyalakṣaṇaḥ;dharmadhātuḥ spraṣṭavyadhātur api na tu dharmadhātur kāyavijñānavijñeyalakṣaṇaḥ;dharmadhātur dharmadhātur api na tu dharmadhātur manovijñānavijñeyalakṣaṇaḥ.dharmadhātū rūpadhātur api na tu dharmadhātū rūpavijñātalakṣaṇaḥ;dharmadhātuḥ śabdadhātur api na tu dharmadhātuḥ śabdavijñātalakṣaṇaḥ;dharmadhātur gandhadhātur api na tu dharmadhātur gandhavijñātalakṣaṇaḥ;dharmadhātū rasadhātur api na tu dharmadhātū rasavijñātalakṣaṇaḥ;dharmadhātuḥ spraṣṭavyadhātur api na tu dharmadhātuḥ spraṣṭavyavijñātalakṣaṇaḥ;dharmadhātur dharmadhātur api na tu dharmadhātur dharmavijñātalakṣaṇaḥ.dharmadhātur ātmadhātuś ca tau samau;dharmadhātuḥ kāmadhātū rūpadhātur ārūpyadhātuś ca te samāḥ;dharmadhātuḥ kāmadhātur nirvāṇadhātuś ca te samāh;dharmadhātuḥ sattvadhātur ākāśadhātuḥ sarvadharmadhātuś ca te samāḥ.

Even though the sphere of total reality is the sphere of form, the sphere of total reality does not have the essential characteristic of being something to be known by eye-consciousness;even though the sphere of total reality is the sphere of sound, the sphere of total reality does not have the essential characteristic of being something to be known by ear-consciousness;even though the sphere of total reality is the sphere of smell, the sphere of total reality does not have the essential characteristic of being something to be known by nose-consciousness;even though the sphere of total reality is the sphere of taste, the sphere of total reality does not have the essential characteristic of being something to be known by tongue-consciousness;even though the sphere of total reality is the sphere of tangibles, the sphere of total reality does not have the essential characteristic of being something to be known by body-consciousness;even though the sphere of total reality is the sphere of moments of existence, the sphere of total reality does not have the essential characteristic of being something to be known by mind-consciousness.Even though the sphere of total reality is the sphere of form, the sphere of total reality does not have the essential characteristic of what is cognized as form;even though the sphere of total reality is the sphere of sound, the sphere of total reality does not have the essential characteristic of what is cognized as sound;even though the sphere of total reality is the sphere of smell, the sphere of total reality does not have the essential characteristic of what is cognized as smell;even though the sphere of total reality is the sphere of taste, the sphere of total reality does not have the essential characteristic of what is cognized as taste;even though the sphere of total reality is the sphere of tangibles, the sphere of total reality does not have the essential characteristic of what is cognized as tangibles;even though the sphere of total reality is the sphere of moments of existence, the sphere of total reality does not have the essential characteristic of what is cognized as moments of existence.The sphere of total reality and the sphere of the self are the same;the sphere of total reality and the world of passion, the world of form and the world of no form are the same;the sphere of total reality and the sphere of existence and the sphere of extinction are the same;the sphere of total reality, the sphere of beings, the sphere of space and the sphere of all moments of existence are the same.

chos kyi dbyiṅs gzugs kyi khams yin mod kyi, chos kyi dbyiṅs mig gi rnam par śes pas rnam par rig par bya ba’i mtshan ñid ni ma yin no źes bya ba daṅ ’og nas chos kyi dbyiṅs gzugs kyi khams yin mod kyi, gzugs su rnam par rig pa’i mtshan ñid ma yin no źes bya ba gñis la goṅ mas ni mig gi yul gyi bya ba mi byed pa ston te, ’og mas ni gzugs kyi mtshan ñid mi ’dzin pa bstan te, de bźin du sgra la sogs par yaṅ ci rigs par sbyar ro.
V. the preceding note.


ci’i phyir de mtshuṅs śe na?

kasya hetos te samāḥ?

Why are they the same?

ci’i phyir de mtshuṅs śe na źes bya ba ni bdag gi khams nas chos thams cad kyi khams kyi bar rnam pa sna tshogs su gnas na ci’i phyir de dag mtshuṅs śe na źes bya ba’i tha tshig go.


stoṅ pa ñid du mtshuṅs pas na, de ni mtshuṅs pa’o;mtshan ma med par mtshuṅs pa daṅ,smon pa med par mtshuṅs pa daṅ,mṅon par ’du mi byed par mtshuṅs pa daṅ,skye ba med par mtshuṅs pa daṅ,’byuṅ ba med par mtshuṅs pa daṅ,dṅos po med par mtshuṅs pa daṅ,chos thams cad tha dad pa med par mtshuṅs pa daṅ,sgrib pa med par mtshuṅs pa daṅ,nam mkha’i khams su mtshuṅs pa daṅ,mya ṅan las ’das pa’i dbyiṅs su mtshuṅs pas de dag mtshuṅs pa’o.

te śūnyatāsamatvāt samā,animittasamatvād,apraṇihitasamatvād,asaṃskārasamatvād,ajātasamatvād,anutpādasamatvāt,abhāvasamatvād,sarvadharmāsaṃbhedasamatvād,anāvaraṇasamatvād,ākāśadhātusamatvāt,te nirvāṇadhātusamatvāt samāh.

They are the same because of their same emptiness,because of their same absence of distinguishing marks,because of their same absence of longing,because of their same absence of formative factors,because of their same absence of birth,because of their same absence of origination,because of their same absence of existence,because of their same homogeneity of all moments of existence,because of their same absence of obscurations,because of their sameness with the sphere of empty space,because of their sameness with the sphere of extinction they are the same.

stoṅ pa ñid du mtshuṅs pas na de ni mtshuṅs pa’o źes bya ba la gaṅ zag gi dṅos po daṅ chos kyi dṅos po raṅ bźin med pa ni stoṅ pa ñid de, ji ltar bdag gi khams la gaṅ zag gi dṅos po med pa daṅ chos kyi dṅos po med pas stoṅ pa yin pa, de bźin du nam mkha’i khams daṅ chos kyi khams de dag kyaṅ gaṅ zag gi dṅos po med pa daṅ chos kyi dṅos po med de stoṅ pa yin par ’dra bas na chos de dag mtshuṅs pa źes bya’o.
mtshan ma med par mtshuṅs pa źes bya ba la de ltar gaṅ zag daṅ chos kyi dṅos po med pas na sa daṅ, chu daṅ, me daṅ, rluṅ daṅ, zla ba daṅ, ñi ma daṅ, ri daṅ, rgya mtsho daṅ, chu kluṅ daṅ, mtsho daṅ, dgon pa daṅ, phyogs daṅ, yul la sogs pa’i dṅos po mtshan ma so sor chad pa’i dṅos po rnams yod pa ma yin pas na mtshan ma med pa źes bya’o.
de ltar na mtshan ma med pas na khams gsum thams cad khams gsum gyi rnam par mi snaṅ ba daṅ, mya ṅan las ’das pa yaṅ mya ṅan las ’das pa’i rnam par mi snaṅ ste, de dag gñi ga la yaṅ cuṅ zad kyaṅ ’dod pa med pa ni smon pa med pa’o.las dge ba daṅ mi dge bas ma bskyed ciṅ, las dge ba daṅ mi dge ba la spyod pa med pa ni mṅon par ’du mi byed pa’o, ’das pa’i dus su ma skyes pa ni skye ba med pa’o, ma ’oṅs pa’i dus su skye bar ’gyur ba med pa ni ’byuṅ ba med pa’o, da ltar gyi dus na gaṅ zag daṅ chos kyi dṅos por yod pa ma yin pa ni dṅos po med pa’o.bdag gi khams nas chos thams cad kyi khams kyi bar dag smos pa rnams don dam pa’i chos kyi dbyiṅs stoṅ pa ñid du ro gcig pa’i raṅ bźin te, mtshan ñid so sor mi ’dra ba med pas na chos thams cad tha dad pa med par mtshuṅs pa źes bya’o.
de dag thams cad kyaṅ śes bya daṅ ñon moṅs pa’i sgrib pa daṅ bral ba raṅ bźin gyis ’od gsal źiṅ dri ma med pa dag par ’dra bas na sgrib pa med par mtshuṅs pa źes bya’o.
nam mkha’i khams ni dmigs pa med pa, raṅ bźin med pa, thogs pa med pa, thams cad du khyab pa yin pa ltar, chos de dag kyaṅ dmigs par bya ba daṅ byed pa daṅ bral ba, gzuṅ ba daṅ ’dzin pa’i raṅ bźin daṅ bral ba, thogs pa med ciṅ thams cad du khyab pa yin pas nam mkha’i khams su mtshuṅs pa źes bya’o.
mya ṅan las ’das pa ni ñon moṅs pa thams cad spaṅs pa, phuṅ po rnams ñe bar źi ba, tshe’i rgyun chad pa, dṅos po’i raṅ bźin thams cad las ’das pa, stoṅ pa ñid kyi raṅ bźin yin pa, de bźin du chos thams cad kyaṅ de’i raṅ bźin yin pas na mya ṅan las ’das pa’i dbyiṅs su mtshuṅs pas de dag mtshuṅs pa źes bya’o.


’dus byas kyi khams la ’jug pa daṅ ’dus ma byas kyi khams la ’jug pa tshad med de;gaṅ bstan pa de la chos kyi dbyiṅs kyi tshul gyi sgo nas ’jug pa, ’di ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i khams la mkhas pa źes bya’o.

apramāṇaḥ saṃskṛtadhātupraveśo ’saṃskṛtadhātupraveśaś ca;yas tasmin nirdeśe dharmadhātusthitidvāreṇa praveśa idam ucyate bodhisattvasya dhātukauśalyam.

[To summarize:]Immeasurable is the entrance into the sphere of the conditioned, and also the entrance into the sphere of the unconditioned;entering that teaching through the gate that is the state [or essence, pure and all-pervading] of the sphere of total reality is the bodhisattva’s skill with the spheres.

khams la mkhas par rgya cher bstan pa rnams bsdus te bśad pa’i phyir ’dus byas kyi khams la ’jug pa daṅ ’dus ma byas kyi khams la ’jug pa tshad med de źes bya ba la sogs pa smos te, goṅ du bśad pa’i tshul gyis ’dus byas daṅ ’dus ma byas kyi chos zab ciṅ rgya che ba ’di tsam mo źes dpag tu mi ruṅ źiṅ, tshad med pa de dag thams cad stoṅ pa ñid du ro gcig par chud pa de la ’dus byas daṅ ’dus ma byas la ’jug pa źes bya’o.de bas na gaṅ bstan pa de la chos kyi dbyiṅs kyi tshul gyi sgo nas ’jug pa, ’di ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i khams la mkhas pa źes dṅos su gsuṅs te, gaṅ ’dus byas daṅ ’dus ma byas kyi chos bstan pa de dag thams cad kyi chos kyi dbyiṅs kyi raṅ bźin du rtogs pa’i khams la mkhas pa’o źes bstan pa’o. sgo nas ’jug ces bya ba ni chos kyi dbyiṅs rtogs par bya ba’i sgo gzugs la sogs pa’i khams rnams la bya ste, khams de dag gi raṅ bźin mi dmigs pa ñid chos kyi dbyiṅs kyi tshul rtogs par byed pa’i sgor dgoṅs pa ste, tshul ni raṅ bźin la bya’o. yaṅ na ’dus byas kyi chos kyaṅ tshad med pas de dag so so’i raṅ bźin rtogs par bya ba yaṅ tshad med pa la, ’dus ma byas kyi khams kyaṅ tshad med de, de dag so so’i raṅ bźin rtogs par bya ba la yaṅ tshad med pas na ’dus byas kyi khams la ’jug pa daṅ ’dus ma byas kyi khams la ’jug pa tshad med pa źes bya’o. gaṅ bstan pa de la chos kyi dbyiṅs kyi tshul gyi sgo nas ’jug pa, ’di ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i khams la mkhas pa źes bya ba la gaṅ bstan pa ni ’dus byas kyi khams daṅ ’dus ma byas kyi khams tshad med pa bstan pa’o, chos kyi dbyiṅs kyi tshul ni chos kyi dbyiṅs kyi raṅ bźin te, dri ma med ciṅ thams cad la khyab pa’o, chos kyi dbyiṅs kyi tshul de ñid chos rnams thams cad rtogs par bya ba’i thabs yin pas na chos kyi dbyiṅs kyi tshul gyi sgo źes bya ste, sgo de nas chos thams cad stoṅ pa ñid du ro gcig par khoṅ du chud pa ni chos kyi dbyiṅs kyi tshul gyi sgo nas ’jug pa ste, de ltar źugs na byaṅ chub sems dpa’i khams la mkhas pa źes bya’o. Cf. Mvy 1720 for dharmadhātusthiti.


de la byaṅ chub sems dpa’i skye mched la mkhas pa gaṅ źe na?

tatra katamad bodhisattvasyāyatanakauśalyam?

3) What then is the bodhisattva’s skill with the fields?


gaṅ chos kyi skye mched la ’jug pa’i ye śes te.

yad dharmāyatanapraveśajñānam.

The knowledge of entering the field of total reality.

khams la mkhas pa’i ’og tu skye mched la mkhas pa bstan te, ji ltar bstan pa bźin du bśad par ’dod nas de la byaṅ chub sems dpa’i skye mched la mkhas pa gaṅ źe na źes bya ba dris so. sems daṅ sems las byuṅ ba rnams skye źiṅ ’phel ba’i sgo ni skye mched de, skye mched la mkhas pa ni skye mched la mkhas pa ste, mkhas pa’i sgra ni skye mched kyi raṅ bźin daṅ mtshan ñid rtogs pa’o. skye mched gaṅ yin pa daṅ ’jig rten na skye mched la mkhas par ’gyur ba bstan pa’i phyir gaṅ chos kyi skye mched la ’jug pa’i ye śes te źes smos te, skye mched ces bya ba’i sgra bśad pa daṅ sbyar na skye ba’i gnas ’ba’ źig la mi bya’i, ’du ba’i gnas la yaṅ bya ste; ’dir yaṅ chos thams cad chos kyi dbyiṅs su ro gcig par ’dus pas na chos kyi dbyiṅs la chos kyi skye mched ces gsuṅs so. ’jug pa ni rtogs pa la bya ste, chos kyi dbyiṅs rnam par dag pa ye śes kyis rtogs na skye mched la mkhas pa źes bya’o.


chos kyi skye mched ni mig gi skye mched yin mod kyi, chos kyi skye mched lta ba’i mtshan ñid ni ma yin no;chos kyi skye mched rna ba’i skye mched yin mod kyi, chos kyi skye mched ñan pa’i mtshan ñid ni ma yin no;chos kyi skye mched sna’i skye mched yin mod kyi, chos kyi skye mched snom pa’i mtshan ñid ni ma yin no;chos kyi skye mched lce’i skye mched yin mod kyi, chos kyi skye mched myaṅ ba’i mtshan ñid ni ma yin no;chos kyi skye mched lus kyi skye mched yin mod kyi, chos kyi skye mched nom pa’i mtshan ñid ni ma yin no;chos kyi skye mched yid kyi skye mched yin mod kyi, chos kyi skye mched chos rnam par rig pa’i mtshan ñid ni ma yin no.chos kyi skye mched gzugs kyi skye mched yin mod kyi, chos kyi skye mched mig gi rnam par śes pas rnam par rig par bya ba’i mtshan ñid ni ma yin no;chos kyi skye mched sgra’i skye mched yin mod kyi, chos kyi skye mched rna ba’i rnam par śes pas rnam par rig par bya ba’i mtshan ñid ni ma yin no;chos kyi skye mched dri’i skye mched yin mod kyi, chos kyi skye mched sna’i rnam par śes pas rnam par rig par bya ba’i mtshan ñid ni ma yin no;chos kyi skye mched ro’i skye mched yin mod kyi, chos kyi skye mched lce’i rnam par śes pas rnam par rig par bya ba’i mtshan ñid ni ma yin no;chos kyi skye mched reg bya’i skye mched yin mod kyi, chos kyi skye mched lus kyi rnam par śes pas rnam par rig par bya ba’i mtshan ñid ni ma yin no;chos kyi skye mched chos kyi skye mched yin mod kyi, chos kyi skye mched yid kyi rnam par śes pas rnam par rig par bya ba’i mtshan ñid ni ma yin te;

dharmāyatanaṃ cakṣurāyatanam api na tu dharmāyatanaṃ darśanalakṣaṇam;dharmāyatanaṃ śrotrāyatanam api na tu dharmāyatanaṃ śravaṇalakṣaṇam;dharmāyatanaṃ ghrāṇāyatanam api na tu dharmāyatanaṃ ghrāṇalakṣaṇam;dharmāyatanaṃ jihvāyatanam api na tu dharmāyatanaṃ rasanalakṣaṇam;dharmāyatanaṃ kāyāyatanam api na tu dharmāyatanam āmarśalakṣaṇam;dharmāyatanaṃ manaāyatanam api na tu dharmāyatanaṃ dharmavijñaptilakṣaṇam.dharmāyatanaṃ rūpāyatanam api na tu dharmāyatanaṃ caksurvijñānavijñeyalakṣaṇam;dharmāyatanaṃ śabdāyatanam api na tu dharmāyatanaṃ śrotravijñānavijñeyalakṣaṇam;dharmāyatanaṃ gandhāyatanam api na tu dharmāyatanaṃ ghrāṇavijñānavijñeyalakṣaṇam;dharmāyatanaṃ rasāyatanam api na tu dharmāyatanaṃ jihvāvijñānavijñeyalakṣaṇam;dharmāyatanaṃ spraṣṭavyāyatanam api na tu dharmāyatanaṃ kāyavijñānavijñeyalakṣaṇam;dharmāyatanaṃ dharmāyatanam api na tu dharmāyatanaṃ manovijñānavijñeyalakṣaṇam.

Even though the field of total reality is [the same as] the field of the eye [in that they are both empty, or, the empty essence (śūnyasvabhāva) of the field of the eye is the sphere of total reality (dharmadhātu) ], the field of total reality does not have the essential characteristic of seeing [since, as mentioned in the preceding paragraph, this exists only in the wrong understanding of the naive];even though the field of total reality is the field of the ear, the field of total reality does not have the essential characteristic of hearing;even though the field of total reality is the field of the nose, the field of total reality does not have the essential characteristic of smelling;even though the field of total reality is the field of the tongue, the field of total reality does not have the essential characteristic of tasting;even though the field of total reality is the field of the body, the field of total reality does not have the essential characteristic of touch;even though the field of total reality is the field of mind, the field of total reality does not have the essential characteristic of cognition of moments of existence.Even though the field of total reality is the field of form, the field of total reality does not have the essential characteristic of being something to be known by eye-consciousness;even though the field of total reality is the field of sound, the field of total reality does not have the essential characteristic of being something to be known by ear-consciousness;even though the field of total reality is the field of smell, the field of total reality does not have the essential characteristic of being something to be known by nose-consciousness;even though the field of total reality is the field of taste, the field of total reality does not have the essential characteristic of being something to be known by tongue-consciousness;even though the field of total reality is the field of tangibles, the field of total reality does not have the essential characteristic of being something to be known by body-consciousness;even though the field of total reality is the field of moments of existence, the field of total reality does not have the essential characteristic of being something to be known by mind-consciousness.

chos kyi skye mched ni mig gi skye mched yin mod kyi, chos kyi skye mched lta ba’i mtshan ñid ni ma yin źes bya ba la sogs pa’aṅ, mig daṅ chos kyi dbyiṅs gñis stoṅ pa ñid kyi mtshan ñid du tha mi dad pas na de skad ces bya ste, gźan ni gaṅ du khams bśad pa daṅ ’dra bar rig par bya’o. yaṅ na mig gi skye mched kyi raṅ bźin stoṅ pa gaṅ yin pa, de ñid chos kyi dbyiṅs yin te, chos kyi dbyiṅs źes bya ba yaṅ de las gźan med pas na chos kyi skye mched ni mig gi skye mched yin mod kyi źes bya ba smos so.
As an authority on the topic ṭ quotes the Prajñāpāramitāhṛdayasūtra, fol. 120a3: de bas na śes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa las kyaṅ: gzugs gaṅ yin pa de ni stoṅ pa’o, stoṅ pa gaṅ yin pa de ni gzugs te źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs so – "Form is emptiness, emtiness is form", Hṛdaya p. 35: yad rūpaṃ sā śūnyatā, yā śūnyatā tad rūpam.


’di ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i skye mched la mkhas pa źes bya’o.

idaṃ bodhisattvasyāyatanakauśalyam.

This is the bodhisattva’s skill with the fields.


gźan yaṅ skye mched la mkhas pa ni:

punar aparam āyatanakauśalyam:

Further concerning skill with the fields:


mig gi skye mched ni bdag daṅ bdag gis stoṅ ṅo; de bźin du rna ba’i skye mched daṅ, sna’i skye mched daṅ, lce’i skye mched daṅ, lus kyi skye mched daṅ, yid kyi skye mched daṅ, gzugs kyi skye mched daṅ, sgra’i skye mched daṅ, dri’i skye mched daṅ, ro’i skye mched daṅ, reg bya’i skye mched daṅ, chos kyi skye mched kyaṅ bdag daṅ bdag gis stoṅ ṅo.

cakṣurāyatanaṃ śūnyam ātmanā cātmīyena ca, evaṃ śrotrāyatanaṃ, ghrāṇāyatanaṃ, jihvāyatanaṃ, kāyāyatanaṃ, manaāyatanaṃ, rūpāyatanaṃ śabsāyatanaṃ, gandhāyatanaṃ, rasāyatanaṃ spraṣṭavyāyatanaṃ, dharmāyatanam api śūnyam ātmanā cātmīyena ca.

The field of the eye is empty of self and of anything belonging to a self, thus with the field of the ear, the field of the nose, the field of the tongue, the field of the body, the field of mind, the field of forms, the field of sound, the field of smell, the field of taste, the field of tangibles, the field of moments of existence is empty of self and of anything belonging to a self.

skye mched la mkhas pa’i rnam graṅs gźan yaṅ bstan par bźed nas gźan yaṅ skye mched la mkhas pa ni: mig gi skye mched ni bdag daṅ bdag gis stoṅ ṅo źes bya ba smos te, mig gi skye mched la sogs pa de dag ñid kyaṅ bdag ma yin la, bdag ces bya ba dbaṅ byed pa gźan gyis yaṅ ma yin pas bdag gis stoṅ pa bya’o. yaṅ na, gaṅ na med pa de la des stoṅ ste, laṅ kar gśegs pa las kyaṅ: ri dvags dgra’i mo’i khaṅ bzaṅs ’di phag daṅ lug la sogs pa med pas stoṅ ṅo, źes gsuṅs te – "... The fields of the eye, etc., themselves are not the self (ātman), and they are empty of anything belonging to a self (ātmīya) since they do not belong to some other dominating power being a self (na cātmeti parādhipatyasya). Or, ’That which is not in a place, of that it is empty’, the Laṅkavatāra says, ’as, for example, there are no pigs or sheep (Skt. version reads ’elephants, cows or sheep’) in the mansion of Mṛgāramātar’, in this way there is no self or anything belonging to a self in the field of eye, thus it is empty."
The quotation from Laṅkā p. 7510-12 is: yad yatra nāsti tat tena śūnyam ity ucyate, tad yathā mahāmate mṛgāramātuḥ prāsāde hastigavaiḍakādyā na santi.
’dir yaṅ mig gi skye mched la bdag daṅ bdag gi med pas na stoṅ pa źes bya ste de bźin du rna ba la sogs pa’i skye mched la yaṅ sbyar ro.


bcom ldan ’das kyis ji skad du: mig ni bdag daṅ bdag gis stoṅ ste, ’di ni de’i raṅ bźin no; de bźin du rna ba daṅ, sna daṅ, lce daṅ, lus daṅ, yid ni bdag daṅ bdag gis stoṅ ste, ’di ni de’i raṅ bźin no; de bźin du gzugs daṅ, sgra daṅ, dri daṅ, ro daṅ, reg bya daṅ, chos rnams ni bdag daṅ bdag gis stoṅ ste, ’di ni de’i raṅ bźin no; źes gsuṅs so.

yathoktaṃ bhagavatā: “cakṣuḥ śūnyam ātmanā cātmīyena ca, tat tasya svabhāvaḥ; evaṃ śrotraṃ ghrāṇo jihvā kāyo manaḥ śūnyam ātmanā cātmīyena ca, tat tasya svabhāvaḥ; evaṃ rūpaṃ śabdo gandho rasaḥ spraṣṭavyaṃ dharmaḥ śūnya ātmanā cātmīyena ca, tat tasya svabhāva” iti.

[Not only has the noble Akṣayamati examined this emptiness with reasoning (yukti), but also] as the Lord [who really has understood it (adhigamya) ] has said: “The eye is empty of self and anything belonging to a self, that is its essence; and thus with the ear, the nose, the tongue, the body, the mind is empty of self and anything belonging to a self, that is its essence; thus with forms, sound, smell, taste, tangibles, a moment of existence is empty of self and anything belonging to a self, that is its essence”.

mig gi skye mched la sogs pa bdag daṅ bdag gis stoṅ par ji ltar khoṅ du chud sñam pa la, ’phags pa blo gros mi zad pas rigs pas brtags na mig gi skye mched la bdag daṅ bdag gis stoṅ par yaṅ ma zad kyi, bcom ldan ’das kyis kyaṅ thugs su chud nas gsuṅs pa bstan pa’i phyir bcom ldan ’das kyis ji skad du: mig ni bdag daṅ bdag gis stoṅ ste, ’di ni de’i raṅ bźin no źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs so; ’di ni źes bya ba’i sgra bdag daṅ bdag gis źes bya ba’i tshig daṅ sbyar te, bdag daṅ bdag gis stoṅ pa ’di ni mig gi skye mched de’i raṅ bźin no źes bya ba tha tshig go.
Saṃyutta IV p. 54: cakkhuṃ kho ānanda suññaṃ attena vā attaniyena vā..., the expression is found in Pāli ibid. p. 296-7; Majjhima I p. 279, II p. 263; Paṭisaṃbhidāmagga I p. 109, II p. 36; Cullaniddesa p. 279; Kathāvatthu p. 67, p. 579; Mahāniddesa p. 222, p. 439.
Pañcaviṃśati p. 25820 has cakṣuḥ kulaputra śūnyam ātmanā cātmīyena ca, evaṃ śrotraṃ
Cf. also the expression in Pras. p. 26212: ātmīyaṃ rūpaṃ tat tasya svabhāva iti.


’di ltar gaṅ skye mched rnams ’bri bar mi byed ciṅ, mi dge ba’i chos kyaṅ mi sogs, dge ba’i chos kyaṅ ’bri bar mi byed la, dge ba daṅ mi dge ba la ’du śes gñis su mi ’gyur ba, ’di ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i skye mched la mkhas pa’o.

evaṃ yad āyatanānām apacayaṃ na karoty akuśaladharmāṇām apy upacayaṃ kuśaladharmānām apacayaṃ na kurvan kuśalākuśaladvayasaṃjñāṃ nāpadyata, idaṃ bodhisattvasyāyatanakauśalyam.

Thus, he does not bring about any decrease of the fields, neither making the bad moments of existence increase nor the good moments of existence decrease he does not fall into conflicting concepts of good and bad, this is the bodhisattva’s skill with the fields.

’di ltar gaṅ skye mched rnams ’bri bar mi byed ciṅ źes bya ba la sogs pa ni goṅ du bśad pa ltar na mig gi skye mched la sogs pa bdag daṅ bdag gis stoṅ ste, raṅ bźin med pa’i phyir mig gi skye mched la sogs pa’i sgo nas sems daṅ sems las byuṅ ba rnams mi skye bar dgag ciṅ dbyer med ces bya ba’i don to; mi dge ba’i chos kyaṅ mi sogs, dge ba’i chos kyaṅ bri ba med pa źes bya ba ni skye mched raṅ bźin gyis stoṅ pas skye mched kyi sgo nas ’dod chags daṅ źe sdaṅ la sogs pa mi dge ba’i chos blaṅ bar mi bya la, mi dge ba’i chos rnams ’phel bar mi byed ces te, dge ba’i chos rnams kyaṅ ’dor bar byed pa ma yin pas na dge ba’i chos kyaṅ bri bar mi byed pa źes bya’o, de ltar mi dge ba’i chos mi sogs la, dge ba’i chos kyaṅ bri bar mi byed na, spoṅ ba daṅ spel bar ’gyur bas gñis su ’du śes par mi ’gyur sñam la dge ba daṅ mi dge ba la ’du śes gñis su mi ’gyur ba, ’di ni źes bya ba la sogs pa smos te, las daṅ rnam par smin pa chud mi gson pas mi dge ba mi sogs śiṅ dge ba’i chos kyaṅ bri bar mi byed mod kyi, don dam par dge ba daṅ mi dge ba gñi ga raṅ bźin med par rtogs pas ’di ni dge ba ’di ni mi dge ba źes ’du śes gñis su mi ’gyur ba ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i skye mched la mkhas pa źes bya’o.


gźan yaṅ skye mched la mkhas pa ni:

punar aparam āyatanakauśalyam:

Further concerning skill with the fields:


mig gi skye mched kyi ’dod chags kyi gnas daṅ rten ni gzugs kyi skye mched de;gaṅ mig gzugs la ’dod chags daṅ bral bar mthoṅ la, ’dod chags daṅ bral ba’i chos kyaṅ mṅon sum du mi byed pa, ’di ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i skye mched la mkhas pa źes bya’o.de bźin du rna ba’i skye mched kyi sgra’i skye mched daṅ, sna’i skye mched kyi dri’i skye mched daṅ, lce’i skye mched kyi ro’i skye mched daṅ, lus kyi skye mched kyi reg bya’i skye mched daṅ, yid kyi skye mched kyi ’dod chags kyi gnas daṅ rten ni chos kyi skye mched de;gaṅ yid chos la ’dod chags daṅ bral bar mthoṅ la, ’dod chags daṅ bral ba’i chos kyaṅ mṅon sum du mi byed pa, ’di ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i skye mched la mkhas pa źes bya’o.

rūpāyatanaṃ cakṣurāyatanarāgasya sthānaṃ niśrayaś ca;yac cakṣū rūpe vigatarāgaṃ paśyati na ca vigatarāgadharmaṃ sākṣātkarotīdam ucyate bodhisattvasyāyatanakauśalyam.evaṃ śabdāyatanaṃ śrotrāyatanasya, gandhāyatanaṃ ghrāṇāyatanasya, rasāyatanaṃ jihvāyatanasya, spraṣṭavyāyatanaṃ kāyāyatanasya; dharmāyatanaṃ manaāyatanarāgasya sthānaṃ niśrayaś ca.yan mano dharme vigatarāgaṃ paśyati, na ca vigatarāgadharmaṃ sākṣātkarotīdam ucyate bodhisattvasyāyatanakauśalyam.

The basis and support of greed in the eye-field is the field of form;whenever the eye sees without greed for form, and one does not realize the moment of existence without greed, this is called the bodhisattva’s skill with the fields.Thus [the basis and support of greed] in the ear-field (p. 72) is the field of sound, in the nose-field the field of smell, in the tongue-field the field of taste, in the body-field the field of tangibles.The basis and support of greed in the mind-field is the field of moments of existence; whenever the mind sees without greed for moments of existence and one does not realize the moment of existence without greed, this is called the bodhisattva’s skill with the fields.

yaṅ skye mched kyi rnam pa gźan bstan par ’dod nas gźan yaṅ skye mched la mkhas pa ni: mig gi skye mched kyi ’dod chags kyi gnas daṅ rten ni gzugs kyi skye mched de; gaṅ mig gzugs la ’dod chags daṅ bral bar mthoṅ la, ’dod chags daṅ bral ba’i chos kyaṅ mṅon sum du mi byed pa, ’di ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i skye mched la mkhas pa źes bya’o źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs so. gzugs kha dog mdzes pa dbyibs daṅ ldan pa mthoṅ nas ’dod chags skye bas na mig gi skye mched kyi ’dod chags kyi gnas daṅ rten ni gzugs kyi skye mched do, mig gis gzugs mthoṅ nas gzugs la ’dod chags la sogs pa skye bar ’dod chags kyi rgyu naṅ gi dṅos po daṅ phyi’i dṅos po rnams ṅo bo ñid kyis med pas gzugs la ’dod chags daṅ bral du zin kyaṅ, ’dod chags daṅ bral ba’i chos źi ba phyogs gcig pa yaṅ mṅon du mi len la gzugs la sogs pa ’khor ba’i chos kyaṅ mi spoṅ ba ’di ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i skye mched la mkhas pa’o źes bya ba’i don te, sgra la sogs pa la yaṅ ci rigs par sbyar ro.


skye mched ces bya ba ni, ’phags pa’i skye mched daṅ, ’phags pa ma yin pa’i skye mched do.de la ’phags pa’i skye mched ni gaṅ lam yaṅ dag par bsgrub pa’o;’phags pa ma yin pa’i skye mched ni gaṅ lam daṅ mi ’thun pa’o.

āyatanam ity āryāyatanam anāryāyatanaṃ ca.tatrāryāyatanaṃ yā mārgasamyakpratipattih;anāryāyatanaṃ yā mārgapratikūlatā.

Fields are the fields of the holy and the fields of the unholy.There, the field of the holy is right progress on the way;the field of the unholy is what is in opposition to the way.

skye mched kyi don rgyas par bśad pa bsdus te bstan pa’i phyir ’phags pa’i skye mched daṅ ’phags pa ma yin pa’i skye mched do źes bya ba smos te, mdor na skye mched ni rnam pa gñis te, ’phags pa’i skye mched daṅ ’phags pa ma yin pa’i skye mched do. de la ñon moṅs pa rnams las riṅ du soṅ źiṅ ñon moṅs pa spaṅs pa ni ’phags pa ste, de rnams skye źiṅ ’byuṅ ba’i sgo la ’phags pa’i skye mched ces bya’o. de bas na mdo las kyaṅ: ’phags pa gaṅ źe na? gaṅ ’dod chags ma lus par spaṅs pa daṅ, źe sdaṅ ma lus par spaṅs pa daṅ, gti mug ma lus par spaṅs pa’o, źes gsuṅs so. gaṅ ñon moṅs pa rnams ma spaṅs pa ni ’phags pa ma yin pa ste, de dag skye źiṅ ’byuṅ ba’i sgo ni ’phags pa ma yin pa’i skye mched ces bya’o. de bas na mdo las: so so’i skye bo gaṅ źe na? gaṅ ’phags pa’i chos rnams ma thob pa ste: ñe bar bsams pas sems pa daṅ, ñes par bya ba’i las byed pa daṅ, ñes par smra ba brjod pa’o, źes gsuṅs so.de la ’phags pa rnams skye źiṅ ’byuṅ ba’i sgo gaṅ yin pa bstan pa’i phyir ’phags pa’i skye mched ni gaṅ lam yaṅ dag par bsgrub pa’o źes bya ba smos te, dge ba’i bśes gñen la brten nas dam pa’i chos ñan pa daṅ, mñan pa rnams gtan la ’bebs śiṅ sems pa daṅ, bsams pa rnams źi gnas lhag mthoṅ gi sgo nas brten te; daṅ po dran pa ñe bar gźag pa bźi sgom pa daṅ, de nas dro bar gyur pa’i dus na yaṅ dag pa’i spoṅ ba bźi sgom pa daṅ, de nas spyi bo’i tshe rdzu ’phrul gyi rkaṅ pa bźi sgom pa daṅ, de nas bzod pa’i dus na dbaṅ po lṅa sgom pa daṅ, de nas ’jig rten pa’i chos kyi mchog gi dus na stobs lṅa sgom pa daṅ; de nas mthoṅ ba’i lam la byaṅ chub kyi yan lag bdun sgom pa daṅ, de nas bsgom pa’i lam na ’phags pa’i lam yan lag brgyad pa sgom pa ni lam sgrub pa źes bya ste, lam bsgrub pa las ’phags pa rnams skye źiṅ ’byuṅ bas na lam bsgrub pa ni ’phags pa’i skye mched do.’phags pa ma yin pa skye źiṅ ’byuṅ ba’i sgo bstan pa’i phyir ’phags pa ma yin pa’i skye mched ni gaṅ lam daṅ mi mthun pa’o źes gsuṅs te, dge ba’i bśes gñen las dam pa’i chos ñan pa daṅ, bsam pa’am, sgom pa la mi ’jug pa ni lam daṅ mi mthun pa źes bya’am; yaṅ na źi gnas daṅ lhag mthoṅ phyin ci log tu sgom pa rnams ni ’phags par ’gyur ba med pas na ’phags pa ma yin pa’i skye mched ces bya’o.
yaṅ na, sems can rnam pa bcu ni lam daṅ mi mthun pa ste, bcu gaṅ źe na?
1) rab tu ’bar ba’i sems can daṅ, 2) dgra’i dbaṅ du soṅ ba’i sems can daṅ, 3) sdug bsṅal gyis gzir ba’i sems can daṅ, 4) mun pas sgrib pa’i sems can daṅ, 5) lam ṅan par źugs pa’i sems can daṅ, 6) ’chiṅ ba chen po daṅ ldan pa’i sems can daṅ, 7) zas mchog dug daṅ ’dres pa la źen pa’i sems can daṅ, 8) lam rab tu stor ba’i sems can daṅ, 9) lam log par źugs pa’i sems can daṅ, 10) ñam chuṅ ba’i sems can no. de la 1) rab tu ’bar ba’i sems can ni gaṅ ’dod pa’i bde ba la chags pa rnams so; 2) dgra’i dbaṅ du soṅ ba’i sems can ni dge ba la źugs pa bdud kyis bar chad byas nas dge ba btaṅ ba rnams so; 3) sdug bsṅal gyis gzir ba’i sems can ni gaṅ sems can dmyal ba rnams so; 4) mun pas sgrib pa ni rṅon pa la sogs pa log par spyod pa la śin tu źugs pa rnams te, las kyi rnam par smin pa la myos pa’i phyir ro; 5) lam ṅan par źugs pa’i sems can ni yoṅs su mya ṅan las mi ’da’ ba’i chos can rnams te, ’khor ba’i lam rgyun mi ’chad pa’i phyir ro; 6) ’chiṅ ba chen po daṅ ldan pa’i sems can ni lta ba sna tshogs kyi bciṅ ba dam pos bciṅs pa’i mu stegs can thar pa’i lam log par źugs pa rnams so; 7) zas mchog dug daṅ ’dres pa la źen pa’i sems can ni sñoms par ’jug pa’i bde ba la chags te, ji ltar kha zas źim po dug daṅ ’dres pa ’phral du bde ba yaṅ ’chi ba’i rgyur ’gyur ba, de bźin du tiṅ ṅe ’dzin gyi ro la chags pa yaṅ phyis de las ñams par ’gyur ba’i phyir ro; 8) lam stor ba’i sems can ni mṅon pa’i ṅa rgyal can rnams te, thar pa’i lam nor ba’i phyir ro; 9) lam log par źugs pa’i sems can ni ma ṅes pa’i rigs can rnams theg pa chuṅ ṅu’i lam du źugs pa’o; 10) ñam chuṅ ba’i sems can tshogs gñis rdzogs par mi btub pa’i byaṅ chub sems dpa’ rnams te.
This paragraph is quoted from Msa XVII 29-30, p. 1243-15:
pradīptān śatruvaśagān duḥkhākrāntāṃs tamovṛtān /
durgamārgasamārūḍān mahābandhanasaṃyutān //29//
mahāśanaviṣākrāntalolān mārgapranaṣṭakān /
utpathaprasthitān satvān durbalān karuṇāyate //30//
tatra (1) pradīptāḥ kāmarāgeṇa kāmasukhabhaktāḥ / (2) śatruvaśagā mārakṛtāntarāyāḥ kuśale ’prayuktāḥ / (3) duḥkhākrāntāḥ duḥkhābhūtā narakādiṣu / (4) tamovṛtā aurabhrikādayo duścaritaikāntikāḥ karmavipākasaṃmūḍhatvāt / (5) durgamārgasamārūḍhā aparinirvāṇadharmāṇaḥ saṃsāravartmātyantānupacchedāt / (6) mahābandhanasaṃyutā anyatīrthyāḥ mokṣasaṃprasthitā nānākudṛṣṭigāḍhabandhanabaddhatvāt / (7) mahāśanaviṣākrāntalolāḥ samāpattisukhasaktāḥ / teṣāṃ hi tat kliṣṭaṃ samāpattisukham / yathā mṛṣṭam aśanaṃ viṣākrāntaṃ / tataḥ pracyāvanāt / (8) mārgapraṇaṣṭakā abhimānikā mokṣamārgabhrāntatvāt / (9) utpathaprasthitā hīnayānaprayuktā aniyatā / (10) durbalā aparipūrṇasaṃbhārā bodhisatvāḥ / [ity ete daśavidhāḥ satvā bodhisatvakaruṇāyā ālambanaṃ] /
de ni lam daṅ mi mthun pa źes bya’o. lam daṅ mi mthun pas na de dag la ’phral du ’phags par ’gyur ba med pa’i phyir, ’phags pa ma yin pa’i skye mched do.


de la byaṅ chub sems dpa’ lam la gnas nas, lam daṅ mi ’thun pa la spyod pa’i sems can rnams la sñiṅ rje chen po skyed ciṅ, lam gyi skye mched kyaṅ mi ’dor ba, ’di ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i skye mched la mkhas pa źes bya’o.

tatra bodhisattvamārge sthito mārgapratikūlacariteṣu sattveṣu mahākaruṇām utpādayati mārgāyatanaṃ ca notsṛjatīdam ucyate bodhisattvasyāyatanakauśalyam.

Established on the way of the bodhisattvas he produces great compassion towards beings practising things in opposition to the way, and yet he does not give up the field of the way; this is called the bodhisattva’s skill with the fields.

de la byaṅ chub sems dpa’ lam la gnas nas źes bya ba ni goṅ du bśad pa’i lam de la gnas pa’o. lam daṅ mi mthun pa la spyod pa’i sems can rnams la sñiṅ rje chen po bskyed ciṅ źes bya ba la, lam daṅ mi mthun pa la gnas pa’i sems can bcu ba rnams te, sems can de dag la sñiṅ rje chen po bskyed pa’o. lam gyi skye mched kyaṅ mi ’dor ba źes bya ba ni lam gyi skye mched las ñams par yaṅ mi ’gyur źes bya ba’i tha tshig ste, de ltar śes pa de ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i skye mched la mkhas pa źes bya’o.


de la byaṅ chub sems dpa’i bden pa la mkhas pa gaṅ źe na?

tatra katamad bodhisattvasya satyakauśalyam?

4) What then is the bodhisattva’s skill with truths?

skye mched la mkhas pa bśad pa’i ’og tu bden pa la mkhas pa bstan te, ji ltar bstan pa bźin du bśad par ’dod nas de la byaṅ chub sems dpa’i bden pa la mkhas pa gaṅ źe na, de la źes bya ba’i don ni sṅar bśad pa bźin no. gaṅ de bźin gśegs pas gsuṅs śiṅ bśad pa rnams ni phyin ci ma log pa, ma nor ba de kho na ñid mi slu ba yin pas na bden pa źes bya’o, bden pa de la mkhas pa bden pa la mkhas pa ste, bden pa’i raṅ bźin daṅ mtshan ñid phyin ci ma log par rtogs pa’o.
Cf. Bbh. p. 29217ff: punar anekavidham avitathārthena tāvad ekam eva satyaṃ. na dvitīyam asti. dvividham satyam. saṃvṛtisatyaṃ parmārthasatyaṃ ca. trividhaṃ satyaṃ. lakṣaṇasatyaṃ vāksatyaṃ kriyāsatyaṃ ca. caturvidhaṃ duḥkhasatyaṃ yāvan mārgasatyaṃ.


’jug pa bźi ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i bden pa la mkhas pa yin te.’jug pa bźi gaṅ źe na?

catuṣpraveśaṃ bodhisattvasya satyakauśalyam.katame catvāraḥ praveśāḥ?

The bodhisattva’s skill with truths consists in four entrances [of understanding or knowledge].Which four entrances?

’jug pa bźi ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i bden pa la mkhas pa yin te źes bya ba la rtogs pa bźi’am, śes pa bźi ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i bden pa la mkhas pa źes bya ba ste, ’phags pa’i bden pa bźi rtogs pa la bya bar dgoṅs so. bstan pa daṅ bśad pa’i tshul du khoṅ du chud par bya ba’i phyir ’jug pa bźi gaṅ źe na źes bya ba la sogs pa smos te, rtogs pa bźi gaṅ źe na źes bya ba’i tha tshig go, gaṅ ’di sdug bsṅal śes pa daṅ źes bya ba la sogs pas ni bstan pa’i tshul bśad do.


gaṅ ’di: a) sdug bsṅal śes pa daṅ; 72 ::: b) kun ’byuṅ ba śes pa daṅ; c) ’gog pa śes pa daṅ; d) lam śes pa’o.de la sdug bsṅal śes pa źes bya ba ni gaṅ phuṅ po rnams kyi mi skye bar śes pa’o;kun ’byuṅ ba śes pa źes bya ba ni gaṅ sred pa legs par ’joms pa’i śes pa’o;’gog pa śes pa źes bya ba ni ma rig pa daṅ bag la ñal ba rnams mi ’byuṅ ba’o;lam śes pa źes bya ba ni mñam pa ñid du gyur pa’i chos thams cad la sgro mi ’dogs pa ste;de ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i bden pa śes pa’o.

yad idam duḥkhajñānaṃ samudayajñānaṃ nirodhajñānaṃ mārgajñānam.tatra duḥkhajñānam iti yat skandheṣv anutpādajñānam,samudayajñānam iti yat tṛṣṇāyāṃ sunihatajñānam,nirodhajñānam ity avidyānuśayāpravṛttiḥ,mārgajñānam iti sarveṣu samatābhūteṣu dharmeṣv asamāropaḥ,tad bodhisattvasya satyajñānam.

Knowledge of suffering, knowledge of origin, knowledge of cessation and knowledge of the way.There, knowledge of suffering is the knowledge that the parts of personality are unborn,knowledge of origin is the knowledge that thirst has been vanquished,knowledge of cessation is the non-activity of ignorance and propensities,while knowledge of the way is when one does not impute anything to any moments of existence in that they are the same,that is the bodhisattva’s knowledge of the truths.

Interpretations of the Four Truths are presented in ṭ.: de la sdug bsṅal śes pa źes bya ba ni źes bya ba la sogs pas bśad pa’i tshul bstan to. ci’i phyir ’phags pa’i bden pa bźi bśad ce na? kun nas ñon moṅs pa daṅ rnam par byaṅ ba’i phyogs kyi ’bras bu daṅ rgyu mdor phyin ci ma log par bstan pa’i phyir ’phags pa’i bden pa bźi bśad do. de la kun nas ñon moṅs pa’i ’bras bu mdor phyin ci ma log par bstan pa ni sdug bsṅal gyi bden pa’o; kun nas ñon moṅs pa’i phyogs kyi rgyu mdor phyin ci ma log par bstan pa ni kun ’byuṅ ba’i bden pa’o; rnam par byaṅ ba’i phyogs kyi ’bras bu mdor phyin ci ma log par bstan pa ni ’gog pa’i bden pa’o, rnam par byaṅ ba’i phyogs kyi rgyu mdor phyin ci ma log par bstan pa ni lam gyi bden pa’o. yaṅ na nad daṅ, nad kyi gźi daṅ, nad med pa daṅ, sman lta bur bstan pa’i phyir bden pa bźi ñid du bśad de, mi maṅ mi ñuṅ źes bya ba sbyar ro. de la nad lta bu ni sdug bsṅal gyi bden pa’o, nad kyi gźi lta bu ni kun ’byuṅ gyi bden pa’o, nad med pa lta bu ni ’gog pa’i bden pa’o, sman lta bu ni lam gyi bden pa’o. yaṅ na me daṅ, śiṅ daṅ, me źi ba daṅ, me ’gog pa’i rgyu lta bu yin pas ’phags pa’i bden pa bstan te, me lta bu ni sdug bsṅal gyi bden pa ste, me’i gduṅ ba daṅ ’dra bar sdug bsṅal gyi gduṅ ba daṅ ldan pa’i phyir ro, śiṅ lta bu ni kun ’byuṅ ba’i bden pa ste, śiṅ me skye ba’i rgyu byed pa bźin du kun ’byuṅ ba yaṅ sdug bsṅal skyed pa’i rgyu byed pa’i phyir ro, me źi ba lta bu ni ’gog pa’i bden pa ste, me’i gduṅ ba źi ba daṅ ’dra bar sdug bsṅal gyi gduṅ ba źi ba’i phyir ro, me źi ba’i rgyu lta bu ni lam gyi bden pa ste, ’gog pa thob pa’i rgyur gyur pa’i phyir ro. yaṅ na bu lon daṅ, dbul ba daṅ, bu lon sbyaṅs pa daṅ, gter lta bu yin pas bden pa bźi’o, bu lon lta bu ni sdug bsṅal gyi bden pa ste, rtag tu yid mi bde ba’i gduṅ ba daṅ ldan pas so, dbul ba lta bu ni kun ’byuṅ ba’i bden pa ste, dbul ba’i rgyus bu lon chags pa daṅ ’dra bar kun ’byuṅ ba’i rgyus sdug bsṅal skyed pa’i phyir ro, bu lon sbyaṅs pa lta bu ni ’gog pa’i bden pa ste, bu lon sbyaṅs na bu lon gyi mi bde ba med pa bźin du sdug bsṅal rnams med pa’i phyir ro, gter lta bu ni lam gyi bden pa ste, gter bu lon sbyoṅ ba’i rgyur gyur pa daṅ ’dra bar lam ni ’gog pa ’thob pa’i rgyur gyur pa’i phyir ro. sdug bsṅal śes pa gaṅ yin pa bstan pa’i phyir de la sdug bsṅal śes pa źes bya ba ni gaṅ phuṅ po rnams mi skye bar śes pa’o źes bya ba gsuṅs te, spuṅs śiṅ tshogs su gyur pa’i phyir phuṅ po ste, de’aṅ gzugs daṅ, tshor ba daṅ, ’du śes daṅ, ’du byed daṅ, rnam par śes pa’i phuṅ pa’o, phuṅ po de dag sgyu ma daṅ gzugs brñan tsam du snaṅ mod kyi, ṅo bo ñid kyi skye ba med pas na mi skye ba’o, ’di ltar phuṅ po lṅa rnams las ’phags pa’i ñan thos dag sdug bsṅal ba daṅ mi rtag pa la sogs par rtogs pa ni ma yin gyi, thog ma nas ṅo bo ñid kyis ma skyes par śes pa ni sdug bsṅal śes pa’o; kun ’byuṅ ba śes pa bstan pa’i phyir gaṅ sred pa legs par ’joms pa’i śes pa’o źes bya ba smos te, de la sred pa gaṅ źe na? gaṅ mdo las bcom ldan ’das kyis: yaṅ srid pa ’byuṅ bar byed pa daṅ, dga’ ba’i ’dod chags daṅ ldan pa daṅ, de dag de dag la mṅon par dga’ ba’i sred pa’o źes gsuṅs pa’o; de la sred pa ni sgo gsum gyis źugs pa yin te, yaṅ ’byuṅ ba’i srid pa ’dod pa daṅ, yul ’dod pa’o, de la yaṅ ’byuṅ ba’i srid pa ’dod pa ’di yaṅ srid pa ’dod pa ’byuṅ ba byed pa yin no, yul ’dod pa ni rnam pa gñis te, yul thob pa rnams la yid bde źiṅ lhag par chags pa daṅ ldan pa daṅ, yul ma thob pa rnams la kun tu sbyor bar ’dod pa daṅ ldan pa’o, de la yul thob pa rnams la yid bde źiṅ lhag par chags pa daṅ ldan pa gaṅ yin pa de ni dga’ ba’i ’dod chags daṅ ldan pa źes bya’o, yul ma thob pa rnams la kun tu sbyor bar ’dod pa daṅ ldan pa gaṅ yin pa de ni de dag la mṅon par dga’ ba źes bya’o; legs pa ’joms pa’i śes pa ni srid pa de dag ma lus par spaṅ ba’i thabs śes pa ste, ’joms pa źes bya ba ni spoṅ ba’i don to; ñan thos dag ltar kun ’byuṅ ba’i bden pa la rgyu daṅ rkyen la sogs par rtogs pa ni ma yin gyi, sdug bsṅal gyi phuṅ po ’byuṅ ba’i rgyu ’dod chags kyi raṅ bźin sred pa źes bya ba rab tu spaṅ ba’i thabs śes pa ni kun ’byuṅ ba śes pa źes bya’o. ’gog pa śes pa bstan pa’i phyir ’gog pa śes pa źes bya ba ni ma rig pa daṅ bag la ñal rnams mi ’byuṅ ba’o źes gsuṅs te, de yaṅ ma rig pa mi ’byuṅ ba daṅ, bag la ñal rnams mi ’byuṅ ba’o źes bya bar sbyar ro; de la ma rig pa ni de kho na la kun tu gti mug pa ste, ma rig pa ma lus par spaṅs nas phyis de’i rgyud la mi skye bar ’gyur ba ni ma rig pa mi ’byuṅ ba’o; bag la ñal gyi sgras ’dod chags la sogs pa ñon moṅs pa gźan gyi bag la ñal la bya ste, de dag ma lus par spaṅs nas phyis de’i rgyud la mi skye ba ni bag la ñal rnams mi ’byuṅ ba’o; bag la ñal smos pas ma rig pa yaṅ smras pa yin mod kyi, ma rig pa ni ñon moṅs pa thams cad ’byuṅ ba’i rgyu ste, gtso bo yin par bstan pa’i phyir miṅ gis bkar te smos te; yaṅ na ma rig pa bag la ñal bas na ma rig pas bag la ñal te, ma rig pa la sogs pa’i bag la ñal rnams thog ma nas ma skyes pas mtha’ ’gag pa yaṅ med pa ni ma rig pa daṅ bag la ñal rnams mi ’byuṅ ba źes bya’o; ’gog pa’i bden pa la ’phags pa ñan thos dag ltar źi ba daṅ gya nom pa la sogs pa rtog pa ni ma yin gyi, ma rig pa la sogs pa bag la ñal rnams thog ma nas ma skyes pas mtha’ ’gag pa yaṅ med par śes pa ni ’gog pa źes bya’o. lam śes pa bstan pa’i phyir lam śes pa źes bya ba ni mñam pa ñid du gyur pa’i chos thams cad la sgro mi ’dogs pa ste źes bya ba smos te, lam gyi bden pa la yaṅ ’phags pa ñan thos pa dag ltar ñon moṅs pa’i phyogs spoṅ ba daṅ rnam par byaṅ ba’i phyogs sgrub par rtogs pa ni ma yin gyi, ñon moṅs pa daṅ rnam par byaṅ ba’i phyogs gñi ga yaṅ mñam pa ñid du rtogs pas de ñid la sgro ’dogs pa med pa ni lam śes pa źes bya’o; yaṅ na chos thams cad ni nam mkha’ daṅ ’dra bar ro gcig pas mñam pa ñid du gyur pa’o, mñam pa ñid du gyur pa’i chos de dag las spaṅ ba daṅ, blaṅ ba daṅ, rtag pa daṅ, mi rtag pa daṅ, yod pa daṅ, med pa daṅ, skye ba daṅ, mi skye ba la sogs par sgro mi ’dogs pa ni lam śes pa’o. de ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i bden pa śes pa’o źes bya ba la bden pa bźi po goṅ du bśad pa lta bu’i tshul du śes pa ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i bden pa śes pa źes bya’o.


de la byaṅ chub sems dpa’ ’phags pa’i bden pa bźi po de dag la de lta bus śes rab daṅ ye śes kyis rab tu śes kyaṅ, sems can la lta ba’i phyir mṅon sum du mi byed ciṅ, sems can rnams kyaṅ yoṅs su smin par byed de. ’di ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i bden pa la mkhas pa źes bya’o.

tatra bodhisattvas tāni catvāri satyāni evaṃ prajñayā jñānena ca prajānann api sattvāvekṣayā na sākṣātkaroti, sattvān paripācayati, idam ucyate bodhisattvasya satyakauśalyam.

When, even though he understands those four truths with that kind of insight and knowledge, he does not realize them – for the sake of living beings – but matures living beings, it is called the bodhisattva’s skill with truths [including both insight and expedient means (prajñopāyaparigṛhīta) ].

byaṅ chub sems dpa’i bden pa śes pa de dag kyaṅ śes rab daṅ thabs kyis yoṅs su zin pa yin par bstan pa’i phyir de la byaṅ chub sems dpa’ ’phags pa’i bden pa bźi po de dag la de lta bur śes rab daṅ ye śes kyis rab tu śes kyaṅ źes bya ba la sogs pa smos te, ’phags par ’gyur ba’i bden pa yin pas na ’phags pa’i bden pa’am, ’phags pa rnams kyis bden pa de dag de kho na lta bu yin par bden pa’i sgo nas yaṅ dag pa ji lta ba bźin mkhyen ciṅ gzigs kyi, byis pa rnams kyis yaṅ dag pa ji lta ba bźin du mi śes mi mthoṅ bas na, de’i phyir ’phags pa bden pa rnams źes bya’o. yaṅ na ’phags pa saṅs rgyas daṅ saṅs rgyas kyi ñan thos rnams kyis bśad pa’i bden pa yin pas na ’phags pa’i bden pa ste, ’phags pa ma yin pas bśad rnams kyaṅ de bźin gśegs pa rnams kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis ’chad pa daṅ, bcom ldan ’das kyi bstan pa ’dzin pa daṅ, ’phags par ’gyur ba’i rgyu byed pas na ’phags pa’i bden pa źes bya’o. de lta bur źes bya ba ni goṅ du bstan pa lta bur ro. raṅ gi mtshan ñid rtogs pa ni śes rab yin la, spyi’i mtshan ñid rtogs pa ni ye śes so, yaṅ na skabs ’dir śes rab bśad pas śes rab ñid, goṅ du bśad pa lta bu’i tshul du stoṅ par rtogs pa la ye śes źes bya ste, ’di ni śes rab kyis zin pa bstan to. sems can la lta ba’i phyir mṅon sum du mi byed ciṅ sems can rnams kyaṅ yoṅs su smin par byed de źes bya ba ni de ltar bden pa bźi rtogs kyaṅ sñiṅ rje chen pos sems can gyi don gyi phyir ñan thos bźin du źi ba phyogs gcig pa’i mya ṅan las ’das pa mṅon du mi byed ciṅ thabs rnam pa sna tshogs kyis sems can smin par yaṅ byed do, ’di ni thabs kyis zin par bstan to. ’di ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i bden pa la mkhas pa’o źes bya ba la thabs daṅ śes rab kyis yoṅs su zin pa goṅ du bśad pa lta bur bden pa bźi po śes pa ’di ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i bden pa la mkhas pa’o – "... Understanding the individual characteristics (svalakṣaṇa) is insight (prajñā), while understanding the general characteristics (sāmānyalakṣaṇa) is knowledge (jñāna). In this case, however, the insight mentioned is just insight, and knowledge is the understanding of emptiness (śūnyatādhigama) in the way explained above; it is taught that this [viz. the bodhisattva’s way of behaviour] is included in insight (prajñāparigṛhīta). He does not realize them – for the sake of living beings - but matures living beings, the sūtra says; though understanding the four truths he does not realize extinction (nirvāṇa) – exclusively (ekāntika) peaceful (śānta) – like the disciples (śrāvaka), so that, with great compassion for the sake of living beings, he may mature living beings with expedient means; it is taught that this [viz. the bodhisattva’s way of behaviour] is included in expedient means (upāyaparigṛhīta). This is called the bodhisattva’s skill with truths, it says, the knowledge of the four truths as described above is included in insight and expedient means (prajñopāyaparigṛhīta)."


gźan yaṅ byaṅ chub sems dpa’i bden pa rnam pa gsum ste;

punar aparaṃ trividhaṃ bodhisattvasya satyam.

Further, the bodhisattva’s truth is of three kinds.


rnam pa gsum gaṅ źe na?gaṅ ’di: a) kun rdzob kyi bden pa daṅ; b) don dam pa’i bden pa daṅ; c) mtshan ñid kyi bden pa’o.

katamat traividhyam?yad idaṃ saṃvṛtisatyaṃ paramārthasatyaṃ lakṣaṇasatyam.

What three?Concealed truth, the highest truth and the truth of essential characteristics.

bden pa’i mtshan ñid gźan yaṅ bstan par bźed nas gźan yaṅ byaṅ chub sems dpa’i bden pa rnam pa gsum ste źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs te, gźan yaṅ źes bya ba ni goṅ du bden pa bźi bśad pa tsam du yaṅ ma zad kyi, bden pa rnam pa gsum yaṅ yod de źes bya bar dgoṅs pa’o. ’dir yaṅ bstan pa daṅ bśad pa’i tshul du rig par bya ste, gaṅ ’di kun rdzob kyi bden pa daṅ źes bya ba la sogs pa ni bstan pa’i tshul lo, de la kun rdzob kyi bden pa gaṅ źe na źes bya ba la sogs pa ni bśad pa’i tshul lo. kun rdzob ñid bden pa yin pas kun rdzob kyi bden pa ste, sgyu ma daṅ smyig rgyu tsam ji ltar snaṅ ba rnams de bźin du bya ba byed pa’i phyir ro. don dam pa ñid bden pa yin pas don dam pa’i bden pa ste, mi slu ba’i bdag ñid du pyin ci ma log pa’i phyir ro. mtshan ñid bden pa yin pas na mtshan ñid kyi bden pa yin pa ste, chos thams cad ro gcig par ma nor ba’i phyir ro.
ci’i phyir bden pa rnam pa gsum bśad ce na? sems can rnam pa gsum gyi don du dgoṅs nas bden pa rnam pa gsum bśad de, sems can rnam pa gsum ni yoṅs su ma smin pa’i sems can daṅ, yoṅs su smin pa’i sems can daṅ, chos ñid zab mo la kun tu mgo rmoṅs pa’i sems can no. de la yoṅs su ma smin pa’i sems can gyi don kun rdzob kyi bden pa bstan to; yoṅs su smin pa’i sems can gyi don du don dam pa’i bden pa bstan to; chos ñid zab mo la kun tu mgo rmoṅs pa’i sems can gyi don du mtshan ñid kyi bden pa bstan to – "Why are the truths explained as being of three kinds? Having in mind the good of three kinds of beings (trividhasattvārthaṃ saṃdhāya) the truths are explained as being of three kinds, and those three kinds of beings are (1) the beings who are not matured (aparipācita), (2) those who are matured (paripācita), and (3) those who are deluded as to the deep nature of the moments of existence (gaṃbhīradharmatā)......
de bas na ’phags pa sa bcu’i mdo las kyaṅ: sems can gźan gyi bsam pa ji lta ba bźin du tshim par byed pas kyaṅ kun rdzob kyi bden pa rab tu śes so, bgrod pa gcig pu la yaṅ dag par gźol bas don dam pa’i bden pa rab tu śes so, raṅ daṅ spyi’i mtshan ñid rtogs pas mtshan ñid kyi bden pa rab tu śes so źes gsuṅs so – "Thus it is also said in the noble Daśabhūmikasūtra: ’He knows the concealed truth to please other beings according to their intentions, he knows the highest truth to attain the one principle, he knows the truth of essential characteristics to understand individual and general characteristics’."
The quotation is from Dbh. p. 4223-26: sa parasatvānāṃ yathāśayasaṃtoṣaṇāt saṃvṛtisatyam prajānāti, ekanayasamavasaraṇāt paramārthasatyam prajānāti, svasāmānyalakṣaṇānubodhāl lakṣaṇasatyam prajānāti. Dbh., in the sections 5c-d, also deals with satyakauśalya.


de la kun rdzob kyi bden pa gaṅ źe na?’jig rten gyi tha sñad daṅ, yi ge daṅ, sgra daṅ, brdas bstan pa ji sñed pa’o.don dam pa’i bden pa ni: gaṅ la sems kyi rgyu ba med pa ste, yi ge lta ci smos.mtshan ñid kyi bden pa ni: gaṅ ’di mtshan ñid thams cad mtshan ñid gcig pa ste; mtshan ñid gcig po yaṅ mtshan ñid med pa’o.

tatra katamat saṃvṛtisatyam?lokavyavahāro yāvad akṣaraśabdasaṃketanirdiṣṭam.paramārthasatyaṃ yatra cittasyāpy apracāraḥ, kaḥ punar vādo ’kṣarāṇām?lakṣaṇasatyaṃ yad idaṃ sarvalakṣaṇam ekalakṣaṇam, ekalakṣaṇam alakṣaṇam.

(p. 73) What is concealed truth?Worldly conventions, all that is expressed with syllables, words and designations.The highest truth is where there is no activity even of thoughts, so how can one speak of that of syllables?The truth of characteristics [which really is the same as the highest truth, a way to understand the highest truth] is that all characteristics have one characteristic, and that one characteristic is the absence of characteristics.

de la kun rdzob kyi bden pa bśad par bźed nas ’jig rten gyi tha sñad daṅ, yi ge daṅ, sgra daṅ, brdas bstan pa ji sñed pa źes gsuṅs te, ji sñed pa źes bya ba’i sgra thams cad daṅ sbyar te, ’jig rten gyi tha sñad ji sñed pa daṅ, yi ges bstan pa ji sñed pa daṅ, sgras bstan pa ji sñed pa daṅ, brdas bstan pa ji sñed pa źes bya bar sbyar ro. ji sñed kyi sgra ni ji tsam yod pa’i don draṅs te, ’jig rten gyi tha sñad ji tsam yod pa źes bya ba’i tha tshig go. de la ’jig rten gyi tha sñad ni bstan pa’o; lhag ma rnams ni bśad pa ste: yi ge a daṅ ka la sogs pa gsuṅ rab kyi luṅ daṅ ’brel pa rnams so; sgra ni gsuṅ rab kyi luṅ daṅ ’brel pa ’du byed mi rtag ces bya ba la sogs pa’i tshig gi rkaṅ pa rnams so; brda ni don ston par nus śiṅ khoṅ du chud par nus pa’i tshig gi rkaṅ pa rnams so. ji sñed ces bya ba’i tshig gi luṅ ’ba’ źig gi ma yin gyi, ’jig rten gyi yig ge daṅ sgra la sogs pa ci tsam yod pa rnams kyaṅ sdud de, de yaṅ yid kyi daṅ ṅag gi sgo nas ston pa rnam pa gñis so; de la yid kyis ston pa ni ji ltar brgya byin la yid kyis chos mṅon par bśad pa daṅ, de dag gis kyaṅ raṅ gi the tshom yid la btags pa daṅ, lan kyaṅ yid kyis tshigs su bcad pas glan no, mdo de daṅ de dag las ’byuṅ ba lta bu’o; ṅag gis bstan pa ni tshig gi rig byed rnam pa sna tshogs ñan pa’i gaṅ zag rnams kyi rna bar soṅ ba rnams so, de dag gis ni mdor na ’di skad du: gdul bar bya ba’i sems can rnams kyi dbaṅ du ji tsam du tha sñad brjod pa thams cad kun rdzob kyi bden pa yin no, źes bstan te, de ltar dkon mchog sprin gyi mdo las kyaṅ: rigs kyi bu, chos bcu daṅ ldan na byaṅ chub sems dpa’ kun rdzob la mkhas pa rnams yin no, bcu gaṅ źe na? ’di lta ste, gzug su’aṅ ’dogs la, don dam par na gzugs su’aṅ mi dmigs śiṅ mi chags so; de bźin du tshor ba daṅ, ’du śes daṅ, ’du byed daṅ, rnam par śes par kyaṅ ’dogs la, don dam par na rnam par śes par kyaṅ mi dmigs śiṅ mṅon par mi chags so źes bya ba nas saṅs rgyas kyi chos rnams su’aṅ ’dogs la, don dam par na saṅs rgyas kyi chos su yaṅ mi dmigs śiṅ mṅon par mi chags so; byaṅ chub tu’aṅ ’dogs la, byaṅ chub sems dpar yaṅ mi dmigs śiṅ de la mṅon par mi chags so; rigs kyi bu, de lta bas na miṅ daṅ, ’dogs pa daṅ, tha sñad de ni kun rdzob ces bya ste, kun rdzob kyi chos rnams la don dam pa med kyi, kun rdzob kyi chos med par yaṅ don dam pa bstan par mi nus so źes gsuṅs so.125b4-126a2: de las bzog pa ni don dam pa ste, de bstan par bźed nas don dam pa’i bden pa ni gaṅ la sems kyi rgyu ba yaṅ med pa ste, yi ge lta ci smos źes bya ba gsuṅ so. don dam pa ni skye ba daṅ, mi skye ba daṅ, bsam du yod pa daṅ, bsam du med pa daṅ, rtag pa daṅ, mi rtag pa daṅ, brjod du yod pa daṅ, brjod du med pa daṅ, ’gog pa daṅ, mi ’gog pa daṅ, śes par ruṅ ba daṅ, śes par mi ruṅ ba daṅ, rtag pa daṅ, mi rtag pa źes bya ba la sogs pa’i spros pa thams cad las ’das pa yin pas sems kyi rgyu ba med pa źes bya ste, sems daṅ sems las byuṅ ba’i spyod yul las ’das te, don dam pa daṅ de’i rig pa’i ye śes gñis su med pa’i phyir sems kyi yul du yaṅ mi ’gyur na yi ge lta ci smos źes bya ba’i tha tshig go. de bas na dkon mchog sprin gyi mdo las kyaṅ: rigs kyi bu, chos bcu daṅ ldan na byaṅ chub sems dpa’ don dam pa la mkhas pa rnams yin no, bcu gaṅ źe na? ’di lta ste, mi skye ba’i chos ñid daṅ ldan pa rnams yin, mi ’gog pa’i chos ñid daṅ, mi ’jig pa’i chos ñid daṅ, mi len mi ’dor ba’i chos ñid daṅ, tshig gi spyod yul las yaṅ dag par ’das pa’i chos ñid daṅ, smrar med pa’i chos ñid daṅ, spros pa med pa’i chos ñid daṅ, brjod du med pa’i chos ñid daṅ, źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅ so.
The Sanskrit fragment in Pras. p. 3742 reads jñānasya; cittasya is, however, confirmed by T1 p. 197b9 心行 xin xing, and also by Satyadvayavibhaṅgavṛtti (cf. Masamichi Ichigo in Taishūkyō no sōgōteki kenkyū p. 107): gaṅ la sems rgyu ba yaṅ med na).


de la byaṅ chub sems dpa’ kun rdzob kyi bden pa bstan pas kyaṅ yoṅs su mi skyo;don dam pa’i bden pa mṅon sum du byed par yaṅ mi ltuṅ;mtshan ñid kyi bden pas bden pa gcig tu rtogs kyaṅ, sems can rnams kyaṅ yoṅs su smin par byed de;’di ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i bden pa la mkhas pa źes bya’o.

tatra bodhisattvaḥ saṃvṛtisatyanirdeśena na parikhidyate,paramārthasatyasākṣātkaraṇe ’pi na patati;lakṣaṇasatyenaikasatyam adhigacchann api sattvān paripācayati;idam ucyate bodhisattvasya satyakauśalyam.

There the bodhisattva does not get tired of teachings of concealed truth [understanding things by insight (prajñā) to be non-existent (abhāva) like an illusion, a dream or a reflection],does not fall into realizing the highest truth [not being concerned, like the disciples, only with the peace of extinction and suchness (tathatā) ];even though understanding the one truth by means of the truth of characteristics he matures living beings;this called the bodhisattva’s skill with truths [including both insight and expedient means (prajñopāyaparigṛhīta) ].

de la mtshan ñid kyi bden pa bśad par bźed nas mtshan ñid kyi bden pa gaṅ źe na źes khoṅ nas dris pa daṅ mtshan ñid kyi bden pa ni: gaṅ ’di mtshan ñid thams cad mtshan ñid gcig pa ste źes bya ba gsuṅs te, ’di ltar sa’i mtshan ñid sra ba daṅ, chu’i mtshan ñid gśer ba daṅ, źes bya ba nas gzugs kyi mtshan ñid thogs pa daṅ bcas pa daṅ, tshor ba’i mtshan ñid myoṅ bar byed pa źes bya ba la sogs pa thams cad ni mtshan ñid gcig pa ste, de bźin ñid kyi mtshan ñid du ’dra ba’i phyir ro. mtshan ñid gcig po de’i mtshan ñid kyaṅ gaṅ źe na? de’i phyir mtshan ñid gcig po yaṅ mtshan ñid med pa’o źes bya ba gsuṅs te, de bźin ñid de ni mtshan ñid du bgraṅ ba thams cad las ’das pa ste, skye ba daṅ, ’gag pa daṅ, yod pa daṅ, med pa daṅ, rtag pa daṅ, mi rtag pa la sogs pa gaṅ gi mtshan ñid kyaṅ ma yin pas na mtshan ñid med pa’o. mtshan ñid med pa’i bden pa ’di yaṅ don dam pa’i bden pa ñid de, de la gźan ma yin na ci’i phyir don dam pa’i bden pa źes bya ba daṅ mtshan ñid kyi bden pa źes bya ba gñis su bśad? de ni bden te, de las gźan ma yin mod kyi, ’dis don dam pa mtshon par byed, khoṅ du chud par byed pas na mtshan ñid kyi bden pa ste. de bas na mtshan ñid kyi bden pa ni don dam pa la ’jug pa’i sgo lta bur gźag go. yaṅ na sems can rnam pa gsum gyi don gyi phyir bden pa rnam pa gsum bśad de, ñes pa med do.byaṅ chub sems dpa’i bden pa rnam pa gsum yaṅ thabs daṅ śes rab kyis yoṅs su zin pa yin te, de bstan pa’i phyir de la byaṅ chub sems dpa’ kun rdzob kyi bden pa bstan pas kyaṅ yoṅs su mi skyo ba źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs te, sems can gyi don du byaṅ chub sems dpa’ kun rdzob kyi bden pa tha sñad daṅ, yi ge daṅ, brda la sogs pa gźan la bstan kyaṅ kun rdzob kyi bden pa la yid ’byuṅ źiṅ skyo ba med de, śes rab kyis zin pas de dag sgyu ma daṅ, rmi lam daṅ, gzugs brñan lta bur dṅos po med par khoṅ du chud pa’i phyir ro. don dam pa’i bden pa mṅon sum du byed par yaṅ mi ltuṅ źes bya ba ni thabs kyis yoṅs su zin pas ji ltar ’phags pa ñan thos rnams źi ba phyogs gcig pa’i mya ṅan las ’das pa la gnas pa lta bur de bźin ñid ’ba’ źig gi phyogs su yaṅ gnas par mi byed ces bya ba’i don to.mtshan ñid kyi bden pa gcig tu rtogs kyaṅ sems can rnams yoṅs su smin par byed de źes bya ba ni mtshan ñid kyi bden pa khoṅ du chud pas don dam pa daṅ, kun rdzob kyi bden pa daṅ, sdug bsṅal daṅ, kun ’byuṅ ba daṅ, ’gog pa daṅ, lam la sogs pa’i bden pa rnams de bźin ñid kyi mtshan ñid du ro gcig par rtogs kyaṅ thabs rnam pa sna tshogs kyis theg pa rnam pa gsum du gar rigs rigs su sems can rnams yoṅs su smin par byed de, de lta bur thabs daṅ śes rab kyis yoṅs su zin pa’i bden pa rtogs pa ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i bden pa la mkhas pa źes bya’o.
ṭ. fol. 126b5-127a6 then quotes in an abridged form Paripākapaṭala in Bbh p. 78ff, on paripāka: de la yoṅs su smin pa gaṅ źe na? de yaṅ mdor rnam pa gsum ste: 1) yoṅs su smin pa’i raṅ bźin daṅ, 2) yoṅs su smin par bya ba’i gaṅ zag daṅ, 3) yoṅs su smin pa’i rnam pa rab tu dbye ba’o. 1) yoṅs su smin pa’i raṅ bźin ni dper na ’bras bu smin par gyur na rdol par ’os pa daṅ ’bras bu smin nas nam kun tu bza’ bar ’os pa’i dus na yoṅs su smin pa źes bya ba, de bźin du dge ba’i chos rnams kyi sa bon yaṅ nas yaṅ du bsten pa daṅ ldan pas ñon moṅs pa daṅ śes bya’i sgrib pa spoṅ bar nus pa daṅ rjes su mthun pa’i lus daṅ sems las su ruṅ ba rñed nas ñon moṅs pa daṅ śes bya’i sgrib pa spoṅ ba’i mthu daṅ ldan pa ni yoṅs su smin pa’i raṅ bźin źes bya’o. 2) yoṅs su smin par bya ba’i gaṅ zag ni rnam pa bźi ste, ñan thos kyi rigs can daṅ, raṅ saṅs rgyas kyi rigs can daṅ, saṅs rgyas kyi rigs can daṅ, rigs med pa’i gaṅ zag go. de la rigs can gsum ni theg pa gsum du yoṅs su smin par bya’o, rigs med pa’i gaṅ zag kyaṅ lha daṅ mi’i bde ’gror yoṅs su smin par bya’o. 3) yoṅs su smin pa’i rnam pa rab tu dbye ba yaṅ mdor na gsum ste, a) dbaṅ po yoṅs su smin pa daṅ, b) dge ba’i rtsa ba yoṅs su smin pa daṅ, c) śes pa yoṅs su smin pa’o. de la a) dbaṅ po yoṅs su smin pa ni tshe daṅ, mdog daṅ, rigs daṅ, dbaṅ phyug phun sum tshogs pa daṅ, tshig btsun pa daṅ, dbaṅ che bar grags pa daṅ, mir gyur pa daṅ, rig pa’i gnas rnams la mkhas pa’o. b) dge ba’i rtsa ba yoṅs su smin pa ni gaṅ raṅ bźin gyis ñon moṅs pa śas chuṅ ba las na raṅ bźin gyis sdig pa mi dge ba’i chos la sems mi ’jug ciṅ sgrib pa chuṅ ba daṅ, rtog pa ñuṅ ba daṅ, draṅ źiṅ mthun par ’dzin pa yin no. c) śes pa yoṅs su smin pa ni dran pa daṅ ldan pa, yid gźuṅs pa daṅ ldan pa, legs par smras pa daṅ ñes par smras pa’i chos rnams kyi don kun śes par nus śiṅ lhan cig skyes pa’i śes rab kyis raṅ gi sems la yod pa’i ñon moṅs pa sel nus pa’i mthu daṅ ldan pa’o.
Bbh. p. 781-7922: tatra paripākaḥ katamaḥ. paripākaḥ samāsataḥ ṣaḍbhir ākārair veditavyaḥ. svabhāvato ’pi paripācyapudgalato ’pi paripākaprabhedato ’pi [paripākopāyato ’pi paripācakapudgalato ’pi paripakvapudgalalakṣaṇato ’pi] ca.
1) tatrāyaṃ paripākasvabhāvaḥ kuśaladharmabīje sati kuśalānāṃ dharmāṇām āsevanānvayād yā kleśajñeyāvaraṇaprahāṇaviśuddhyanukūlā kāyacittakarmaṇyatā kalyatā samyakprayoganiṣṭhā [yatra sthitāḥ śāstāraṃ vā āgamyānāgamya vā śāstāraṃ bhavyo bhavati pratibalo ’nantaraṃ kleśāvaraṇaprahāṇaṃ vā sākṣātkartuṃ jñeyāvaraṇaprahāṇaṃ vā]. tad yathā vraṇo yadā paripāṭanāya niṣṭhāgato bhavaty anaṃtaraṃ pāṭanārhaḥ. sa paripakva ity ucyate. [ghaṭaghaṭīśarāvādi ca mṛnmayaṃ bhāṇḍaṃ yadā paribhogāya bhavaty anantaraṃ paribhogārhaṃ. tadā paripakva ity ucyate]. phalāni vā āmrapanasādīni yadā paribhogāya niṣṭhāgatāni bhavaṃty anantaraṃ paribhogārhāṇi. tadā paripakvānīty ucyaṃte. evam eva kuśalānāṃ dharmāṇām āsevanānvayād yāsau samyakprayoganiṣṭhā anantaraṃ viśuddhaye saṃvartate. sa paripākasvabhāvaḥ.
2) tatra paripācyāḥ pudgalāḥ samāsataś catvāraḥ. śrāvakagotraḥ śrāvakayāne. pratyekabuddhagotraḥ pratyekabuddhayāne. buddhagotro mahāyāne paripācayitavyaḥ. agotrastho ’pi pudgalaḥ sugatigamanāya paripācayitavyo bhavati. [bodhisattvānāṃ buddhānāṃ ca bhagavatāṃ ity ete catvāraḥ pudgalāḥ eṣu caturṣu vastuṣu paripācayitavyāḥ. evaṃ paripācyapudgalataḥ paripāko veditavyaḥ.]
3) tatra paripākaprabhedaḥ katamaḥ. samāsataḥ ṣaḍvidhaḥ. indriyaparipākaḥ. kuśalamūlaparipākaḥ. jñānaparipākaś ca [mṛdumadhyādhimātraś ca paripākaḥ].
a) tatrendriyaparipāko yā āyurvarṇakulaiśvaryasaṃpad ādeyavacanatā maheśākhyatā manuṣyatvaṃ [mahotsāhatā yām āśrayaparipākaphalasaṃpadam āgamya bhavyo bhavaty ātaptānuyogāyāparikhinnamānasaś ca] sarvavidyāsthānasamudāgamābhiyogeṣu.
b) kuśalamūlaparipākaḥ katamaḥ. yā prakṛtyā mandarajaskatāyām āgamya prakṛtyaivāsya pāpakeṣv akuśaleṣu cittaṃ na krāmati. mandanivaraṇaś ca bhavati mandavitarkaḥ ṛjupradakṣiṇagrāhī.
c) jñānaparipākaḥ katamaḥ. smṛtimāṃ bhavati medhāvī [pratibalaś] ca bhavati subhāṣitadurbhāṣitānāṃ dharmāṇām arthasya ājñānāya [udgrahaṇāya dhāraṇāya prativedhāya]. sahajayā prajñayā samanvāgato bhavati yāṃ prajñām āgamya bhavyo bhavati pratibalaḥ sarvato ’tayaṃtaṃ sarvasaṃkleśāc cittaṃ vimocayituṃ.
yoṅs su smin par byed pa ni theg pa gsum gyi rigs can gyi gaṅ zag rnams so so’i theg pa’i chos rnams daṅ po bstan pa daṅ, de nas bsam pa daṅ, bsgom pa la sogs pa’i rim pas khad kyis ñon moṅs pa daṅ śes bya’i sgrib pa spoṅs su btsud de, raṅ raṅ gi ’bras bu la ’god pa’o. The last paragraph of ṭ summarizes the rest of the Bbh-chapter.
Notes to the Sanskrit text: 1) ṭ tribhir 2) Bracketed parts, here and in the following, are not found in ṭ 3) The vraṇa and phala examples are confounded in ṭ, and the text is also further abridged. 4) ṭ trividhaḥ


gźan yaṅ bden pa rnam pa gñis te.rnam pa gñis po gaṅ źe na?gaṅ ’di: a) tha sñad kyi bden pa daṅ; b) don dam pa’i bden pa’o.

punar aparaṃ dvividhaṃ satyaṃ.katamad dvaividhyam?yad idaṃ vyavahārasatyaṃ paramārthasatyaṃ ca.

Further, truth is of two kinds.What two?Truth of conventions [to teach the holy way (āryamārga), or things known through worldly knowledge (laukikajñāna) ], and the highest truth [to teach the fruit of the way, (mārgaphala), or things known through supramundane knowledge (lokottarajñāna) ].

bden pa’i rnam pa gźan yaṅ bstan par bźed na gźan yaṅ bden pa rnam pa gñis te źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs te, gźan yaṅ źes bya ba ni sṅar bśad pa’i don du blta’o. ’dir yaṅ bstan pa daṅ bśad pa’i tshul khoṅ du chud par bya ba’i phyir rnam pa gñis po gaṅ źe na? gaṅ ’di tha sñad kyi bden pa daṅ don dam pa’i bden pa źes bya ba bstan pa’i tshul bśad do. de la tha sñad kyi bden pa ni gaṅ dus su źes bya ba la sogs pas bśad pa’i tshul bstan to. ’jig rten gyi tha sñad rnams bden pas na tha sñad kyi bden pa ste, ji ltar snaṅ ba tsam du bden pa’i phyir ro. de bas na mdo las kyaṅ: ’jig rten rnams las gaṅ yod par bden pa la yaṅ de bden no źes gsuṅs so. don dam pa ñid bden pas na don dam pa’i bden pa ste, ji ltar gnas pa las gźan du mi ’gyur ba’i phyir ro. de bas na mdo las kyaṅ: ’dus byas rnams ni bslu bas na brdzun pa yin gyi, ’dus ma byas ni bden pa’o źes gsuṅs so. ci’i phyir bden pa gñis bśad ce na? ’phags pa’i lam daṅ lam gyi ’bras bu bstan par bya ba’i phyir bden pa gñis bśad de: ’phags pa’i lam bstan pa’i phyir tha sñad kyi bden pa bśad do, lam de’i ’bras bu bstan par bya ba’i phyir don dam pa’i bden pa bśad do. yaṅ na ’jig rten pa’i śes pa’i yul daṅ ’jig rten las ’das pa’i śes pa’i yul la dgoṅs nas bden gñis bśad de: ’jig rten pa’i śes pa’i yul la dgoṅs nas tha sñad kyi bden pa bśad do, ’jig rten las ’das pa’i śes pa’i yul la dgoṅs nas don dam pa’i bden pa bśad do.


de la tha sñad kyi bden pa ni: gaṅ dus su bden par smra ba ste; gaṅ ’di sdug bsṅal gyi bden pa daṅ, kun ’byuṅ ba’i bden pa daṅ, ’gog pa’i bden pa daṅ, lam gyi bden pa daṅ,’jig rten gyi tha sñad daṅ, yi ge daṅ, sgra daṅ, brdas bstan pa ji sñed pa’o.don dam pa’i bden pa gaṅ ’di brjed pa med pa’i chos can mya ṅan las ’das pa ste.de ci’i phyir źe na?rtag tu chos kyi de bźin ñid kyi phyir,de’i rigs ni rtag pa’i phyir ro.

tatra vyavahārasatyaṃ yā kāle satyavāditā yad idaṃ duḥkhasatyaṃ samudayasatyaṃ nirodhasatyaṃ mārgasatyaṃ;lokavyavahārasatyaṃ yāvad akṣaraśabdasaṃketanirdiṣṭam.paramārthasatyaṃ yad idam asaṃmoṣadharma nirvāṇam.tat kasya hetoḥ?nityadharmatathatātvāt,tadgotranityatvāt.

[Non-confused (abhrānta) and pure worldly knowledge attained after the experience (pṛṣṭhalabdhaṃ laukikaṃ jñānam):] The truth of conventions is speaking the truth at the time [one comes back from concentration beyond thought-constructions (nirvikalpasamādhi), explaining the truths as experienced to mature those to be educated], the truth of suffering, the truth of origin, the truth of cessation and the truth of the way;[and confused (bhrānta) worldly knowledge:] the conventions of the world, all that is expressed with syllables, sounds and designations.The highest truth is the moment of existence never lost, extinction.Why?Because it is always the state of things such as they are,because the essence of that [state of things] is always there.

de la tha sñad kyi bden pa bstan pa’i phyir tha sñad kyi bden pa ni źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs te, tshig gis mṅon par brjod pa maṅ po ni tha sñad do, brjod pa des khoṅ du chud par ’gyur ba’i bden pa ni tha sñad kyi bden pa’o. tha sñad kyi bden pa de’aṅ rnam pa gñis te, ma ’khrul pa’i ’jig rten pa’i śes pa’i yul daṅ, ’khrul pa’i ’jig rten pa’i śes pa’i yul lo. de la ma ’khrul pa’i ’jig rten pa’i śes pa ni rjes las thob pa dag pa ’jig rten pa’i ye śes te, de’i yul bstan pa’i phyir gaṅ dus su bden pa smra ba ste, gaṅ ’di sdug bsṅal gyi bden pa daṅ źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs pa’o. de la gaṅ dus su bden par smra ba źes bya ba ni de bźin khoṅ du chud pa daṅ ldan pa’i gaṅ zag rnam par mi rtog pa’i tiṅ ṅe ’dzin las laṅs nas bdag gis ji ltar myoṅ ba’i don ’dul ba rnams yoṅs su smin pa’i dus daṅ sbyar te, rjes las thob pa dag pa ’jig rten pa’i ye śes kyis ’di ni sdug bsṅal gyi bden pa ’di ni kun ’byuṅ ba’i bden pa’o źes phyin ci ma log par ’chad ciṅ ston pa ni dus su bden par smra ba źes bya’o. ’khrul pa’i ’jig rten pa’i śes pa’i yul bstan pa’i phyir ’jig rten gyi tha sñad daṅ źes bya ba la sogs pa smras te, ’jig rten gyi tha sñad yi ge daṅ ’brel pa’i sgras bstan pa’i brda ni ’jig rten gyi tha sñad daṅ yi ge daṅ sgra daṅ brdas bstan pa źes bya ste, ’jig rten gyi tha sñad thams cad ni brdzun pa yin pas na ’khrul pa’o. yaṅ na gdul ba’i dus su bden par smra ba ni tha sñad kyi bden pa źes bya ste, de la bden pa gaṅ źe na? gaṅ sdug bsṅal gyi bden pa daṅ źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs pa’o. smra ba gaṅ źe na? ’jig rten gyi tha sñad daṅ źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs te, don du na ’jig rten gyi tha sñad daṅ mthun pa’i yi ge daṅ sgra daṅ brdas sdug bsṅal la sogs pa bden pa bźi bstan pa ni tha sñad kyi bden pa źes bya’o.don dam pa’i bden pa bstan par bya ba’i phyir don dam pa’i bden pa ni gaṅ ’di brjed pa med pa’i chos can mya ṅan las ’das pa źes bya ba gsuṅs te, ’jig rten las ’das pa’i ye śes dam pa’i yul lam ’bras bu yin pas na don dam pa’o. gaṅ brjed pa med pa’i chos daṅ ldan pa ni brjed pa med pa’i chos can te, skye ba daṅ ’jig pa med pa’i raṅ bźin thog ma nas ṅo bo ñid kyis ’od gsal ba de bźin ñid bslu ba med pa’i chos can de ni don dam pa’i bden pa źes bya’o – "...
