The essentially unborn and undestroyed, originally brilliant, true suchness is the highest truth (anudayavyayādiprakṛtiprabhāsvarāvitathatathatādharma tad paramārthasatyam iti)."
de ci’i phyir źe na źes bya ba ni de bźin ñid de ci’i phyir bslu ba med pa’i chos can źes bya ba źe na źes bya ba’i tha tshig go; bslu ba med pa’i chos can gyi rgyu bstan pa’i phyir rtag tu chos kyi de bźin ñid kyi phyir, de’i rigs ni rtag pa’i phyir ro źes bya ba gsuṅs te, de’i rigs źes bya ba ni de bźin ñid de’i raṅ bźin no. de bźin ñid de’i raṅ bźin ni skye ba daṅ ’jig pa med pa’i raṅ bźin las gźan du mi ’gyur bas rtag pa ste, de bas na mi bslu ba źes bya ba, ji ltar rtag ce na? rtag tu chos kyi de bźin ñid kyi phyir te, chos kyi de bźin ñid kyi ṅo bo la ni so so’i skye bo daṅ, ’phags pa’i dus na yaṅ de la mtshan ñid tha dad du gyur pa med pa’i phyir ro. de la mi bslu ba’i don ci raṅ bźin gźan du gnas la gźan du mi ston pa ni mi bslu ba ste, ji ltar ’dus byas ’dus byas kyi ṅo bo ñid du med na, de ni de’i ṅo bo ñid du snaṅ bas na bslu ba źes bya ba’i don dam pa ni raṅ bźin gźan du mi ’gyur te, de la de bźin du ston par byed pas na mi bslu ba źes bya’o. de bas na mdo las kyaṅ: mi bslu ba’i chos can mya ṅan las ’das pa ni bden pa gcig pu’o, ’du byed thams cad daṅ snod kyi ’jig rten ni brdzun pa bslu ba’i chos can no źes gsuṅs so.


de la byaṅ chub sems dpa’ tha sñad kyi bden pa bstan pas kyaṅ yoṅs su mi skyo; don dam pa’i bden pa mṅon sum du byed par yaṅ mi ltuṅ la sems can rnams kyaṅ yoṅs su smin par byed pa; ’di ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i bden pa la mkhas pa źes bya’o.

tatra bodhisattvo vyavahārasatyena na parikhidyate, paramārthasatyasākṣātkaraṇe ’pi na patati, sattvān paripācayati, idam ucyate bodhisattvasya satyakauśalyam.

[Including both insight and expedient means (prajñopāyaparigṛhīta):] There the bodhisattva does not get tired of conventional truth, and does not fall into realizing the highest truth, but matures living beings; this is called the bodhisattva’s skill with truths.

’dir yaṅ thabs daṅ śes rab kyis yoṅs su zin pa bstan pa’i phyir ro: de la byaṅ chub sems dpa’ tha sñad kyi bden pa bstan pas kyaṅ yoṅs su mi skyo źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs te, tha sñad kyi bden pa bstan pa ni sdug bsṅal daṅ kun ’byuṅ ba la sogs pa bdag gis gźan la bśad pa’am, gźan gyis bdag la bstan pa ste, yoṅs su mi skyo ba ni śes rab kyi tha sñad kyi bden pa thams cad don dam par dṅos po med par khoṅ du chud pas de dag las yid byuṅ źiṅ skrag pa daṅ dṅos por ’dzin par mi ’gyur źes bya ba’i don to. don dam pa’i bden pa mṅon sum du byed par yaṅ mi ltuṅ la źes bya ba ni chos thams cad sgyu ma daṅ rmi lam lta bur khoṅ du chud de, de yaṅ ma brtags na gcig tu dga’ ba tsam med pa ma yin źes rig pa’i thabs kyis yoṅs su zin pas na, de kho na ñid ’ba’ źig la yaṅ gnas par mi byed la, thabs daṅ śes rab kyis sems can rnams yoṅs su smin par byed pa ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i bden pa la mkhas pa źes bya ba’i don to.


gźan yaṅ bden pa ni gcig ste, gñis su med do.de la bden pa gcig ni: gaṅ ’di chos thams cad la sgro ’dogs pa med ciṅ, sgro ’dogs par ltuṅ ba’i sems can rnams kyaṅ bden pa la rab tu ’dzud pa’o.

punar aparam ekam eva satyaṃ na dvitīyam asti.tatraikasatyaṃ yo ’yaṃ sarvadharmeṣv asamāropaḥ, samāropapatitānāṃ sattvānāṃ satyāvatāraṇatā.

Further, truth is one, there is no second.The one truth is not to impute anything to any moment of existence, but to bring living beings who have fallen into such imputation to truth.

chos ’di pa daṅ phyi rol pa rnams lta ba rnam pa sna tshogs la mṅon par źen pa’i gñen por gźan yaṅ bden pa ni gcig ste, gñis su med do źes bya ba gsuṅs so. gñis su med do źes bya bas ni ’dir bden pa gcig bstan pa las ma gtogs pa rnams yaṅ dag pa ma yin par ston pa’o. Cf. Bbh. p. 29217-18; quoted supra ad ṭ fol. 122a5-7.bden pa gcig po gaṅ źe na źes khoṅ nas dris pa daṅ de la bden pa gcig ni gaṅ ’di chos thams cad la sgro ’dogs pa med ciṅ, sgro ’dogs par ltuṅ ba’i sems can rnams kyaṅ bden pa la rab tu gzud pa’o źes bya ba gsuṅs te, chos thams cad brjod pa med pa’i raṅ bźin yin pa la, gal te miṅ daṅ tshig daṅ yi ge dag gis gaṅ zag daṅ chos kyi ṅo bo ñid dam bye brag tu ’dogs na de ni sgro ’dogs pa yin te, chos rnams kyi raṅ bźin ji skad du btags pa de dag ma yin pa’i phyir ro. de ltar chos rnams la sgro mi ’dogs śiṅ, de bźin ñid kyi raṅ bźin du yaṅ śes par byed la, sgro ’dogs par ltuṅ ba spros pas tshogs la mṅon par źen pa’i sems can rnams kyaṅ brjod du med pa’i bden pa de la rab tu ’dzud pa ni bden pa gcig ces bya’o.
Cf. infra.


de la byaṅ chub sems dpa’ sgro ’dogs pa’i bden pa bstan pas kyaṅ mi skyo la, sgro ’dogs pa med pa’i bden pa gcig bstan pa yaṅ mṅon sum du mi byed ciṅ, sems can rnams kyaṅ yoṅs su smin par byed pa;’di ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i bden pa la mkhas pa źes bya’o.

tatra bodhisattvaḥ samāropasatyanirdeśena na parikhidyate, asamāropaikasatyanirdeśam api na sākṣātkaroti, sattvān paripācayati;idam ucyate bodhisattvasya satyakauśalyam.

[Insight and expedient means (prajñopāya):] There the bodhisattva does not get tired of teachings imputed [with existence and non-existence], and does not realize the one truth of non-imputation, but matures living beings;this is called the bodhisattva’s skill with truths.

’dir yaṅ thabs daṅ śes rab kyis bstan pa’i phyir de la byaṅ chub sems dpa’ sgro ’dogs pa’i bden pa bstan pas kyaṅ mi skyo la źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs te, de ltar bden pa gcig po de ni tshig gi spyod yul ma yin yaṅ, sems can de la gzud pa’i thabs gźan med pas ’dus byas daṅ ’dus ma byas źes bya ba la sogs pa’i tshig gis sgro btags nas ston pa ni sgro ’dogs pa’i bden pa ste, de dag bstan pas kyaṅ mi skyo źes bya ba’i don to. bśad pa gźan ni sṅa ma bźin du blta’o.


gźan yaṅ phuṅ po lṅa ni sdug bsṅal ba ste, gaṅ phuṅ po lṅa rnams kyi mtshan ñid, ’di ni sdug bsṅal źes bya’o;gaṅ gis sdug bsṅal gyi mtshan ñid de stoṅ par rtogs pa, ’di ni sdug bsṅal la sdug bsṅal du śes pa ’phags pa’i bden pa’o.

punar aparaṃ pañcaskandhā duḥkhāḥ, yat pañcaskandhānāṃ lakṣaṇam idaṃ duḥkham iti.yas tad duḥkhalakṣaṇaṃ śūnyam adhigacchatīdaṃ duḥkhe duḥkhajñānam āryasatyam.

Further [to elucidate the four truths mentioned above], the five parts of personality are filled with suffering; the essential character of the five parts of personality is suffering.When one understands that essential character of suffering to be empty [and not like a substance (sadbhāva) as the disciples believe], this is the holy truth of knowledge of suffering as suffering.

goṅ du bden pa bźi bśad pa’i rnam graṅs bstan par bźed de, sdug bsṅal gaṅ yin pa bstan pa’i phyir gźan yaṅ phuṅ po lṅa ni sdug bsṅal ba ste, gaṅ phuṅ po lṅa rnams kyi mtshan ñid, ’di ni sdug bsṅal źes bya’o źes gsuṅs te, de la daṅ po daṅ bar ma daṅ tha ma’i sdug bsṅal rnams bsdus pa’i don gyis ni gzugs la sogs pa’i phuṅ po lṅa ni sdug bsṅal ba źes bya ste, de la daṅ po’i sdug bsṅal ni skye ba’o, bar gyi sdug bsṅal ni na ba daṅ rga ba daṅ ’dod pa mi rñed pa la sogs pa’o, tha ma’i sdug bsṅal ni ’chi ba ste, sdug bsṅal de dag ñe bar len pa’i phuṅ po lṅa’i gnas der ’dus pas na phuṅ po lṅa ni sdug bsṅal ba źes bya ste, de la phuṅ po lṅa rnams kyi sdug bsṅal gyi mtshan ñid gaṅ yin pa sdug bsṅal yin par ston to.ji ltar sdug bsṅal śes pa bstan pa’i phyir gaṅ gis sdug bsṅal gyi mtshan ñid de stoṅ par rtogs pa, ’di ni sdug bsṅal la sdug bsṅal du śes pa ’phags pa’i bden pa’o źes gsuṅs te, ’phags pa ñan thos dag ltar sdug bsṅal gyi dṅos po yod par lta ba ma yin gyi, gaṅ zag gaṅ gis goṅ du bśad pa’i sdug bsṅal ñid kyaṅ raṅ bźin med ciṅ mi dmigs par rtogs pa, de ni sdug bsṅal la sdug bsṅal du śes pa ’phags pa’i bden pa źes bya’o.
For this kind of expression where the relative pronoun is related to an implied correlative in the genitive cf. Rkp p. 2713-303, e. g. ... dhāraṇīmatir bodhisattva āha / yo bhagavan na traidhātukaṃ na trīṇi saṃyojanāni na traividyatāṃ na tṛyānatāṃ na skandhadhātvāyatanāni na kalpayati na vikalpayati na hāniṃ na vṛddhiṃ na sāmīcīkaroty eṣa evābhisaṃbodhaḥ // ... akṣayamatir bodhisattva āha / yas trimaṇḍalapariśuddhyā pāramitāsv abhyāsaṃ karoty anupalaṃbhayogena na rajyate na virajyata eṣa evābhisaṃbodhaḥ // ...
T1 p. 197b23 reads ṛD qiu – spṛhayati (?)


gaṅ phuṅ po lṅa’i sred pa’i rgyu daṅ lta ba’i rgyu bag la ñal ba, ’di ni kun ’byuṅ ba źes bya’o;gaṅ gis sred pa’i rgyu daṅ lta ba’i rgyu de dag mi len pa daṅ, sgro mi ’dogs pa daṅ, reg par mi byed pa, ’di ni kun ’byuṅ ba la kun ’byuṅ bar śes pa ’phags pa’i bden pa źes bya’o.

yaḥ pañcaskandhānāṃ tṛṣṇāhetudṛṣtihetvanuśayo ’yaṃ samudaya iti.yas tau tṛṣṇāhetudṛṣṭihetū nopādatte na samāropayati na spṛśatīdaṃ samudaye samudayajñānam āryasatyam.

The proclivity of thirst as a cause and view-points as a cause for the five parts of personality is the origin in question.When one does not grasp, impute [existence or non-existence] to, or touch the cause of thirst and the cause of view-points, this is the holy truth of knowledge of origin as origin.

kun ’byuṅ ba gaṅ yin pa bstan pa’i phyir gaṅ phuṅ po lṅa’i sred pa’i rgyu daṅ lta ba’i rgyu bag la ñal ’di ni kun ’byuṅ ba źes gsuṅs te, phuṅ po lṅa po de dag skyed pa’i rgyu ni phuṅ po lṅa’i rgyu ste, de yaṅ sred pa’i rgyu daṅ lta ba’i rgyu las phuṅ po lṅa la skye’o. de la sred pa daṅ lta ba ni sṅar bśad par zad do, sred pa daṅ lta ba de dag ñid rgyu yin pas sred pa’i rgyu daṅ lta ba’i rgyu źes bya ste, bag la ñal yaṅ de gñis la bya’o. ji ltar kun ’byuṅ ba śes pa bstan pa’i phyir gaṅ gis sred pa’i rgyu daṅ lta ba’i rgyu de dag mi len pa daṅ źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs te, mi len pa ni sred pa daṅ lta ba la mtshan mar mi ’dzin pa’o, sgro mi ’dogs pa ni de dag la med pa daṅ yod par mi lta ba’o, reg par mi byed pa ni de dag gi raṅ bźin la rtog par mi byed pa’am, sred pa daṅ lta ba la spyod par mi byed pa’o; des ni ’di skad bstan te, phuṅ po lṅa’i rgyu sred pa daṅ lta ba rnams raṅ bźin gyis mi dmigs śiṅ dṅos po med par rtogs na kun ’byuṅ ba la kun ’byuṅ bar śes pa ’phags pa’i bden pa źes bya’o.


gaṅ phuṅ po lṅa rnams śin tu zad de ’gags nas, sṅon gyi mthar mi ’byuṅ ba daṅ, phyi ma’i mthar mi ’pho ba daṅ, da ltar byuṅ bar phyin pa med pa, ’di ni ’gog pa ’phags pa’i bden pa ste,de la gaṅ gis de ltar śes pa, ’di ni ’gog pa la ’gog par śes pa ’phags pa’i bden pa źes bya’o.

yat pañcaskandhā atyantakṣīṇaniruddhāḥ pūrvāntāsaṃbhūtā aparāntācyutāḥ pratyutpannāsaṃprāptā idaṃ nirodha āryasatyam iti.tatra ya evaṃ jānātīdaṃ nirodhe nirodhajñānam āryasatyam.

That the five parts of personality have completely perished and ceased, not being born in the beginning, not dying in the end and not possible to reach in the present, this is the holy truth of cessation.When one knows it in this way, this is the holy truth of knowledge of cessation as cessation.

’gog pa’i bden pa’i raṅ bźin gaṅ yin pa bstan pa’i phyir gaṅ phuṅ po lṅa rnams śin tu zad de ’gags nas, sṅon gyi mthar mi ’byuṅ ba daṅ źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs so, śin tu zad pa ni phuṅ po lṅa bskyed pa’i rgyu sred pa’i bag la ñal daṅ lta ba’i bag la ñal spaṅs pas skyed ba’i rgyun chad pa’o, ’gags pa ni skye ba gźan daṅ mtshams mi sbyor źiṅ ma ’oṅs pa’i phuṅ po skyed pa’i rgyu mi byed pa’o; yaṅ na skad cig ma re re la skye ba med pas na śin tu zad pa źes bya’o, tshe’i ñiṅ mtshams gcig nas gcig tu mtshams sbyor źiṅ skye ba med pas na ’gag pa’o; yaṅ na skye ba’i mtshan ñid daṅ bral ba’i phyir śin tu zad pa’o, ’jig pa’i chos daṅ bral ba’i phyir śin tu ’gag pa’o; de ñid kyi don gsal bar bstan pa’i phyir sṅon gyi mthar mi ’byuṅ ba daṅ phyi ma’i mthar mi ’pho ba daṅ, da ltar byuṅ bar phyin pa med pa źes bya ba gsuṅs te, sṅon gyi mthar mi ’byuṅ ba ni ’das pa’i dus su yaṅ ma skyes pa’o, phyi ma’i mthar mi ’pho ba ni da ltar gyi dus nas phuṅ po lṅa’i rgyu las daṅ ñon moṅs pa ma lus par spaṅs śiṅ, phuṅ po lṅa yaṅ raṅ bźin med pas ma ’oṅs pa’i dus kyi tshe daṅ mtshams sbyor ba med pa’o, da ltar byuṅ bar phyin pa med pa ni ’das pa’i las daṅ ñon moṅs pas da ltar gyi dus su’aṅ skyes pa med pa ste, de ltar dus sum du yaṅ phuṅ po lṅa ma skyes pa de ni ’gog pa’i bden pa’i raṅ bźin no. ji ltar na ’gog pa’i bden pa śes pa bstan pa’i phyir de la gaṅ gis de ltar śes pa, ’di ni źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs te, phuṅ po lṅa po skye ba med pa’i mtshan ñid la gaṅ zag gaṅ gis goṅ du bśad pa lta bur ’gog pa’i bden pa ṅo bo ñid kyis stoṅ ste, skye ba daṅ ’gag pa med par khoṅ du chud ciṅ mi dmigs par śes pa ni ’gog pa la ’gog par śes pa ’phags pa’i bden pa źes bya’o.


lam gaṅ la brten te, sdug bsṅal śes pa daṅ, kun ’byuṅ ba śes pa daṅ, ’gog pa śes pa la reg ciṅ gñis su med pa’i ye śes su ’jog pa, de ni sdug bsṅal ’gog par ’gro ba’i lam ’phags pa’i bden pa źes bya ste;gaṅ ’di la stoṅ pa ñid du śes pa, ’di ni lam la lam du śes pa ’phags pa’i bden pa źes bya’o.

yan mārgam āśritya duḥkhajñānaṃ samudayajñānaṃ nirodhajñānaṃ spṛśann advayajñānam bhāvayati tad duḥkhanirodhagaminī pratipad āryasatyam.yad iha śūnyatājñānam idaṃ mārge mārgajñānam āryasatyam.

The way relying on which one touches the knowledge of suffering, the knowledge of origin and the knowledge of cessation [that is, one does not see suffering and origin as the negative side (kṛṣṇapakṣa) and cessation as the positive side (śuklapakṣa) ], but cultivates knowledge without conflicts, this is (p. 74) the holy truth of the way to cessation of suffering.Knowledge of emptiness in this is the holy truth of knowledge of the way as the way.

lam gyi bden pa’i raṅ bźin bstan pa’i phyir lam gaṅ la brten te, sdug bsṅal śes pa daṅ, kun ’byuṅ ba śes pa daṅ, ’gog pa śes pa la reg ciṅ źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs so, lam gaṅ la brten te źes bya ba ni sdug bsṅal daṅ kun ’byuṅ ba daṅ, ’gog pa gsum raṅ bźin gyis stoṅ par khoṅ du chud pa’i lam gaṅ la gnas te źes bya ba’i tha tshig go, reg ciṅ źes bya ba ni sdug bsṅal daṅ kun ’byuṅ ba gñis la nag po’i phyogs su’aṅ mi lta, ’gog pa la dkar po’i phyogs su’aṅ mi lta źes bya ba’i don to, gñis su med pa’i ye śes su ’jog ces bya ba ni de gñis dbyer med par khoṅ du chud ces bya ba’i don to. de ltar ’jog pa’i ye śes de ni lam ’phags pa’i bden pa źes bya ste, sdug bsṅal ’gog par ’gro ba źes bya ba ni sdug bsṅal ’gog pa ’thob pa’am, chud par byed pa’i lam źes bya ba’i don to. ji ltar na lam gyi bden pa śes par gyur pa bstan pa’i phyir ro. gaṅ ’di la stoṅ pa ñid du śes pa, ’di ni lam la lam du śes pa ’phags pa’i bden pa’o źes bya ba gsuṅs te, de lta bu’i lam gyi bden pa de yaṅ stoṅ pa ñid du rtogs te, mi dmigs par khoṅ du chud pa de ni lam la lam du śes pa ’phags pa’i bden pa źes bya’o.


gaṅ gis ’phags pa’i bden pa bźi po ’di dag la de ltar ye śes kyis rtog ciṅ, bden pa’i rtog pas mi rtog pa, ’di ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i bden pa la mkhas pa źes bya’o.

ya imāni catvāry āryasatyāny evaṃjñānena pratyavekṣate na satyakalpanayā pratyavekṣata idam ucyate bodhisattvasya satyakauśalyam.

[To summarize:] When he sees the four holy truths with such knowledge, and does not see them through thought-constructions regarding truths, this is called the bodhisattva’s skill with truths.

bden pa rgya cher bśad pa rnams bsdus te bstan pa’i phyir gaṅ gis ’phags pa’i bden pa bźi po ’di dag la de ltar ye śes kyis rtog ciṅ, bden pa’i rtog pas mi rtog pa, ’di ni źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs te, gaṅ gis źes bya ba ni gaṅ zag gaṅ gis so, ’phags pa’i bden pa bźi po ’di dag la źes bya ba ni sdug bsṅal la sogs pa pa bden pa bźi goṅ du bśad pa rnams la’o, de ltar ye śes rtog ciṅ źes bya ba ni goṅ du bśad pa’i tshul du bden pa bźi po de dag ṅo bo ñid kyis stoṅ par khoṅ du chud pa’o, bden pa’i rtog pas mi rtog pa źes bya ba ni ’phags pa’i bden pa de dag ñid ṅo bo ñid kyis med par khoṅ du chud pas bden pa de dag la bden par yaṅ mi ’dzin ces bya ba’i don to, de lta bu ni ’phags pa’i bden pa la mkhas pa źes bya’o.


gźan yaṅ tshor ba thams cad sdug bsṅal te, ’di ni sdug bsṅal źes bya’o;tshor ba de la rnam par ’byed ciṅ rig par śes pa, ’di ni sdug bsṅal la sdug bsṅal du śes pa ’phags pa’i bden pa źes bya’o.tshor ba de rgyu gaṅ gis kun ’byuṅ ba, ’di ni kun ’byuṅ ba źes bya ste; gaṅ gis rgyu de yaṅ dag pa ji lta ba bźin du rab tu śes pa, ’di ni kun ’byuṅ ba la kun ’byuṅ bar śes pa ’phags pa’i bden pa źes bya’o.gaṅ tshor ba thams cad rgyun chad de, tshor ba med pa yaṅ tshor źiṅ, tshor ba ’gog pa la yaṅ rtog la sems can la lta ba’i phyir tshor ba ’gog pa mṅon sum du yaṅ mi byed pa, ’di ni ’gog pa la ’gog par śes pa ’phags pa’i bden pa źes bya’o.tshor ba gaṅ gis bsgrubs pa’i lam, de ni gziṅs lta bu ste; gaṅ tshor ba ’dod pa, de ni lam ’dod pa ma yin no. ’di ni lam la lam du śes pa ’phags pa’i bden pa źes bya’o.

punar aparam sarvavedanā duḥkhā idaṃ duḥkham iti.tāṃ vedanāṃ vicinoti vidyayā jānātīdam duḥkhe duḥkhajñānam āryasatyam.sā vedanā hetunā yena samudetīdaṃ samudaya iti, yena sa hetur yathābhūtaṃ prajñāyata idaṃ samudaye samudayajñānam āryasatyam.yaḥ sarvavedanāṃ vicchinatty avedanāṃ ca vedayati, vedanānirodhaṃ pratyavekṣate sattvāvekṣayā ca vedanānirodhaṃ na sākṣātkarotīdaṃ nirodhe nirodhajñānam āryasatyam.yayā vedanayā pratipanno mārgaḥ sā kolopamā, yā vedanākāmatā sā na mārgakāmatā, idam mārge mārgajñānam āryasatyam.

Further, [to teach the four truths in other aspects:] all feelings are suffering, this is the suffering in question.One discerns feeling and knows it through knowledge, this is the holy truth of knowledge of suffering as suffering.The cause by which that feeling arises is called origin, and that [insight (prajñā) ] by which this cause is known as it is, this is the holy truth of knowledge of origin as origin.When one interrupts every feeling and experiences non-feeling, and, though regarding the cessation of feeling, one does not realize the cessation of feeling, for the sake of living beings, this is the holy truth of knowledge of cessation as cessation.The feeling by which the way is realized is like a raft, while desire for feeling is not desire for the way. This is the holy truth of knowledge of the way as the way.

’phags pa’i bden pa bźi’i rnam pa gźan yaṅ bśad par bźed de, sdug bsṅal gyi bden pa’i raṅ bźin bstan pa’i phyir gźan yaṅ tshor ba thams cad sdug bsṅal te źes bya ba gsuṅs so, de la tshor ba thams cad ni sdug bsṅal gyi tshor ba daṅ, bde ba’i tshor ba daṅ, bde ba yaṅ ma yin sdug bsṅal ba yaṅ ma yin pa’i tshor ba’o; de la sdug bsṅal gyi tshor ba ni raṅ bźin gyis sdug bsṅal bas sdug bsṅal ba’o, bde ba’i tshor ba daṅ bde ba yaṅ ma yin sdug bsṅal ba yaṅ ma yin pa’i tshor ba ni mthar sdug bsṅal du ’gyur ba daṅ, ’du byed kyi sdug bsṅal gyis khyab pas sdug bsṅal ba ste, tshor ba thams cad sdug bsṅal ba ’di ni sdug bsṅal gyi bden pa’i raṅ bźin no.ji ltar na sdug bsṅal gyi raṅ bźin śes par ’gyur ba bstan pa’i phyir tshor ba de la rnam par ’byed ciṅ rig par śes pa źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅ so, tshor ba de la źes bya ba ni goṅ du bśad pa’i tshor ba rnam pa gsum la’o, rnam par ’byed ces bya ba ni sdug bsṅal gyi tshor ba ni raṅ bźin gyis sdug bsṅal bas khyab pa daṅ bde ba’i tshor ba ni ’gyur ba’i sdug bsṅal bas khyab pa daṅ, bde ba yaṅ ma yin sdug bsṅal ba yaṅ ma yin pa’i tshor ba ni ’du byed kyi sdug bsṅal gyis khyab par bye brag phyed ciṅ źes bya ba’i don to, rig par śes pa źes bya ba ni tshor ba de dag kyaṅ mi dmigs par khoṅ du chud ces bya ba’i don te, goṅ du bśad pa lta bur tshor ba thams cad sdug bsṅal yin par bye brag phyed ciṅ mi dmigs pa śes pa de ni sdug bsṅal la sdug bsṅal du śes pa ’phags pa’i bden pa źes bya’o.kun ’byuṅ ba’i raṅ bźin bstan pa’i phyir tshor ba de rgyu gaṅ gis kun ’byuṅ ba, de ni kun ’byuṅ ba źes bya ste źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs te, goṅ du bśad pa’i tshor ba de dag rgyu gaṅ gis bskyed ciṅ phyuṅ ba’i rgyu de ni kun ’byuṅ ba źes bya ste, tshor ba kun ’byuṅ ba’i rgyu ni reg pa ste, reg pa las tshor ba ’byuṅ bas na reg pa la kun ’byuṅ ba źes bya’o. de bas na mdo las reg pa’i rkyen gyis tshor ba, tshor ba’i rkyen gyis sred pa la sogs pa gsuṅs so. ji ltar na kun ’byuṅ ba śes par ’gyur ba bstan pa’i phyir gaṅ gis rgyu de yaṅ dag pa ji lta ba bźin du rab tu śes pa źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs te,
gaṅ gis śes bya ba ni gaṅ zag gaṅ gis sam śes rab gaṅ gis śes bya ba’i don to: alternatively "that [person (pudgala)] by which this cause is known as it is, this is [his] holy truth of knowledge of origin as origin".
rgyu de źes bya ba ni tshor ba’i rgyu reg pa ste źes bya ba’i tha tshig go. yaṅ dag pa ji lta ba bźin du rab tu śes źes bya ba’i tshor ba ’byuṅ ba’i rgyu de stoṅ pa ñid du phyin ci ma log par khoṅ du chud ces bya ba’i don to.’gog pa’i bden pa’i raṅ bźin gaṅ yin pa daṅ, ji ltar na ’gog pa’i bden pa śes par ’gyur ba bstan pa’i phyir gaṅ tshor ba thams cad rgyun chad de, tshor ba med pa yaṅ tshor źiṅ źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs te, goṅ du smos pa lta bu’i tshor ba rnam pa thams cad du rgyun chad de med par gyur pa de ni ’gog pa’i bden pa’i raṅ bźin no, de lta bu’i tshor ba med pa ’gog pa’i bden pa phyin ci ma log par śes te, rnam par mi rtog pa’i ye śes la yaṅ gnas la sems can la lta ba’i phyir ’gog pa’i bden pa yaṅ mṅon du mi byed pa, de ni ’gog pa la ’gog par śes pa ’phags pa’i bden pa źes bya’o.lam gyi bden pa’i raṅ bźin bstan pa’i phyir tshor ba gaṅ gis bsgrubs pa’i lam, de ni gziṅs lta bu źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs te, ’phags pa’i lam la gnas na tshor ba’i raṅ bźin goṅ du bśad pa lta bur tshor ba thams cad sdug bsṅal ba’am, tshor ba de ñid ṅo bo ñid kyis stoṅ par rtogs par byed pa’i lam de la tshor bas bsgrubs pa’i lam źes bya ste, lam de yaṅ bsgrubs par bya ba’i chos rnams grub nas dor dgos pa’i phyir gziṅs lta bu źes bya’o; yaṅ na ’phags pa’i lam la brten nas sdug bsṅal gyi raṅ bźin du gyur pa’i tshor ba de las sgrol źiṅ de dag spoṅ bar byed pas na lam ni rgya mtsho las sgrol ba’i gziṅs daṅ ’dra’o. ji ltar lam gyi raṅ bźin śes par ’gyur ba bstan pa’i phyir gaṅ tshor bar ’dod pa, de ni lam ’dod pa ma yin no źes bya ba ni gaṅ tshor ba rnam pa gsum la chags pa de ni phyin ci log la mṅon par źen pa yin pas, ’phags pa’i lam la gnas pa ma yin źes bya ba’i tha tshig go.


gaṅ de ltar bden pa bźi po ’di mthoṅ ba daṅ, rnam par dag pas mñam par rtog pa, ’di ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i bden pa la mkhas pa źes bya’o.

ya imāni catvāry āryasatyāny evaṃ paśyati, viśuddhyā samāni pratyavekṣata idam ucyate bodhisattvasya satyakauśalyam.

[To summarize:] When he sees the four holy truths in this way and sees them as the same because of purity, it is called the bodhisattva’s skill with truths.

bden pa rgya cher bstan pa’i don rnams bsdus te bstan pa’i phyir de ltar bden pa bźi po ’di mthoṅ ba daṅ źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs te, gaṅ źes bya ba ni gaṅ źag gaṅ ṅo, de ltar bden pa bźi po ’di mthoṅ źes bya ba ni goṅ du bśad pa’i tshul ltar bden pa bźi mthoṅ ba la rnam par dag pas mñam par rtogs pa źes bya ba ni ye śes rnam par dag pas źe’am, bden pa bźi po ñid raṅ bźin gyis rnam par dag pas bden pa thams cad mtshan ñid gcig ciṅ raṅ bźin gcig par rtogs pa źes bya ba’i don to.


gźan yaṅ, mdor na, skye ba ni sdug bsṅal ba ste, ’di ni sdug bsṅal źes bya’o; gaṅ mi skye ba la rtog pa’i śes pa, ’di ni sdug bsṅal la sdug bsṅal du śes pa ’phags pa’i bden pa źes bya’o.srid pa’i rkyen gyis skye ba ste, srid pa gaṅ yin pa, de kun ’byuṅ ba’o; gaṅ srid pa ’jig pa śes pa, ’di ni kun ’byuṅ ba la kun ’byuṅ bar śes pa ’phags pa’i bden pa źes bya’o.skye ba thams cad ni skye ba med pa ste, mi skye ba ni ’gog pa’o; gaṅ ma skyes pa, de la ’gog pa gaṅ yaṅ med de;gaṅ ’gog pa med par śes pa, ’di ni zad pa’i ’gog pa śes pa ’phags pa’i bden pa źes bya’o. gaṅ de ltar bgraṅ ba daṅ, ’jal ba daṅ, tshol ba daṅ, rtogs pa daṅ, ’jug pa’i śes pa, ’di ni lam la lam du śes pa ’phags pa’i bden pa źes bya’o.

punar aparaṃ saṃkṣepato jātir duḥkhā, idaṃ duḥkham iti yad ajātipratyavekṣanajñānam idaṃ duḥkhe duḥkhajñānam āryasatyam.jātir bhavapratyayena, yo bhavaḥ sa samudayaḥ, yad bhavavibhavajnānam, idaṃ samudaye samudayajñānam āryasatyam.sarvajātir ajātir, ajātir nirodham, yad ajātaṃ tatra na kiṃcin nirodham, yad anirodhajñānam idaṃ kṣayanirodhajñānam āryasatyam.yad evaṃrūpaṃ gaṇanātulanaiṣaṇāprativedhapraveśajñānam idaṃ mārge mārgajñānam āryasatyam.

Further, [to teach yet another repetition of the four truths, to teach in brief what is the essence (svabhāva) of suffering, etc.:]In short, birth is suffering, this is the suffering in question, while knowledge of seeing non-birth is the holy truth of knowledge of suffering as suffering.Because of the condition of existence, there is birth, existence is the origin; knowledge of the inexistence of existence is the holy truth of knowledge of the origin as the origin.All birth is without birth, non-birth is cessation, but in what is unborn there is no cessation; knowledge of no cessation is the holy truth of disappearance and cessation.The knowledge which consists in that kind of calculating, considering, seeking, penetrating and entering, this is the holy truth of knowledge of the way as the way.

bden pa’i rnam graṅs gźan bstan par bźed de, sdug bsṅal la sogs pa’i raṅ bźin mdor bsdus nas bstan pa’i phyir gźan yaṅ, mdor na, skye ba ni sdug bsṅal ba ste źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs so.phuṅ po lṅa mṅon par smin te, skye ba sdug bsṅal sna tshogs daṅ ldan pas na skye ba sdug bsṅal ba źes bya’o.
yaṅ na, ñiṅ mtshams sbyor bar byed pa’i las kyi bag chags bsags pa’i khyad par de daṅ de dag gis lha daṅ mi la sogs pa’i ’gro ba de daṅ de dag tu phuṅ po daṅ, khams daṅ, skye mched blaṅs par gyur pa ni skye ba źes bya’o.
yaṅ na, skye ba rnam pa lṅa ste: 1) chos rtogs pa’i skye ba daṅ; 2) mṅal du gnas pa’i skye ba daṅ; 3) rigs kyi gnas phun sum tshogs pa’i skye ba daṅ; 4) sems can gyi ris mthun pa’i ṅo bo mthun par gyur pa’i skye ba daṅ; 5) so sor byuṅ ba’i skye ba’o. 1) de la chos rtogs pa’i skye ba ni de bźin gśegs pas bśad pa’i gsuṅ rab kyi don rtogs nas sras su gyur pa ste, de bas na mdo las kyaṅ źal nas skyes pa, ’phags pa’i chos ’dul ba las skyes źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs so; 2) mṅal du gnas pa’i skye ba ni sa bon las myu gu, myu gu las ’dab ma bźin du mer mer po daṅ nur nur po la sogs pa’i rim pas skyes pa’o; 3) rigs kyi gnas phun sum tshogs pa’i skye ba ni nor bu rin po che indranīla’i rigs daṅ indranīla chen po’i rigs śes bya ba bźin du rgyal rigs su gyur pa daṅ, bram ze’i rigs su gyur pa’o; 4) sems can gyi ris mthun par ṅo bo mthun par skye ba ni dper na śiṅ rnam pa sna tshogs la ta la ta lar ris mthun pa daṅ, seṅ ldeṅ seṅ ldeṅ du ris mthun pa bźin du sems can rnams la mi daṅ mir ris mthun pa la sogs pa’o; 5) so sor byuṅ ba’i skye ba ni me tog daṅ ’bras bu ’byuṅ ba bźin du phuṅ po daṅ khams daṅ skye mched rnams byuṅ bar gyur pa ste; de ltar skye ba rnam pa lṅa las kyaṅ ’dir 1) mṅal du gnas pa’i skye ba daṅ 5) so sor ’byuṅ ba’i skye ba la bya bar dgoṅs so. skye ba de dag rnam pa gñis kyi phyir sdug bsṅal ba ste, gnod pa’i raṅ bźin gyis sdug bsṅal ba daṅ, sdug bsṅal gźan gyi rten du gyur pa’i phyir ro. de la gnod pa’i raṅ bźin gyis sdug bsṅal ba ni mi’i mṅal na źu ba’i gnas daṅ ma źu ba’i gnas kyi bar na gnas pa daṅ, mṅal nas phyir byuṅ ba’i tshe mi gtsaṅ ba’i rdzas rnam pa sna tshogs kyis btsir ba na ri’i thim par bcug pa bźin du yan lag la dpag tu med pa’i sdug bsṅal ’byuṅ bas na skye ba sdug bsṅal ba’o. sdug bsṅal gźan gyi rten du gyur pa ni skye bar gyur na rga ba la sogs pa’i sdug bsṅal rnams źar la ’byuṅ bas na skye ba sdug bsṅal ba źes bya ste, ’di ni sdug bsṅal gyi bden pa’i raṅ bźin no. ji ltar na sdug bsṅal gyi bden pa śes par ’gyur ba bstan pa’i phyir gaṅ mi skye ba la rtog pa’i śes pa ’di ni źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs te, skye ba de ni don dam par skye ba med ciṅ mi dmigs par rtogs pa de ni sdug bsṅal la sdug bsṅal du śes pa bden pa źes bya’o źes bya ba’i tha tshig go.kun ’byuṅ ba’i bden pa’i raṅ bźin bstan pa’i phyir srid pa’i rkyen gyis skye ba ste, srid pa gaṅ yin pa kun ’byuṅ ba’o źes bya ba gsuṅs te, ñiṅ mtshams sbyor ba’i rgyur gyur pa las rnam pa sna tshogs kyi bag chags bsags pa ni srid pa źes bya’o, rten ciṅ ’brel bar ’byuṅ ba’i yan lag bcu gñis las srid pa’i rkyen gyis skye ba źes ’byuṅ ste, srid pa de las skye ba kun tu ’byuṅ ba’i phyir srid pa la kun tu ’byuṅ ba źes bya’o; ji ltar kun ’byuṅ ba śes pa bstan pa’i phyir gaṅ srid pa ’jig pa śes pa źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs te, srid pa ’jig pa śes pa źes bya ba ni srid pa’i raṅ bźin med par śes pa źes bya ba’i don to.’gog pa’i bden pa’i raṅ bźin bstan pa’i phyir skye ba thams cad ni skye ba med pa ste, mi skye ba ni ’gog pa’o źes gsuṅs te, skye ba rnam pa lṅa bśad pa la sogs pa phyi daṅ naṅ gi dṅos po skye ba thams cad ni don dam par na skye ba med pa ste, gaṅ skye ba med pa mi skye ba de ni ’gog pa’i bden pa’o. ji ltar na ’gog pa’i bden pa śes pa bstan pa’i phyir gaṅ mi skye ba de la ’gog pa gaṅ yaṅ med de źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs te, ’gog pa ni skye ba la brten pa ste, skyes par gyur na ’jig par ’gyur ba’i phyir ro, ’di ltar ma skyes na ’jig pa med pas na ma skyes pa de la ’gog pa gaṅ yaṅ med pa źes bya’o, gaṅ ’gog pa med par śes pa, ’di ni zad pa’i ’gog pa śes pa źes bya la, skye ba thams cad skye ba med ciṅ mi skye ba’i mtshan ñid kyi ’gog pa gaṅ yin pa de ñid kyaṅ raṅ bźin gyis med par śes pa ni mi skye ba’i mtshan ñid mi ’gog pa źes bya’o.lam gyi bden pa’i raṅ bźin daṅ ji ltar lam gyi bden pa śes pa bstan pa’i phyir gaṅ de ltar bgraṅ ba’am, ’jal ba źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs te, goṅ du bśad pa ltar sdug bsṅal ci ’dra ba daṅ, kun ’byuṅ ba daṅ ’gog pa ci ’dra ba ṅes par rtog ciṅ gtan la ’bebs la lam gyi bden pa źes bya ste, de dag phyin ci ma log par śes pa ni lam gyi bden pa śes pa’o. bgraṅ ba daṅ ’jal ba źes bya ba ni gtan la ’bebs śiṅ śes par byed ces bya ba’i tha tshig go. yaṅ na, gaṅ gis ’phags pa’i bden pa bźi ston pa’i mdo sde la sogs pa’i miṅ daṅ tshig daṅ yi ge rnams kyi graṅs ji sñed ’byuṅ ba la rtog pa ni bgraṅ ba śes pa źes bya’o; gaṅ gis gñis bzuṅ nas gñis kun tu rtog pa ste, miṅ kun tu bzuṅ nas don kun rtogs pa daṅ, don kun tu bzuṅ nas miṅ kun rtogs pa ni ’jal ba śes pa’o; gaṅ gis ’phags pa’i bden pa’i miṅ kun ’dzin pa sṅon du byas nas don rtogs pa ’jug pa ni tshol ba śes pa źes bya’o;
ṭ. fol.133a4-b7 enumerates eleven kinds of spiritual penetration to paraphrase prativedha: rab tu rtogs pa’i sbyor ba bcu gcig ni rtogs pa śes pa ste, bcu gcig po śes pa gaṅ źe na? 1) glo bur du byuṅ ba rab tu rtogs pa daṅ, 2) yaṅ dag par snaṅ ba’i rgyu mtshan rab tu rtogs pa daṅ, 3) don mi dmigs pa rab tu rtogs pa daṅ, 4) dmigs pa mi dmigs pa rab tu rtogs pa daṅ, 5) chos kyi dbyiṅs rab tu rtogs pa daṅ, 6) gaṅ zag la bdag med pa rab tu rtogs pa daṅ, 7) chos la bdag med pa rab tu rtogs pa daṅ, 8) bsam pa chuṅ ṅu rab tu rtogs pa daṅ, 9) rgya chen po’i bdag ñid chen po’i bsam pa rab tu rtogs pa daṅ, 10) ji ltar chos khoṅ du chud pa’i chos rnam par gźag pa rab tu rtogs pa daṅ, 11) rnam par gźag pa’i chos rab tu rtogs pa’o.
1) ’phags pa’i bden pa bźi miṅ daṅ don du btags pa de dag thams cad ni yaṅ dag pa ma yin pa la glo bur du btags pa yin no źes khoṅ du chud pa ni glo bur du byuṅ ba rab tu rtogs pa źes bya’o; de ni drod kyi dus na’o. 2) dṅos po thams cad yod pa ma yin pa la gzuṅ ba daṅ ’dzin pa lta bur snaṅ ba ni yaṅ dag par snaṅ ba’o, snaṅ ba de dag gi rgyu yaṅ sems daṅ sems las byuṅ ba yin pas na sems daṅ sems las byuṅ ba ni snaṅ ba’i rgyu mtshan no, gzuṅ ba daṅ ’dzin pa de dag snaṅ ba ni sems daṅ sems las byuṅ ba la snaṅ ste źes rtogs pa ni yaṅ dag par snaṅ ba’i rgyu mtshan rab tu rtogs pa ste; ’di ni spyi bo’i tshe na’o. 3) don ni gzugs la sogs pa phyi’i yul rnams te, de dag med par rtogs pa ni don med dmigs par rtogs pa ste; ’di ni bzod pa’i dus so. 4) de ltar gzuṅ ba med na ’dzin pa yaṅ mi ’jug pas phyi’i yul la ’dzin pa’i sems med par rtogs pa ni dmigs pa mi dmigs pa rab tu rtogs pa źes bya ste; de ni ’jig rten pa’i chos kyi mchog gi dus na’o. 5) de ltar gzuṅ ba daṅ ’dzin pa gñis mi dmigs par gyur nas thams cad du ’gro ba’i don gyi de bźin ñid rtogs pa ni chos kyi dbyiṅs rab tu rtogs pa ste; ’di ni mthoṅ ba’i lam gyi tshe’o. 6) de ltar mthoṅ ba’i lam gyi tshe ’phags pa ñan thos rnams kyis ni mthoṅ bas spaṅ bar bya ba’i ñon moṅs pa’i sgrib pa spaṅs nas gaṅ zag la bdag med par rab tu rtogs so. 7) byaṅ chub sems dpa’ rnams kyis ni mthoṅ bas spaṅ bar bya ba’i ñon moṅs pa daṅ śes bya’i sgrib pa che loṅ spaṅs nas gaṅ zag daṅ chos la bdag med pa gñis rtogs so. 8) de lta bas na ’phags pa ñan thos rnams kyis ni gaṅ zag la bdag med tsam rtogs pa daṅ, bdag gi don gyi phyir źugs pas na bsam pa chuṅ ṅu rab tu rtogs pa źes bya’o. 9) byaṅ chub sems dpa’ rnams kyis ni gaṅ zag daṅ chos la bdag med pa rtogs la bdag daṅ gźan gyi don gyi phyir źugs pas na de dag gi rtogs pa ni rgya chen po’i bdag ñid kyi bsam pa rab tu rtogs pa źes bya’o. 10) sa daṅ po’i tshe chos rnams kyi de bźin ñid khoṅ du chud pa ni ji ltar chos khoṅ du chud pa’o. de ltar khoṅ du chud nas khoṅ du chud pa’i chos kyi yon tan rnams rtogs pa ni ji ltar khoṅ du chud pa’i chos rnam par gźag pa rab tu rtogs pa źes bya’o. 11) de nas bsgom pa’i chos rnams sems la yaṅ dag par ’jog ciṅ, bsgom pa’i lam gyi dus na bsgom pa’i chos daṅ yon tan rnams rtogs pa ni rnam par gźag pa’i chos rab tu rtogs pa źes bya’o.
The same enumeration is found in Msa. p. 588-13: prativedhaprāyogikaś ca / sa punar ekādaśavidho veditavya 1) āgantukatvaprativedhataḥ, 2) saṃkhyānanimittaprativedhato, 3) ’rthānupalambhaprativedhata, 4) upalambhānupalambhaprativedhato, 5) dharmadhātuprativedhataḥ, 6) pudgalanairātmyaprativedhato, 7) dharmanairātmyaprativedhato, 8) hīnāśayaprativedhata, 9) udāramahātmyāśayaprativedhato, 10) yathādhigamadharmavyavasthānaprativedhato, 11) vyavasthāpitadharmaprativedhataś ca /
The explanations are an abbreviated form of the commentary in Sūtrālaṃkāravṛttibhāṣya mi fol. 172a5-173a5 on Msa.
ṭ. 133b7-134a2: gaṅ gis rnam pa gñis la ñe bar ’jug ste, yi ge rnams tshad yod pa la ’jug pa daṅ, miṅ daṅ tshig gi tshad med pa la ’jug ste, de ltar ’jug pa ni ’jug pa śes pa’o. ’di ltar bgraṅ ba daṅ, ’jal ba daṅ, tshol ba daṅ, rtogs pa daṅ, ’jug pa rnam pa lṅa ni ’phags pa lam ste, de ltar śes na lam la lam du śes pa ’phags pa’i bden pa źes bya’o.


gaṅ bden pa’i śes pa ’di la ’jug ciṅ, bden pa’i śes pa la yaṅ mi gnas pa, ’di ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i bden pa la mkhas pa źes bya’o.

ya idaṃ satyajñānaṃ praviśann api satyajñāne na tiṣṭhatīdam ucyate bodhisattvasya satyakauśalyam.

[To summarize:] When he enters this knowledge of truths, but does not remain in the knowledge of truths, it is called the bodhisattva’s skill with truths.

ji ltar bśad pa’i don rnams bsdus te bstan pa’i phyir gaṅ bden pa’i śes pa ’di la ’jug ciṅ źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs te, bden pa’i śes pa la ’jug pa ni bden pa bźi po goṅ du bśad pa rnams stoṅ par rtogs pa’o; bden pa’i śes pa la yaṅ mi gnas źes bya ba ni sems can gyi don du lta bas ji ltar stoṅ par rtogs pa de ’ba’ źig gi phyogs la yaṅ gnas par mi byed ces bya ba’i don to.


de la byaṅ chub sems dpa’i rten ciṅ ’brel bar ’byuṅ ba la mkhas pa gaṅ źe na?

tatra katamad bodhisattvasya pratītyasamutpādakauśalyam?

(p. 75) 5) What then is the bodhisattva’s skill with dependent origination?

bden pa la mkhas pa bśad pa’i ’og tu rten ciṅ ’brel bar ’byuṅ ba la mkhas pa bstan pas ji ltar bstan pa bźin du bśad par bźed nas de la byaṅ chub sems dpa’i rten ciṅ ’brel bar ’byuṅ ba la mkhas pa gaṅ źe na źes dris so. de la źes bya ba’i don ni goṅ du smos pa daṅ ’dra’o.
rgyu daṅ rkyen la brten nas dus mñam du ’bras bu ’byuṅ ba ni rten ciṅ ’brel bar ’byuṅ ba ste, de la mkhas pa ni rten ciṅ ’brel bar ’byuṅ ba la mkhas pa’o – "Origination of the fruit in the same moment depending on causes and conditions is dependent origination (hetupratyayān āśritya samānakālaphalotpādaḥ pratītyasamutpādaḥ), skill with this is skill with dependent origination (tatra kauśalyaṃ pratītyasamutpādakauśalyam)."
On samānakāla cf. Kośa p. 9616 and 1451ff.
de ni de skad du rten ciṅ ’brel bar ’byuṅ ba’i mtshan ñid phyin ci ma log par rtogs pa ni rten ciṅ ’brel bar ’byuṅ ba la mkhas pa yin par ston to. de bas na rten źes bya ba daṅ, ’brel źes bya ba daṅ, ’byuṅ źes bya ba’i tshig gsum gyis rnam pa gsum ’gog par byed de; rnam pa gsum ni 1) rgyu med par smra ba daṅ, 2) rgyu mi ’dra bar smra ba daṅ, 3) med par smra ba’o. de la 1) rten ces bya ba ni rgyu daṅ rkyen la brten te ’byuṅ ba yin pas na, ’dis ni rgyu med par smra ba ’gog par byed do. 2) ’brel ces bya ba’i sgra ni mthun pa la bya ste, rgyu daṅ ’bras bu mthun pa las skye’i, mi mthun pa las ma yin te, dper na ma rig pa las ’du byed ’byuṅ gi, dbaṅ phyug daṅ byed pa po las mi ’byuṅ ba; ’dis ni mi mthun pa’i rgyur smra ba ’gog par byed do. 3) ’byuṅ ba’i sgra ni rgyu daṅ ’bras bu bar chad med par skye ba la bya ste, ’dis ni med par smra ba ’gog par byed do.
Cf. Abhidharmasamuccaya p. 2615-16: ahetuviṣamahetukātmābhiniveśatyājanārtham, p. 1008-9: balaiḥ kiṃ karma karoti / ahetuviṣamahetuvādaṃ pratyākhyāyākṛtābhyāgamavāde
ca samyagabhyudayamārgaṃ deśayati ..., and Pras p. 1011: ahetvekahetuviṣamahetusaṃbhūtatvaṃ.
ci’i phyir rten ciṅ ’brel te ’byuṅ ba bśad ce na? ’gro ba ’di dag ma rig pa’i rkyen las skye’o. mi mthun pa’i rgyu daṅ rgyu med pa las mi skye’o, źes bstan pa’i phyir bśad do – "Why is origination in dependence taught? It is taught because these states of existence (gati) originate from the condition of ignorance (avidyāpratyaya), not from some inappropriate cause (viṣamahetu) or without cause (ahetuka)".


’di lta ste: tshul bźin ma yin pa kun ’byuṅ ba las ma rig pa kun ’byuṅ ṅo;ma rig pa kun ’byuṅ ba las ’du byed kun ’byuṅ ṅo;’du byed kun ’byuṅ ba las rnam par śes pa kun ’byuṅ ṅo;rnam par śes pa kun ’byuṅ ba las miṅ daṅ gzugs kun ’byuṅ ṅo;miṅ daṅ gzugs kun ’byuṅ ba las skye mched drug kun ’byuṅ ṅo;skye mched drug kun ’byuṅ ba las reg pa kun ’byuṅ ṅo;reg pa kun ’byuṅ ba las tshor ba kun ’byuṅ ṅo;tshor ba kun ’byuṅ ba las sred pa kun ’byuṅ ṅo;sred pa kun ’byuṅ ba las len pa kun ’byuṅ ṅo;len pa kun ’byuṅ ba las srid pa kun ’byuṅ ṅo;srid pa kun ’byuṅ ba las skye ba kun ’byuṅ ṅo;skye ba kun ’byuṅ ba las rga śi daṅ, mya ṅan daṅ, smre sṅags ’don pa daṅ, sdug bsṅal ba daṅ, yid mi bde ba daṅ, ’khrug pa rnams ’byuṅ ste,de ltar na sdug bsṅal gyi phuṅ po chen po ’ba’ źig po ’di ’byuṅ bar ’gyur ro.

yad idam ayoniśaḥsamudayād avidyā samudeti,avidyāsamudayāt saṃskārāḥ samudyanti,saṃskārasamudayād vijñānaṃ samudeti,vijñānasamudayān nāmarūpaṃ samudeti,nāmarūpasamudayāt ṣaḍāyatanaṃ samudeti,ṣaḍāyatanasamudayāt sparśaḥ samudeti,sparśasamudayād vedanā samudeti,vedanāsamudayāt tṛṣṇā samudeti,tṛṣṇāsamudayād upādānaṃ samudeti,upādānasamudayād bhavaḥ samudeti,bhavasamudayāj jātiḥ samudeti,jātisamudayāj jarāmaraṇaśokaparidevaduḥkhadaurmanasyopāyāsāḥ samudyanti,evam asya kevalasya mahato duḥkhaskandhasya samudayo bhavati.

[Dependent origination in the regular way (anuloma), to teach the bewilderment (moha) in entering existence; (saṃsāra);it should be known through the character of its division into members (aṅgavibhāgalakṣaṇatas):]From the origin of being superficial [having concepts of permanence with regard to the impermanent (anitye nityasaṃjñā), pleasure with regard to suffering (duḥkhe sukhasaṃjñā), purity with regard to the impure (aśubhe śubhasaṃjñā), self with regard to the selfless (anātmīye ātmasaṃjñā) ] ignorance originates,from the origin of ignorance formative factors originate,from the origin of formative factors consciousness originates,from the origin of consciousness name and form originate,from the origin of name and form the six senses originate,from the origin of the six senses touch originates,from the origin of touch feeling originates,from the origin of feeling thirst originates,from the origin of thirst grasping originates,from the origin of grasping existence originates,from the origin of existence birth originates,from the origin of birth ageing, death, sorrow, lamentation, suffering, depression and despair originate.thus this great mass of utter suffering originates.

yaṅ na, 1) ’khor bar ’jug pa la rmoṅs pa daṅ, 2) ’khor ba las ldog pa la rmoṅs pa bsal ba’i phyir rten ciṅ ’brel bar ’byuṅ ba lugs daṅ mthun par ’byuṅ ba daṅ, lugs las bzlog pa’i mtshan ñid rnam pa gñis bśad do. de la 1) ’khor bar ’jug pa la rmoṅs pa ni rgyu gaṅ gis ’khor bar skye bar ’gyur ba’i rgyu mi śes pa ste, mi śes pa de bsal ba’i phyir tshul bźin ma yin pa kun ’byuṅ ba las ma rig pa kun ’byuṅ ṅo źes bya ba gsuṅs so. 2) ’khor ba las ldog pa ni mya ṅan las ’das pa ste, rgyu gaṅ gis ’khor ba las ’grol źiṅ mya ṅan las ’da’ bar ’gyur ba mi śes pa de bsal ba’i phyir tshul bźin ma yin pa ’gags pas ma rig pa ’gag ces bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs so.
In accordance with Abhidharmasamuccaya p. 283-5: katham anulomapratilomataḥ / saṃkleśānulomapratilomato ’pi vyavadānānulomapratilomato ’pi pratītyasamutpādasyānulomapratilomanirdeśo draṣṭavyaḥ // Cf. next note.de la rten ciṅ ’brel bar ’byuṅ ba lugs daṅ mthun par ’byuṅ ba yaṅ mtshan ñid rnam pa bźir rig par bya ste: 1) yan lag rnam par dbye ba’i mtshan ñid daṅ, 2) yan lag bsdu ba’i mtshan ñid daṅ, 3) yan lag gi kun nas ñon moṅs pa bsdu ba’i mtshan ñid daṅ, 4) bdag med pa rkyen las ’byuṅ ba’i mtshan ñid do.
yan lag rnam par dbye ba’i mtshan ñid (1) las brtsams te gsuṅs pa ’di lta ste, tshul bźin ma yin pa kun ’byuṅ ba las ma rig pa kun ’byuṅ ṅo źes bya ba la sogs pa’o.
The divisions 1, 2 and 3 are based on divisions 2, 3 and 6 in the treatment of pratītyasamutpāda in Abhidharmasamuccaya, p. 2612-16: 1) lakṣaṇato ’py 2) aṅgavibhāgato ’py 3) aṅgasamāsato ’py 4) aṅgapratyayatvavyavasthānato ’py 5) aṅgakarmavyavasthānato ’py 6) aṅgasaṃkleśasaṃgrahato ’pi 7) arthato ’pi 8) gambhīryato ’pi 9) prabhedato ’py 10) anulomapratilomato ’pi pratītyasamutpannaṃ draṣṭavyam / No. 4 is not in Abhidharmasamuccaya.
Abhidharmasamuccaya p. 2617-18: katham aṅgavibhāgataḥ / dvādaśāṅgāni / dvādaśāṅgaḥ pratītyasamutpādaḥ avidyā saṃskārā vijñānaṃ nāmarūpaṃ ṣaḍāyatanaṃ sparśo vedanā tṛṣṇopādānaṃ bhavo jātir jarāmaraṇaṃ ca //
The paragraphs corresponding to the divisions 2 and 3 of ṭ do not apply to the mūla, but only to the commentary in ṭ itself. Paragraph 4, however, is again concerned with the mūla. Cf. infra.
’di lta ste źes bya ba ni tshig gi mgo draṅ ba’am, tshig gi rkyen du bźag pa’o.de la mi rtag pa la rtag par ’du śes pa daṅ, sdug bsṅal ba la bde bar ’du śes pa daṅ, mi gtsaṅ ba la gtsaṅ bar ’du śes pa daṅ, bdag med pa la bdag tu ’du śes pa ni tshul bźin ma yin pa ste, kun ’byuṅ ba las śes bya ba ni tshul bźin ma yin pa kun tu skyes par ’gyur ba las ma rig pa kun ’byuṅ bar ’gyur te, ma rig pa kun du skye bar ’gyur ro, źes bya ba’i don to. ’dir tshul bźin ma yin pa smos pa ni ma rig pa’i rgyu bstan pa’i phyir smos pa yin te, ’byuṅ ba’i don ni lhag ma rnams la yaṅ de bźin du sbyar bar bya’o. de la 1) gcig pur ’du śes pa daṅ, 2) ril por ’du śes pa daṅ, 3) rtag par ’du śes pa daṅ, 4) brtan par ’du śes pa daṅ, 5) ther zug tu ’du śes pa daṅ, 6) bde bar ’du śes pa ni ma rig pa źes bya’o. 1) sa daṅ chu daṅ me daṅ rluṅ daṅ nam mkha’ la sogs pa tha dad pa mi ’dra ba du ma ’dus pas bskyed na ’di la gcig pur sems pa ni gcig pur ’du śes pa’o. 2) sa la sogs pa de dag kyaṅ rdul phra rab tha dad pa las ’byuṅ ba yin na, de la gcig pur sems pa ni ril por ’du śes pa’o. 3) skad cig ma re re la yaṅ mi rtag par gyur nas gźan daṅ gźan du gyur na, gnas nas kyaṅ bdag ces ’dzin, phyis kyaṅ bdag ñid ’dug go sñam du sems pa ni rtag par ’du śes pa’o. 4) med pa las ’byuṅ ba la gaṅ yod pa las skye bar ’dzin pa ni brtan par ’du śes pa’o. yaṅ na ’di dag thams cad dṅos po med pa sgyu ma lta bu yin na, bdag ñid can du dṅos por sems pa ni brtan par ’du śes pa’o. 5) byuṅ nas med par ’gyur ba la yaṅ rdza ma’i byi ru ltar bdag ma ’oṅs pa’i dus su ’pho bar ’dzin pa ni ther zug tu ’du śes pa’o. 6) ’jig rten gsum daṅ ’dus byas thams cad ni sdug bsṅal gsum gyi mes gduṅs pas sdug bsṅal daṅ ldan pa yin na, gaṅ gcig pu bzaṅ po’i ṅo bor ’dzin pa de ni bde bar ’du śes pa’o.
Cf. Śālistamba p. 912-15: tatrāvidyā katamā / yaiṣām eva ṣaṇṇāṃ dhātūnām ekasaṃjñā piṇḍasaṃjñā nityasaṃjñā dhruvasaṃjñā śāśvatasaṃjñā sukhasaṃjñā ātmasaṃjñā sattvajīvajantupoṣapuruṣapudgalasaṃjñā manujamānavasaṃjñā ahaṃkāramamakārasaṃjñā / evamādi vividham ajñānam iyam ucyate ’vidyeti /de ltar kun tu gti mug pa’i rgyus lus daṅ ṅag daṅ yid kyi las rnam pa sna tshogs byed pa ni ’du byed do. yaṅ na, ’du byed rnam pa gsum ste, 1) bsod nams ma yin par ñe bar ’gro ba’i ’du byed daṅ, 2) bsod nams su ñe bar ’gro ba’i ’du byed daṅ, 3) mi g-yo bar ñe bar ’gro ba’i ’du byed do. 1) de la sdig pa’i las byed pa la mṅon par chags pa tshe rabs gźan daṅ las kyi ’bras bu la kun tu gti mug pas med par lta ba rnams ni bsod nams ma yin pa’i las mṅon par ’du byed do. 2) ma rig pas rmoṅs par gyur pa srid pa daṅ srid pa’i loṅs spyod la yon tan du lta źiṅ bde bar ’du śes pa rnams ni bsod nams kyi las mṅon par ’du byed do. 3) ma rig pa’i rkyen gyis sñoms par ’jug pa’i ro la chags par lta bas sred pa daṅ lta ba daṅ ṅa rgyal gyi śas che ba’i bsam gtan rnams ni mi g-yo ba’i las mṅon par ’du byed de, de bas na ma rig pa kun ’byuṅ ba las ’du byed kun ’byuṅ ba źes bya’o.
Cf. Abhidharmasamuccaya p. 2626-272: avidyā kiṃkarmakā / bhave sattvān saṃmohayati pratyayaś ca bhavati saṃskārāṇām // saṃskārāḥ kiṃkarmakāḥ / gatiṣu ca sattvān vibhajanti pratyayāś ca bhavanti vijñānavāsanāyāḥ // Bhāṣya p. 3211-17: avidyā bhave sattvān saṃmohayati, tad āvṛtteḥ pūrvāntāparāntamadhyāntānāṃ yathābhūtāparijñānāt / yata evaṃ vicikitsati – kiṃ nv aham abhūvam atīte ’dhvany āho svin nāham abhūvam ity evamādi / pratyayaś ca bhavati saṃskārāṇām, tadvaśena punarbhavikakarmopacayāt / saṃskārā gatiṣu ca sattvān vibhajanti, karmavaśena sattvānāṃ gatyantaragamanavaicitryāt / pratyayāś ca bhavanti vijñānasya vāsanāyāḥ, āyatyā nāmarūpābhinirvṛttaye bījapoṣaṇāt /
Cf. Śālistamba p. 119ff: evam avidyāyāṃ satyāṃ trividhāḥ saṃskārā abhinirvartante / puṇyopagā apuṇyopagā aneñjyopagāḥ / ...de la ma’i mṅal du daṅ po ñid du skad cig ma gcig la źugs pa’i sems, phuṅ po daṅ khams daṅ skye mched kyi bag chags kyis yoṅs su bsgos pa sṅon gyi las kyis ’phaṅs pa’i sa bon thams cad pa’i kun gźi rnam par śes pa ni ’dir ’du byed kyi rkyen las byuṅ ba’i rnam par śes pa yin par dgoṅs so. (Translated in the introduction.)
Abhidharmasamuccaya p. 121-2: cittaṃ katamat / skandhadhātvāyatanavāsanāparibhāvitaṃ sarvabījakaṃ ālayavijñānaṃ; (cf. Bhāṣya p. 119-14); cf. also p. 272-3 and Bhāṣya p. 3217-19: vijñānaṃ karmabandhaṃ dhārayati, saṃskārāhitavāsanāsahotpatteḥ / pratyayaś ca bhavati nāmarūpasya, mātuḥ kukṣau vijñānāvakrāntyā nāmarūpavivṛddhigamanāt /de nas skad cig ma gñis phan chad mer mer po daṅ nur nur po la sogs pa daṅ bcas pa’i rnam par śes pa ni miṅ daṅ gzugs so. de la miṅ ni tshor ba daṅ, ’du śes daṅ, ’du byed daṅ, rnam par śes pa’i phuṅ po’o. gzugs ni bstan du yod la thogs pa daṅ bcas pa daṅ, bstan du med pa la thogs pa daṅ bcas pa daṅ, bstan du yaṅ med la thogs pa yaṅ med pa ste, de gñis gcig tu bsdoms nas miṅ daṅ gzugs źes bya’o.mig gi skye mched nas yid kyi bar du drug ni skye mched drug go. de la mig gi skye mched ni lta ba’i bdag ñid can daṅ ba’i raṅ bźin gzugs la dmigs par byed pa ste; lhag ma la yaṅ de bźin du sbyar ro.yul daṅ dbaṅ po daṅ rnam par śes pa rnams rgyu daṅ ’bras bu’i mtshan ñid du dus mñam pa ñid du tshogs pa ni reg pa’o. de la dbaṅ po daṅ yul ni rgyu’i mtshan ñid do, de gñis la brten nas de ma thag tu rnam par śes pa skye bas na rnam par śes pa ni ’bras bu’i mtshan ñid do.bde ba daṅ, sdug bsṅal ba daṅ, bde ba yaṅ ma yin sdug bsṅal ba yaṅ ma yin pa’i myoṅ ba ni tshor ba źes bya’o. de la lus daṅ dbaṅ po daṅ rnam par śes pa la phan par byed pa’i bdag ñid ni bde ba’i tshor ba’o; lus daṅ dbaṅ po daṅ rnam par śes pa la gnod par byed pa’i bdag ñid ni sdug bsṅal gyi tshor ba’o; lus daṅ dbaṅ po daṅ rnam par śes pa la phan gnod gñi ga mi byed pa ni bde ba yaṅ ma yin sdug bsṅal ba yaṅ ma yin pa’i tshor ba’o.sred pa daṅ sred pa’i loṅs spyod la rgyun du spyod kyaṅ tshva chu ’thuṅs pa daṅ ’dra bar ṅoms pa daṅ tshim pa med pa ni sred pa źes bya’o. de’aṅ dus gsum tha dad pa’i dbye bas sred pa rnam pa gsum du ’gyur te: 1) lta ba’i sred pa daṅ, 2) mṅon par dga’ ba’i sred pa daṅ, 3) mṅon par chags pa’i sred pa’o. de la 1) ’das pa’i dus su mthoṅ ba’i sred pa daṅ, thos pa daṅ rig pa’i dṅos po ’gags par gyur pa rnams daṅ yaṅ phrad par ’dod pa ni lta ba’i sred pa źes bya’o. 2) ma ’oṅs pa’i dus na raṅ gi lus rnam pa sna tshogs daṅ yo byad rnam pa maṅ po daṅ ldan par smon pa ni mṅon par dga’ ba’i sred pa’o. 3) da ltar gyi dus kyi phuṅ po daṅ yo byad la chags pas mi gtoṅ ba ni mṅon par chags pa’i sred pa źes bya’o. yaṅ na, 1) ’dod pa’i sred pa daṅ, 2) srid pa’i sred pa daṅ, 3) mi srid pa’i sred pa daṅ, 4) lta ba’i sred pa ste, bźi’o. de la 1) ’dod pa’i sred pa ni mthoṅ ba daṅ bsgom pas spaṅ bar bya ba ’dod pa’i khams kyi ’dod chags so. 2) srid pa’i sred pa ni mthoṅ ba daṅ bsgom pas spaṅ bar bya ba’i gzugs daṅ gzugs med pa’i khams kyi ’dod chags so. 3) mi srid pa’i sred pa ni thar pa la mṅon par chags pa’o. 4) lta ba’i sred pa ni ’jig tshogs la sogs pa lta ba lṅa la chags pa’o.de la len pa yaṅ rnam pa bźi ste, 1) ’dod pa len pa daṅ, 2) tshul khrims daṅ brtul źugs len pa daṅ, 3) lta ba len pa daṅ, 4) bdag tu smra ba len pa’o. de la 1) ’dod chags rnam pa gsum ni ’dod pa len pa źes bya ste, a) ’dod pa’i ’dod chags daṅ, b) chos kyi ’dod chags daṅ, c) yul gyi ’dod chags so. a) ’dod pa’i ’dod chags ni skyes pa daṅ bud med gñis kyis gñis sprod pa las chags pa’o. b) mu stegs can gyi chos la chags pa ni chos kyi ’dod chags so. c) ’dod pa lṅa’i yon tan la chags pa ni yul gyi ’dod chags so. 2) khyi daṅ ba laṅ la sogs pa’i dka’ thub ’dzin pa ni tshul khrims daṅ brtul źugs len pa źes bya’o. 3) chad pa daṅ rtag pa la sogs pa lta ba sna tshogs la źugs pa ni lta ba len pa’o) 4. bdag yod par lta źiṅ chags pa ni bdag tu smra ba len pa źes bya’o.ñiṅ mtshams sbyor ba’i rgyur gyur pa’i las rnam pa sna tshogs kyi bag chags bsags pa ni srid pa źes bya ste, de yaṅ ’dod pa’i srid pa daṅ, gzugs kyi srid pa daṅ, gzugs med pa’i srid pa ste, rnam pa gsum mo.las kyi bag chags rnam pa sna tshogs pa bsags pa’i khyad par la ñiṅ mtshams sbyor ba de daṅ de dag phuṅ po daṅ khams daṅ skye mched la sogs pa mṅon par grub pa ni skye ba źes bya’o.mer mer po daṅ, nur nur po daṅ, mkhraṅ gyur pa daṅ, rkaṅ lag ’gyus pa nas gźon nu daṅ, laṅ tsho dar la bab pa’i bar gyi stobs daṅ, mthu daṅ, gzi brjid daṅ, mdaṅs la sogs pa gźan du ’gyur te, ñams ni rga ba’o. yaṅ na, laṅ tsho bcom pa daṅ, na tshod ñams pa daṅ, ’byuṅ ba chen po rnams bri ba daṅ, ’du byed rnams rñiṅs par gyur pa daṅ, lus lhod par gyur pa daṅ, yan lag rnams śig śig por gyur pa daṅ, kha dog daṅ dbyibs mi mdzes pa daṅ, dbaṅ po rnams ñam chuṅ ba daṅ, dran pa daṅ rtogs pa daṅ blo gros rnams rab tu ñams pa daṅ, ’jig pa la mṅon du bltas pa ni rga ba’o. de la laṅ tsho bcom pa ni dar la bab pa med par gyur pa’o. na tshod ñams pa ni byis pa daṅ gźon nu’i spyod pa daṅ tshul rnams bral ba’o. ’byuṅ ba chen po rnams bri ba ni sa la sogs pa ’byuṅ ba rnams źum par gyur pa ste, śa sla ba daṅ gñer ma can du gyur pa’o. ’du byed rnams rñiṅs par gyur pa ni dar la babs la laṅ tsho’i byad gzugs sar pa daṅ bral bar gyur pa’o. lus lhod par gyur pa ni ldaṅ ba daṅ ’dug pa la lus lci ba’o. yan lag śig śig por gyur pa ni rkaṅ pa daṅ lag pa la sogs pa rnams tshigs tshigs su so sor gyes śiṅ ñams daṅ mthu med par gyur pa’o. kha dog daṅ dbyibs mi sdug pa ni śa daṅ khrag skams la rus pa phyir snaṅ ba daṅ, khabs nag pos khebs pa daṅ, gñer ma daṅ skra dkar gyis gaṅ ba’o. dbaṅ po rnams ñam chuṅ ba ni mig la sogs pa’i dbaṅ po rnams mthoṅ ba daṅ thos pa mi gsal ba’o. dran pa daṅ rtogs pa daṅ blo gros rab tu ñams pa ni sṅon smras pa daṅ thos pa rnams mi dran źiṅ brjed pa’o. ’jig pa la mṅon du bltas pa ni ’chi ba’i dus daṅ khad ñe ba’o. yaṅ na rga ba rnam pa gñis te: rten ñams pa daṅ, brten pa ñams pa’o. de la rten ñams pa ni ’di ltar ’byuṅ ba chen po las gyur pa, khrag daṅ śa daṅ tshil daṅ rkaṅ daṅ rus pa la sogs pa bri bas de’i rgyus na rgyug pa daṅ rgal ba daṅ mchoṅ ba daṅ bskum pa daṅ rmyoṅ ba daṅ ’oṅ ba daṅ ’gro ba la sogs pa’i bya ba ni mi nus śiṅ, lus kyi brtson ’grus daṅ stobs mthu chuṅ ba’o. de la brten pa ñams pa ni mig la sogs pa’i dbaṅ po rnams lta ba daṅ ñan pa la sogs pa la mi gsal bar ’jug ciṅ, de’i rgyus na dran pa daṅ rtogs pa daṅ blo gros la sogs pa ñams śiṅ sems kyi stobs daṅ brtson ’grus bri ba’o. dbaṅ po rnams ñams pa las de’i rgyu ba sems daṅ sems las byuṅ ba rnams mi mthun pa ni ’chi ba ste, sems daṅ sems las byuṅ ba rgyus med par gyur pa na gaṅ zag de śi ba źes bya’o. de la ’chi ba yaṅ rnam pa gñis te, raṅ gi ṅaṅ gis ’chi ba daṅ, ñe bar bcom pas ’chi ba’o. raṅ gi ṅaṅ gis ’chi ba ni tshe zad pa daṅ bsod nams zad nas ’chi ba’o. ñe bar bcom pa ni mtshon cha daṅ dbyig pa la sogs pa’i rkyen gyis śi ba’o. yaṅ na ’chi ba rnam pa gsum ste, rjes su skad cig mas ’chi ba daṅ, ñe bar bcom pas ’chi ba daṅ, rgyu zad pas ’chi ba’o. de la rjes su skad cig mas ’chi ba ni skad cig ma re re la yaṅ ’chi ba źes bya’o. ñe bar bcom pas ’chi ba dug daṅ mtshon la sogs pa phog nas śi ba’o. rgyu zad pas ’chi ba ni tshe riṅ por gyur pa’i las zad pas gaṅ ’chi bar gyur pa’o. mya ṅan daṅ smre sṅags ’don pa la sogs pa ni rga śi’i yan lag tu gtogs te, de la mdza ba daṅ bral ba daṅ, mi mdza’ ba daṅ phrad pa’i rnam par rtog pa las skyes pa’i sems kyi gduṅ ba ni mya ṅan ces bya’o. sems kyi gduṅ ba’i rgyu las tshig tu smra ba rnam pa sna tshogs ’byin pa ni smre sṅags ’don pa’o. khams rnams ’khrugs pas yul mṅon du gyur pa la yaṅ dbaṅ pos ’dzin par mi nus śiṅ rmoṅs pa’i gnod pas reg par gyur pa ni sdug bsṅal ba źes bya’o. yul mṅon du ma gyur pa rnams dbaṅ pos gzuṅ bar chags pa skye ba ni yid mi bde ba’o. źe sdaṅ las byuṅ ba’i rgyu lus daṅ sems ñon moṅs par gyur pa ni ’khrug pa źes bya’o. yaṅ na bu smad la sogs pa daṅ yo byad rnams la gtoṅ mi nus śiṅ chags pa ni mya ṅan ces bya’o. mya ṅan las laṅs pa’i tshig tu smra ba ni smre sṅags ’don pa’o. rnam par śes pa’i tshogs lṅa daṅ ldan pa’i mi bde ba myoṅ ba ni sdug bsṅal lo. yid la byed pa daṅ ldan pa yid kyi sdug bsṅal ni yid mi bde ba’o. gźan yaṅ de la sogs pa sṅon rgyal po’i źam ’briṅ byed byed pa las dben pa daṅ, tshoṅ byed byed pa las khe med pa la sogs pa ñes pa byas pa rnams dran nas mi dga’ ba ni ’khrug pa źes bya’o.
1) D thabs 2) N par 3) D rtog 4) N om. ni 5) N om. daṅ 6) N ñams 7) N sṅon 8) N khas 9) N rten 10) N brten 11) N brgal 12) N blta 13...13) D om. 14) N rtog 15) D rgyus for rgyu ba 16) N pa 17) N phogs 18) N ’chi 19) DN nas 20) N po 21) N rtogs 22) D źes 23) N rnam 24) D źabs 25) N byedde ltar rten ciṅ ’brel bar ’byuṅ ba rgyas par bśad nas, de’i don bsdus te bstan pa’i phyir de ltar sdug bsṅal gyi phuṅ po chen po ’ba’ źig po ’di ’byuṅ bar ’gyur ro źes bya ba gsuṅs so. de ltar źes bya ba ni goṅ du bśad pa ltar na’o. sdug bsṅal gyi phuṅ po ni sdug bsṅal gsum daṅ brgyad la sogs pa sdug bsṅal maṅ po daṅ ldan pas so. chen po ’khor ba thog ma med pa nas rgyun du sdug bsṅal bar gyur pa’i phyir ro. ’di źes bya ba ni gzugs la sogs pa’i chos rnams la bya’o. ’ba’ źig ni bdag daṅ bdag gi daṅ bral ba’i phyir ro. ’byuṅ bar ’gyur ro źes bya ba ni skye bar ’gyur ro źes bya ba’i don to.The second paragraph according to the divisions from Abhidharmasamuccaya mentioned supra, aṅgasamāsatas, "from the point of view of summarizing the members of the pratītyasamutpāda", does not correspond to any part of the text in the mūla, only to ṭ. in fol. 137b7-138a4: de la yan lag bsdu ba ni de ltar rten ciṅ ’brel bar ’byuṅ ba yan lag bcu gñis su phye ba de yaṅ bsdus na yan lag gñis su blta ste, 1) riṅ ba’i rgyu daṅ, 2) ñe ba’i rgyu’o. 1) de la riṅ ba’i rgyu ni dper na sa bon daṅ myu gu lta bu ste, ’bras bu daṅ thag riṅ ba’i phyir ro. 2) ñe ba’i rgyu ni me tog la sogs pa lta bu ste, ’bras bu daṅ thag ñe ba’i phyir ro – "... 1) The distant cause is like seed and sprout (bījāṅkura), they are far from the fruit (phala). 2) The immediate cause is like the flower, etc. (puṣpādi), it is near by the fruit (phala).
The beginning of the paragraph is possibly based on Kośabhāṣya p. 15022-5111: tad yathā bījād aṅkurakāṇḍapattrādīnāṃ prabhavo bhavaty evaṃ kleśāt kleśakarmavastūnām / ... yathā cānapoddhṛtamūlā vanaspatayaś chināś chinnāḥ punar api prarohanty evam anapoddhṛtakleśamūlā gatayaḥ / yathā ca vṛkṣāḥ kālena kālaṃ puṣpaphalānāṃ prasotāro bhavanty evaṃ kleśā apy asakṛt kleśakarmavastūnāṃ hetur bhavanti / yathā ca tuṣāvanaddās taṇḍulāḥ prarohaṇasamarthā bhavanti na kevalā evaṃ kleśaprāptatuṣāvanaddhaṃ karma janmāntaravirohaṇe samarthaṃ na kevalam ity evaṃ tāvat kleśo bījādivad veditavyaḥ / ... yathā ca puṣpaṃ phalotpattāv āsannaṃ kāraṇam, evaṃ karmāṇi vipākotpattau veditavyāni /
de la riṅ ba’i rgyu yaṅ rnam pa gsum du blta ste, a) jis ’debs, b) ji ’debs, c) ji ltar ’debs pa’o. a) jis ’debs śe na? ma rig pa daṅ, ’du byed daṅ, rnam par śes pas ’debs pa’o. b) ji ’debs śe na? miṅ daṅ gzugs daṅ, skye mched drug daṅ, reg pa daṅ, tshor ba rnams ’debs so. c) ji ltar ’debs śe na? ma rig pa las byuṅ ba’i ’du byed kyis ci bsgrubs pa’i bag chags kun gźi la ’debs so.
ñe ba’i rgyu yaṅ rnam pa gsum du blta ste, a) jis mṅon du phyuṅ b) ji mṅon du phyuṅ, c) ji ltar mṅon du phyuṅ ba’o. de la a) jis mṅon du phyuṅ ba ni sred pa daṅ, len pa daṅ, srid pas mṅon du phyuṅ ṅo. b) ji mṅon du phyuṅ ba ni skye ba’o. c) ji ltar mṅon du phyuṅ ba ni sred pa daṅ len pas kun gźi la btab pa’i sa bon srid pa me tog lta bur kha ’bye źiṅ ’bu bar ’byin te, de dag gi ñes dmigs bstan pa ni rga śi’o.
This piece is based on Abhidharmasamuccaya 2620-23: katham aṅgasamāsato ’pi / ākṣepakāṅgam ākṣiptāṅgam abhinirvarttakāṅgam abhinirvṛttyaṅgaṃ ca // ākṣepakāṅgaṃ katamat / avidyā samskārā vijñānaṃ ca // ākṣiptāṅgaṃ katamat / nāmarūpaṃ ṣaḍāyatanaṃ sparśo vedanā ca // abhinirvarttakāṅgaṃ katamat / tṛṣṇā upādānaṃ bhavaś ca // abhinirvṛttyaṅgaṃ katamat / jātir jarāmaraṇaṃ ca //. The Bhāṣya (p. 3110-12) also has the relative pronouns yena and yat: etāvac ca pravṛttinirdeśe nirdeṣṭavyam yad uta hetukāle yenākṣipyate yac cākṣipyate phalakāle yenābhinirvartyate yac cābhinirvartyate tad etat sarvam ebhir aṅgair nirdiṣṭaṃ veditavyam / ... Point c) in ṭ, the yathā, is however omitted by these texts in both cases: "How are they thrown? The habits (vāsanā) produced by the factors (saṃskāra) arising from ignorance (avidyā) are thrown into the store-consciousness (ālayavijñāna). .... How they are produced: The seeds (bīja) thrown (ākṣipta) into the store-consciousness (ālayavijñāna) by thirst (tṛṣṇā) and grasping (upādāna) open up into existence (bhava) like a flower which opens and bloooms. To teach the calamity (ādhīnava) of these things one mentions ageing and death (jarāmaraṇa)".
Then follows the third paragraph according to the divisions from Abhidharmasamuccaya mentioned supra, aṅgasaṃkleśasaṃgrahatas, "from the point of view of condensing the impurities in the pratītyasamutpāda," which also does not correspond to any part of the text in the mūla, only to ṭ. fol. 138a4-6: yan lag gi kun nas ñon moṅs pa bsdu ba ni rten ciṅ ’brel bar ’byuṅ ba yan lag bcu gñis po ’di dag ñon moṅs pa rnam pa gsum du bsdu ste, a) ñon moṅs pa’i kun nas ñon moṅs par bsdu ba daṅ, b) las kyi kun nas ñon moṅs pa daṅ, c) skye ba’i kun nas ñon moṅs par bsdu ba’o. a) de la ma rig pa daṅ, sred pa daṅ, len pa gsum ni ñon moṅs pa’i kun nas ñon moṅs par bsdu’o. b) ’du byed daṅ, rnam par śes pa daṅ, sred pa gsum ni las kyi kun nas ñon moṅs par bsdu ste, rnam par śes pa yaṅ las kyi bag chags kyi rten yin pas der bsdu’o. c) lhag ma rnams ni skye ba’i kun nas ñon moṅs par bsdu’o.
Abhidharmasamuccaya p. 2714-16: katham aṅgasaṃkleśasaṃgrahataḥ / yā cāvidyā yā ca tṛṣṇā yac copādānam ity ayaṃ kleśasaṃkleśasaṃgraha / ye ca saṃskārā yac ca vijñānaṃ yaś ca bhava ity ayaṃ karmasaṃkleśasaṃgrahaḥ / śeṣāṇi janmasaṃkleśasaṃgrahaḥ //


g-yo ba med pa, byed pa med pa, bdag po med pa, yoṅs su ’dzin pa med pa’i chos ji ltar gnas pa bźin du ’byuṅ ste,gaṅ ’di la śes pa, ’di ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i rten ciṅ ’brel bar ’byuṅ ba la mkhas pa źes bya’o.

niśceṣṭanirīhāsvāmikāparigrahā dharmā yathāsthānaṃ saṃbhavanti.yad atra jñānam idam ucyate bodhisattvasya pratītyasamutpādakauśalyam.

[Teaching it according to the character of being without a self but arising from conditions (anātmapratyayotpannalakṣaṇatas):]The moments of existence originate in their proper places without movement, inactive, without an owner, not as something to be owned.Knowledge concerning this is the bodhisattva’s skill with dependent origination.

The fourth paragraph according to the divisions mentioned supra, this title is not mentioned in Abhidharmasamuccaya; ṭ. fol. 138a6-7: bdag med pa’i rkyen las byuṅ ba’i mtshan ñid bstan pa’i phyir g-yo ba med pa byed pa med pa źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs te,g-yo ba med pa ni ma rig pa yaṅ ’di ltar bdag gis ’du byed bskyed do sñam du mi sems la, ’du byed kyaṅ ’di ltar bdag ni ma rig pas bskyed do sñam du sems pa med pa’i phyir ro; byed pa med pa ni ma rig pa la sogs pa skyed pa’i rkyen tsam byed pa yin yaṅ ’du byed skyed pa la byed pa po’i mtshan ñid ma yin pa’i phyir ro; bdag po med pa źes bya ba ni de dag la dbaṅ phyug la sogs pa dbaṅ byed par gyur pa’i mtshan ñid kyi bdag po gaṅ yaṅ med pa’i phyir ro; yoṅs su ’dzin pa med pa źes bya ba ni bdag daṅ sems can daṅ gaṅ zag la sogs pa sñiṅ por gyur pa gaṅ gis kyaṅ byin gyis ma brlabs pa’i phyir ro; chos ji ltar gnas pa bźin du ’byuṅ ste źes bya ba ni rgyu gaṅ yin pa las ’bras bu gaṅ ’byuṅ ba ni chos ji ltar gnas pa bźin du ’byuṅ ba źes bya ste, dbaṅ phyug la sogs pa las ’du byed mi ’byuṅ gi ma rig pa’i rgyu las ’du byed ’byuṅ ba’o.gaṅ ’di la śes pa ni źes bya ba la sogs pa, ’di la źes bya ba ni ’di ltar źes bya ba’i sgra draṅs te, gaṅ tshul bźin ma yin pa kun ’byuṅ ba las ma rig pa kun ’byuṅ ba las skye ba kun ’byuṅ ba las rga śi la sogs pa kun ’byuṅ bar zad kyi, de las gźan pa’i g-yo ba po daṅ byed pa po la sogs pa med par śes pa ’di ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i rten ciṅ ’brel bar ’byuṅ ba la mkhas pa rnams źes bya’o.


gźan yaṅ gaṅ dge ba’i rgyu las byuṅ ba’am, mi dge ba’i rgyu las byuṅ ba’am, mi g-yo ba’i rgyu las byuṅ ba’am, ’khor ba’i rgyu las byuṅ ba’am, mya ṅan las ’das pa’i rgyu las byuṅ ba, de dag thams cad byaṅ chub sems dpas yaṅ dag pa ji lta ba bźin du rab tu śes te:sems can gaṅ dbaṅ po’i rgyu las ’jug pa tshad mar byed pa, de ni dbaṅ po’i rgyu las byuṅ źiṅ, las kyi rgyu las byuṅ ba ste, ’bras bu’i rgyu las ’grub par byed do, źes zin pa daṅ ma zin pa’i chos rnams la gaṅ de ltar rgyu kun ’byuṅ ba las skye ba la mkhas pa, ’di ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i rten ciṅ ’brel bar ’byuṅ ba la mkhas pa źes bya’o.

punar aparaṃ yaḥ kuśalahetuko ’kuśalahetuko ’niñjahetukaḥ saṃsārahetuko nirvāṇahetukas, tān sarvān bodhisattvo yathābhūtaṃ prajānāti:yaḥ sattva indriyahetupraveśaṃ pramāṇīkaroti sa indriyahetukaḥ, karmahetukaḥ phalahetuniṣpattiṃ karotīty upāttānupātteṣu dharmeṣu yad evaṃ hetusamudayotpādakauśalyam, idam ucyate bodhisattvasya pratītyasamutpādakauśalyam.

Further, what is caused by the good [such as birth as a god or human being in the sphere of passion (kāmadhātu) ], caused by the bad [such as birth in the three evil destinies (apāya) of the sphere of passion (kāmadhātu) ], caused by the neutral [or immovable actions of meditation (dhyāna) and states of concentration (samāpatti), causing birth in the worlds of form and the formless worlds, (rūpârūpyaloka), not being moved by the wind of thought-constructions (vikalpa), etc.], what is causing existence, what is causing extinction [namely, the holy ways (āryamārga) ], all of that the bodhisattva knows as it is:“The being that makes into his authority an understanding caused by [the mentioned] abilities [good, bad, etc.], he has those abilities as cause, (p. 76) and having his actions as cause he effects completion [of the actions] in accordance with the fruit as [a final] cause.” Thus skill with birth as having the origin in causes among moments of existence acquired or not yet acquired is called the bodhisattva’s skill with dependent origination.

rten ciṅ ’brel bar ’byuṅ ba la mkhas pa’i rnam graṅs gźan yaṅ bstan par bźed nas gźan yaṅ gaṅ dge ba’i rgyu las byuṅ ba’am, mi dge ba’i rgyu las byuṅ ba’am źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs so.
dge ba ni srog gcod pa las phyir ldog pa la sogs pa dge ba bcu’i las kyi lam rnams so. rgyu de las byuṅ ba ni ’dod pa’i khams su lha daṅ mir skye ba’o.
mi dge ba ni srog gcod pa mi dge ba bcu’i las kyi lam rnams so. rgyu de las byuṅ ba ni ’dod pa’i khams su ṅan soṅ gsum du skye ba’o.
mi g-yo ba ni bsam gtan daṅ sñoms par ’jug pa rnams so. rgyu de las byuṅ ba ni gzugs daṅ gzugs med pa’i khams su skye ba’o. khams gñis kyi las la ci’i phyir mi g-yo ba’i las śes bya źe na? de dag gi las sems rtse gcig pa’i mtshan ñid la rnam par rtog pa’i rluṅ gis bskyod par mi nus pas na mi g-yo ba źes bya’o. yaṅ na, ji ltar ’dod pa na spyod pa’i las ’gro ba gźan du ’gro ba yin yaṅ, de ma yin pa rkyen gźan gyi dbaṅ gis bskyod de, ’gro ba de rnam par smin pa bźin du rnam par smin pa la g-yo ba med pas na mi g-yo ba źes bya’o. de’i don ni ’di yin te, ’dod pa na spyod pa’i sems can gyi las byas pas sbyin pa yoṅs su btaṅ nas mi’i naṅ du mi’i loṅs spyod myoṅ bar ’gyur ba las mi de ñid kyis tshul khrims ñams pa la sogs pa’i las byas pa’i dbaṅ gis mir skye ba’i rnam par smin pa bskyod nas rgyal po’am blon po’i ba laṅ ṅam rtar skye ba lta bur gzugs daṅ gzugs med pa’i khams kyi las la rnam par smin pa g-yo med pas na mi g-yo ba źes bya’o.
’khor bar skye ba’i rgyu ni ’khor ba’i rgyu ste, ’di ltar dge ba daṅ mi dge ba daṅ mi g-yo ba’i las zag pa daṅ bcas pa rnams so. rgyu de las byuṅ ba ni ’khor ba ñid do.
mya ṅan las ’das par gyur pa’i rgyu ni mya ṅan las ’das pa’i rgyu ste, ’phags pa’i lam rnams so; de las byuṅ ba ni mya ṅan las ’das pa’o. de la mya ṅan las ’das pa’aṅ rnam pa gñis te, 1. cha gcig spaṅs pa’i mya ṅan las ’das pa daṅ, 2. cha gñis spaṅs pa’i mya ṅan las ’das pa’o. de la 1. cha gcig spaṅs pa’i mya ṅan las ’das pa ni mthoṅ ba daṅ bsgom pas spaṅ bar bya ba’i ñon moṅs pa’i cha spaṅs te, phuṅ po’i lhag ma daṅ bcas pa’i mya ṅan las ’das pa’o. 2. cha gñis spaṅs pa’i mya ṅan las ’das pa ni ji ltar ñon moṅs pa’i cha spaṅs pa bźin du phuṅ po’i cha yaṅ spaṅs pa ste, phuṅ po’i lhag ma yaṅ ma lus par spaṅs pa’i mya ṅan las ’das pa’o.
de dag thams cad ces bya ba ni goṅ du bśad pa’i dge ba’i rgyu daṅ, mi dge ba’i rgyu daṅ, mi g-yo ba’i rgyu daṅ, ’khor ba’i rgyu daṅ, mya ṅan las ’das pa’i rgyu las byuṅ ba de dag thams cad ces bya ba’i don to.139a6-b3 says: sems can gaṅ dbaṅ po’i rgyu la jug pa tshad mar byed pa, de ni dbaṅ po’i rgyu las byuṅ źiṅ, las kyi rgyu las byuṅ ba ste ’bras bu’i rgyu grub par byed do źes bya ba la, dbaṅ po ñid dge ba daṅ, mi dge ba daṅ, ’khor ba daṅ, mya ṅan las ’das pa rnams byed pa daṅ ’grub pa’i rgyu yin pas na dbaṅ po’i rgyu ste; de ltar dbaṅ po’i rgyu las chos de dag ’byuṅ gi, byed pa po la sogs pas byas pa ma yin par śes pa ni dbaṅ po’i rgyu las ’jug pa tshad mar byed pa ste, de dag ni dge ba daṅ, mi dge ba daṅ, ’khor ba daṅ, mya ṅan las ’das pa kun kyaṅ dbaṅ po daṅ las kyi rgyu las byuṅ źiṅ dge ba la sogs pa ’bras bu’i rgyu dbaṅ po las grub par byed do źes zin pa’i chos rnams la yaṅ śes la ma zin pa’aṅ las kyi rgyu las ’byuṅ bar śes na rten ciṅ ’bral bar ’byuṅ ba la mkhas pa yin par sbyar ro. gaṅ de ltar rgyu kun ’byuṅ ba las skye ba la mkhas pa źes bya ba ni gaṅ goṅ du bśad pa ltar rgyu smin par gyur pa las ’bras bu skye bar śes pa ’di ni źes bya ba’i don to.


gźan yaṅ rten ciṅ ’brel bar ’byuṅ ba la mkhas pa ni

punar aparaṃ pratītyasamutpādakauśalyam:

Further, skill with dependent origination is:


tshul bźin ma yin pa ’gags pas ma rig pa ’gag;ma rig pa ’gags pas ’du byed ’gag;’du byed ’gags pas rnam par śes pa ’gag;rnam par śes pa ’gags pas miṅ daṅ gzugs ’gag;miṅ daṅ gzugs ’gags pas skye mched drug ’gag;skye mched drug ’gags pas reg pa ’gag;reg pa ’gags pas tshor ba ’gag;tshor ba ’gags pas sred pa ’gag;sred pa ’gags pas len pa ’gag;len pa ’gags pas srid pa ’gag;srid pa ’gags pas skye ba ’gag;skye ba ’gags pas rga śi daṅ, mya ṅan daṅ, smre sṅags ’don pa daṅ, sdug bsṅal ba daṅ, yid mi bde ba daṅ, ’khrug pa rnams kyaṅ ’gag par ’gyur te;de ltar sdug bsṅal gyi phuṅ po chen po ’ba’ źig po ’gag par ’gyur ro.

ayoniśonirodhād avidyānirodhaḥ,avidyānirodhāt saṃskāranirodhaḥ,saṃskāranirodhād vijñānanirodhaḥ,vijñānanirodhān nāmarūpanirodhaḥ,nāmarūpanirodhāt ṣaḍāyatananirodhaḥ,ṣaḍāyatananirodhāt sparśanirodhaḥ,sparśanirodhād vedanānirodhaḥ,vedanānirodhāt tṛṣṇānirodhaḥ,tṛṣṇānirodhād upādānanirodhaḥ,upādānanirodhād bhavanirodhaḥ,bhavanirodhāj jātinirodhaḥ,jātinirodhāj jarāmaraṇaśokaparidevaduḥkhadaurmanasyopāyāsā nirudhyante,evam asya kevalasya mahato duḥkhaskandhasya nirodho bhavati.

[Dependent origination in the reverse way (pratiloma), to teach going out of existence, namely extinction (nirvāṇa):]From cessation of being superficial comes cessation of ignorance,from cessation of ignorance comes cessation of formative factors,from cessation of formative factors comes cessation of consciousness,from cessation of consciousness comes cessation of name and form,from cessation of name and form comes cessation of the six senses,from cessation of the six senses comes cessation of touch,from cessation of touch comes cessation of feeling,from cessation of feeling comes cessation of thirst,from cessation of thirst comes cessation of grasping,from cessation of grasping comes cessation of existence,from cessation of existence comes cessation of birth,from cessation of birth ageing, death, sorrow, lamentation, suffering, depression and despair cease,thus this great mass of utter suffering ceases.

de ltar lugs daṅ mthun pa’i mtshan ñid bstan nas, lugs las bzlog pa’i mtshan ñid bstan pa’i phyir gźan yaṅ rten ciṅ ’brel bar ’byuṅ ba’i mtshan ñid la mkhas pa ni źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs pa’o. Cf. supra.’di lta ste, śiṅ med na me daṅ du ba mi ’byuṅ ba daṅ, sa bon med na myu gu mi skye ba bźin du ñon moṅs pa ’gags na, de las skyes pa’i ’bras bu mi ’byuṅ ba’i phyir tshul bźin ma yin pa ’gags pas ma rig pa ’gag ces bya’o. ji ltar ma rig pa la sogs pa ’gags pa yaṅ rten ciṅ ’brel bar ’byuṅ ba źes bya źe na? smras pa: ñes pa med de; ’di la gtan med par dgag pa la ni ma rig pa la sogs pa ’gag go źes mi bya’i, dper na mar me’i rkyen gyis mun pa ’gags na snaṅ ba ñid skye ba daṅ, sman bcud kyis len zos na nad med pa la bde ba skye ba, de bźin du lam bsgoms pa’i mthus ma rig pa daṅ mi mthun pa gaṅ rig pa skye bar ’gyur ba, de ni ma rig pa ’gags pa źes bya ste, de ltar goṅ nas goṅ du ’du byed la sogs pa daṅ mi mthun pa’i gnas ’byuṅ ba la ’du byed la sogs pa ’gags par blta’o.


g-yo ba med pa, byed pa med pa, bdag po med pa, yoṅs su ’dzin pa med pa’i chos ji ltar gnas pa bźin du ’gog par ’gyur ro.gaṅ ’di la mkhas pa, ’di ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i rten ciṅ ’brel bar ’byuṅ ba la mkhas pa źes bya’o.

niśceṣṭanirīhāsvāmikāparigrahā dharmā yathāsthānaṃ nirudhyante.yad iha kauśalyam idam ucyate bodhisattvasya pratītyasamutpādakauśalyam.

The moments of existence cease in their proper places without movement, inactive, without an owner, not as something to be owned.Skill in this is the bodhisattva’s skill with dependent origination.




gźan yaṅ chos thams cad ni rgyu la rag lus pa’o, rkyen la rag lus pa’o, tshogs la rag lus pa’o.chos gaṅ rgyu daṅ, rkyen daṅ, tshogs pa la rag lus pa, de bdag la rag ma lus pa’o, sems can la rag ma lus pa’o, srog la rag ma lus pa’o, gaṅ zag la rag ma lus pa’o.gaṅ bdag la rag ma lus pa daṅ, sems can la rag ma lus pa daṅ, srog la rag ma lus pa daṅ, gaṅ zag la rag ma lus pa, de ’di na źe’am, sṅa ma na źe’am, gźan na źes bgraṅ ba ci yaṅ med de.gaṅ de ltar rtog pa, ’di ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i rten ciṅ ’brel bar ’byuṅ ba la mkhas pa źes bya’o.

punar aparam sarvadharmā hetvadhīnāḥ pratyayādhīnāḥ sāmagryadhīnāḥ.ye dharmā hetupratyayasāmagryadhīnās te nātmādhīnā na sattvādhīnā na jīvādhīnā na pudgalādhīnāḥ.yan nātmādhīnaṃ na sattvādhīnaṃ na jīvādhīnaṃ na pudgalādhīnaṃ na tasya kācid atreti vā pūrvasminn iti vānyatreti vā gaṇanā.ya evaṃ pratyavekṣata idam ucyate bodhisattvasya pratītyasamutpādakauśalyam.

Further, all moments of existence are dependent on causes, dependent on conditions, dependent on combinations of these.And the moments of existence that are dependent on causes, conditions and their combinations are not dependent on a self, a being, a soul or a person.What is not dependent on a self, a being, a soul or a person, no calculation like “here”, “before” or “other place” belongs to that.When he considers things in this way it is the bodhisattva’s skill with dependent origination.

gźan yaṅ chos rnams mthun pa’i rgyu las byuṅ ba daṅ, mi mthun pa’i rgyu las mi ’byuṅ bar śes pa ni rten ciṅ ’brel bar ’byuṅ ba la mkhas pa’o źes bstan par bźed nas gźan yaṅ chos thams cad ni rgyu la rag lus pa’o źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs te, chos thams cad ni naṅ gi chos daṅ phyi’i chos rnams so. de la naṅ gi chos ni ma rig pa’i rkyen gyis ’du byed la sogs pa’o; phyi’i chos ni sa bon daṅ myu gu la sogs pa’o.
ṭ. fol. 140a1-b4 then explains the different hetu, pratyaya and sāmagrī: rgyu la rag lus pa ni chos de dag rgyu drug la brten nas skye’o źes bya ba’i don to. de la rgyu drug po gaṅ źe na? 1) byed pa’i rgyu daṅ, 2) lhan cig ’byuṅ ba’i rgyu daṅ, 3) skal ba mñam pa’i rgyu daṅ, 4) mtshuṅs par ldan pa’i rgyu daṅ, 5) kun tu ’gro ba’i rgyu daṅ, 6) rnam par smin pa’i rgyu’o.
1) de la byed pa’i rgyu ni chos de dag skye ba na gzugs daṅ sems la sogs pa mtshan ñid de dag bdag ñid ma gtogs par chos gźan thams cad ni byed pa’i rgyu ste, skye ba la bgegs mi byed pa’i ṅo bor gnas pa’i phyir ro; Kośabhāṣya p. 8226: saṃskṛtasya hi dharmasya svabhāvavarjyāḥ sarvadharmāḥ kāraṇahetur utpādaṃ prati / avighnabhāvāvasthānāt /
2) chos gaṅ dag gcig la gcig gi ’bras bur gyur pa de ni lhan cig byuṅ ba’i rgyu ste; ’di lta ste: ’byuṅ ba chen po bźi rnams lhan cig skye ba na phan tshun skyed par byed pas gcig la gcig lhan cig ’byuṅ ba’i rgyu’o; Kośabhāṣya 8319: ye dharmāḥ parasparaphalās te parasparaḥ sahabhūhetur yathā ... catvāri mahābhūtāny anyonyaṃ sahabhūhetuḥ /
3) de bźin du sems daṅ sems las byuṅ ba daṅ ’dod pa na spyod pa’i sdug bsṅal mthoṅ bas spaṅ bar bya ba’i chos sṅar skyes pa rnams phyis skyes pa daṅ ma skyes pa rnams kyi skal ba mñam pa’i rgyu’o. de bźin du dge ba daṅ mi dge ba daṅ luṅ du ma bstan pa rnams daṅ yaṅ sbyar ro; Kośabhāṣya p. 8510: sadṛśā dharmāḥ sadṛśānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ sabhāgahetus tad yathā kuśalāḥ pañca skandhāḥ kuśalānām anyonyaṃ, kliṣṭāḥ kliṣṭānām, avyākṛtā avyākṛtānāṃ rūpam avyākṛtaṃ pañcānām /
4) mtshuṅs par ldan pa’i rgyu ni sems daṅ sems las byuṅ ba gaṅ dag skad cig ma gaṅ la brten nas gnas pa’i dbaṅ po rnams so; abridges Kośabhāṣya p. 8820-22: samāna āśrayo yeṣāṃ te cittacaittāḥ anyonyaṃ saṃprayuktahetuḥ / samāna ity abhinnas tad yathā ya eva cakṣurindriyakṣaṇaś cakṣurvijñānasyāśrayaḥ, sa eva tatsaṃprayuktānāṃ vedanādīnām eva yāvan mana-indriyakṣaṇo manovijñānatatsaṃprayuktānāṃ veditavyaḥ /
5) sṅar skyes pa’i ñon moṅs pa rnams phyis skyes pa daṅ ma skyes pa’i raṅ gi sa pa rnams kyis kun tu ’gro ba’i rgyu yin pa’i phyir kun tu ’gro ba’i rgyu’o; Kośabhāṣya p. 893: svabhūmikāḥ pūrvotpannāḥ sarvatragā dharmāḥ paścimānāṃ kliṣṭānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ sarvatragahetuḥ /
6) mi dge ba daṅ dge ba zag pa daṅ bcas pa’i chos rnams ni rnam par smin pa’i rgyu’o; Kośabhāṣya p. 8919: akuśalāḥ kuśalasāsravāś ca dharmā vipākahetuḥ /
rkyen la rag lus źes bya ba ni rkyen bźi la brten nas skye źes ba’i don to. rkyen bźi ni 1) rgyu’i rkyen daṅ, 2) dmigs pa’i rkyen daṅ, 3) mtshuṅs pa de ma thag pa’i rkyen daṅ, 4) bdag po’i rkyen to.
1) de la rgyu’i rkyen ni gaṅ ’bras bu skyed pa la rgyu’i dṅos por gnas pa ste, sa bon la sogs pa daṅ kun gźi rnam par śes pa bag chags daṅ bcas pa’o; gźan dag ni gźan du ’chad de: byed pa’i rgyu ma gtogs par rgyu rnam pa lṅa rnams ni rgyu’i rkyen to źe’o; Abhidharmasamuccaya p. 289-10: hetupratyaya katamaḥ / ālayavijñānaṃ kuśalavāsanā ca // "Others explain it otherwise:" kāraṇahetuvarjyāḥ pañca hetavo hetupratyayaḥ / (Kośabhāṣya p. 988).
2) dmigs pa gaṅ la sems daṅ sems las byuṅ ba gaṅ dmigs nas skye bar ’gyur pa’i dmigs pa de dag ni de’i dmigs pa’i rkyen te; de’aṅ ci rigs par chos thams cad rnam par śes pa drug gi dmigs pa’i rkyen to; abridging Kośabhāṣya p. 1004-6: yathāyogaṃ cakṣurvijñānasya saṃprayogasya rūpam / śrotravijñānasya śabdaḥ / ghrāṇavijñānasya gandhaḥ / jihvāvijñānasya rasaḥ / kāyavijñānasya spraṣṭavyam / manovijñānasya sarvadharmāḥ / yo dharmo yasya dharmasyālambanaṃ na kadācit sa dharmas taddharmasya nālambanam /
3) mya ṅan las ’das par ’jug pa’i tha ma’i sems ma gtogs par sems daṅ sems las ’byuṅ ba’i rgyu rnams ni mtshuṅs pa de ma thag pa’i rkyen to; Kośabhāṣya p. 9810: arhataḥ paścimān apāsyotpannāś cittacaittāḥ samanantarapratyayaḥ /
4) byed pa’i rgyu ñid bdag po’i rkyen to; Kośabhāṣya p. 10013: ya eva kāraṇahetuḥ sa evādhipatipratyayaḥ /
tshogs pa la rag lus źes bya ba ni rgyu daṅ rkyen rnams ’dus nas ’bras bu bskyed nus pa’i mthu daṅ ldan par gnas pa la brten nas ’bras bu skye źes bya ba’i don to. mthun pa’i rgyu las byuṅ ba bstan nas mi mthun pa’i rgyu las mi ’byuṅ bar bstan pa’i phyir chos gaṅ rgyu daṅ rkyen daṅ tshogs pa la rag lus pa de bdag la rag ma lus źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs te, gźan dag gis btags pa’i bdag la sogs pa la brten te mi skye źes bya ba’i don to.
On hetu cf. also Mvy. 2260-65; Kośa LVP p. ii. 245ff with other references; and Vyākhyā i. p. 18617ff; on pratyaya cf. Mvy. 2267-70; Kośa p. 983ff, LVP ii. p. 299ff, Vyākhyā i. p. 2328ff; Bbh. p. 9826-998; Abhidharmasamuccaya p. 287ff.de ’di na źe’am, sṅa ma źe’am, gźan źes bgraṅ ba ci yaṅ med de źes bya ba ni bdag la ji ltar rag ma lus pa daṅ sems can la sogs pa la rag ma lus pas na da lta’i dus su yaṅ ’di na źes bgraṅ du med, ’das pa’i dus su yaṅ ’di ’dra ba źig ces bgraṅ du med, ma ’oṅs pa’i dus su yaṅ ’di ltar ’gyur źes bgraṅ du med pa’i don to. yaṅ na chos thams cad ni rgyu la rag lus źes bya ba ni phyi daṅ naṅ gi rten ciṅ ’brel bar ’byuṅ ba rnams rgyu daṅ ’brel ba la skye źes bya ba’i tha tshig ste, de la phyi rol gyi rten ciṅ ’brel bar ’byuṅ ba’i rgyu daṅ ’brel ba gaṅ źe na? ’di lta ste, sa bon las myu gu, myu gu las ’dab ma źes bya ba la sogs pa’o. de la naṅ gi rten ciṅ ’brel bar ’byuṅ ba rgyu daṅ ’brel ba gaṅ źe na? ma rig pa’i rkyen gis ’du byed, ’du byed kyi rkyen gyis rnam par śes pa źes bya ba la sogs pa’o. rkyen la rag lus pa źes bya ba ni phyi daṅ naṅ gi rten ciṅ ’brel bar ’byuṅ ba yaṅ rkyen daṅ ’brel ba la skye źes bya ba’i don to. phyi’i rten ciṅ ’brel bar ’byuṅ ba’i rkyen gaṅ źe na? ’di lta ste, sa daṅ, chu daṅ, me daṅ, rluṅ daṅ, nam mkha’ daṅ, dus kyi khams rnams śes gaṅ gsuṅs pa’o. naṅ gi rten ciṅ ’brel bar ’byuṅ ba’i rkyen gaṅ źe na? sa daṅ, chu daṅ, me daṅ, rluṅ daṅ, nam mkha’ daṅ, rnam par śes pa’i khams rnams śes gaṅ gsuṅs pa’o. tshogs pa la rag lus pa źes bya ba ni rgyu daṅ rkyen ma tshaṅ bar ma gyur pa la rten źes bya ba’i don to. (153a)
Then, in ṭ. fol. 141a2-5, there follow several abridged quotations from the Śālistambasūtra, summarizing this text, to elucidate the paragraph: de bas na sā lu ljaṅ pa’i mdo las kyaṅ rgyu’i skabs su: sa bon med na myu gu mi ’byuṅ ste, me tog med na ’bras bu’i bar du yaṅ mi ’byuṅ ṅo źes gsuṅs pa daṅ; rkyen gyi skabs su: ’di rnams med par sa bon las myu gu skye bar mi ’gyur gyi, nam phyi rol gyi sa’i khams ma tshaṅ ba med par gyur pa la źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs so; naṅ gi rten ciṅ ’brel bar ’byuṅ ba la yaṅ rgyu’i skabs su: gal te ma rig pa ma byuṅ na ’du byed kyaṅ mi ’byuṅ ba źig na, de bźin du skye ba ma byuṅ du zin na rga śi’i bar du yaṅ mi mṅon pa źig na, ’di ltar ma rig pa yod pa las ’du byed rnams skye źiṅ ’byuṅ bar ’gyur ro źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs pa daṅ; rkyen gyi skabs su yaṅ: rkyen ’di dag med par lus skye bar mi ’gyur gyi, nam sa’i khams tshaṅ źiṅ źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs pa’o; ṭ. fol. 141a2 [hetvadhikāre]a, Śāl p. 413-14: asati bīje ’ṅkuro na bhavati, yāvad asati puṣpe
phalaṃ na bhavati; ṭ. fol. 141a2 [pratyayādhikāre], Śāl p. 512-13: asatsv eṣu pratyayeṣu bījād
aṅkurasyābhinirvṛttir na bhavati / yadā bāhyaś ca pṛthivīdhātur avikalo bhavati / ṭ. fol. 141a3-4 [ādhyātmikasyāpi pratītyasamutpādasya hetvadhikāre], Śāl p. 79-11: avidyā cen nābhaviṣyat naiva saṃskārāḥ prajñāsyante / evaṃ yāvaj jātiś cen nābhaviṣyat jarāmaraṇaṃ na prajñāsyate / atha satyām avidyāyāṃ saṃskārāṇām abhinirvṛttiṃ bhavati / ṭ. fol. 141a4-5 [pratyayādhikāre ’pi], Śāl p. 815-16: asatām eṣāṃ pratyayānāṃ kāyasyotpattir na bhavati / yadā ādhyātmikaḥ pṛthivīdhātur avikalo bhavati.
