ṭ. then again comments on Akṣ in fol. 141a5-b1: chos gaṅ rgyu daṅ rkyen daṅ tshogs pa la rag lus pa de źes bya ba ni phyi daṅ naṅ gi chos gaṅ rgyu daṅ rkyen daṅ rgyu rkyen ’brel pa las skyes pa’i chos de dag ni bdag las mi skye, sems can las mi skye źes bya ba’i don to. de bas na mdo sde de ñid las phyi’i rten ciṅ ’brel bar ’byuṅ ba’i skabs su: de la sa’i khams kyaṅ ’di ltar bdag gi sa bon rten pa’i bya ba bya’o sñam du mi sems so źes bya ba nas myu gu de yaṅ bdag gis ma byas, pha rol gyis ma byas, gñis kas ma byas, dbaṅ pos ma sprul, dus kyis ma bsgyur, raṅ bźin las ma byuṅ, rgyu med pa las kyaṅ ma skyes te źes gsuṅs pa daṅ; naṅ gi rten ciṅ ’brel bar ’byuṅ ba’i skabs su yaṅ: ma rig pa yaṅ ’di ltar bdag gis ’du byed skyed do sñam du mi sems so źes bya ba nas bdag ma yin no, sems can ma yin, srog ma yin źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs pa’i phyir ro; ṭ. fol. 141a6-7 [bāhyasya pratītyasamutpādasyādhikāre], Śāl p. 515-16, 63-5: tatra pṛthivīdhātor naivaṃ bhavati ahaṃ bījasya saṃdhāraṇakṛtyaṃ karomīti / [yāvat] sa cāṅkuro na svayaṃkṛto na parakṛto nobhayakṛto neśvarakṛto na kālapariṇamito na prakṛtisaṃbhūto nāpy ahetusamutpannaḥ / ṭ. fol. 141a7-b1 [ādhyātmikasyāpi pratītyasamutpādasyādhikāre], Śāl p. 712, 99-10: tatrāvidyāyā naivaṃ bhavati ahaṃ saṃskārān abhinirvartayāmīti / [yāvan] nātmā na sattvo na jīva [ity ādi]. ṭ. fol. 141b1-3: de na ’di na źe’am, sṅa ma na źe’am, gźan na źes bgraṅ ba ci yaṅ med de źes bya ba ni chos gaṅ rgyu daṅ rkyen daṅ tshogs pa la rag lus pas bdag daṅ sems can la rag ma lus pa’i chos de ni da ltar ci yin? źes brtag tu med pa daṅ, sṅon gyi dus na ci ’dra? źes brtag tu med pa daṅ, ma ’oṅs pa’i dus na ci lta bur ’gyur źes brtag tu med ces bya ba’i don to. de bas na sā lu ljaṅ pa’i mdo las kyaṅ: ji bdag ’das pa’i dus na byuṅ ba źig gam, ’on te ma byuṅ ba źig? sñam du sṅon gyi mtha’ la mi rtog; ma ’oṅs pa’i dus na jir ’gyur, ji lta bur ’gyur? źes ma ’oṅs pa’i dus la mi rtog go; ’di ji źig, ci źig yod, cir ’gyur? sems can ’di dag gaṅ nas ’oṅs, ’di nas śi ’phos nas goṅ du ’gro bar ’gyur? źes da ltar byuṅ ba la mi rtog go źes gsuṅs so; Śāl p. 1812-192: na sa pūrvāntaṃ pratisarati kiṃ nv aham abhūvam atīte ’dhvani, āhosvin nābhūvam atīte ’dhvani / ko nv aham abhūvam atīte ’dhvani, kathaṃ nv aham abhūvam atīte ’dhvani / aparāntaṃ vā punar na pratisarati kiṃ nv ahaṃ bhaviṣyāmy anāgate ’dhvani / ahosvin na bhaviṣyāmy anāgate ’dhvani / ko nu bhaviṣyāmy anāgate ’dhvani, kathaṃ nu bhaviṣyāmy anāgate ’dhvani / pratyutpannaṃ vā punar na pratisarati kiṃ nv idaṃ kathaṃ nv idaṃ ke santaḥ ke bhaviṣyāmaḥ, ayaṃ sattvaḥ kuta āgataḥ, sa itaś cyutaḥ kutra gamiṣyatīti /. The last quotation is somewhat abridged in ṭ.


gźan yaṅ gaṅ byaṅ chub sems dpa’ byaṅ chub kyi rkyen thams cad ñe bar gźog la, rkyen de dag kyaṅ zad ciṅ ’gog par rtog ste, sems can la lta ba’i phyir zad ciṅ ’gog pa’i ye śes su yaṅ mi ’jog pa, ’di ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i rten ciṅ ’brel bar ’byuṅ ba la mkhas pa źes bya’o.

punar aparaṃ yo bodhisattvaḥ sarvabodhipratyayān upasthāpayati, teṣāṃ ca pratyayānāṃ kṣayanirodhatvaṃ pratyavekṣamāṇaḥ sattvāvekṣayā kṣayanirodhajñāne na sthāpyata idam ucyate bodhisattvasya pratītyasamutpādakauśalyam.

Further, [to teach knowledge of dependent origination avoiding the two extremes (antadvayavivarjita):] when the bodhisattva produces all the conditions for awakening, and then sees the destruction and cessation of those conditions [that they really are empty], but does not get stuck in the knowledge of their destruction and cessation, out of regard for living beings, it is called the bodhisattva’s skill with dependent origination.

gźan yaṅ rten ciṅ ’brel bar byuṅ ba mtha’ gñis daṅ bral ba śes pa ni rten ciṅ ’brel bar ’byuṅ ba la mkhas pa yin no źes bstan par bźed nas, gźan yaṅ gaṅ byaṅ chub sems dpa’ byaṅ chub kyi rkyen thams cad kyaṅ ñe bar gźog źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs te, de la ye śes phun sum tshogs pa daṅ, spaṅs pa phun sum tshogs pa ni byaṅ chub ces bya ste, byaṅ chub ni ye śes daṅ spaṅs pa’i mtshan ñid yin pa’i phyir ro.
de la ye śes phun sum tshogs pa rnam pa bźi ste: 1) thams cad śes pa daṅ, 2) rnam pa thams cad du śes pa daṅ, 3) ’bad pa med par śes pa daṅ, 4) ma bstan par śes pa’o. 1) thams cad śes pa ni phuṅ po daṅ khams daṅ skye mched la sogs pa śes bya’i dṅos po ma lus par śes pa’o; 2) rnam pa thams cad du śes pa ni de dag kyaṅ mi rtag pa’am, bdag med pa’i rnam par śes pa’am, dus gsum thams cad du śes pa ste, nams kyaṅa śes pa de la ñams pa med pa’o; 3) ’bad pa med par śes pa ni tiṅ ṅe ’dzin la sogs pa’i rgyu la mi ltos śiṅ brtsal ba med par lhun gyis grub par śes pa’o; 4) ma bstan par śes pa ni mkhan po daṅ slob dpon gyi man ṅag med par raṅ ’byuṅ gi ye śes kyis chos thams cad raṅ ñid kyis mṅon par byaṅ chub pa’i phyir ro.
spaṅs pa phun sum tshogs pa yaṅ rnam pa lṅa ste: 1) ñon moṅs pa’i sgrib pa spaṅs pa daṅ, 2) śes bya’i sgrib pa spaṅs pa daṅ, 3) śin tu spaṅs pa daṅ, 4) bag chags daṅ bcas pa spaṅs pa daṅ, 5) sñoms par ’jug pa’i sgrib pa thams cad spaṅs pa’o. 1) de la ñon moṅs pa’i sgrib pa spaṅs pa ni ’dod chags la sogs pa mthoṅ ba daṅ bsgom pa’i lam gyis spaṅ bar bya ba’i ñon moṅs pa rnams spaṅs pa’o; 2) śes bya’i sgrib pa spaṅs pa ni phuṅ po daṅ khams daṅ skye mched la gzuṅ ba daṅ ’dzin pa’i mṅon par chags pa’i bag chags ñon moṅs pa can ma yin pa mi śes pa spaṅs pa’o; 3) śin tu spaṅs pa ni sgrib pa de gñis phyis sems kyi rgyud la ’byuṅ źiṅ skye ba med par spaṅs pa’o; 4) bag chags daṅ bcas par spaṅs pa ni sgrib pa de gñis kyi bag la ñal rtsa nas bton pa’o; 5) sñoms par ’jug pa thams cad kyi sgrib pa spaṅs pa ni mthar gyis gnas pa’i sñoms par ’jug pa dgu daṅ zad par gyi skye mched daṅ zil gyis gnon pa’i skye mched rnams thob par bya ba la bar du gcod pa rnams spaṅs pa’o.
rgyu daṅ rkyen gaṅ gis bla na med pa’i byaṅ chub thob par ’gyur ba’i rgyu daṅ rkyen de rnams ñe bar sgrub pa la byaṅ chub kyi rkyen rnams kyaṅ ñe bar gźog la źes bya ste, rgyu daṅ rkyen kyaṅ bsod nams daṅ ye śes kyi tshogs so. rkyen de dag kyaṅ zad ciṅ ’gog par rtogs te źes bya ba ni byaṅ chub kyi rgyu daṅ rkyen rnams ṅo bo ñid med par śes pa’am, ma rig pa’i rkyen gyis ’du byed ’byuṅ ba la sogs pa rkyen goṅ du smos pa rnams ṅo bo ñid med par śes pa źes bya ba’i don to. sems can la lta ba’i phyir zad ciṅ ’gog pa’i ye śes su mi ’jog ces bya ba ni de ltar de bźin mya ṅan las ’das pa stoṅ pa’i mtshan ñid rtogs kyaṅ sems can gyi don du mya ṅan las ’das pa ’ba’ źig la gnas par mi byed ces bya ba’i don to.
The paragraph seems to be based upon Kośabhāṣya p. 41514ff., bhāṣya on Kośa vii. 34: ...sarvapuṇyajñānasaṃbhārasamudāgamataḥ dharmakāyapariniṣpattitaḥ arthacaryayā ca lokasya / .... caturvidhā ca phalasaṃpat / jñānasaṃpat prahāṇasaṃpat prabhāvasaṃpad rūpakāyasaṃpac ca / ... jñānasaṃpat punaś caturvidhā / anupadiṣṭajñānaṃ sarvatrajñānaṃ sarvathājñānam ayatnajñānaṃ ca / caturvidhā prahāṇasaṃpat / sarvakleśaprahāṇam atyantaprahāṇaṃ savāsanāprahāṇaṃ sarvasamādhisamāpattyāvaraṇaprahāṇaṃ ca ... / The explanations of the concepts are, however, found only in ṭ.


de la byaṅ chub sems dpa’i dus gsum la mkhas pa gaṅ źe na?

tatra katamad bodhisattvasya tryadhvakauśalyam?

(p. 77) 6) What then is the bodhisattva’s skill with the three times?

rten ciṅ ’brel bar ’byuṅ ba bśad pa’i don du dus gsum la mkhas pa bstan pas ji ltar bstan pa bźin du bśad par bźed nas de la byaṅ chub sems dpa’i dus gsum la mkhas pa gaṅ źe na źes dris so.
dus gsum po de yaṅ dus ñid la rnam pa gsum yod pa ma yin gyi, sems daṅ sems las byuṅ ba la dus gsum du bźag ste, sems daṅ sems las byuṅ ba’i dṅos po de dag ñid rgyu daṅ ’bras bu bcas par ’das te źig pa ni ’das pa’i dus źes bya, rgyu daṅ ’bras bu da duṅ ma skyes pa la ni ma ’oṅs pa’i dus źes bya, rgyu daṅ ’bras bu skyes nas ma źig gi bar du ni da ltar byuṅ ba’i dus źes bya ste; dṅos po ’das pa daṅ ma ’oṅs pa daṅ da ltar byuṅ ba rnams ci ’dra ba la mkhas pa ni dus gsum la mkhas pa źes bya’o. Translated in the introduction.


gaṅ bdag daṅ sems can gźan gyi ’das pa’i sems daṅ sems las byuṅ ba dge ba daṅ mi dge ba rnams rjes su dran pa ste, mi dge ba’i sems daṅ sems las byuṅ ba rnams dran nas kyaṅ rnam par smod pa daṅ, dge ba’i sems daṅ sems las byuṅ ba rnams dran nas kyaṅ byaṅ chub tu yoṅs su sṅo ba, ’di ni ’das pa la mkhas pa’o.

yātmanaḥ parasattvānāṃ cātītānāṃ kuśalānām akuśalānāṃ ca cittacaittasikānām anusmṛtir, akuśalānāṃ cittacaittasikānām anusmṛtya ca vigarhanā, kuśalānām cittacaittasikānām anusmṛtya ca bodhipariṇāmanā, idam atītakauśalyam.

Remembering one’s own and other beings’ past thoughts and contents of thought, good and bad; and having remembered, rejecting bad thoughts and contents of thought; having remembered, transforming into awakening the good thoughts and contents of thought; this is skill with the past.

’das pa’i dus la mkhas pa bstan pa’i phyir gaṅ bdag daṅ sems can gźan gyi źes bya ba la sogs pa smos te, dge ba daṅ, mi dge ba daṅ, ’brel pa’i sems daṅ sems las byuṅ ba gaṅ yin pa ni sems daṅ sems las byuṅ ba dge ba daṅ mi dge ba rnams źes bya’o, gaṅ bdag daṅ sems can gźan gyis ’das pa’i dus na dge ba ni ’di lta bu źig byas, mi dge ba ni ’di lta bu źig byas źes bdag daṅ gźan gyis dge ba daṅ mi dge ba byas pa ma brjed pa ni rjes su dran pa’o; de tsam gyi ’das pa’i dus la mkhas pa yin nam źe na? ma yin par bstan pa’i phyir mi dge ba’i sems daṅ sems las byuṅ ba źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs te, ’di yaṅ bdag daṅ gźan gyi mi dge ba daṅ ’brel pa’i sems daṅ sems las byuṅ ba dran nas źes bya ba daṅ sbyar ro; byaṅ chub tu bsṅo ba źes bya ba ni dge ba byas pa rnams bla na med pa’i byaṅ chub thob pa’i rgyur gyur ces smon pa’o.


gaṅ ma ’oṅs pa’i sems daṅ sems las byuṅ ba, dge ba’i rtsa ba’i tshogs la ṅes par sems śiṅ, byaṅ chub mṅon du ’gyur ba’i las sems te: bdag gi dge ba’i sems bskyed pa gaṅ dag skye bar ’gyur ba, de dag ni bla na med pa yaṅ dag par rdzogs pa’i byaṅ chub tu yoṅs su bsṅo bar bya’o; mi dge ba’i sems daṅ sems las byuṅ ba rnams kyi skabs mi dbye, źes, gaṅ de lta bur sems la bsgo ba, de ni ma ’oṅs pa la mkhas pa’o.

yānāgatānaṃ cittacaittasikānāṃ kuśalamūlānāṃ nidhyāptir, bodher āmukhīkarmasamanvāhārah: ye ma utpatsyante kuśalāś cittotpādās tān tv anuttarāyām samyaksaṃbodhaye parināmayiṣyāmi, akuśalānāṃ cittacaittasikānām avakāśaṃ na kariṣyāmīti yaivaṃ cittabhāvanā, idam anāgatakauśalyam.

Being absorbed in future roots of the good, being thoughts and contents of thoughts, concentrating on making awakening present [in the following way]: “I will transform into incomparable perfect awakening all appearances of good thoughts and contents of thought that appear in me, and I will give the bad thoughts and contents of thought no chance,” cultivating thought in this way is skill with the future.

ma ’oṅs pa’i dus la mkhas pa bstan pa’i phyir gaṅ ma ’oṅs pa’i sems daṅ sems las byuṅ ba źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs te, ma ’oṅs pa na bdag gi bsod nams daṅ ye śes kyi tshogs bla na med pa’i byaṅ chub thob pa’i rgyu bdag daṅ gźan la phan par byed pa’i rkyen du gyur pa’i dge ba’i rtsa ba rnams gnod mi za bar bya’o źes sems pa ni dge ba’i rtsa ba’i tshogs la ṅes par sems pa źes bya’o; don de ñid bstan pa’i phyir byaṅ chub mṅon du ’gyur ba’i las sems te źes bya ba gsuṅs te, byaṅ chub thob par ’gyur ba’i dge ba’i las bya bar sems pa ni byaṅ chub mṅon du ’gyur ba’i las sems pa źes bya’o; don de ñid ji lta bu yin pa gsal bar bstan pa’i phyir bdag gi dge ba’i sems bskyed pa gaṅ dag ces bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs te, dge ba daṅ ’brel pa’i sems ni dge ba’i sems so, bskyed pa ni da ltar gyi dus na dge ba’i sems skyes zin pa’o, skye bar ’gyur ba ni ma ’oṅs pa’i dus na dge ba daṅ ’brel pa’i sems gnod mi za bar skye bar ’gyur ba’o; de dag ces bya ba ni dus gñis kyi dge ba’i sems ñid la sñegs te, da ltar gyi dus na dge ba’i sems skyed pa daṅ ma ’oṅs pa’i dus na skye bar ’gyur ba de dag ces bya ba’i don to, ni źes bya bas dge ba de dag theg pa gñis daṅ lha daṅ mi’i bde ’gror mi sṅo źes bya bar ston to, byaṅ chub ces bya ba ni byaṅ chub thob par bya ba’i phyir źes bya ba’i tha tshig go, skabs ni mi dbye źes bya ba ni ma ’oṅs pa’i mi dge ba’i sems daṅ sems las byuṅ ba skye ba’i skabs mi dbye źes bya bar ston to; goṅ du bśad pa’i don rnams bsdus te bstan pa’i phyir gaṅ de lta bur sems la bsgo ba, de ni źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs te, de lta bur sems la bsgo źes bya ba ni ji nas da ltar gyi dus nas dge ba’i sems bskyed pa daṅ, ma ’oṅs pa’i dus na dge ba’i sems skye bar ’gyur ba de dag ṅes par byaṅ chub tu bsṅo la, ma ’oṅs pa’i mi dge ba’i sems daṅ sems las byuṅ ba skye ba’i skabs mi dbye’o źes de lta bur de nas sems la bsgo źiṅ sems la ’jog par byed pa de ni źes bya ba’i don to


da ltar byuṅ ba la mkhas pa gaṅ źe na? gaṅ da ltar byuṅ ba’i sems daṅ sems las byuṅ ba rnams tshul bźin sbyor bas dge ba’i rtsa ba mṅon par ’du byed pa daṅ, mi dge ba’i sems daṅ sems las byuṅ ba zlog pa daṅ, dge ba’i sems daṅ sems las byuṅ ba rnams byaṅ chub tu mṅon du byed pa ni da ltar byuṅ ba la mkhas pa ste.

katamat pratyutpannakauśalyam? yaḥ pratyutpannānāṃ cittacaittasikānāṃ yoniśaḥprayogena kuśalamūlābhisaṃskāraḥ, akuśalānāṃ cittacaittasikānāṃ nivartanaṃ, kuśalānāṃ ca cittacaitasikānāṃ bodher āmukhīkaraṇaṃ pratyutpannakauśalyam.

What then is skill with the present? Producing roots of the good with correct practice in present thoughts and contents of thought, banishing bad thoughts and contents of thought, making good thoughts and contents of thought present for the sake of awakening, is skill with the present.

da ltar byuṅ ba’i dus la mkhas pa bstan pa’i phyir da ltar byuṅ ba la mkhas pa gaṅ źe na źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs te, ’dod ma chags pa la sogs pa dge ba’i rtsa ba byed ciṅ, ’dod chags la sogs pa mi dge ba’i rtsa ba rnams la mi ’jug pa ni tshul bźin sbyor ba źes bya ste, don gźan ni sla bas ma bśad do.


gaṅ ’di dag la mkhas pa, de ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i dus gsum la mkhas pa źes bya’o.

yad eteṣu kauśalyam idam ucyate bodhisattvasya tryadhvakauśalyam.

Skill in these things is the bodhisattva’s skill with the three times.


gźan yaṅ gaṅ ’das pa’i dus kyi chos rnams stoṅ par mos pa daṅ, ma ’oṅs pa’i dus kyi chos rnams stoṅ par mos pa daṅ, da ltar byuṅ ba’i dus kyi chos rnams stoṅ par mos pa ste, de ltar śes rab daṅ ye śes kyi dus gsum stoṅ pa ñid du yaṅ rtog la, ’das pa daṅ, ma ’oṅs pa daṅ, da ltar byuṅ ba’i saṅs rgyas bcom ldan ’das rnams kyi bsod nams thams cad kyi rjes su thabs kyi ye śes kyis yi raṅ bar yaṅ byed de; gaṅ ’di la mkhas pa, de ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i dus gsum la mkhas pa źes bya’o.

punar aparaṃ yātītasye ’dhvani dharmāḥ śūnyā ity adhimuktir, anāgate ’dhvani dharmā śūnyā ity adhimuktiḥ, pratyutpanne ’dhvani dharmāḥ śūnyā ity adhimuktir, evam prajñājñānena tryadhvaśūnyatām pratyavekṣamāṇo ’pi ’tītānāgatapratyutpannānāṃ bhagavatāṃ sarvapuṇyānvitopāyajñānenānumodayati, yad iha kauśalyaṃ tad bodhisattvasya tryadhvakauśalyam.

Further, [to understand rightly with insight (prajñā) and expedient means (upāya) the things in the three times it is said:] confidence in the fact that the moments of existence of the past are empty, confidence in the fact that the moments of existence of the future are empty, confidence in the fact that the moments of existence of the present are empty – though one considers the emptiness of the three times thus with insight and knowledge, one rejoices in the knowledge of expedient means resulting from all the merit of the Buddhas past, present and future – skill in this is the bodhisattva’s skill with the three times.

śes rab daṅ thabs kyi ye śes kyis dus gsum na gnas pa’i dṅos po rnams ji lta ba bźin du phyin ci ma log par khoṅ du chud pa ni dus gsum la mkhas pa yin no źes bstan par bźed nas gźan yaṅ gaṅ ’das pa’i dus kyi chos rnams stoṅ par mos pa źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs te, gaṅ ’das pa’i dus kyi chos phuṅ po daṅ skye mched la sogs pa gaṅ zag daṅ chos kyi dṅos por yod pa ma yin pa yid ches pa ni ’das pa’i dus kyi chos rnams stoṅ par mos pa’o. lhag ma yaṅ de bźin du sbyar te, tshig gźan ni sla bas ma bśad do.


gźan yaṅ ’das pa’i dus na zad pa’i chos rnams phyi ma’i mthar ’phos par mi lta źiṅ, dge ba’i mṅon par ’du byed pa la brtson ’grus kyaṅ mi gtoṅ ste, mi dge ba mṅon par ’du mi byed pa daṅ;gaṅ ma ’oṅs pa’i dus kyi chos rnams mi skye mi ’byuṅ bar rtog ciṅ, byaṅ chub tu bsṅo ba’i brtson ’grus kyaṅ mi ’dor ba daṅ;da ltar byuṅ ba’i dus na chos rnams ’dug pa med ciṅ mi gnas par rtog ste, byaṅ chub sems dpa’ lhag pa’i bsam pa rab tu brtan pa ni byaṅ chub kyi sems kyaṅ mi brjed de,’di ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i dus gsum la mkhas pa źes bya’o.

punar aparam atīte ’dhvani kṣīnān dharmān nāparānte cyutān paśyann api kuśalābhisaṃskāraṇāya vīryaṃ na sraṃsayati nākuśalam abhisaṃskaroti;yo ’nāgate ’dhvani dharmān anutpādān asaṃbhāvān pratyavekṣamāno ’pi bodhipariṇāmanāvīryaṃ na tyajati;pratyutpanne ’dhvani dharmān asthitān apratiṣṭhitān pratyavekṣamāṇo ’pi bodhisattvaḥ sudṛḍhādhyāśayo bodhicittaṃ na saṃpramoṣayati.idam ucyate bodhisattvasya tryadhvakauśalyam.

Further, though he sees that the moments of existence of the past [really (svabhāvena) ] have perished and do not perish in the future [as there is no connection to the future (paścimâpratisaṃdhi) ], he does not slacken his vigour to bring about the good, he does not bring the bad about;though he considers the moments of existence of the future to be unborn and inexistent, he does not give up his vigour in transforming into awakening;though he considers the moments of existence in the present to be not remaining, not abiding, the bodhisattva, very firm in his determination, does not forget the thought of awakening [though this also, according to the highest truth (paramārtha), is not abiding].This is called the bodhisattva’s skill with the three times.

gaṅ yaṅ dus gsum gyi chos rnams mi ’pho ba daṅ, mi skye ba daṅ, mi gnas par rtogs pa ni dus gsum la mkhas pa’o źes bstan par bźed nas gźan yaṅ ’das pa’i dus na źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs so. ’das pa’i dus na zad pa’i chos rnams phyi ma’i mthar ’phos par mi lta źes bya ba ni chos sṅa ma ’das pa rnams ṅo bo ñid kyis ’das te, phyi ma daṅ mtshams mi sbyor bar rtogs kyaṅ źes bya ba’i don to; dge ba’i mṅon par ’du byed pa la brtson ’grus kyaṅ mi gtoṅ stea źes bya ba ni de ltar don dam par mi ’pho yaṅ, las daṅ ’bras bu la yid ches te, sṅa ma’i rgyus phyi ma’i ’bras bu sgrub par śes na dge ba spyod pa’i brtson ’grus kyaṅ mi gtoṅ źes bya ba’i don to; mi dge ba mṅon par ’du mi byed ces bya ba ni de ltar dṅos po med de sṅa ma daṅ phyi mar mi ’pho bas mi dge ba’i las kyi rnam par smin pa med par yaṅ mi bltab ste, de’i phyir mi dge ba mṅon par ’du mi byed do.
gaṅ ma ’oṅs pa’i dus kyi chos rnams mi skye mi ’byuṅ bar rtog ciṅ, byaṅ chub tu bsṅo ba’i brtson ’grus kyaṅ mi ’dor źes bya ba ni don dam par na ma ’oṅs pa’i dus na thob par bya ba’i byaṅ chub ñid mi skye mi ’byuṅ bar rtogs kyaṅ, kun rdzob tu med par mi lta bas byaṅ chub tu bsṅo ba’i brtson ’grus kyaṅ mi gtoṅ ṅo.
da ltar byuṅ ba’i dus na chos rnams ’dug pa med ciṅ mi gnas par rtog ste, byaṅ chub sems dpa’ lhag pa’i bsam pa rab tu brtan pa ni byaṅ chub kyi sems kyaṅ mi brjed de źes bya ba ni don dam par da ltar byuṅ ba’i chos rnams mi gnas pas byaṅ chub kyi sems ñid kyaṅ mi gnas te; byaṅ chub kyi sems la rmoṅs pa’am, brjed par ’gyur ba’i rigs na byaṅ chub sems dpa’ lhag pa’i bsam pa rab tu brtan pa ni spyod lam thams cad du byaṅ chub kyi sems kyaṅ mi brjed do źes bya ba’i don to.


gźan yaṅ gaṅ ’das pa, de ni zad pa’o;ma ’oṅs pa, de ni ma phyin pa’o; da ltar byuṅ ba, de ni gnas pa med pa’o. gaṅ de ltar sems daṅ sems las byuṅ ba skyes pa daṅ, źig pa daṅ, źu ba rnams la rtog ciṅ byaṅ chub sgrub pa’i dge ba’i rtsa ba rnams kyaṅ yaṅ dag par sgrub pa, ’di ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i dus gsum la mkhas pa źes bya’o.

punar aparaṃ yad atītaṃ tad kṣīṇam, yad anāgataṃ tad asaṃprāptaṃ, yat pratyutpannaṃ tasya sthitir nāsti,ya evaṃ cittacaittasikān utpannān bhagnavilīnān pratyavekṣamāṇo ’pi bodhisādhakāni kuśalamūlāni ca samudānayatīdam ucyate bodhisattvasya tryadhvakauśalyam.

Further, the past has perished, the future is not reached, and the present does not abide,when one considers thought and the contents of thought thus as born, destroyed and melted away, but still acquires the roots of good that bring awakening about, this is called the bodhisattva’s skill with the three times.

dus gsum la mkhas pa’i rnam graṅs gźan yaṅ bstan par bźed nas gźan yaṅ gaṅ ’das pa, de ni zad pa’o źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs te, ’das pa’i chos rnams ni rgyu daṅ ’bras bu bcas te, ’gags pas na zad pa źes bya’o, ma ’oṅs pa’i chos rnams ni rgyu daṅ ’bras bu bcas te ma phyin pas na ma phyin pa’o, da ltar byuṅ ba’i chos rnams ni rgyus ’bras bu bskyed nas de ma thag tu ’gags pas na gnas pa med pa’o. de ltar dus gsum gyi mtshan ñid bstan nas, de la mkhas pa bstan pa’i phyir gaṅ de ltar sems daṅ sems las byuṅ ba źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs so, rtog ciṅ źes bya ba’i sgra re re daṅ sbyar te, sems daṅ sems las byuṅ ba skyes pa rnams la rtog pa daṅ, sems daṅ sems las byuṅ ba źig pa rnams la rtog pa daṅ, sems daṅ sems las byuṅ ba źu ba rnams la rtog ces bya bar sbyar ro; de la da ltar gyi sems daṅ sems las byuṅ ba rnams rgyus ’bras bu bskyed de, bskyed ma thag tu rgyu daṅ ’bras bu bcas te, ’gags pas dṅos po med do źes rtog pa ni sems daṅ sems las byuṅ ba skyes pa rnams la rtog pa źes bya’o; ’das pa’i sems daṅ sems las byuṅ ba rnams ni rgyu daṅ bcas te ’bras bu ’gags pas dṅos po med do źes rtog pa ni sems daṅ sems las byuṅ ba’i źig pa rnams la rtog pa źes sbyar ro; ma ’oṅs pa’i sems daṅ sems las byuṅ bas ni rgyu daṅ bcas te ’bras bu ma skyes pas na dṅos po med do źes rtog pa ni źu ba rnams la rtog pa źes bya’o. de ltar dus gsum gyi dṅos po rnams yaṅ dag par na dṅos po med pas dge ba’i tshogs rnams kyaṅ dṅos po med pa’i phyir tshogs gñis kyaṅ mi ’grub pa ma sñam pa la byaṅ chub sgrub pa’i dge ba’i rtsa ba rnams kyaṅ yaṅ dag par sgrub pa źes bya bar smos te, tshogs gaṅ gis byaṅ chub sgrub par byed pa’i tshogs kyi mtshan ñid dge ba’i rtsa ba ni byaṅ chub sgrub pa’i dge ba’i rtsa ba źes bya ste, de yaṅ bsod nams daṅ ye śes kyi tshogs kyi mtshan ñid do, de ni ’di skad du don dam pas dus gsum gyi dṅos po rnams kyaṅ raṅ bźin med mod kyi, kun rdzob tu ji lta ji ltar las byas pa de lta de ltar ’bras bu med pa ma yin te, de bas na bla na med pa’i byaṅ chub thob par byed pa’i rgyu bsod nams daṅ ye śes kyi tshogs kyaṅ sgrub par byed ces bya bar ston to.
Cf. Kpv. 97-98: yadi tāvad atītaṃ cittaṃ tat kṣīṇaṃ, yād anāgataṃ cittaṃ tad asaṃprāptaḥ, atha pratyutpannasya cittasya sthitir nāsti. ... cittaṃ hi kāśyapa nadīsrotasadṛśaṃm anavasthitam utpannaṃ bhagnavilīna. Cf. also supra, ṭ. fol. 79a2 and mūla p. 487.


gźan yaṅ gaṅ mṅon par śes pa la mkhas pas ’das pa’i dus rjes su dran te, sṅon dge ba’i rtsa ba bskyed pa rnams rjes su dran nas byaṅ chub tu yoṅs su sṅo ba daṅ;gaṅ ma ’oṅs pa’i dus na dge ba’i sems bskyed pa rnams rab tu śes pa daṅ de la smon pa yoṅs su rdzogs par byed pa daṅ;gaṅ da ltar byuṅ ba’i dus na dge ba’i rtsa ba skyes śiṅ byuṅ ba rnams yid la byed ciṅ, gnas par byed de, byaṅ chub tu yoṅs su sṅo ba;’di ni dus gsum la mkhas pa źes bya’o.

punar aparaṃ yābhijñākauśalyenātītasya ’dhvano ’nusmṛtiḥ, pūrvāvaropitān kuśalamūlān anusmṛtya ca bodhipariṇāmanā;yad anāgate ’dhvani kuśalānāṃ cittotpādānāṃ prajñānaṃ tatra praṇidhānaparipūrir;yaḥ pratyutpanne ’dhvany utpannotpannānāṃ kuśalamūlānāṃ manasikāraḥ sthitikāro bodhipariṇāmanā;idam ucyate tryadhvakauśalyam.

Further, remembering the past by means of skill in supernormal knowledge, and, having remembered roots of the good planted in the past, transforming them into awakening;knowledge of future productions of good thoughts and then fulfilling one’s vows;applying mental effort and making roots of the good stay as they arise in the present, transforming them into awakening;this is skill with the three times.

gźan yaṅ mṅon par śes pa lṅa daṅ ldan pas dus gsum gyi dṅos po rnams khoṅ du chud ciṅ dran te, bdag gi dge ba’i rtsa ba chud mi za bar byed pa ni dus gsum la mkhas pa’o źes bstan par bźed nas gźan yaṅ gaṅ mṅon par śes pa la mkhas pa źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs so. mṅon par śes pa daṅ ldan pa ni mṅon par śes pa la mkhas pa’am, yaṅ na mṅon par śes pas dṅos po rnams śes śiṅ dran te, dge ba’i rtsa ba byas pa rnams chud mi gson pa’i mṅon par śes pa ’das pa’i dus rjes su dran te źes bya ba ni sṅon gyi gnas rjes su dran pa’i mṅon par śes pas ’das pa’i dus na mi dge ba ci byas pa daṅ, dge ba ci byas pa ma brjed pa ni ’das pa’i dus dran pa’o; de ltar dran pa yaṅ ma zad kyi sṅon dge ba’i rtsa ba bskyed pa rnams rjes su dran nas byaṅ chub tu yoṅs su sṅo bar byed pa ni ’das pa’i dus la mkhas pa źes bya’o.
gaṅ ma ’oṅs pa’i dus na dge ba’i sems bskyed pa rnams rab tu śes pa daṅ źes bya ba ni ’dir yaṅ sṅon gyi gnas rjes su dran pa’i mṅon par śes pa daṅ, ’chi ’pho daṅ skye ba śes pa’i mṅon par śes pas ma ’oṅs pa’i dus na dge ba’i sems skye bar ’gyur ba rnams śes śiṅ mthoṅ źes bya bar sbyar te, ma ’oṅs pa na byaṅ chub tu sems bskyed nas ’dod ma chags pa daṅ, źe mi sdaṅ ba daṅ, gti mi mug pa’i dge ba’i rtsa ba’i rgyu las sbyin pa daṅ, tshul khrims la sogs pa dge ba rnams gdon mi za bar skye bar śes pa ni ma ’oṅs pa’i dge ba’i sems skyed pa rnams rab tu śes pa źes bya’o; de ltar śes nas kyaṅ da lta ñid kyi dus na dge ba de dag yoṅs su rdzogs te, bla na med pa’i byaṅ chub kyi tshogs su gyur cig par sems la mṅon par ’du byed ciṅ re ba ni de la smon pa yoṅs su rdzogs par byed pa’o.
da ltar byuṅ ba’i dus la mkhas pa yaṅ rnam pa gsum ste, a) phyin ci ma log par byed pa daṅ, b) mi ñams par byed pa daṅ, c) ’bras bu gźan du mi ’gyur bar byed pa ste, de la a) gaṅ da ltar byuṅ ba’i dus la dge ba’i rtsa ba skyes śiṅ byuṅ ba rnams yid la byed ciṅ źes bya bas phyin ci ma log par byed pa bstan te, dge ba’i rtsa ba skyes śiṅ byuṅ ba la phyin ci ma log par yaṅ daṅ yaṅ yid la byed pa’i phyir ro; b) gnas par byed ces bya ba ni mi ñams par byed pa bstan te, dge ba’i rtsa ba skyes śiṅ byuṅ ba goṅ nas goṅ du khyad par du ’bogs par byed pa’i phyir ro; c) byaṅ chub tu yoṅs su bsṅo ba źes bya bas ’bras bu gźan du mi ’gyur bar byed pa bstan te, da ltar byuṅ ba’i dus su dge ba byas te gnas par gyur pa rnams lha daṅ klu la sogs pa’i ’bras bu thob par mi bsṅo’i, bla na med pa’i byaṅ chub thob par bsṅo ba’i phyir ro.


gźan yaṅ gaṅ sems can thams cad yoṅs su smin par bya ba’i phyir ’das pa’i bsod nams kyi tshogs dran nas, sems can gaṅ dag ji ltar smin par bya ba, de dag thams cad de bźin du yoṅs su smin par byed de;ma ’oṅs pa’i dus kyi sems can gaṅ dag saṅs rgyas mñes par bya bas yoṅs su smin par bya ba, de dag thams cad de bźin du yoṅs su smin par byed pa daṅ;da ltar byuṅ ba’i sems can gaṅ dag chos bstan pa’am, rdzu ’phrul gyi cho ’phrul gyis yoṅs su smin par bya ba, de dag thams cad kyaṅ de bźin du yoṅs su smin par byed de;

punar aparaṃ yaḥ sarvasattvānāṃ paripākārtham atītapuṇyasaṃbhāram anusmṛtya ye sattvā yathā paripācayitavyās tān sarvān tathā paripācayati;anāgate ’dhvani ye sattvā buddhārāgaṇena paripācayitavyās tān sarvān tathā paripācayati;pratyutpannāḥ ye sattvā dharmadeśanārddhiprātihāryeṇa paripācayitavyās tān sarvān tathā paripācayati.

(p. 78) Further, he matures living beings the way they are to be matured, remembering the acquisition of merit in the past for the sake of maturing all living beings;he matures accordingly all living beings in the future who are to be matured by paying respect to the Buddhas;and he matures all those living beings of the present who are to be matured by the miracles of teaching religion and magic.

dus gsum gyi bsod nams kyi tshogs ci byas pas, sems can yoṅs su smin par byed pa ni dus gsum la mkhas pa yin no źes bstan par bźed nas gźan yaṅ gaṅ sems can thams cad yoṅs su smin par bya ba’i phyir źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs so; sems can thams cad ces bya bas ni rigs lṅa daṅ ldan pa’i gaṅ zag rnams bsdus te, de dag so so’i theg pa daṅ, lha daṅ mi’i bde ’gror ’gog pa ni yoṅs su smin par bya ba ste, phyir źes bya ba ni de’i ched du’o; ’das pa’i bsod nams kyi tshogs dran nas źes bya ba ni bdag gi sṅon dge ba ’di daṅ ’di byas so źes sbyin pa daṅ tshul khrims la sogs pa bsod nams kyi tshogs ci byas pa ma brjed pa ni dran pa’o; sems can gaṅ dag ji lta bur yoṅs su smin par bya ba de dag thams cad de bźin du yoṅs su smin par byed ces bya bas sṅon byas pa’i bsod nams de dag dran pa tsam du ma zad kyi, bsod nams de dag gi mthus sems can ji sñed cig ji ltar smin par bya ba de dag thams cad de bźin du smin par byed ces bya ba’i tha tshig go.
ma ’oṅs pa’i dus kyi sems can gaṅ dag saṅs rgyas mñes par bya bas yoṅs su smin par bya ba, de dag thams cad de bźin du yoṅs su smin par byed ces bya ba ni saṅs rgyas mñes par bya ba’i sgo nas ma ’oṅs pa’i sems can yoṅs su smin par bya ba ni ma ’oṅs pa’i dus kyi sems can gaṅ dag saṅs rgyas mñes par bya bas yoṅs su smin par bya ba źes bya ste, de ni ’di skad du de bźin gśegs pa de dag gi druṅ du soṅ nas dam pa’i chos mñan pa daṅ, bsam pa daṅ, bsgom pa la sogs pa sgrub pa’i mchod pa daṅ mñes par byas nas, de la brten te sems can ji sñed cig yod pa ji ltar yoṅs su smin par bya ba, de sñed cig de bźin yoṅs su smin par byed ces bya ba ston to.
da ltar byuṅ ba’i sems can rnams la chos bstan pa’am, rdzu ’phrul gyi cho ’phrul gyis yoṅs su smin par bya ba de dag thams cad kyaṅ de bźin du yoṅs su smin par byed de źes bya ba la, cho ’phrul gyi sgra gñi ga daṅ sbyar te, a) chos bstan pa’i cho ’phrul daṅ b) rdzu ’phrul gyi cho ’phrul źes bya bar sbyar ro.
The two kinds of miracles are explained in ṭ. fol.145b4-146a4, dharmadeśanaprātihārya divided into ādeśanāprātihārya and anuśāsanīprātihārya, and ṛddhiprātihārya divided into five:
a) de la chos bstan pa’i cho ’phrul yaṅ rnam pa gñis te, 1) kun brjod pa’i cho ’phrul daṅ, 2) rjes su bstan pa’i cho ’phrul lo. de la 1) kun brjod pa’i cho ’phrul ni sems can rnams kyi khams daṅ raṅ bźin daṅ bag la ñal rnams la btags nas de dag la de bźin du brjod pa’o. 2) rjes su bstan pa’i cho ’phrul ni de ltar gdul bya de dag brda sprad nas bstan pa la btsud de, ’di ni sdug bsṅal gyi bden pa, ’di ni kun ’byuṅ gi bden pa, ’di ni ’gog pa’i bden pa, ’di ni lam gyi bden pa’o źes bden pa bźi la sogs pa ’chad pa’o.
b) rdzu ’phrul gyi cho ’phrul ni dbaṅ lṅa daṅ ldan pa ste, 1) gcig tu gyur nas maṅ por ’gyur ba daṅ, maṅ po gyur nas gcig tu ’gyur ba daṅ, snaṅ ba daṅ mi snaṅ ba la dbaṅ bas sprul pa la dbaṅ ba daṅ, 2) rtsig pa la yaṅ thad kar ’gro, rab la yaṅ thad kar ’gro ba la sogs pa la dbaṅ bas ’gro ba la dbaṅ ba daṅ, 3) nam mkha’ la mṅon du ’phags te spyod lam rnam bźi byed pa daṅ, chu la yaṅ mi nub par ’gro ste, sa chen po la bya ba bźin byed pa la dbaṅ bas gnas pa la dbaṅ ba daṅ, 4) mi’i ’gro ba ’di na gnas bźin du lha’i ’gro bar gtogs pa, zla ba daṅ ñi ma ’di gñis ’di ltar rdzu ’phrul che ba, ’di ltar mthu che ba ’di ltar gzi brjid che ba la’aṅ lag pas ’dzin ciṅ kun tu ñug par byed pas lus la dbaṅ ba daṅ, 5) tshaṅs pa’i ’jig rten gyi bar du sems can rnams la lus kyi dbaṅ sgyur bas khams khyad par can la dbaṅ ba ste, de ltar dbaṅ lṅa daṅ ldan pas gdul bya’i sems can ’dun par byed pa ni rdzu ’phrul gyi cho ’phrul lo.
da ltar gyi sems can kha cig chos bstan pa’i cho ’phrul gyis yoṅs su smin par bya ba yin, sems can kha cig rdzu ’phrul gyi cho ’phrul gyis yoṅs su smin par bya ba yin te, de la byaṅ chub sems dpa’i cho ’phrul gaṅ gis sems can gaṅ yoṅs su smin par bya ba cho ’phrul des sems can de yoṅs su smin par byed do.
de bas na sems can yoṅs su smin par bya ba de dag thams cad kyaṅ de bźin du yoṅs su smin par byed do źes gsuṅs so.
Cf. Kośa vii, 47-8, Msa v, 4-5; the divisions of ṛddhiprātihārya are similarly described in Dbh 3M p. 34-5; Śbh p. 6311-413; other references in Edg. s. v. prātihārya.


gaṅ dus gsum ’di dag la bdag gi don daṅ, gźan gyi don daṅ, byaṅ chub kyi don de dag ma chags pas yoṅs su rdzogs par byed pa, ’di ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i dus gsum la mkhas pa źes bya’o.

ya eteṣu tryadhvasv ātmarthapararthabodhyartham asaktataḥ paripūrayati, idam ucyate bodhisattvasya tryadhvakauśalyam.

[To summarize], when he in these three times fulfils his own aims, others’ aims and the aim of awakening by way of non-attachment [that is, by way of threefold purity (trimaṇḍalapariśuddhinayena), consisting in not grasping for substance (bhāva) in any of the three aspects, to wit one’s own aims, others’ aims and the aim of awakening], it is called the bodhisattva’s skill with the three times.

146a4-147a2: dus gsum la mkhas pa goṅ du bśad pa rnams kyi don bsdus te, bstan par bźed nas gaṅ dus gsum ’di dag la źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs te, gaṅ źes bya ba ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’ daṅ sbyar te, byaṅ chub sems dpa’ gaṅ źes bya ba’i don to, dus gsum ’di dag ces bya ba ni goṅ du bśad pa’i ’das pa daṅ, ma ’oṅs pa daṅ, da ltar gyi dus dag la’o, ma chags pas yoṅs su rdzogs par byed ces bya ba’i tshig goṅ ma’i tshig gsum char daṅ yaṅ sbyar te, bdag gi don la ma chags pas yoṅs su rdzogs par byed pa daṅ gźan gyi don la ma chags pas yoṅs su rdzogs par byed pa daṅ, byaṅ chub kyi don la ma chags pas yoṅs su rdzogs par byed ces bya bar sbyar ro.
de la bdag yoṅs su smin par ’gyur ba’am, bdag la phan par ’gyur ba’i don ni bdag gi don te, de yaṅ spaṅs pa daṅ sgrub pa’i mtshan ñid rnam pa gñis so.
de la spaṅ ba yaṅ rnam pa gsum ste, 1) ñon moṅs pa spaṅ ba daṅ, 2) sdug bsṅal spaṅ ba daṅ, 3. śin tu spaṅ ba’o. de la 1) ñon moṅs pa spaṅ ba ni ’jig rten gyi lam sa goṅ ma la źi bar lta źiṅ, sa ’og ma la skyon du lta bas cuṅ zad med pa’i skye mched man chad kyis ñon moṅs pa thaṅ cig rtse bcil ba daṅ, ’jig rten las ’das pa mthoṅ ba daṅ bsgom pa’i lam gyis ’dod chags la sogs pa ñon moṅs pa’i bag chags kyaṅ ma lus par bton pa’o. de la 2) sdug bsṅal spaṅ ba ni ṅan soṅ gsum du skye ba’i sdug bsṅal daṅ khams gsum du skye ba’i sdug bsṅal ma lus par spaṅs pa’o. 3) śin tu spaṅ ba ni ñon moṅs pa daṅ sdug bsṅal spaṅs pa de dag lan cig spaṅs nas phyis ci nas kyaṅ de’i sems kyi rgyud la mi skye bar byed pa’o.
de la sgrub pa la yaṅ rnam pa gñis te, 1) ’jig rten gyi bde ba sgrub pa daṅ, 2) ’jig rten las ’das pa’i bde ba sgrub pa’o. 1) ’jig rten gyi bde ba sgrub pa ni ji srid du ’jig rten las ’das pa’i bde ba ma thob kyi bar du lha daṅ mi’i bde ’gror skye bar byed pa’o. 2) ’jig rten las ’das pa’i bde ba yaṅ rnam pa gñis te, a) bla na yod pa daṅ, b) bla na med pa’o. de la a) bla na yod pa ni ñan thos daṅ raṅ saṅs rgyas kyi theg pa la brten nas phuṅ po lhag ma daṅ bcas pa daṅ phuṅ po lhag ma yaṅ ma lus pa spaṅs pa’i mya ṅan las ’das pa ’thob pa’o. b) bla na med pa ni theg pa chen po la brten nas bdag daṅ gźan gyi don phun sum tshogs pa’i rten du gyur pa ni mi gnas pa’i mya ṅan las ’das pa ’thob pa’o.
sems can gźan yoṅs su smin par byas pa’am gźan la phan par byas pa’i don ni gźan gyi don te, de yaṅ spaṅ ba daṅ sgrub pa la bkod pa goṅ ma bźin du rnam pa gñis su rig par bya’o.
byaṅ chub ñid don dam pas na byaṅ chub kyi don to. byaṅ chub kyi sgras ’dir byaṅ chub rnam pa gsum la bya bar rig par bya ste, de dag ni ’phags pa’i ’bras bu yin pa’i phyir ro. yaṅ na, stobs daṅ mi ’jigs pa daṅ ma ’dres pa la sogs pa saṅs rgyas kyi chos rnams yoṅs su smin par bya ba’i phyir ’phags pa’i lam sgom par byed pa ni byaṅ chub kyi don ces bya’o.
ma chags pas yoṅs su rdzogs par byed ces bya ba ni bdag daṅ gźan daṅ byaṅ chub kyi don rnam pa gsum char la yaṅ dṅos por ’dzin pa med ciṅ, ’khor gsum yoṅs su dag pa’i tshul gyis mthar phyin par byed pa de ni źes bya ba’i don to.


de la byaṅ chub sems dpa’i theg pa thams cad la mkhas pa gaṅ źe na?

tatra katamad bodhisattvasya sarvayānakauśalyam?

7) What then is the bodhisattva’s skill with all the ways?


gsum po ’di dag ni theg pa ste ṅes par ’byin pa’o. gsum po gaṅ źe na? ’di lta ste: a) ñan thos kyi theg pa daṅ, b) raṅ saṅs rgyas kyi theg pa daṅ, c) theg pa chen po’o.

trīnīmāni yānāni nairyāṇikāni; katamat trayam? yānīmāni śrāvakayānaṃ pratyekabuddhayānaṃ mahāyānam.

These three ways are conducive to deliverance. Which three? The way of disciples, the way of isolated buddhas and the great way.


gźan yaṅ theg pa gñis te. gñis gaṅ źe na? lha’i theg pa daṅ mi’i theg pa’o.

punar aparaṃ yānadvayam. katamad dvayam? devayānaṃ manuṣyayānaṃ ca.

Further, the ways are two. Which two? The way of the gods and the way of men.

dus gsum la mkhas pa bśad pa’i ’og tu theg pa kun la mkhas pa bstan pas, ji ltar bstan pa bźin du bśad par bźed nas de la byaṅ chub sems dpa’i theg pa thams cad la mkhas pa gaṅ źe na źes dris te, theg pa thams cad la mkhas pa ni theg pa kun la mkhas pa ste, theg pa thams cad kyi rgyu daṅ raṅ bźin daṅ ’bras bu phyin ci ma log par rtogs pa’o. de la theg pa thams cad ni bsdus na rnam pa gñis te, a) ’jig rten las ’das pa’i theg pa daṅ, b) ’jig rten gyi theg pa’o.
a) ’jig rten las ’das pa’i theg pa bstan par bźed nas gsum po ’di dag ni theg pa ste ṅes par ’byin pa’o źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs te, ñan thos daṅ, raṅ saṅs rgyas daṅ, byaṅ chub sems dpa’i theg pa ’di gsum ni ’jig rten las ’das pa’i theg pa źes bya ste, ci’i phyir źe na? ’khor ba las ’byin par byed pa’i phyir ro.
b) The ways of gods and men, being laukika, as different from the three lokottara, mentioned before but leading to them, are explained in detail in ṭ. fol. 147a5-b5: ’jig rten gyi theg pa bstan par bźed nas gźan yaṅ theg pa gñis te, gñis gaṅ źe na? lha’i theg pa daṅ mi’i theg pa’o źes bya ba gsuṅs pa’o. de la lha rnams kyi theg pa yin pas na lha’i theg pa daṅ, mi rnams kyi theg pa yin pas na mi’i theg pa’am lhar ’gyur ba’i theg pa daṅ mi ’gyur ba’i theg pa ni lha’i theg pa daṅ daṅ mi’i theg pa źes bya’o.
de la lha’i sgras ni rgyal chen bźi la sogs pa ’dod pa’i khams lha drug daṅ, gzugs kyi khams kyi lha daṅ, nam mkha’ mtha’ yas la sogs pa gzugs med pa’i khams kyi lha rnams bsdu’o. theg pa’i sgras ni bsod nams su ñe bar ’gro ba’i ’du byed srog gcod pa las phyir log pa la sogs pa dge ba bcu’i las kyi lam daṅ, rtog pa daṅ bcas dpyod pa daṅ bcas pa źes bya ba la sogs pa zag pa daṅ bcas pa’i gzugs kyi khams kyi bsam gtan bźi daṅ, nam mkha’ mtha’ yas so źes bya ba la sogs pa gzugs med pa’i khams kyi sñoms par ’jug pa bźi mi g-yo ba ñe bar ’gro ba’i mtshan ñid rnams bsdus te ’du byed de gñis kyis lha’i gnas de dag thob par byed ciṅ der ’gro bas na lha’i theg pa źes bya’o.
mi’i sgras ni gliṅ bźi na gnas pa’i skyes pa daṅ bud med ces bya ba la sogs pa bsdus te, theg pa’i sgras ni dge ba bcu’i las kyi raṅ bźin bsod nams su ñe bar ’gro ba’i ’du byed la bya’o. kha cig na re: bsod nams ma yin par ñe bar ’gro ba srog gcod pa la sogs pa mi dge ba’i las kyi lam bcu po rnams kyis kyaṅ ṅan soṅ gsum du ’gro źiṅ skye bar byed pas ’dis ’gro ba daṅ ’dir ’gro ba źes bya la sogs pa theg par bstan pa’i mtshan ñid yod na ’dir ’jig rten pa’i theg pa’i naṅ du ṅan soṅ gsum rnams ci’i phyir theg pa ma bsdus śe na? theg pa źes bya ba’i don ni rgyus bde ba skyed par byed pa daṅ, ’bras bu’i tshe ’phags pa’i bden pa rtogs pa’i snod du ruṅ ba la bya ste, mi dge ba bcu’i las kyi lam rnams la ’dis ’gro ba daṅ ’dir ’gro ba źes bya ba bstan du ruṅ yaṅ mi dge ba’i las kyi lam gyi rgyu ñid sdug bsṅal skyed par byed pa daṅ ’bras bu’i tshe na yaṅ ’phags pa’i bden pa rtogs pa’i snod du mi ruṅ bas na theg pa źes mi bya’o.


de la byaṅ chub sems dpa’i ñan thos kyi theg pa la mkhas pa gaṅ źe na?

tatra katamad bodhisattvasya śrāvakayānakauśalyam? p. 79

What then is the bodhisattva’s skill with the way of disciples? (p. 79)

ñan thos kyi theg pa la mkhas pa bstan par bźed nas de la byaṅ chub sems dpa’i ñan thos kyi theg pa la mkhas pa gaṅ źe na źes dris pa la sogs pa’o, byaṅ chub sems dpa’ rnams kyis mkhas par bya ba’i ñan thos kyi theg pa ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i ñan thos kyi theg pa la mkhas pa ste, ñan thos kyi theg pa gaṅ źe na źes bya ba’i tha tshig go.
’dis ’gro bas na theg pa ste, gaṅ gis ’gro źe na? tshul khrims kyi phuṅ po la sogs pas ’gro bas theg pa’i sgra ni bslab pa gsum la bya’o. yaṅ na, ’dir ’gro bas na theg pa ste, des ni rnam par grol ba daṅ rnam par grol ba’i ye śes mthoṅ ba’i phuṅ po la theg pa źes bya bar rig par bya’o – rec: anena gamyata iti yānam, kena gamyate / śīlaskandhādibhir gamyata iti yānaśabdaḥ śikṣātraye / punar api idaṃ gamyata iti yānam, tena vimuktivimuktijñānadarśanaskandhe yānaṃ veditavyam /
theg pa de’i mtshan ñid daṅ rgyu la sogs pa phyin ci ma log par rtogs pa ni ñan thos kyi theg pa la mkhas pa ste, de’aṅ ’og nas ’chad do. de la ñan thos kyi theg pa yaṅ rnam pa drug tu rig par bya ste, 1) rten daṅ, 2) dmigs pa daṅ, 3) rgyu daṅ, 4) sgrub pa daṅ, 5) ’bras bu daṅ, 6) de rab tu rig pa’o.


saṅs rgyas byuṅ ba med par ñan thos kyi theg pa yaṅ med do.

buddhānām anutpāde śrāvakayānam ca nāsti.

[1. Its basis (āśraya):] When the Buddhas are not born there is no way of disciples.

saṅs rgyas byuṅ ba med par ñan thos kyi theg pa yaṅ med do źes bya ba ni dga’ ldan gyi pho braṅ nas byaṅ chub sems dpa’ ’chi ’pho ba bstan te, yum gyi lhums su bltams pa daṅ, btsas pa daṅ, gźon nu la sogs pa’i rim pas sems can gyi don du thabs kyi spyod pa rnam pa sna tshogs mdzad nas khab nas byuṅ ste, dka’ bar spyad pa la sogs pas bstan nas mṅon par saṅs rgyas pa ni saṅs rgyas ’byuṅ ba źes bya ste, saṅs rgyas ’byuṅ ba la brten pa med par ñan thos kyi theg pa ’byuṅ ba yaṅ med do źes bya ba’i don to. ’dis ni rten (1, cf. fol. 148a1) bstan pa yin no.


de ci’i phyir źe na? ñan thos rnams kyi yaṅ dag par lta ba ni pha rol gyi sgra’i rjes su ’gro ba’o.

tat kasya hetoḥ? śrāvakānāṃ samyagdṛṣṭiḥ parato ghoṣānvayā.

[2. Its scope (ālambana):] Why? The right view of the disciples [the view of no self in the personality (pudgalanairātmya) ] is the consequence of the words of others [taught by a Buddha, teacher or preceptor (buddhâcāryôpādhyāya) ].

de ci’i phyir źe na źes bya ba ni rgyu ’dri ba ste, saṅs rgyas ’byuṅ ba med par ñan thos kyi theg pa yaṅ ci’i phyir med ce na źes bya ba’i tha tshig go, de’i lan du ñan thos rnams kyi yaṅ dag par lta ba ni pha rol gyi sgra’i rjes su ’gro ba źes bya ba gsuṅs te, gaṅ chos thams cad la gaṅ zag gi dṅos po med de, gaṅ zag la bdag med pa yaṅ dag pa’i ye śes kyis khoṅ du chud pa ni ñan thos rnams kyi yaṅ dag par lta ba’o; yaṅ dag pa’i lta ba de yaṅ saṅs rgyas sam, mkhan po’am, slob dpon gyis bśad pa’i sgra mñan nas gaṅ zag la bdag med par dmigs par byed pas na pha rol gyi sgra’i rjes su ’gro ba źes bya ste. ’dis ni dmigs par smra ba (2, cf. fol. 148a1) yin no.


de la ñan pa ni gaṅ ’di tshul khrims sdom pa ste, ji ltar bslab pa bcas pa’i rjes su ’jug pa ni tshul khrims kyi phuṅ po yoṅs su rdzogs par ’gyur te;

tatra śravaṇaṃ yo ’yaṃ śīlasaṃvaraḥ, yathā śikṣāprajñaptānuvartakaḥ śīlaskandhaḥ paripūryate.

[3. Its cause (hetu):] There, hearing is concerned with the vow of moral discipline, so that the mass of moral discipline – which is following what the rules declare – is fulfilled.

pha rol gyis bstan pa’i sgra mñan nas źes bśad na ñan pa ni gaṅ źe na? de’i phyir de la ñan pa ni gaṅ ’di’i tshul khrims sdom pa źes bya ba gsuṅs te, ñon moṅs pa’i gduṅ ba sel ciṅ sim par byed pas tshul khrims te, des lus daṅ ṅag gi ñes pa daṅ kha na ma tho ba rnams mi ’byuṅ bar sdom par byed pas na tshul khrims ñid sdom pa ste, de la ñan pa ni de yin no źes bya ba’i don to. ji ltar bslab pa bcas pa’i rjes su ’jug pa ni źes bya ba la, de ltar tshul khrims kyi sdom pa mñan nas ji ltar bcom ldan ’das kyis pham pa bźi daṅ, dge ’dun lhag ma bcu gsum la sogs pa’i tshul khrims ñis brgya lṅa bcu bcas pa bźin du kha na ma tho ba phra rab tsam yaṅ med par slob ciṅ byed pa ni ji ltar bslab pa bcas pa’i rjes su ’jug pa źes bya ste, rgyu des tshul khrims kyi phuṅ po rdzogs par ’gyur bas na ’dis ni rgyu (3, cf. fol. 148a1) smras pa yin no.
ṭ. fol. 148b2: de la sgrub pa (4, cf. fol. 148a1) yaṅ rnam pa gsum ste, 1) tiṅ ṅe ’dzin gyi gnas rab tu sgrub pa daṅ, 2) ye śes kyi rten rab tu sgrub pa daṅ, 3) bya ba byas pa rab tu sgrub pa’o.
tshul khrims kyi phuṅ po rab tu rdzogs par ’gyur te źes bya ba la tshul khrims kyi sgras yan lag drug daṅ ldan pa’i tshul khrims la bya ste, yan lag drug po gaṅ źe na? 1) tshul khrims daṅ ldan par gnas pa źes yan lag daṅ po daṅ, 2) so sor thar pa’i sdom pas bsdams pa źes yan lag gñis pa daṅ, 3) cho ga phun sum tshogs pa źes yan lag gsum pa daṅ, 4) spyod yul phun sum tshogs pa źes yan lag bźi pa daṅ, 5) kha na ma tho ba phra rab tsam dag la yaṅ ’jigs par lta źes yan lag lṅa pa daṅ, 6) bslab pa’i gźi rnams yaṅ dag par blaṅs nas slob ces yan lag drug pa’o.
1) ji ltar tshul khrims daṅ ldan pa yin źe na? yaṅ dag par blaṅs pa’i bslab pa’i gźi rnams la lus kyi las kyi mtha’ ma log pa daṅ, ṅag gi las kyi mtha’ ma log par gyur ciṅ, ma ñams par byed pa daṅ, skyon med par byed pa’o – kathaṃ śīlavān viharati / yathā samātteṣu śi(3)kṣāpadeṣu avipannakāyakarmāntaś ca bhavaty avipannavākkarmāntaś ca / akhaṇḍacārī achidracārī ... quoted from Śbh fol. 2A12-3, S p. 3710-13, D fol. 16a2-3.
2) ji ltar so sor thar pa’i sdom pas bsdams pa yin źe na? dge sloṅ pha daṅ, dge sloṅ ma daṅ, dge bsñen pha daṅ, dge bsñen ma daṅ, dge slob ma daṅ, dge tshul pa daṅ, dge tshul ma’i tshul khrims rnams la so sor thar pa’i sdom pa źes bya ste, de dag kyaṅ sde tha dad par dbye bas sdom pa maṅ du ’gyur med kyi, ’di’i skabs su dge sloṅ gi sdom pa la dgoṅs nas so sor thar pa’i sdom pas bsdams pa źes gsuṅs so – Śbh fol. 2A13-4, S p. 3714-381, D fol. 16a3-4: kathaṃ prātimokṣasamvarasaṃvṛto bhavati / saptanairyāṇikaṃ śīlaṃ prātimokṣasamvara ity ucyate / ta ete nikāyabhedena bahavaḥ samvarā bhavanti / asmiṃs tv arthe bhikṣusamvaram adhiṣṭhāyāha /(4) prātimokṣasamvarasaṃvṛtaḥ /
3) ji ltar cho ga phun sum tshogs pa yin źe na? de ltar spyod lam mam, ’phral gyi bya ba’am, dge ba’i phyogs la rab tu sbyor ba yaṅ ruṅ ste, bya ba thams cad la ’jig rten gyi rjes su ’jug ciṅ ’jig rten gyis dpyas par mi ’gyur ba daṅ, ’dul ba’i rjes su ’jug ciṅ ’dul ba daṅ ’gal bar mi byed pa’o – Śbh fol. 2A14, S p. 382-5, D fol. 16a4-5: katham ācārasampanno bhavati / yathāpi tadīryāpatham itikaraṇīyaṃ vā kuśalapakṣaprayogam vā adhiṣṭhāya lokānuvarttinā lokānutkrāntena vinayānuvarttinā vinayānutkrāntena cācāreṇa samanvāgato bhavati /
4) ji ltar spyod yul phun sum tshogs pa yin źe na? dge sloṅ dag lṅa po ’di dag ni spyod yul ma yin pa ste, gaṅ źe na? smad ’tshoṅ ma daṅ, chaṅ ’tshoṅ ma daṅ, śa ’tshoṅ gi gnas daṅ, rgyal po’i pho braṅ daṅ, gdol ba’i khyim mo źes gsuṅs te, gaṅ de bźin gśegs pas ma gnaṅ ba’i spyod yul de dag spaṅs nas, spyod yul gźan du ’jug par byed pa’o – Śbh fol. 2B14, S p. 405-9, D fol. 17a3-5: katañ ca gocarasampanno bhavati / pañca bhikṣor agocarāḥ / katame pañca / tad yathā ghoṣo veṣaṃ pānāgāraḥ rājakulaṃ caṇḍālakaṭhinam eva pañcamam iti / ya etāṃs tathāgatapratikṣiptān agocarān varjayitvā anyatra gocare caraty [anavadye ta(5)tra kālenaivaṃ gocarasampanno bhavati /]
5) ji ltar kha na ma tho ba phra rab tsam dag la yaṅ ’jigs par lta ba yin źe na? kha na ma tho ba phra rab ces bya ba ni gaṅ bslab pa’i gźi phran tshegs su gyur pa rnams te, de dag ñams par gyur na ’bad pa chuṅ ṅus spoṅ bar byed pa’o. de la ’jigs par lta ba ni gal te bdag la de byuṅ bar gyur na ma thob pa thob par bya ba daṅ, ma rtogs pa rtogs par bya ba daṅ, mṅon sum du ma byas pa mṅon sum du bya ba’i skal ba med ciṅ ṅan soṅ du lhuṅ bar gyur ro sñam nas srog gi phyir yaṅ de dag las ñams par mi byed pa’o – Śbh fol. 2B15-6, 7-8, S p. 411-9, 15-16, D fol. 17a5-b3: katham aṇumātreṣv avadyeṣu bhayadarśī bhavati / aṇumātram avadyam ucyate / kṣudrāṇukṣudrāṇi śikṣāpadāni yeṣv adhyāpattir vyutthānaṃ ca prajñāyate / teṣāṃ yādhyāpattir idam avadyam aṇumātraṃ / punas tathā hi tasyā adhyāpatter alpakṛcchreṇa vyutthiṣṭhate (6) yena tad aṇumātram ity ucyate / tatra kathaṃ bhayadarśī bhavati / mā haivāham eṣām adhyāpattihetor abhavyo vā syām aprāptasya prāptaye anadhigatasyâdhigamāya asākṣātkṛtasya sākṣātkriyāyai apāyago vā syām apāyagāmī .... jīvatahetor api na [saṃdhi(8)bhyo] vyāpadyate /
6) ji ltar bslab pa’i gźi rnams yaṅ dag par blaṅs nas slob pa yin źe na? daṅ po so sor thar pa’i sdom pa len pa’i dus na gsol ba daṅ bźi’i las kyis bsñen par rdzogs par byed pa’i tshe bslab pa’i gźi kha cig mkhan po daṅ slob dpon las thos nas, gźan dag ni zla ba phyed phyed ciṅ so sor thar pa’i mdo ’don pa’i tshe na gaṅ yin pa śes par gyis śig ces bstan nas, de ltar so sor thar pa’i sdom pa thob ste, de phyin chad ni ji ltar blaṅs pa daṅ blaṅ bar dam bcas pa rnams kyaṅ blaṅs nas, lhag chad med par bslab par byed pa’o – Śbh fol. 2B18-2A23, S p. 4119-4216, D 17b4-7, 18a1-2: kathaṃ samādāya śi(2A2)kṣate śikṣāpadeṣu / āha / pūrvvam anena prātimokṣasamvarasamādānajñapticaturthena karmmaṇā upasampadyamānena katipayānāṃ śikṣāpadānāṃ śarīraṃ śrutaṃ sātirekaṃ ca tad anyaṃ divasaṃ śikṣāpadaśataṃ prātimokṣasūtroddiṣṭaṃ pratijñāyevopagataṃ sarvvatra labhiṣyāmīti / ācāryopādhyāyānām antikāc chrutvā ..(2).. tataś ca tena .... prātimokṣasamvaraḥ pratilabdhas tata uttarakālaṃ .... samādāya yathānuśiṣṭaḥ anyūnam adhikaṃ śikṣate /
yan lag drug pa’i tshul khrims kyi tshogs sam tshul khrims maṅ po bsdus pa ni tshul khrims kyi phuṅ po źes bya ste, daṅ po tshul khrims yaṅ dag par blaṅs pa nas brtsams nas tha mar rnam par grol ba’i ye śes la thug gi bar du rdul tsam yaṅ ñams pa daṅ god pa med pa’o. de ltar ñams pa daṅ god pa med pas tshul khrims kyi mthar phyin te, zag pa med pa’i tshul khrims kyi mtshan ñid du gyur pa ni tshul khrims kyi phuṅ po yoṅs su rdzogs pa źes bya’o.
de ltar tshul khrims kyi phuṅ po rgyas par bśad nas de yaṅ mdor bsdus na tshul khrims kyi phuṅ po’i mtshan ñid rnam pa gsum du rig par bya ste: 1) chud mi za ba’i mtshan ñid daṅ, 2) raṅ bźin gyi mtshan ñid daṅ, 3) raṅ bźin gyi yon tan gyi mtshan ñid do – Śbh fol. 2A24-5, S p. 4218-432, D fol. 18a2-4: evaṃ samādāya śikṣate śikṣāpadeṣv ayaṃ tāvad vibhaṃgaḥ śīlasamvarasya vistarakṛtaḥ // tatra kathamaḥ samāsārthaḥ / tathāyaṃ samāsārthas trilakṣaṇa eva śīlaskandhaḥ paridīpito bhagavatā / tadyathā avipraṇāśalakṣaṇaḥ svabhāvalakṣaṇaḥ svabhāvagu(5)ṇalakṣaṇaś ca /
1) de la thaṅ cig tshul khrims daṅ ldan źes bya bas tshul khrims kyi sdom pa chud mi za ba’i mtshan ñid bstan pa yin no – Śbh fol. 2A25, S p. 432-3, D fol. 18a4: yathā katham iti / yat tāvad āha śīlavān viharatîty anena tāvad avipraṇāśalakṣaṇaṃ śīlasamvarasyākhyātaṃ /
2) gaṅ so sor thar pa’i sdom pas bsdams pa źes bya bas ni raṅ bźin gyi mtshan ñid smras so – Śbh fol. 2A25, S p. 433-5, D fol. 18a4-5: yat punar āha prātimokṣasamvarasaṃvṛta iti / anena svabhāvalakṣaṇam ākhyātaṃ /
3) cho ga daṅ spyod yul phun sum tshogs pa źes bya bas ni pha rol la brten nas de ltar yaṅ dag par blaṅs pa’i so sor thar pa’i sdom pa’i yon tan gyi mtshan ñid bstan pa yin te, ’di ltar gźan dag gi cho ga daṅ spyod yul phun sum tshogs par mthoṅ na ma dad pa rnams ni dad par ’gyur, dad pa rnams ni dad pa phyir źiṅ ’phel bar ’gyur ro. gaṅ yaṅ kha na ma tho ba phra rab tsam la yaṅ ’jigs par lta ba daṅ, bslab pa’i gźi rnams yaṅ dag par blaṅs nas slob pa gñis kyis raṅ gi dbaṅ du byas nas tshul khrims kyi yon tan smras pa yin te, ci’i phyir źe na? yaṅ dag par blaṅs pa la rdul tsam yaṅ ñams pa med pa daṅ, bslab pa’i gźi chen po dag blaṅs śiṅ slob pa’i rgyus ṅan soṅ du skye ba’i skal ba med ciṅ ma thob pa la sogs pa yaṅ ’thob par ’gyur pas so – Śbh fol. 2A25-6, 2A27-2B21,, S p. 435-10, p. 4314-20, D fol. 18a5-6, b1-3: [yat punar āha] ācāragocarasampanna iti / anena param upanidhāya tathā samādattasya prātimokṣasamva(6)rasya guṇalakṣaṇam ākhyātaṃ / tathāpy apare tām ācāragocarasampadam upalabhyāprasannāś ca prasīdanti prasannānāṃ ca bhavati bhūyobhāvaḥ / .... yat punar āha / aṇumātreṣv avadyeṣu bhayadarśī samādāya śikṣate śikṣāpadeṣu / anenādhyātmādhipateyaguṇānuśansalakṣaṇam ākhyātaṃ / tat kasya hetor yad asyedam ācāragocarasampannaḥ parādhipateyaṃ guṇānuśansaṃ pratilabheta / api ca śīlam vi(2B2)pātayitvā taddhetus tatpratyayam apāyeṣūpapadyate / abhavyatām vā aprāptasya prāptaye pūrvvavat /. ṭ abbreviates the last portion.
Notes to the Sanskrit text: 1) S ...kāya... for ...vāk... 2) ṭ enumerates the seven 3) ṭ, but not D, reads an inserted na 4) S prati... for prāti... 5) MS ...ya for ...yaṃ 6) MS om. daṇḍa 7) MS ...ms 8) Cf. D bdag .... mi ruṅ ṅo sñam nas .... S sā hai vāha (so ’ha)m ṭ yadi me sā bhaved abhavyo vā syām ... ? 9) S pratijñayev... 10) The syllables la and bhi are partly hidden and somewhat uncertain, S has la(bdhā)ṣyāmîti (lapsyāmîti) 11) MS, S ins. daṇḍa 12) MS, S om. daṇḍa 13) MS aha 14) S // 15) MS, S ...pannaḥ for ...panna iti 16) S tathāpi pare MS uncertain 17) S ...aṃ


tshul khrims kyi phuṅ po yoṅs su rdzogs nas, tiṅ ṅe ’dzin gyi phuṅ po yoṅs su rdzogs par byed pa daṅ;

śīlaskandhaṃ paripūrya samādhiskandhaṃ paripūrayati.

[4. Progress (pratipatti):] Having fulfilled the mass of moral discipline he fulfils the mass of concentration [as thought becomes one-pointed depending on moral discipline].

’dis ni tiṅ ṅe ’dzin gyi gnas rab tu sgrub pa (1, cf. fol. 148b2) bstan te, ’di ltar tshul khrims brten nas sems rtse gcig pa la rab tu reg par ’gyur ba’i phyir ro. de bas na gźuṅ ñid las kyaṅ tshul khrims kyi phuṅ po yoṅs su rdzogs nas tiṅ ṅe ’dzin gyi phuṅ po yoṅs su rdzogs par byed pa źes gsuṅs so.
de la tiṅ ṅe ’dzin gaṅ źe na? ’di la I. dge sloṅ ’dod pa las dben pa, sdig pa mi dge ba’i chos rnams la dben pa, rtog pa daṅ bcas pa, dpyod pa daṅ bcas pa, dben pa las skyes pa’i dga’ ba daṅ bde ba can bsam gtan daṅ po ñe bar bsgrubs nas gnas so. II. de rtog pa daṅ dpyod pa daṅ bral źiṅ naṅ yoṅs su daṅ ste, sems kyi rgyud gcig tu gyur pas rtog pa med pa, dpyod pa med pa’i tiṅ ṅe ’dzin las skyes pa’i dga’ ba daṅ, bde ba can bsam gtan gñis pa ñe bar bsgrubs nas gnas so. III. de dga’ ba’i ’dod chags daṅ bral bas btaṅ sñoms la gnas śiṅ dran pa daṅ śes bźin can yin no, bde ba lus kyis myoṅ la ’phags pa rnams kyis gaṅ de dran pa daṅ ldan pa, bde ba la gnas pa btaṅ sñoms pa’o źes brjod pa ste, dga’ ba med pa’i bsam gtan gsum pa ñe bar bsgrubs nas gnas so. IV. de bde ba yaṅ spaṅs te, sṅa nas sdug bsṅal yaṅ spaṅs śiṅ yid bde ba daṅ yid mi bde ba yaṅ nub pas bde ba yaṅ ma yin sdug bsṅal ba yaṅ ma yin pas btaṅ sñoms daṅ dran pa yoṅs su dag pa bsam gtan bźi pa ñe bar bsgrubs nas gnas so źes gsuṅs pa ni tiṅ ṅe ’dzin źes bya’o – quoted from Śbh fol. 1A26-8, S p. 141-159, D fol. 6b2-6: samādhisanniśrayaḥ katamaḥ / sa ... viviktaṃ kāmair viviktam pāpakair akuśalair dharmaiḥ sa[vitarka]ṃ savicāraṃ vivekajaṃ prītisukhaṃ prathamaṃ dhyānam upasaṃpadya viharati / sa vitarkavicāraṇāṃ (7) vyupaśamād adhyātmasaṃprasādāc cetasa ekotībhāvād avitarkam avicāraṃ samādhijaṃ prītisukhaṃ dvitīyaṃ dhyānam upasampadya viharati / sa prīter virāgād upekṣako viharati smṛtaḥ saṃprajānan sukhaṃ ca kāyena pratisamvedayate yat tad āryā ācakṣate upekṣakaḥ smṛtimān sukhavihārī niṣprītikaṃa tṛtīyaṃ dhyānam upasampadya viharati / (8) sa sukhasya ca prahāṇād duḥkhasya ca prahāṇāt pūrvam eva ca saumanasyadaurmanasyayor astagamād aduḥkhāsukham upekṣāsmṛtipariśuddhaṃ caturthaṃ dhyānam upasampadya viharati / ayam ucyate samādhisanniśrayaḥ / The enumeration of the four dhyānas is based upon the classical description; for references v. Śbh p. 14, n. 1, 2; Edg. s. v. dhyāna, Mvy no. 1478-81.
Then a commentary on the above, based on excerpts from Śbh p. 44914ff:
de la bsam gtan rnams ni rnam pa bźis rnam par gźag ste, 1) mi mthun pa’i phyogs ñams par byed pa daṅ, 2) gñen po bsgom pa daṅ, 3) bsgoms pa’i phan yon daṅ, 4) de gñi ga’i gnas so.
I. dhyāna: 1) de la bsam gtan daṅ po la "’dod pa dag las dben pa sdig pa mi dge ba’i chos rnams las dben pa" źes bya bas mi mthun pa’i phyogs ñams pa bstan te:
"’dod pa dag las dben pa" źes bya ba ni ñon moṅs pa’i ’dod pa daṅ, dṅos po’i ’dod pa’o; ’dod pa dag las dben pa ste, mthuṅs par ldan pa las dben pa daṅ, dmigs pa las dben pa’i phyir ro. "sdig pa mi dge ba’i chos rnams las dben pa" źes bya ba ni gaṅ dag ñon moṅs pa’i ’dod pa’i rgyu las byuṅ ba’i lus daṅ ṅag daṅ yid kyi ñes par spyod par gtogs pa chad pas gcod pa daṅ, mtshon ’debs pa daṅ, ’thab pa daṅ, rtsod pa daṅ, ’gyed pa daṅ, g-yo ba’i tshig daṅ, gnod pa daṅ, brdzun du smra ba la sogs pa de dag las dben pa’o – Śbh fol. 13A62-4, S p. 44914-45013, D fol. 169a3-b1: viviktaṃ kāmair iti / dvividhāḥ kāmāḥ kleśakāmā vastukāmāś ca / kāmaviveko ’pi dvividhaḥ / saṃprayogaviveka ālambanavivekaś ca / viviktaṃ (3) pāpakair akuśalair dharmair iti / upakleśāḥ kāmahetukā akuśalā dharmās tad yathā kāyaduścaritaṃ vāgduścaritaṃ manoduścaritaṃ / daṇḍādānaṃ śastrādānaṃ / kalahabhaṇḍanavigrahavivādaśāṭhyavañcananikṛtimṛṣāvādāḥ sambhavanti / teṣāṃ prahāṇād viviktaṃ pāpakair akuśalair dharmair iti /
2) rnam par rtog pa daṅ rnam par dpyod pa dag skyon du ma mthoṅ bas ’dod pa’i gñen pa de dag gñis daṅ mtshuṅs par ldan pa’i phyir "rtog pa daṅ bcas dpyod pa daṅ bcas pa" źes bya bas gñen po bsgom pa bstan te, rtog pa daṅ dpyod pa gñis kyis ’dod pa daṅ, sdig pa mi dge ba’i chos ’joms par byed pas so – vitarkavicāreṣv adoṣadarśanāt svabhūmi(4)kair vitarkavicāraiḥ kāmaprātipakṣikaiḥ kuśalaiḥ savitarkaṃ savicāram iti / Not verbatim.
3) "dben pa las skyes pa’i dga’ ba daṅ bde ba can" źes bya bas bsgoms pa’i phan yon bstan te, ’dod pa las dben pa’am, sgrib pa las dben pa las skyes pa’i dga’ ba daṅ bde ba ni "dben pa las skyes pa’i dga’ ba daṅ bde ba" źes bya ste, ’dod pa’i don rñed nas gnas ṅan len thams cad daṅ bral bas lus daṅ sems śin tu sbyaṅs te las su ruṅ ba’i phyir ro – prayoganiṣṭho manaskāraḥ kāmavivekaḥ / tasyānantaram utpannaṃ taddhetukaṃ tatpratyayaṃ tenāha vivekajam / īpsitābhilaṣitārthasaṃprāpteḥ prītau cādoṣadarśanāt / sarvadauṣṭulyāpagamāc ca vipulapraśrabdhicittakāyakarmaṇyatayā prītisukham / Not verbatim.
4) "bsam gtan daṅ po ñe bar bsgrubs te gnas" źes bya bas de gñis ka’i gnas bstan te, gñen po bsgom pa daṅ bsgoms pa’i phan yon gñis ni bsam gtan daṅ po’i sems rtse gcig pa las grub pa’i phyir te, ’og ma dag la yaṅ de bźin du sbyar ro. ṭ only provides short comments on the last portion of the first dhyāna, namely prathamaṃ dhyānam upasaṃpadya viharati. The use of Śbh p. 45014-4514, D fol. 169b1-4 seems very limited.
II. dhyāna: 1) "de rtog pa daṅ dpyod pa daṅ bral" źes bya bas bsam gtan gñis pa’i mi mthun pa’i phyogs ñams pa bstan te, bsam gtan daṅ po’i rnam par rtog pa daṅ bcas, rnam par dpyod pa daṅ bcas pa’i tiṅ ṅe ’dzin gyis mtshan ma dag la skyon du mthoṅ nas de las sems bzlog ste, rnam par rtog pa med pa daṅ rnam par dpyod pa med pa’i tiṅ ṅe ’dzin gyis mtshan ma las sems ñe bar ’dogs par byed pa’o – Śbh fol. 13A66-13B61, S p. 4514-13, D fol. 169b5-170a1: savitarkasavicārasamādhinimittebhyaś cittam vyāvarttayitvā avitarkāvicārasamādhinimitteṣūpanibadhnāti /
2) "naṅ yoṅs su daṅ ste, sems kyi rgyud gcig tu gyur" ces bya bas gñen po bsgom pa bstan te, de ltar rtog pa daṅ dpyod pa daṅ bcas pa’i dmigs pa daṅ bral bar byas nas rtse gcig tu dpyod pa’i dmigs pa la ṅaṅ gcig pas źi ba daṅ, rab tu daṅ ba’i sems su ’jog pas na yoṅs su daṅ ba yin la, de de ltar sems ñe bar ’jog pas rnam par rtog pa daṅ bcas rnam par dpyod pa daṅ bcas pas glags daṅ bcas śiṅ, bar chad daṅ bcas pa’i gnas skabs las ’das nas sgom pa goms pas glags med ciṅ bar chad med pa’i gnas skabs thob par ’gyur pas "sems kyi rgyud gcig tu gyur pa" źes bya’o – vyagracāriṇa ālambanād vivecya avyagracāriṇy ālambane ekadharmatayā śāntaṃ prasannaṃ cittaṃ pravarttate / vyavasthā(7)payati / tenāha vitarkavicārāṇāṃ vyupaśamād adhyātmasaṃprasādanāt / sa bhāvanābhyāsāt tasyaivāvitarkāvicārasya samādheḥ vitarkavicārasachidrasāntarām avasthām atikramya niśchidranirantarā(13B6)m avasthāṃ prāpnoti / tenāha / cetasa ekotībhāvāt /
3) "tiṅ ṅe ’dzin las skyes pa’i dga’ ba daṅ bde ba can" źes bya bas bsgoms pa’i phan yon bstan te, bsam gtan daṅ po’i dben pa las skyes pa’i dga’ ba daṅ bde ba las khyad par du ’phags pa bstan to, cf. Śbh p. 45116-22.
4) "bsam gtan gñis pa ñe bar bsgrubs nas gnas" źes bya bas de gñi ga’i gnas bstan to.
III. dhyāna: 1) "de dga’ ba’i ’dod chags daṅ bral bas" źes bya bas bsam gtan gsum pa’i mi mthun pa’i phyogs ñams pa bstan te, tiṅ ṅe ’dzin las skyes pa’i sems dga’ ba’i ’dod chags daṅ bral ba’i phyir ro, cf. Śbh p. 45123ff.
2) "btaṅ sñoms la gnas śiṅ dran pa daṅ śes bźin can yin" źes bya bas gñen po bsgom pa bstan te, rnam par rtog pa daṅ bcas, rnam par dpyod pa daṅ bcas pa de dag daṅ dga’ ba yaṅ spaṅs pas bar chad med par btaṅ sñoms daṅ ldan par gnas so. de yaṅ dga’ ba daṅ ldan pa’i ’du śes yid la byed pa rnams kyi go skabs mi dbye ba’i phyir dran pa ñe bar gnas pa yin la, skyes pa rnams kyaṅ nam yaṅ ji ltar yaṅ daṅ yaṅ du mi blaṅ ba’i phyir śes rab kyis naṅ du gnas pas na "dran pa daṅ ldan źiṅ śes bźin can" źes bya’o – Śbh fol. 13B63-13A71, S p. 4526-45317, D fol. 170b1-171a3: tatra pratame dhyāne vitarkavicārā bhavanti / yena nirantaropekṣā na pravarttate / dvitīye dhyāne (4) prītir bhavati / yenātrāpi nirantaropekṣā na pravarttate / tenāyaṃ dhyāyī prathamadvitīyeṣu dhyāneṣu nāsti tena tṛtīye dhyāne upekṣako viharatīty ucyate / sa upekṣakas sans tathā tathopasthitasmṛtir viharati / yathā yathā te prītisahagatāḥ saṃjñāmanasikārāḥ na samudācaranti / sa cet punar abhāvitatvāt tṛtīyasya dhyāna(5)sya smṛtisaṃpramoṣāt kadācit karhacic citte prītisahagatāḥ saṃjñāmanasikārāḥ samudācaranti / tāṃ laghu laghv eva prajñayā pratividhyati / samyag eva prajānāti / utpannotpannāṃś ca nādhivāsayati / prajahāti vinodayati / vyantīkaroti / cittam adhyupekṣate / tenāha smṛtaḥ saṃprajānann iti / ṭ abridges.
3) "bde ba lus kyis myoṅ la, ’phags pa rnams kyis gaṅ de dran pa daṅ ldan pa bde ba la gnas pa btaṅ sñoms pa’o źes brjod pa ste" źes bya bas bsgoms pa’i phan yon bstan te, de ltar btaṅ sñoms la maṅ du gnas pa de sems g-yeṅ ba med pa’i dga’ ba daṅ ldan pa’i tshor ba spaṅs nas, dga’ ba med pa’i źi ba rab tu źi ba’i tshor ba ’byuṅ ste, de yaṅ de’i tshe gzugs kyi lus daṅ yid kyi lus kyis tshor ba’i bde ba daṅ śin tu sbyaṅs pa’i bde ba myoṅ bar byed pas na "bde ba lus kyis myoṅ ba" źes bya’o. bsam gtan ’og ma gñis la ni de lta bu’i bde ba daṅ btaṅ sñoms med la, goṅ ma la ni btaṅ sñoms yod kyaṅ bde ba med kyi, bsam gtan gsum pa ’di ñid bde ba daṅ btaṅ sñoms kyi gnas yin pas ’phags pa saṅs rgyas rnams daṅ saṅs rgyas kyi ñan thos rnams kyis bsam gtan gsum pa ’di ñid la "dran pa daṅ ldan pa bde ba la gnas pa btaṅ sñoms pa’o" źes gtso bor bsṅags pas na "’phags pa rnams kyis gaṅ de dran pa daṅ ldan pa, bde ba la gnas pa, btaṅ sñoms pa’o źes brjod pa" źes gsuṅs so – tasya tasmin samaye e(6)vam upekṣakasya viharatā smṛtasya saṃprajanyasyāsevanānvayād bhāvanānvayād bahulīkārānvayāt prītisahagataṃ prahīyate tac cittauddhatyakaraṃ / niḥprītikaṃ ca śāntaṃ praśāntaṃ cetasi veditam utpadyate prītiprātipakṣyena / tasmin samaye rūpakāyena manaḥkāyena veditam (13A7) sukhaṃ ca praśrabdhisukhaṃ pratisamvedayate / tenāha sukhaṃ ca kāyena pratisaṃvedayate / tṛtīyāc ca dhyānāt adhas tadrūpaṃ sukhaṃ nāsti nāpi nirantarā upekṣā / tṛtīyād dhyānād ūrdhvaṃ yad apy upekṣopalabhyate / na tu sukhaṃ / tatrādhaḥ sukhopekṣābhāvād ūrdhvañ ca sukhābhāvāt / idaṃ tad āyatanaṃ yad uta tṛtīyaṃ dhyānaṃ yat tad āryā (2) ācakṣate / yat pratilambhavihāriṇaṃ pudgalam adhikṛtya upekṣakaḥ smṛtimāṃ sukhavihārī tṛtīyaṃ dhyānam upasaṃpadya viharatīti / āryāḥ punaḥ buddhāś ca buddhaśrāvakāś ca /
IV. dhyāna: 1) "de bde ba yaṅ spaṅs te, sṅa nas sdug bsṅal yaṅ spaṅs śiṅ yid bde ba daṅ yid mi bde ba yaṅ nub pas" źes bya bas bsam gtan bźi pa’i mi mthun pa’i phyogs ñams pa bstan te, "bde ba yaṅ spaṅs" źes bya ba ni bsam gtan gsum pa daṅ ldan pa’i bde ba bsam gtan bźi pa ’dis spaṅs par bstan pa’o. "sdug bsṅal yaṅ spaṅs" źes bya ba ni bsam gtan gñis pa spaṅs pa yaṅ bsdus te bstan pa’o. "yid bde ba nub pas" śes bya ba ni bsam gtan gsum pas dga’ ba spaṅs pa bstan pa’o. "yid mi bde ba nub pas" śes bya ba ni bsam gtan gñis pas spaṅs pa bstan pa’o – Śbh fol. 13A74-6, S p. 4548-17, D fol. 171b1-4: tatra caturthadhyānasamāpattikāle sukhasya ca prahāṇād dvitīyadhyānasa(5)māpattikāle duḥkhasya tṛtīyadhyānasamāpattikāle saumanasyasyāstagamāt prathamadhyānasamāpattikāle daurmanasyasya /
3) "bde ba yaṅ ma yin sdug bsṅal ba yaṅ ma yin pa btaṅ sñoms daṅ dran pa yoṅs su dag pa" źes bya bas bsgoms pa’i phan yon bstan te, tshor ba goṅ ma bźi po spaṅs pas sdug bsṅal yaṅ ma yin bde ba yaṅ ma yin pa’i tshor ba daṅ ldan pa daṅ, bsam gtan gsum pa’i tshe btaṅ sñoms daṅ dran pa yod kyaṅ yoṅs su ma dag pa, ’di’i tshe yoṅs su dag pa daṅ ldan par bstan pa’o – asti tāvat sukhaduḥkhasya prahāṇād aduḥkhāsukhaivāsya vedanāvaśiṣṭā bhavati / tenāha / aduḥkhāsukhā / tasmin samaye ...(6)... [teṣāṃ ca prahāṇād] yā tatropekṣā / smṛtiś ca sā pariśuddhā bhavati /
4) "bsam gtan bźi pa ñe bar bsgrubs te gnas" źes bya bas de gñi ga’i gnas bstan to.
Notes to the Sanskrit text: 1) Brackets: hole in MS 2) MS om. daṇḍa 3) S savitarkasavicārāṇāṃ 4) MS ...jāna sukhaṃ 5) MS, S ins. daṇḍa 5a) MS, S om. niṣprītikaṃ which is supplied from D. The standard version, as also supported by D, has sukhaṃ viharatīti for sukhavihārī 6) S om. daṇḍa 7...7) With D sṅa nas sdug bsṅal ba yaṅ spaṅs śiṅ and ṭ, cf. Mvy 1481; MS, S om. 8) S ...rvva.. 9) S om. ca 10) For astaṃgama, for the form cf. e. g. Kośa p. 435. 11) MS om. daṇḍa 12) As D, ṭ; MS, S kāmavitarko 13) As D; MS, S om. iti and daṇḍa 14) D ins. rtog pa daṅ bcas pa / dpyod pa daṅ bcas pa źes bya ba ni equivalent of savitarkaıṃ savicāram iti 15) As D, ṭ; MS, S avitaraka... 16) MS ...prati... 17) As D; MS, S ...cāraṃ for ...cāram iti / 18) D ins. dben pa las źes bya ba ni equivalent of vivekam iti 19) MS ...kaṃ for ...kaḥ, MS, S om. daṇḍa, D ins. skyes pa źes bya ba ni equivalent of jam iti 20) MS, S om. daṇḍa, D ins. dga’ ba daṅ bde ba can źes bya ba ni equivalent of prītisukham iti 20b) S ...taḥ 21) S vā doṣa... 22) D does not have any equivalent of praśrabdhi, ṭ, however, has. S ...śrabdhi ci... 23) MS, S om. daṇḍa 24) S ...viviktebhaś for samādhinimittebhaś 25) S ...varta... 26) S om. daṇḍa, D ins. sems kyi rgyud gcig tu gyur pas źes bya ba ni equivalent of cetasa ekotībhāvād 27) S sabhāvanābhy... 28) S vitarkavicārasya samādheḥ sachidra... for vitarkavicārasachidra.. MS ...am for ...ām 28a) MS, S sic, ayaṃ dhyāyī corrupt ?, D has de lta bas na bsam gtan daṅ po daṅ / bsam gtan gñis pa de dag la btaṅ sñoms śas cher med pas 29) D ins. dran pa daṅ śes bźin can yin źes bya ba ni equivalent of smṛtaḥ saṃprajānann iti 30) As D kun ’byuṅ bar mi ’gyur MS, S om. na 31) S karhicit cf. Edg. s. v. karhacit Beginning and end of lines 3-5 are very indistinct. 32) MS ...prajāna S ...prajānān 33...33) In D (fol. 171a2-3) this part is moved to after buddhaśrāvakāś ca /, but ṭ has it in the same place as MS. D seems right in following the order of the mūla text, in which niṣprītikam comes at the end. D has dga’ ba med pa źes bya ba ni at the beginning of this piece, equivalent of niṣprītikam iti. S om. daṇḍa after ...pakṣyena 34) S om. bhāvanãnvayād 35) S om. ca 36) As D fol. 171a3 dga’ ba’i gñen po MS, S / prītiprātidvandvyena 37) D fol. 170b5 ins. bde ba lus kyis myoṅ ba źes bya ba ni equivalent of kāyena pratisamvedayata iti 38) MS, S vedita 39...39) S om. 40) D ins. ’phags pa rnams kyis gaṅ de la dran pa daṅ ldan pa bde ba la gnas pa btaṅ sñoms pa’o źes brjod pa ste źes bya ba ni equivalent to yat tad āryā ācakṣate upekṣakaḥ smṛtimān sukhaṃ viharatīti 41) S ...aṃ 42) S vṛddhāś ca vṛddhaśrāvakāś 43) S tan na 44) S ...aṅga... 45) ṭ has bsam gtan gñis pa - dvitīyadhyāna 46) As D de la tshor ba’i lhag ma bde ba yaṅ ma yin / sdug bsṅal yaṅ ma yin pa ñi tshe yod pas na / MS, S vedanā viśiṣṭā bhavati


tiṅ ṅe ’dzin gyi phuṅ po yoṅs su rdzogs nas, śes rab kyi phuṅ po yoṅs su rdzogs par byed pa daṅ;

samādhiskandhaṃ paripūrya prajñāskandhaṃ paripūrayati.

Having fulfilled the mass of concentration he fulfils the mass of insight [into the four truths, as true insight arises from one-pointedness].

’di ni ye śes kyi rten du rab tu sgrub pa (2, cf. fol.148b2) bstan te, sems rtse gcig tu ’gyur na yaṅ dag pa ji lta ba bźin du rab tu śes par ’gyur ba’i phyir ro. de bas na mdo las kyaṅ tiṅ ṅe ’dzin gyi phuṅ po yoṅs su rdzogs nas śes rab kyi phuṅ po yoṅs su rdzogs par byed pa daṅ źes gsuṅs te, de la śes rab kyi phuṅ po ’di ni sdug bsṅal ’phags pa’i bden pa’o źes yaṅ dag pa ji lta ba bźin du śes pa daṅ, ’di ni sdug bsṅal kun ’byuṅ ba ’phags pa’i bden pa’o źes yaṅ dag pa ji lta ba bźin du śes pa daṅ, ’di ni sdug bsṅal ’gog pa ’phags pa’i bden pa’o źes yaṅ dag pa ji lta ba bźin du śes pa daṅ, ’di ni sdug bsṅal ’gog par ’gro bar byed pa’i lam ’phags pa’i bden pa’o źes yaṅ dag pa ji lta ba bźin du śes pa ste ’phags pa’i bden pa bźi phyin ci ma log par śes pa ni śes rab kyi phuṅ po yoṅs su rdzogs par byed pa źes pa’o.


śes rab kyi phuṅ po yoṅs su rdzogs nas, rnam par grol ba’i phuṅ po yoṅs su rdzogs par byed pa daṅ;

prajñāskandhaṃ paripūrya vimuktiskandhaṃ paripūrayati.

[5. Its fruit (phala):] Having fulfilled the mass of insight he fulfils the mass of deliverance [as he realizes the elimination of the vices by means of pure knowledge (suviśuddhajñānena klesaprahāṇaṃ sākṣātkaroti) ].

’di ni bya ba byas pa rab tu sgrub pa (3, cf. fol. 148b2) bstan te, ’di ltar ye śes śin tu rnam par dag pas ni ñon moṅs pa spaṅs pa mṅon sum du byed pa’i phyir ro. de bas na mdo las kyaṅ śes rab kyi phuṅ po yoṅs su rdzogs nas rnam par grol ba’i phuṅ po yoṅs su rdzogs par byed pa źes gsuṅs te, de yaṅ tshul khrims rnam par dag pa ni ’gyod pa med par ’gyur ro, ’gyod pa med na dga’ ba daṅ mchog tu dga’ ba daṅ śin tu rnam par sbyaṅs pa daṅ bde bar ’gyur ro, bde bar gyur pa’i sems mñam par ’jog go, sems rnam par gźag na yaṅ dag pa ji lta ba bźin du rab tu śes, yaṅ dag pa ji lta ba bźin du mthoṅ bar ’gyur ro, yaṅ dag pa ji lta ba bźin du śes śiṅ mthoṅ bas skyo bar ’gyur ro, skyo bar ’gyur na ’dod pa’i zag pa las sems rnam par grol ba daṅ, srid pa’i zag pa daṅ ma rig pa’i zag pa las sems rnam par grol te, rgyud la dri ma med pa ’thob par ’gyur pas na rnam par grol ba’i phuṅ po yoṅs su rdzogs par byed pa źes bya’o.
’dis ni ’bras bu (5, cf. fol. 148a1) bstan te, rnam par grol ba’i phuṅ po ni bslab pa gsum la źugs pa’i ’bras bu yin pa’i phyir ro.


rnam par grol ba’i phuṅ po yoṅs su rdzogs nas, rnam par grol ba’i ye śes mthoṅ ba’i phuṅ po yoṅs su rdzogs par byed pa ste;

vimuktiskandhaṃ paripūrya vimuktijñānadarśanaskandhaṃ paripūrayati.

[6. Knowledge of it (tatpravedanā):] Having fulfilled the mass of deliverance he fulfils the mass of vision of the knowledge of deliverance [thus having freed thought from the vices of the threefold world he knows deliverance itself].

de ltar khams gsum gyi ñon moṅs pa las sems rnam par grol nas de’i ’og tu rnam par grol ba ñid śes śiṅ rig pa’i ye śes skyes te, de bas na mdo las kyaṅ rnam par grol ba’i phuṅ po yoṅs su rdzogs nas rnam par grol ba’i ye śes mthoṅ ba’i phuṅ po yoṅs su rdzogs par byed ces gsuṅs so.
’dis ni de rab tu rig pa (6, cf. fol. 148a1) bstan te, rnam par grol ba’i ’og tu bdag gi sdug bsṅal ni śes par byas, kun ’byuṅ ba ni spaṅs, ’gog pa ni mṅon sum du byas, lam ni bsgoms pas de sdug bsṅal śes par bya mi dgos, kun ’byuṅ ba spaṅ mi dgos, ’gog pa mṅon sum du bya mi dgos, lam bsgom mi dgos te, skye ba zad do, tshaṅs par spyad pa bsten to, bya ba byas so, srid pa ’di las gźan mi śes so źes khoṅ du chud pa’i phyir ro.


gaṅ ’di la mkhas pa, ’di ni ñan thos kyi theg pa la mkhas pa źes bya’o.

yad iha kauśalyam idam ucyate śrāvakayānakauśalyam.

Skill in this is called skill with the way of disciples.


gźan yaṅ ñan thos kyi theg pa la mkhas pa ni gaṅ bsod nams daṅ bsod nams ma yin pa daṅ mi g-yo ba’i ’du byed rnams la rnam par smod pa daṅ;khams gsum pa thams cad la yid byuṅ źiṅ ’dod chags daṅ bral ba daṅ;’du byed thams cad la mi rtag pa daṅ sdug bsṅal bar rtog pa daṅ;chos thams cad la bdag med par rtog pa daṅ;mya ṅan las ’das pa źi ba la mṅon par dga’ ba daṅ;skad cig kyaṅ srid par skye bar mi ’dod pa daṅ;rtag tu ’jigs par lta ba daṅ;rtag tu yid mi rton pa daṅ;phuṅ po rnams la gsod par ’du śes pa daṅ;khams rnams la sbrul gdug pa lta bur rtog pa’i ’du śes pa daṅ;skye mched rnams la groṅ stoṅ lta bur ’du śes pa daṅ;skye ba’i gnas thams cad la mi smon pa’i ’du śes pa daṅ;mya ṅan las ’das pa la gnas daṅ skyabs su ’du śes pa daṅ;

punar aparam śrāvakayānakauśalyaṃ yā puṇyāpuṇyāniñjyānāṃ saṃskārāṇāṃ vigarhaṇā;nirvidvirāgatā sarvasmiṃs traidhātuke;anityaduḥkhapratyavekṣā sarvasaṃskāreṣv;anātmapratyavekṣā sarvadharmeṣu;śāntanirvāṇābhiratiḥ;na kṣaṇam api bhavopapattispṛhā;nityaṃ bhayadarśitā;nityam aviśvāsatā;ghātakasamjñā skandheṣu;āśīviṣasaṃjñā dhātuṣu;śūnyagrāmasaṃjñā āyataneṣu;apraṇidhānasaṃjñā sarvopapattisthāneṣu;sthānaśaraṇasaṃjñā nirvāṇe.

Further, skill with the way of disciples is [1. counteracting the adversary (vipakṣadūṣaṇa) ] rejecting the formative factors, meritorious, non-meritorious or neutral;disgust and absence of passion for the whole threefold world;discerning the impermanence and suffering in all conditioned things;discerning the egolessness in all moments of existence;delight in peace and extinction;no desire for birth in existence, not even for a second;regarding [existence (bhava) ] always with fear;constant absence of security [regarding existence (bhava) ];conceiving of the parts of personality as a killer;conceiving of the spheres of sense-perception as snake-venom;conceiving of the fields of sense-perception as an empty village;conceiving no wishes regarding any kind of birth;[and 2. seeing the good qualities of the stage of the antidote (pratipakṣabhūmiguṇadarśitā):] conceiving of extinction as one’s proper abode, one’s refuge.

gźan yaṅ ñan thos kyi theg pa la mkhas pa ni źes bya bas ñan thos kyi theg pa la mkhas pa rnam graṅs gźan du ston te, mkhan po daṅ slob dpon gyis bśad pa’i sgra la brten nas gaṅ zag la bdag med par dmigs pa ni ñan thos te, ñan thos de dag gi theg pa ni ñan thos kyi theg pa’o. de yaṅ rnam pa gñis su rig par bya ste, 1) mi mthun pa’i phyogs sun ’byin pa daṅ, 2) gñen po’i sa la yon tan du lta ba’o. de la 1) mi mthun pa’i phyogs sun ’byin pa ni gaṅ bsod nams daṅ bsod nams ma yin pa źes bya ba nas brtsams te, skye ba’i gnas thams cad la mi smon źes bya ba yan chad kyis bstan to; 2) gñen po’i sa la yon tan du lta ba ni mya ṅan las ’das pa la gnas daṅ skyabs su ’du śes pa źes bya bas bstan to. de bas na gaṅ gis ’gro ba daṅ, gaṅ du ’gro ba’i phyir de gñis ni ñan thos kyi theg pa ste, gaṅ gis ’gro ba ni mi mthun pa’i phyogs sun ’byin pa’i ’du śes kyis ’gro ba’o, gaṅ du ’gro ba ni mya ṅan las ’das pa’i sar ’gro ba’o.
mi mthun pa’i phyogs sun ’byin pa yaṅ rnam pa gñis te, 1) rgyu spoṅ ba daṅ, 2) ’bras bu spoṅ ba’o. rgyu spoṅ ba la yaṅ rnam pa gñis te, las spoṅ ba daṅ ñon moṅs pa spoṅ ba’o. las spoṅ ba’i dbaṅ du byas nas gaṅ bsod nams daṅ źes bya ba la sogs pa smos te, ’du byed gsum ni khams gsum du skye ba’i rgyu byed par mthoṅ nas de rnams la rnam par smod par byed de, rnam pa sna tshogs su smod pa ni rnam par smod pa ste, sun ’byin par byed pa’o. de’aṅ rnam pa gñis te, sṅon byas pa spoṅ ba daṅ, phyis mi byed pa’o; de la sṅon byas pa spoṅ ba ni ’du byed rnam pa gsum sṅon spyad pa’i bag chags yod pa la ’phags pa’i lam gyis sbyoṅ ba’o; phyis mi byed pa ni phyin chad ’du byed rnam pa gsum gyi las la mi ’jug pa’o. ñon moṅs pa spoṅ ba yaṅ rnam pa gñis te, a) de’i ’bras bu sdug bsṅal gyi bdag ñid du mthoṅ bas de la mi dga’ ba daṅ, b) de’i rgyus sdug bsṅal bskyed par mthoṅ bas spoṅ bar ’dod pa’o.khams gsum thams cad la yid byuṅ źiṅ źes bya bas de’i ’bras bu sdug bsṅal gyi bdag ñid du mthoṅ bas de la mi dga’ ba bstan te, khams gsum ni ’dod pa’i khams daṅ, gzugs kyi khams daṅ, gzugs med pa’i khams dag go. de la ’dod pa’i khams ni gliṅ bźi daṅ, ’dod pa’i khams kyi lha drug daṅ, sems can dmyal ba daṅ, dud ’gro daṅ, yi dags rnams so. gzugs kyi khams ni tshaṅs ris daṅ, tshaṅs pa mdun na ’don daṅ, tshaṅs chen źes bya ba la sogs pa gnas bcu drug dag go. gzugs med pa’i khams ni nam mkha’ mtha’ yas skye mched ces bya ba la sogs pa bźi’o. yid byuṅ ba ni khams gsum la skyo ba’o, ’dod chags daṅ bral ba źes bya bas de’i rgyus sdug bsṅal bskyed par mthoṅ bas spoṅ bar ’dod pa bstan te, khams gsum ni ñon moṅs pa spaṅs pa ni ’dod chags daṅ bral ba’o.’bras bu spoṅ ba’i dbaṅ du byas nas, ’du byed thams cad la mi rtag ces bya ba la sogs pa smos so. thams cad kyi sgra daṅ rtog pa’i sgra gñi ga daṅ sbyar te ’du byed thams cad la mi rtag par rtog pa daṅ, ’du byed thams cad la sdug bsṅal bar rtog pa źes bya bar sbyar ro.
rgyu daṅ rkyen gyis bskyed pa’i phuṅ po daṅ khams daṅ, skye mched la sogs pa’i chos rnams ni ’du byed thams cad de, de dag mi rtag pa gñis kyis ’jig par byed pa ni ’du byed thams cad la mi rtag pa rtog pa źes bya’o.
de la mi rtag pa rnam pa gñis ni 1) ’jig pas mi rtag pa daṅ, 2) skad cig mas ’joms pas mi rtag pa’o:
de la 1) ’jig pas mi rtag pa ni mthar ’chi bar ’gyur ba ste, mnar med pa nas brtsams nas srid pa’i rtse mo’i bar du de na gnas pa’i sems can rnams raṅ gi gnas nas ’phos pas so. 2) skad cig mas ’joms pas mi rtag pa ni skad cig ma re re la yaṅ ’jig ciṅ skye ba’i phyir ro.
’du byed thams cad sdug bsṅal rnam pa brgyad daṅ ldan par śes pa ni sdug bsṅal bar rtog pa źes bya ste, sdug bsṅal rnam pa brgyad ni 1) skye ba’i sdug bsṅal daṅ, 2) rga ba’i sdug bsṅal daṅ, 3) na ba’i sdug bsṅal daṅ, 4) śi ba’i sdug bsṅal daṅ, 5) mi sdug pa daṅ phrad pa’i sdug bsṅal daṅ, 6) sdug pa daṅ bral ba’i sdug bsṅal daṅ, 7) gaṅ ’dod pa de btsal te mi rñed pa’i sdug bsṅal daṅ, 8) mdor na ñe bar len pa’i phuṅ po lṅa sdug bsṅal ba’o. The paragraph seems based upon Abhidharmasamuccaya p. 3713ff: api khalu duḥkhalakṣaṇaprabhedā aṣṭau / jātir duḥkhaṃ jarā duḥkhaṃ vyādhir duḥkhaṃ maraṇaṃ duḥkham apriyasaṃprayogo duḥkhaṃ yad apīccan na labhate tad api duḥkhaṃ saṃkṣiptena pañcopādānaskandhā duḥkham // The text of ṭ in the following is, however, different and more copious:
de la 1) skye ba ni mi daṅ lha la sogs pa’i ’gro ba de daṅ de dag tu phuṅ po daṅ khams daṅ skye mched mṅon par ’grub pa’o. ci’i phyir skye ba sdug bsṅal ba źes bya źe na? rnam pa gñis kyi phyir te, a) raṅ bźin gyis sdug bsṅal ba daṅ, b) sdug bsṅal gźan gyi rten du gyur pa’i phyir ro – Abhidharmasamuccaya: jātiḥ kim upādāya duḥkham / saṃbādhaduḥkhtāṃ tadanyaduḥkhāśrayatāṃ copādāya / Rec ṭ: jātiḥ kim upādāya duḥkham / svabhāvaduḥkhatām anyaduḥkhāśrayatāṃ copādāya /
2) de la rgas pa ni phuṅ po gźan du gyur pa ste, laṅ tsho bcom pa daṅ, na tshod ñams pa la sogs pa la’o. ci’i phyir rga ba sdug bsṅal ba źes bya źe na? ñe du ’khor rnams kyis śin tu byams śiṅ yid du ’oṅ bar bya ba daṅ, ’gro ba bzaṅ mo’i mig daṅ yid kyis rjes su mthun par byed pa’i kha dog daṅ dbyibs śin tu mdzes pa de rga ba’i ser bas phog nas mi mdzes pa daṅ, ’khums pa daṅ źigs par snaṅ bas ñe du’i phyogs rnams kyaṅ śin tu mi dga’ bar byed kyi, ’gro ba bzaṅ mos kyaṅ spoṅ bar byed pas rga ba sdug bsṅal ba’o – Abhidharmasamuccaya: jarā kim upādāya duḥkham / kāle vipariṇatiduḥkhatā upādāya //
3) de la khams mi mthun pa ’phel bar gyur pa ni na ba ste, sa la sogs pa’i khams śas che chuṅ du gyur pa’o. ci’i phyir na sdug bsṅal ba źes bya źe na? rab tu mi bzad pa’i nad kyi khyad par gyis thebs nas nags chen po mes tshig pa’i nad du chud pa rab tu tsha ba’i me lces reg pa skad chen po ’byin pa bźin sdug bsṅal ba’i mes reg pa na mi bzad pa’i skad cher ’byin pas na sdug bsṅal ba źes bya’o – Abhidharmasamuccaya: vyādhi kim upādāya duḥkham / bhūteṣu vipariṇatiduḥkhatām upādāya //
4) de la ’chi ba ni dbaṅ po rnams ñams pa las de’i rgyus sems daṅ sems las byuṅ ba rnams mi rgyu ba’o, sems daṅ sems las byuṅ ba rnams mi rgyu bar gyur pa na gaṅ zag de śi ba źes bya’o. ci’i phyir śi ba sdug bsṅal ba źes bya źe na? ’di ltar śi bar gyur na yid du ’oṅ źiṅ sems la gcags pa’i pha ma daṅ ñe du daṅ grogs la sogs pa daṅ bral źiṅ, nor daṅ ’bru daṅ, bran daṅ bu tsha la sogs pa gtaṅ bar dka’ ba rnams daṅ bral te mi ’dod bźin du bsad sar bkri ba’i btson daṅ ’dra bar sdug bsṅal dpag tu med pa skyed par byed pas na ’di las sdug bsṅal gźan med pa’i phyir ’chi ba sdug bsṅal ba’o – Abhidharmasamuccaya: maraṇaṃ kim upādāya duḥkham / jīvitavipraṇāśaduḥkhatām upādāya //
5) mi sdug pa daṅ phrad pa ni mi dge ba’i las byas pa’i rgyus sems can dmyal ba pa la sogs pa ’bras bu yid du mi ’oṅ ba daṅ phrad pa’o. ci’i phyir mi sdug pa daṅ phrad pa sdug bsṅal ba źes bya źe na? khyim mtshes mi bgruṅs pa daṅ ’dra bar gnod pa byed pa’i bdag ñid yin pa daṅ, dug gi śiṅ bźin du sdug bsṅal skyed pa’i rgyu byed pa daṅ, zug rṅus zug bźin du lus daṅ sems la gnod pa byed pa daṅ, skye bo mi bgruṅs pa daṅ dgra daṅ phrad na źe sdaṅ skye bar byed pa bźin du źe sdaṅ skyed pa’i gnas su gyur pa’i phyir sdug bsṅal ba źes bya’o – Abhidharmasamuccaya: apriyasaṃyogaḥ kim upādāya duḥkham / saṃyogajaduḥkhatām upādāya //
