6) sdug pa daṅ bral ba ni sems can gyi graṅ su gtogs pa’am, sems can gyi graṅs su ma gtogs pa yaṅ ruṅ, yid du ’oṅ ba’i dṅos po daṅ bral ba’o. ci’i phyir sdug pa daṅ bral ba sdug bsṅal ba źes bya ba źe na? sdug pa daṅ bral bar dogs pa’am, mthoṅ ba’am, rjes su dran pas kyaṅ mya ṅan daṅ, smre sṅags ’don pa daṅ, yid mi bde ba daṅ, ’khrugs1 pa’i sdug bsṅal ’gyur bar byed pas na, sdug pa daṅ bral ba sdug bsṅal ba’o – Abhidharmasamuccaya: priyaviprayogaḥ kim upādāya duḥkham / viprayogajaduḥkhatām upādāya //
7) ’dod pa btsal te ma rñed pa ni sdug bsṅal ba daṅ bral ba la yaṅ mi phrad par ’dod pa daṅ, bde ba daṅ phrad pa daṅ yaṅ mi ’bral bar ’dod pa de btsal na ma grub pa’o. yaṅ na sdug pa daṅ phrad par ’dod pa daṅ, mi sdug pa daṅ bral bar ’dod pa las sdug pa daṅ ma phrad la mi sdug pa daṅ phrad par gyur pa ni gaṅ ’dod pa btsal te ma rñed pa źes bya’o. ci’i phyir gaṅ ’dod pa btsal te ma rñed pa sdug bsṅal ba źes bya źe na? sdug bsṅal skye ba’i rgyur gyur ba’i phyir te, dus gsum du’aṅ bdag gis gaṅ btsal pa de ma rñed do źes sdug bsṅal skye ba’i phyir ro – Abhidharmasamuccaya: yad apīcchan na labhate tat kim upādāya duḥkham / kāmyaphalābhāvajaduḥkhatām upādāya //
8) mdor na ñe bar len pa’i phuṅ po lṅa sdug bsṅal ba źes bya ba ni ñe bar len pa’i phuṅ po lṅar sdug bsṅal thams cad ’dus te, sdug bsṅal gyi rten yin pa’i phyir de skad ces bya’o – Abhidharmasamuccaya: saṃkṣiptena pañcopādānaskandhāḥ kim upādāya / dauṣṭhulyaduḥkhatām upādāya, but cf. ibid, line 16: tad anyaduḥkhāśrayatāṃ copādaya referring to jāti.chos thams cad la bdag med par rtog pa daṅ źes bya ba la chos thams cad ni ’dus byas daṅ ’dus ma byas daṅ, zag pa daṅ bcas pa daṅ zag pa med pa’o. gaṅ na gaṅ med par śes pa chos thams cad la bdag med par rtog pa ste, chos de dag la mu stegs can gyis brtag pa’i bdag rtag pa med par khoṅ du chud pa’o.mya ṅan las ’das pa źi ba la mṅon par dga’ ba źes bya ba la, mya ṅan las ’das pa ni sdug bsṅal spaṅs pa daṅ, ’dod chags la sogs pa spaṅs pa’i phyir źi ba’o. yaṅ na mya ṅan las ’das pa rnam pa gñis te, phuṅ po’i lhag ma daṅ bcas pa’i mya ṅan las ’das pa daṅ, phuṅ po’i lhag ma ma lus par spaṅs pa’i mya ṅan las ’das pa’o. de la źi ba źes bya bas phuṅ po’i lhag ma daṅ bcas pa’i mya ṅan las ’das pa bstan te, ñon moṅs pa thams cad spaṅs nas phuṅ po tsam yod pa’i phyir ro. mya ṅan las ’das pa źes bya bas phuṅ po’i lhag ma ma lus pa spaṅs pa’i mya ṅan las ’das pa bstan te, ñon moṅs pa daṅ phuṅ po gñi ga yaṅ spaṅs pa’i phyir ro. mṅon par dga’ ba ni de thob par mos pa daṅ, de ’thob par ’dod pa’o.skad cig kyaṅ srid par skye bar mi ’dod pa źes bya ba la cuṅ zad kyaṅ khams gsum du skye bar ma mos źes bya ba’i tha tshig ste, ci’i phyir źe na? khams gsum mtha’ dag rtag ru ’du byed kyi sdug bsṅal daṅ rjes su ’brel ciṅ des khyab par mthoṅ bas so.rtag tu ’jigs par lta źes bya ba ’dir yaṅ srid pa la źes bya bar sbyar te, sdug bsṅal gyi sdug bsṅal daṅ ldan pa’am, ñon moṅs pa ’byuṅ gnas yin par mthoṅ bas na rtag tu ’jigs par lta’o.rtag tu yid mi rton ces bya ba ’dir yaṅ srid pa la źes bya bar sbyar te, thaṅ cig bde ba rnams kyaṅ phyis sdug bsṅal ba’i rgyur gyur par ’gyur ba’i sdug bsṅal daṅ ldan pa’i phyir rtag tu yid mi rton pa’o.phuṅ po rnams la gsod par ’du śes daṅ źes bya ba la dper na gśed pos gsod ciṅ sdug bsṅal skyed par byed pa, de bźin du phuṅ po la bdag tu dmigs na yaṅ skye rga na ’chi’i sdug bsṅal skye bar mthoṅ bas de dag phuṅ po rnams la gsod par ’du śes so.
khams rnams la sbrul gdug pa lta bur rtog pa’i ’du śes źes bya ba la, ji ltar sbrul gdug pas sdug bsṅal daṅ ñon moṅs pa bskyed pa, de bźin du mig la sogs pa’i khams brten nas gzugs la sogs pa’i khams la dmigs nas ’dod chags daṅ źe sdaṅ la sogs pa’i ñon moṅs pa ’byuṅ bar khoṅ du chud pas na khams rnams la sbrul gdug pa lta bur rtog pa’i ’du śes pa źes bya’o.
skye mched rnams la groṅ stoṅ pa lta bur ’du śes pa daṅ źes bya ba la, ji ltar groṅ stoṅ pa na skye bo dag rgyu ba mi gnas pas stoṅ pa, de bźin du skye mched bcu gñis kyaṅ miṅ daṅ gzugs tsam du zad kyi, bdag daṅ bdag gir med par rtog pas na skye mched rnams la groṅ stoṅ lta bur ’du śes pa źes bya’o.skye ba’i gnas thams cad la mi smon pa’i ’du śes źes bya ba la skye ba’i gnas ni bźi ste: 1) mṅal nas skye ba daṅ, 2) rdzus te skye ba daṅ, 3) sgo ṅa las skye ba daṅ, 4) drod gśer las skye ba’o. skyes na de’i rgyus skye ba daṅ, rga ba daṅ, na ba daṅ, ’chi ba la sogs pa’i sdug bsṅal ’byuṅ bar mthoṅ bas skye gnas de dag tu skye bar mi ’dod ciṅ skye ba mi tshol bas na mi smon pa’i ’du śes źes bya’o.gñen po’i sa la yon tan du lta ba yaṅ rnam pa gñis te, rnam par grol ba’i bde ba’i rten du gyur pa daṅ, ’khor ba las brgal źiṅ sdug bsṅal kun spaṅs par blta ba’o. ’di lta ste, mya ṅan las ’das pa ni ’khor ba’i gñen po yin te, mya ṅan las ’das pa la rnam par grol ba’i bde ba thams cad kyi rten du lta bas mya ṅan las ’das pa la gnas su ’du śes pa źes bya’o. de ñid la ’khor ba las brgal źiṅ sdug bsṅal thams cad spaṅs par lta bas na skyabs su ’du śes pa’o. Cf. also supra, ṭ. fol. 152b1-2.


gaṅ ’di ltar ston pa daṅ, rab tu ston pa daṅ, ’di ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i ñan thos kyi theg pa la mkhas pa źes bya’o.

yaivaṃrūpā deśanā prakāśanedam ucyate bodhisattvasya śrāvakayānakauśalyam.What then is the bodhisattva’s skill with the way of isolated buddhas?

Teaching and explaining thus is called the bodhisattva’s skill with the way of disciples.


de la byaṅ chub sems dpa’i raṅ saṅs rgyas kyi theg pa la mkhas pa gaṅ źe na?

tatra katamad bodhisattvasya pratyekabuddhayānakauśalyam?

What then is the bodhisattva’s skill with the way of isolated buddhas?

ñan thos kyi theg pa la mkhas pa bstan nas raṅ saṅs rgyas kyi theg pa la mkhas pa bstan pa’i phyir de la byaṅ chub sems dpa’i raṅ saṅs rgyas kyi theg pa la mkhas pa gaṅ źe na źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs te, byaṅ chub sems dpa’ rnams kyis śes par bya ba’i raṅ saṅs rgyas kyi theg pa ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i raṅ saṅs rgyas kyi theg pa źes bya ste,
gaṅ dag bskal pa gcig gis ye śes kyi tshogs yoṅs su bskaṅs te, gźan gyi man ṅag med par ’phags pa’i lam thob nas, khams gsum pa’i ’dod chags daṅ bral bar źugs pa de dag ni sñiṅ rje chen po med pas gźan la luṅ dbog pa’i bya ba med pa daṅ, bdag gcig pu saṅs rgyas par byed pas raṅ saṅs rgyas so – "Having fulfilled the accumulation of knowledge (jñānasaṃbhāra) in one kalpa (a hundred kalpas (kalpaśata)? cf. infra), attaining the holy way (āryamārga) without the instruction of others, and entering the state of no passion for the threefold world, they do not teach others since they have no great compassion (mahākaruṇā). Waking up alone they are isolated buddhas (ekākino budhyante pratyekabuddhāḥ)".
Cf. Pratyekabuddhabhūmi p. 346-10: yathāpīhaikatyaḥ prathameṇa pratyekabuddhamārgeṇa paripūrṇakalpaśatasaṃbhāraḥ / kalpaśatasyātyayād asati ca buddhānām utpāde anācāryakaṃ saptatriṃśadbodhipakṣyān dharmān bhāvayitvā pratyekāṃ bodhim abhisaṃbudhyate ca sarvakleśaprahāṇam arhattvaṃ sākṣāt karoti //
raṅ saṅs rgyas de dag rnam par grol ba’i sar phyin par byed pa’i theg pa ni raṅ saṅs rgyas kyi theg pa ste, gaṅ źe na źes bya ba ni raṅ saṅs rgyas kyi theg pa la mkhas pa dris pa’o. de yaṅ rnam pa gsum du rig par bya ste, 1) rgyu daṅ, 2) rkyen daṅ, 3) ’bras bu’o.


rnam pa gaṅ daṅ rkyen gaṅ gis raṅ saṅs rgyas rnams ṅes par ’byuṅ bar ’gyur ba’i rnam pa de dag daṅ rkyen de dag byaṅ chub sems dpas yaṅ dag pa ji lta ba bźin du rab tu śes te.de dag gaṅ źe na?

yair ākārair yaiḥ pratyayaiḥ pratyekabuddhā niryāsyanti, tān ākārāṃs tān pratyayān bodhisattvo yathābhūtaṃ prajānāti.te katame?

The forms [or rather, causes (hetu) ] and conditions by which the isolated buddhas escape the world, these the bodhisattva knows as they are.What are they?

de rnam pa gaṅ źes bya bas rgyu 1) bstan pa yin te, rgyu gaṅ dag gis bya ba’i tha tshig go; rkyen gaṅ źes bya bas rkyen 2) bstan pa yin no; raṅ saṅs rgyas ’byuṅ źes ’bras bu 3) bstan pa yin te, khams gsum las byuṅ nas ñon moṅs pa thams cad spaṅs te, mya ṅan las ’das par gyur pa ni raṅ saṅs rgyas rnams ’byuṅ bar ’gyur źes bya’o; yaṅ dag pa ji lta ba bźin du rab tu śes źes bya ba ni rgyu daṅ rkyen daṅ ’bras bu rnams phyin ci ma log par khoṅ du chud ces bya ba’i don te, de ltar khoṅ du chud pa ni raṅ saṅs rgyas kyi theg pa la mkhas pa yin no źes bya bar sbyar ro. de dag gaṅ źe na rgyu daṅ, rkyen daṅ, ’bras bu de dag gaṅ źe na źes bya ba’i don te, de gsum bstan pa’i phyir ’di lta ste źes gsuṅs so. de la 1) ’dun pa daṅ brtson ’grus źes bya ba nas brtsams te, rab tu dben par gnas mal ’cha’ ba źes bya ba yan chad kyis rgyu bstan yin no, 2) bsñen par dka’ źes bya ba nas brtsams te, raṅ ’byuṅ gi ye śes kyis rab tu rgal źes bya ba yan chad kyis rkyen bstan to, 3) dmigs pa la gnas pa thob ces bya ba nas brtsams te, dmigs pa gaṅ yaṅ ruṅ ba la rkyen gyis ye śes rtogs pa źes bya ba yan chad kyis ’bras bu bstan to.
Cf. Pratyekabuddhabhūmi p. 3410-13: yathāpīhaikatyo dvitīyatṛtīyābhyāṃ pratyekabuddhamārgābhyāṃ tena hetunā tena pratyayena asaty evaṃ buddhānām utpāde anācāryakaṃ saptatriṃśadbodhipakṣyān dharmān bhāvayitvā dharmābhisamayaṃ karoti.


’di lta ste: ’dun pa daṅ, brtson ’grus daṅ, bag yod pa chen pos ñan thos kyi lta bu ma yin pa’i sbyin pa’i bsod nams kyi tshogs sogs pa daṅ, tshul khrims kyi bsod nams kyi tshogs sogs pa daṅ;thos pa ñuṅ ba la chos kyi nan tan byed pa daṅ;saṅs rgyas bcom ldan ’das la yaṅ rim gro daṅ bsñen bkur byed pa la yaṅ źum pa med pa daṅ;dbaṅ po bar ma daṅ;rtag tu rab tu ’byuṅ ba la gźol ba daṅ;don ñuṅ ba daṅ; byed pa ñuṅ ba daṅ;’du ’dzi la mi dga’ źiṅ dben pa la dga’ ba daṅrab tu dben par gnas mal ’cha’ ba daṅ;

yaduta na śrāvakabhūto dānapuṇyasaṃbhāropacayaḥ śīlapuṇyasaṃbhāropacayo mahācchandavīryāpramādena;dharmapratipattiḥ alpaśrutatve;upasthānaparyupāsanānavalīnatā buddheṣu bhagavatsu;madhyendriyatā;nityapravrajyānimnatā;alpārthatā, alpakṛtyatā;asaṃgaṇikārāmatā, vivekaratiḥ,praviviktaśayanāsanatā.

[1. The causes (hetu) are:]Heaping up the accumulation of merit from giving, heaping up the accumulation of merit from morality, not like that of the disciples, but caused by great eagerness, vigour and absence of negligence;progress in religion with little learning;no despondency in serving the Lords and Buddhas;having medium abilities;being always bent on the ascetic life;having small ambitions [namely, one’s own peace, liberation and extinction], and doing few things [for others’ peace and extinction because of small compassion, making no effort for the sake of this];[having few vices] being [bodily] displeased with social life, [mental] delight in solitude [being far from the thought-constructions of cupidity and aversion (rāgadveṣavikalpa) ],having lodgings in solitude [e. g. under a tree or in a cave].

de la rgyu rnam pa gsum ste, 1) bsags pa’i rgyu daṅ, 2) saṅs rgyas mñes par byed pa’i rgyu daṅ, 3) rigs so.1) de la bsags pa yaṅ rnam pa gñis te, a) gaṅ gis bsags pa daṅ, b) gaṅ bsags pa’o. de la a) gaṅ gis bsags pa ni ’dun pa daṅ, bag yod pa daṅ, brtson ’grus chen po gsum gyis bsags so; b) gaṅ bsags pa ni sbyin pa daṅ, tshul khrims daṅ, thos pa gsum bsags so.
a) gaṅ gis bsags pa yaṅ rnam pa gsum ste, rgyu daṅ, rkyen daṅ, sgrub pa’o; de la chen po’i sgra ni ’dun pa la sogs pa’i tshig gsum po so so daṅ yaṅ sbyar te, ’dun pa chen po daṅ, brtson ’grus chen po daṅ, bag yod pa chen po źes bya bar sbyar ro. de la ’dun pa ni dkon mchog daṅ bden pa daṅ las la yid ches nas ’di kho na bden gyi, gźan du ma yin no źes ’dzin pa’o, ’dis ni rgyu smras pa yin te, yid ches par gyur na brtson ’grus rtsom pas so. brtson ’grus źes bya ba la, spaṅ bar bya ba ma lus par spoṅ ba daṅ, thob par bya ba thob par byed pa la sems spro ba ni brtson ’grus te, ’dis ni rkyen bstan pa yin te, dge ba sgrub pa rnams brtson ’grus la brten pa’i phyir ro. bag yod pa źes bya ba la gcig pu dgon pa na gnas śiṅ ’du ’dzi daṅ mi ’dre ba ni bag yod pa ste, ’dis ni sgrub par byed pa bstan pa yin no. ci’i phyir źe na? spaṅ bar bya ba daṅ bsgrub par bya ba gñis ni bag yod par bsgrubs so.
b) gaṅ bsags pa yaṅ rnam pa gsum ste, loṅs spyod kyi rgyu bsags pa daṅ, bde ’gro’i rgyu bsags pa daṅ, rnam par grol ba’i rgyu bsags pa’o; yaṅ na ser sna’i gñen po bsags pa daṅ, ’dod pa la chags pa’i gñen po bsags pa daṅ, ñon moṅs pa’i gñen po bsags pa’o; de la chen po źes bya ba ni raṅ saṅs rgyas kyi ’dun pa daṅ brtson ’grus la sogs pa ñan thos dag pas lhag pas na chen po źes bya’o, ñan thos kyi lta bu ma yin pa’i źes bya ba ni ñan thos kyi bas śas che źes bya ba’i don to, sbyin pa’i bsod nams kyi tshogs sogs pa źes bya bas ser sna’i gñen po bsags pa bstan te, sbyin pas rnam par grol ba thob pa’i rgyur gyur pa rnams ni tshogs bsags pa źes bya’o, tshul khrims kyia bsod nams kyi tshogs bsags pa źes bya bas ’dod pa la chags pa’i gñen po bsags pa bstan to. gaṅ gis, gaṅ gaṅ gi phyir tshul bsruṅs pa ni tshul khrims te, gaṅ gis bsruṅs pa ni mi dge ba bcu las ldog ciṅ rnam par grol ba ’dod pa’i sems kyis so, gaṅ bsruṅs pa ni yan lag drug pa’i tshul khrims bsruṅ ba’o, gaṅ gi phyir bsruṅ ba ni mya ṅan las ’das pa thob par bya ba’i phyir bsruṅ ba’o. thos pa ñuṅ ba la chos kyi nan tan byed ces bya bas ñon moṅs pa’i gñen po bsags pa bstan te, thos pa la mi dga’ bas cuṅ zad thos pa ni thos pa ñuṅ ba’o, chos kyi nan tan byed ces bya ba ni byaṅ chub kyi phyogs kyi chos rnams bsgoms śiṅ sgrub par byed ces bya ba’i don to. de ni ’di skad du ñan thos ltar thos pa mi maṅ bar thos thos pa cuṅ zad cig gis chos kyi nan tan byed do źes bstan pa’o.2) saṅs rgyas mñes par byed pa yaṅ rnam pa gñis te, chos ñid kyis mñes par byed pa daṅ, zaṅ ziṅ gis mñes par byed pa’o. saṅs rgyas bcom ldan ’das la yaṅ rim gro daṅ źes bya bas chos ñid kyis mñes par byed pa bstan te, ma rig pa’i gñid las saṅ ciṅ śes bya thams cad thugs su chud pas na saṅs rgyas so. bdud bźi bcom pas na bcom ldan ’das te, des ji skad du bstan pa’i bka’ luṅ daṅ bslab pa’i tshig las ’da’ bar mi byed pa ni saṅs rgyas bcom ldan ’das la rim gror byed pa daṅ bsñen bkur byed pa źes bya bas zaṅ ziṅ gis mñes par byed pa bstan te, bskal pa brgya’i bar du phyag ’tshal ba daṅ bskor ba daṅ gos la sogs pas bsñen bkur byed pa’i phyir ro. Cf. Pratyekabuddhabhūmi p. 3316: kalpaśataṃ buddhotpādam ārāgayati; and ibid. p. 3320-21, p. 3328-29.
źum pa med ces bya ba ni mñes pa rnam pa gñis byed pa la sems spro źiṅ spa goṅ ba med ces bya ba’i don to. des ni mdor na gaṅ la, gaṅ, gaṅ gis mñes par byed pa bstan te, gaṅ la mñes par byed pa ni saṅs rgyas bcom ldan ’das la’o; gaṅ ni rim gro byed pa daṅ bkur stis so, gaṅ gis ni źum pa med pa’i sems kyis so.
mdo gźan dag las raṅ saṅs rgyas gźan la ma mñan par raṅ gi blos chos rtogs pa daṅ, saṅs rgyas ’jig rten du mi ’byuṅ ba’i tshe raṅ saṅs rgyas ’byuṅ ṅo źes bśad pa yaṅ raṅ saṅs rgyas zag pa med pa’i chos mṅon par rtogs pa’i tshe gźan gyi luṅ la mi brten pa daṅ, raṅ saṅs rgyas kyi ’bras bu thob nas, gdod saṅs rgyas mi bźugs pa na ’byuṅ ba la bya’i, ’dir ni daṅ po slob ciṅ tshogs bsog pa la bya bas ñes pa med do – "According to other sūtras the isolated buddhas are born at the time when no Buddhas are born in the world, not serving other Buddhas but understanding the dharma with their own intelligence (mati). The isolated buddha is not dependent on the instructions of others at the time he realizes the unsullied moments of existence (anāsravadharmābhisamaya); having attained the fruit (phala) of an isolated buddha he becomes that when no Buddha is there, but here [in this sūtra] one is concerned with the beginning when he is learning and accumulating, so there is no mistake [in saying that he is serving the Lords and Buddhas]".3) rigs kyaṅ rnam pa gsum ste, a) ṅa rgyal spyod pa’i rigs daṅ, b) sñiṅ rje chuṅ ba’i rigs daṅ, c) ñon moṅs pa chuṅ ba’i rigs so.
a) ṅa rgyal spyod pa’i rigs kyaṅ rnam pa gñis te, dbaṅ po ’briṅ daṅ sbyor ba dam pa la gnas pa’o. dbaṅ po bar ma źes bya bas dbaṅ po ’briṅ bstan te, dbaṅ po rnam pa gsum ste, rab daṅ, bar ma daṅ, tha ma’o. raṅ saṅs rgyas rnams ni dbaṅ po bar ma ste, dbaṅ po ’briṅ gi rigs can no.
The division into the three-fold gotra is modelled after Pratyekabuddhabhūmi p. 337-14: pratyekabuddhagotraṃ katamat / tatra trilakṣaṇaṃ veditavyaṃ / prakṛtyā pratyekabuddhāḥ prāg evābhisaṃbodhān mandarajaskagotrā bhavanti / ye naiṣām saṃsarge cittam na krāmanty ekārāmatāyāṃ krāmanti / prakṛtyā pratyekabuddhāḥ prāg evābhisaṃbodhān mandakāruṇyā bhavanti / ye naiṣām dharmadeśanāyāṃ sattvārthakriyāyāṃ cittam na krāmanty alpotsukavihāritāyāṃ krāmanti / prakṛtyā pratyekabuddhāḥ prāg evābhisaṃbodhān madhyendriyaś (sic, read -yā) bhavanti mānacaritajātīyāś ca / ye nācāryaṃ niḥpratidvandvam abhisaṃbodham abhilaṣanti //rtag tu rab tu ’byuṅ ba la gźol źes bya bas sbyor ba dam pa la gnas pa bstan te, rtag tu ni dus thams cad do.
ji skad du bcom ldan ’das kyis bśad pa: skra daṅ kha spu bregs gos ṅur smrig bgos te, yaṅ dag par dad pas khyim nas khyim med par rab tu byuṅ źes gsuṅs pas ni rab tu byuṅ ba la gźol ba’o. Cf. kesamassuṃ oharetvā kāsāyāni vatthāni acchādetvā agārasmā anagāriyaṃ pabbajati, phrase quoted passim, for Pāli references v. Pāli Concordance and PTSD, s.v. agāra, agāriya, kesamassu, kāsāya.
’dis dge sloṅ gi phun sum tshogs pa rnam pa bźi bstan te, cha lugs phun sum tshogs pa daṅ, las phun sum tshogs pa daṅ, bsam pa phun sum tshogs pa daṅ, gnas phun sum tshogs pa’o. de la skra daṅ ka spu bregs te gos ṅur smrig bgos źes bya bas cha lugs phun sum tshogs pa bstan te, cha lugs ’di ni ñon moṅs pa daṅ ñe ba’i ñon moṅs pa daṅ mi mthun pa yin pas, khyim na gnas pa’i cha lugs phun sum tshogs pa’o. yaṅ dag par źes bya bas las phun sum tshogs pa bstan te, gsol ba daṅ bźi’i las kyis rab tu byuṅ ba’i phyir ro. dad pas źes bya bas bsam pa phun sum tshogs pa bstan te, rgyal po daṅ rkun po’i ’jigs pas rab tu byuṅ ba ni ma yin gyi, dad pas rab tu byuṅ ba’i phyir ro. khyim nas khyim med par rab tu byuṅ źes bya bas gnas phun sum tshogs pa bstan te, khyim na gnas pa rnams kyi gnas rab tu mi bzad pa de btaṅ nas khyim med pa’i śiṅ druṅ la sogs pa la gnas pas so.b) sñiṅ rje chuṅ ba’i rigs kyaṅ rnam pa gñis te, bdag ’ba’ źig gi don la ’jug pa daṅ, gźan gyi don mi byed pa’o. de la don ñuṅ ba źes bya bas bdag ’ba’ źig gi don la ’jug pa bstan te, bdag źi bar bya ba daṅ, grol bar bya ba daṅ, mya ṅan las ’das par bya ba tsam las bya ba gźan mi byed pa’i phyir ro. byed pa ñuṅ źes bya bas gźan gyi don mi byed pa bstan te, gźan źi bar bya ba daṅ, mya ṅan las ’das par bya ba la mi ’bad par bya bas so.c) ñon moṅs pa chuṅ ba’i rigs kyaṅ rnam pa gsum ste, 1) lus dben pa la dga’ ba daṅ, 2) sems dben pa la dga’ ba daṅ, 3) gnas dben pa la dga’ ba’o.
1) ’du ’dzi la mi dga’ źiṅ źes bya bas lus dben pa la dga’ ba bstan te, raṅ bźin gyis ’gro ba maṅ po daṅ ’dre bar ma mos śiṅ bse ru bźin du gcig pur gnas par mos pa’i phyir ro. Cf. Pratyekabuddhabhūmi p. 3421-23: naikāṃśena ekārāmo bhavaty ekavihārī / api tu vargavihārī bhavati / śiṣṭo vihāras tasyāpi yathā khaḍgaviṣāṇakalpaś ca //
2) dben pa la dga’ ba źes bya bas sems dben pa la dga’ ba bstan te, de dag ’dod pa daṅ khoṅ khro ba’i rnam par rtog pa riṅ du spoṅ bar mos pas so.
3) rab tu dben par gnas mal ’cha’ ba źes bya bas gnas dben pa la dga’ ba bstan te, śiṅ druṅ daṅ ri sul na gnas ’cha’ ba’i phyir ro.


bsñen par dka’ ba daṅ;mthu che ba daṅ;sbyin pa’i gnas kyi sa la mṅon par dga’ ba daṅ;rgyun mi ’chad par rten ciṅ ’brel bar ’byuṅ ba la lta ba daṅ;ṅes par ’byuṅ ba’i dbyiṅs gcig la rtog pa daṅ;raṅ byuṅ gi ye śes kyis rab tu rgal ba daṅ;

durāsadatā;mahānubhāvatā;dakṣiṇīyabhūmyabhiratiḥ;satatasamitapratītyasamutpādadarśanatā;niḥsaraṇaikadhātupratyavekṣā;svayaṃbhujñānaprottīrṇatā.

[2. The conditions (pratyaya) are:]being difficult to overpower [having few vices and great virtue];having great magical power;being delighted by [the fruit of religious practice] the stage where one is to be honoured [namely, that of an arhat];continuous reflection on dependent origination;having in view the one sphere which is deliverance;transcending [the three worlds (traidhātuka) ] by means of self-originated knowledge.

rkyen kyaṅ rnam pa bźi ste, 1) yon tan daṅ, 2) gnas pa daṅ, 3) rtogs pa daṅ, 4) ’byuṅ ba’o.1) yon tan yaṅ rnam pa gsum ste, a) ñon moṅs pa chuṅ źiṅ dge ba che ba daṅ, b) rdzu ’phrul che ba daṅ, c) ’bras bu’i sa la mṅon par dga’ ba’o.
a) bsñen par dka’ źes bya bas ñon moṅs pa chuṅ źiṅ dge ba che bar bstan te, mthu daṅ gzi brjid daṅ byin rnams la gźan gyis zil gyis mi non źiṅ des gźan zil gyis gnon pa’i phyir ro.
b) mthu che ba źes bya bas rdzu ’phrul che ba bstan te, stod nas me ’bar ba daṅ, smad nas chu draṅ mo’i rgyun ’bab pa daṅ, gcig tu gyur nas maṅ por ’gyur ba daṅ, maṅ por gyur nas gcig tu ’gyur ba la sogs pa’i mthu daṅ ldan pa’i phyir ro.
c) sbyin pa’i gnas kyi sa la mṅon par dga’ ba źes bya bas ’bras bu’i sa la dga’ ba bstan te, sbyin pa’i gnas kyi sa ni ’gro ba thams cad kyi bsod nams kyi źiṅ du gyur pa’i dus dgra bcom pa’i ’bras bu thob pa ste, mṅon par dga’ ba ni ’bras bu de thob par bya bar sems mos pa’o.2) rgyun mi ’chad par rten ciṅ ’brel bar ’byuṅ ba la lta ba źes bya bas gnas pa bstan te, rgyun mi ’chad pa źes bya bas ni rtag tu źes bya ba’i don to. rgyu daṅ rkyen la brten nas dus mñam du ’bras bu ’byuṅ ba ni rten ciṅ ’brel bar ’byuṅ ba ste, de yaṅ phyi daṅ naṅ gi rnam pa gñis so: de la phyi’i rten ciṅ ’brel ba ni sa bon gyi rkyen gyis myu gu la sogs pa’o; naṅ gi rten ciṅ ’brel bar ’byuṅ ba ni ma rig pa’i rkyen gyis ’du byed ces bya ba la sogs pa’o. lta ba ni phyi naṅ gi chos ’di rgyu rkyen las ’byuṅ ba tsam du zad kyi, bdag daṅ byed pa po med par rtog pa’o.3) ṅes par ’byuṅ ba’i dbyiṅs gcig la rtog pa źes bya bas rtog pa bstan te, ṅes par ’byuṅ ba’i dbyiṅs ni mya ṅan las ’das pa’i dbyiṅs so, mya ṅan las ’das pa ’ba’ źig tu gnas pa daṅ ’gro bar sems pa ni ṅes par ’byuṅ ba’i dbyiṅs gcig la rtog pa źes bya’o.4) raṅ ’byuṅ gi ye śes kyis rab tu rgal ba źes bya bas ’byuṅ ba bstan te, bdag ñid kyi śes rab daṅ ye śes kyis gaṅ zag la bdag med par rtogs nas ñon moṅs pa spaṅs te, khams gsum las rgal bar gyur pa ni raṅ ’byuṅ gi ye śes kyis rab tu rgal ba źes bya’o.


dmigs pa la ’jug pa ’thob pa daṅ;bsam gtan daṅ, rnam par thar pa daṅ, tiṅ ṅe ’dzin daṅ, sñoms par ’jug pa la rgyun ma chad pa daṅ;gźan gyi driṅ la mi ’jog pa’i ye śes skyed pa daṅ;dmigs pa gaṅ yaṅ ruṅ ba la rkyen gyi ye śes rtogs pa ste;

ālambanapraveśaprāpaṇatā;dhyānavimokṣasamādhisamāpattisātatyam;aparapraṇeyajñānotpādatā;anyatarānyatarālambane pratyayajñānāvabodhatā.

[3. The fruit (phala) is:]Attaining the [ability of] entering [by means of concentration] an object [of meditation, like dependent origination];continuity of the meditations, deliverances, concentrations and states of concentration;producing knowledge [of the unborn] which is not dependent on the instructions of others;awakening to the knowledge of conditions involved with any object.

’bras bu thob pa yaṅ rnam pa gñis te, 1) tiṅ ṅe ’dzin thob pa daṅ, 2) mṅon par byaṅ chub pa thob pa’o.1) tiṅ ṅe ’dzin thob pa yaṅ rnam pa gñis te, a) mi g-yo ba thob pa daṅ, b) rgyun du yid la byed pa thob pa’o.
a) dmigs pa la ’jug pa thob pa daṅ źes bya bas mi g-yo ba thob pa bstan te, dmigs pa ni rten ciṅ ’brel bar ’byuṅ ba la sogs pa tiṅ ṅe ’dzin gyi yul rnams so. ’jug pa thob pa ni yul la dmigs pa’i tshe sems rtse gcig pa la gnas pa thob ste, phyi rol du mi g-yeṅ bar nus pa’o.
b) bsam gtan daṅ, rnam par thar pa daṅ, tiṅ ṅe ’dzin daṅ, sñoms par ’jug pa rgyun mi chad pa ces bya bas rgyun du yid la byed pa thob pa bstan te, rgyun mi chad pa ni de dag la rgyun du yid la byed pa’o. Cf. Msa. p. 922: sātatyamanaskāraḥ.2) mṅon par byaṅ chub pa yaṅ rnam pa gñis te, a) ston pa daṅ rjes su ston pa med par mṅon par byaṅ chub pa daṅ, b) rten ciṅ ’brel bar ’byuṅ ba mṅon par byaṅ chub pa’o.
a) gźan gyi driṅ la mi ’jog pa’i ye śes bskyed pa daṅ źes bya bas ston pa daṅ rjes su ston pa med par mṅon par byaṅ chub pa bstan te, mkhan po daṅ slob dpon gyi man ṅag mi rten par zad la mi skye ba’i ye śes skyed par byed ces bya ba’i don to – (rec:) ācāryopādhyāyopadeśam anāśrito nirodhe ’nutpādajñānam utpādayatīty arthaḥ.
b) dmigs pa gaṅ yaṅ ruṅ ba la rkyen gyi ye śes rtogs pa ste źes bya bas rten ciṅ ’brel bar ’byuṅ ba mṅon par byaṅ chub par bstan te, dmigs pa’i yul gaṅ yaṅ ruṅ ste, chos thams cad rten ciṅ ’brel bar ’byuṅ ba’i ṅo bo ñid du śes śiṅ khoṅ du chud ces bya ba’i don to.


gaṅ de ltar ’chad pa daṅ, ston pa daṅ, rab tu ston pa, ’di ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i raṅ saṅs rgyas kyi theg pa la mkhas pa źes bya’o.

yaivaṃrūpā vyākhyā deśanā prakāśanedam ucyate bodhisattvasya pratyekabuddhayānakauśalyam.

Expounding, teaching and explaining thus is called the bodhisattva’s skill with the way of isolated buddhas.

de ltar źes bya ba ni goṅ du bśad pa’i tshul ltar ro, ’chad pa ni don to, ston pa ni tshig go, rab tu ston pa ni don daṅ tshig go; yaṅ na rgyu ston pa ni ’chad pa’o, rkyen ’chad pa ni ston pa’o, ’bras bu ’chad pa ni rab tu ston pa’o.


de la byaṅ chub sems dpa’i theg pa chen po la mkhas pa gaṅ źes na? byaṅ chub sems dpa’i theg pa chen po la mkhas pa ni dpag tu med de, de las phyogs tsam źig bstan to.

tatra katamad bodhisattvasya mahāyānakauśalyam? bodhisattvasya mahāyānakauśalyam aprameyaṃ tasmāt tatra diṅmātram upadiṣṭam.

(p. 80) What then is the bodhisattva’s skill with the great way? The bodhisattva’s skill with the great way is immeasurable, so only an indication of it is taught.

byaṅ chub sems dpa’i theg pa la mkhas pa bstan pa’i phyir de la byaṅ chub sems dpa’i theg pa chen po la mkhas pa gaṅ źes na źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs so. byaṅ chub sems dpa’ rnams kyi khoṅ du chud par bya ba’i theg pa’am, byaṅ chub sems dpa’ rnam mi gnas pa’i mya ṅan las ’da’ bar phyin par byed pa’i theg pa ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i theg pa ste, ’dis ’gro bas theg pa’am, ’dir ’gro bas theg pa’o. de la ’dis ’gro ba ni pha rol tu phyin pa daṅ sa rnams kyis ’gro bas na de dag la theg pa źes bya’o. ’dir ’gro ba ni saṅs rgyas kyi sar ’gro ba ste, de la theg pa źes bya’o.
theg pa yaṅ yin la chen po yaṅ yin pas theg pa chen po ste, chen po rnam pa bdun pa daṅ ldan pa’i phyir ro. chen po rnam pa bdun ni 1) chos che ba daṅ, 2) sems bskyed pa che ba daṅ, 3) bsam pa che ba daṅ, 4) mos pa che ba daṅ, 5) tshogs che ba daṅ, 6) dus che ba daṅ, 7) thob pa che ba’o:
1) śes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa stoṅ phrag brgya la sogs pa mdo sde tshad med pa’i phyir chos che ba’o. 2) sems can thams cad kyi don du bla na med pa yaṅ dag par rdzogs pa’i byaṅ chub tu sems bskyed pas sems bskyed pa che ba’o. 3) bdag daṅ gźan mñam pa ñid kyi bsam pa thob pas na bsam pa che ba’o. 4) zab ciṅ rgya che ba’i mdo sde la mos pa’i phyir mos pa che ba’o. 5) skad cig ma re re la yaṅ bsod nams kyi tshogs dpag tu med pa sogs pas na tshogs che ba’o. 6) bskal pa chen po graṅs med pa gsum gyi bar du rgyun du sbyar bas na dus che ba’o. 7) bla na med pa’i byaṅ chub kyi ’bras bu thob pas na thob pa che ba’o.
theg pa de’i raṅ bźin daṅ, rgyu daṅ ’bras bu la sogs pa rtogs pa ni theg pa chen po la mkhas pa’o. gaṅ źe na? źes bya ba ni dris pa’o. byaṅ chub sems dpa’i theg pa chen po la mkhas pa ni dpag tu med de źes bya ba la, theg pa ni bla na med pa’i byaṅ chub tu phyin par byed pa ste, theg pa de las ’das pa daṅ ma ’oṅs pa daṅ da ltar gyi dus kyi sems can graṅs med tshad med pa rnams ’tshaṅ rgya ba’i phyir theg pa de tshad med do, theg pa tshad med pas de la mkhas pa’i śes rab kyaṅ tshad med pa’i phyir theg pa chen po la mkhas pa ni dpag tu med do źes gsuṅs so. de ltar theg pa chen po tshad med pas na thams cad bstan par mi nus te, de bas na de las phyogs tsam źig bstan to źes gsuṅs te, mdo tsam źig bstan to źes bya ba’i don to.
tshad med pa de yaṅ yon tan bcu gcig tu rig par bya ste, 1) sems bskyed pa’i yon tan daṅ, 2) śes bya’i sgrib pa spaṅs te śes pa khoṅ du chud pa’i yon tan daṅ, 3) rgyu bsags pa’i yon tan daṅ, 4) spyod pa dag pa’i yon tan daṅ, 5) mṅon par byaṅ chub pa’i yon tan daṅ, 6) mñam par phan ’dogs pa’i yon tan daṅ, 7) ñan thos daṅ so so’i skye bo’i lam las rgal ba’i yon tan daṅ, 8) bgegs bcom pa’i yon tan daṅ, 9) ñon moṅs pa daṅ ñe ba’i ñon moṅs pa spaṅs pa’i yon tan daṅ, 10) bdag daṅ gźan gyi don phun sum tshogs pa’i yon tan daṅ, 11) ’bras bu phun sum tshogs pa’i yon tan no.
Eleven qualities of the immeasurable are enumerated both in ṭ and in the mūla, though the number given above is ten.


theg pa de ni sems can thams cad kyi go skabs ’byed pas na, dpag tu med pa’o;theg pa de ni chags pa med pa’i ye śes la btaṅ ba ste, sgrib pa med pa’o;theg pa de ni sems can thams cad ñe bar ’tsho ba ste, bsod nams kyi tshogs daṅ dge ba’i rtsa ba thams cad bsags pa’o;theg pa de ni sems can thams cad kyi sems kyi spyod pa la las su ruṅ ba’i phyir, pha rol tu phyin pa thams cad yoṅs su sbyaṅ ba byas pa’o;theg pa de ni thogs pa med par byaṅ chub kyi sñiṅ por ’gro bas na, thams cad mkhyen pa’i ye śes kyi tshogs ñams su len par byed pa’o;theg pa de ni sems can thams cad sbyin pa’i gnas kyi phyir, sems can thams cad la thogs pa med pa’i ’od zer mñam par gtoṅ ba’o;theg pa de ni saṅs rgyas kyi chos thams cad mṅon sum du gyur pa’i phyir, lam ṅan pa’i ’jigs pa thams cad las ’das pa’o;theg pa de ni byaṅ chub kyi phyogs kyi chos thams cad daṅ rten ciṅ ’brel bar ’byuṅ ba’i rgyal mtshan daṅ ba dan bsgreṅ ba ste, bdud daṅ, phas kyi rgol ba daṅ, ṅan pa’i tshogs can gyi tshogs thams cad rab tu ’joms pa’o;theg pa de ni saṅs rgyas kyi theg pa sgrib pa med par gyur pa ste, mtha’ daṅ, mtha’ med pa daṅ, rtag pa daṅ, chad pa daṅ, ’byuṅ ba daṅ, ’jig pa daṅ, lta bar gyur pa thams cad daṅ, kun nas ldaṅ ba daṅ, sgrib pa daṅ, chod pa daṅ, the tshom daṅ, ’gyod pa sel ba’o;theg pa de ni lhag pa’i bsam pa daṅ sñiṅ rje chen pos phye bas na, chos thams cad phun sum tshogs pa, rin po che thams cad daṅ ldan pa phun sum tshogs pa thams cad rñed pa, mi slu ba’i lam du ’gro ba, sems can thams cad ñe bar ’tsho ba’o;theg pa de ni thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med pa ste, stobs bcu daṅ, mi ’jigs pa daṅ, saṅs rgyas kyi chos ma ’dres pa daṅ, mtshan daṅ dpe byad bzaṅ po daṅ, lus daṅ ṅag daṅ sems kyi rgyan gyis brgyan pa ste;

tad yānam aprameyaṃ sarvasattvāvakāśatvāt;tad yānam anāvaraṇam asaṅgajñānopanāmitam;tad yānaṃ sarvapuṇyasaṃbhārakuśalamūlopacayaṃ sarvasattvopajīvyam;tad yānaṃ sarvapāramitākṛtaparikarmaṃ sarvasattvānāṃ cittacaryākarmaṇyatayā;tad yānaṃ sarvajñajñānasaṃbhāropādānam apratihatabodhimaṇḍagamanatvāt;tad yānaṃ sarvasattveṣu samāpratihataraśmipramocakaṃ sarvasattvadakṣiṇeyatayā;tad yānaṃ sarvakumārgabhayātikrāntaṃ sarvabuddhadharmasaṃmukhībhūtatayā;tad yānaṃ sarvamāraparapravādikugaṇigaṇapramathi sarvabodhipakṣikadharmapratītyasamutpādasamucchritadhvajapatākam;tad yānaṃ sarvāntānantaśāśvatocchedabhavavibhavadṛṣṭigataparyutthānāvaraṇanīvaraṇavicikitsākaukṛtyāpaham anāvaraṇabhūtaṃ buddhayānam;tad yānaṃ sarvadharmasaṃpatsarvaratnasaṃpatprāptyaviṣaṃvādakapathagamanasarvasattvopajīvakam mahādhyāśayakaruṇāprabhāvitatvāt;tad yānaṃ daśabalavaiśāradyāveṇikabuddhadharmalakṣaṇānuvyañjanakāyavākcittālaṃkārālaṃkṛtaṃ sarvato ’navadyam.

That way is immeasurable since it opens up a possibility for all living beings;that way is unhindered being bent upon unattached knowledge;that way is the accumulation of all merit and roots of good, and thus nourishes all beings;that way is the fulfilment of all the perfections since it relates to the mental behaviour of all beings;that way is attaining the accumulation of knowledge which leads to omniscience since it is going unhindered to the place of awakening;that way emits unhindered rays of light similarly on all beings since all beings are to be honoured;that way is beyond fear of any bad ways since all qualities of a Buddha are made manifest;that way vanquishes all the assemblies of the Evil One, antagonists and bad teachers as it flies the flags and banners of the conditions conducive to awakening and dependent origination;that way does away with all viewpoints concerning limits or absence of limits, eternalism or nihilism, existence or nonexistence, [and further,] the appearance [of vices], hindrances, obstructions, doubt and regret, as it is the unhindered Buddha-way;that way possesses all the parts of religious practice, the attainment of possessing all jewels [being religious ways], traversing the true way [leading to the extinction which is found nowhere (apratiṣṭhitanirvāṇa) ], it nourishes all beings, since it is distinguished by its great determination and compassion;that way is adorned with ornaments for body, speech and mind, being the ten powers, the intrepidities, and the special qualities of the Buddha and the characteristics and marks of beauty [on the body], and so it is faultless.

1. theg pa de ni sems can thams cad kyi go skabs ’byed pas na, dpag tu med pa’o źes bya bas sems bskyed pa’i yon tan bstan te, sems can tshad med pa rnams bla na med pa’i byaṅ chub tu ’god ciṅ mṅon par ’tshaṅ rgya ba’i skabs ’byed pas na go skabs ’byed pa źes bya ste, theg pa de yaṅ de’i rgyur gyur pa’i phyir, sems can dpag tu med pas de yaṅ dpag tu med pa’o. rnam pa gñis kyis dpag tu med pa ste, a) rgya che ba daṅ, b) tshad med pa’o; a) ci tsam du bsgrub par bya ba’i dge ba’i rtsa ba ’jig rten daṅ ’jig rten las ’das pa thams cad sgrub par byed pas rgya che bas so, b) dge ba’i rtsa ba de dag thams cad kyaṅ sems can gyi don du sgrub par bya ba’i phyir tshad med pa’o. yaṅ na byaṅ chub tu sems bskyed pa’i tshe sems can ’ga’ yaṅ ma bkol bar sems can tshad med pa thams cad bla na med pa yaṅ dag par rdzogs pa’i byaṅ chub tu bsgral lo źes sems bskyed pas na sems can thams cad kyi go skabs ’byed pa źes bya ste, sems can dpag tu med pa’i phyir theg pa de yaṅ dpag tu med pa’o.2. theg pa de ni chags pa med pa’i ye śes la btaṅ ba ste, sgrib pa med pa’o źes bya bas śes bya’i sgrib pa spaṅs te śes pa khoṅ du chud pa’i yon tan bstan te, śes bya’i sgrib pa thams cad spaṅs nas śes par bya ba’i dṅos po rnams skyu ru ra lag mthil du bźag pa bźin du gsal bar mkhyen pa’i ye śes ni chags pa med pa’i ye śes te, theg pa de’i ye śes rgyur gyur pa’o; theg pa des ye śes thob par byed pas na theg pa de ni chags pa med pa’i ye śes la btaṅ ba źes bya’o; de ltar sgrib pa med pa’i ye śes kyi rgyur gyur pas theg pa de yaṅ sgrib pa med pa źes bya’o.3. theg pa de ni sems can thams cad ñe bar ’tsho ba ste, bsod nams kyi tshogs daṅ dge ba’i rtsa ba thams cad bsags pa’o źes bya bas rgyu bsags pa’i yon tan bstan te, tshogs ji lta ba bsags pas sems can thams cad kyi sems kyi gsos su ’gyur ba’i mthu daṅ ldan pas sems can thams cad ñe bar ’tsho ba źes bya’o, bsod nams kyi tshogs ni sbyin pa daṅ tshul khrims la sogs pa’o, dge ba’i rtsa ni ’dod ma chags pa daṅ, źe mi sdaṅ ba la sogs pa’o.4. theg pa de ni sems can thams cad kyi sems kyi spyod pa la las su ruṅ ba’i phyir, pha rol tu phyin pa thams cad yoṅs su sbyaṅ bar byas pa’o źes bya bas spyod pa dag pa’i yon tan bstan te, sems can thams cad kyi sems kyi rgyud la gnas pa sbyin pa la sogs pa’i mi mthun pa’i phyogs ser sna daṅ ’chal pa’i tshul khrims la sogs pa theg pa des spaṅs pas na sems can gyi sems kyi spyod pa la las su ruṅ ba źes bya’o; de ltar ser sna la sogs pa spaṅs pa daṅ sbyin pa la sogs pa pha rol tu phyin pa rnams sbyaṅ ba byas par gyur ro, yoṅs su rdzogs par ’gyur źes bya ba’i don to.5. theg pa de ni thogs pa med par byaṅ chub kyi sñiṅ por ’gro bas na thams cad mkhyen pa’i ye śes kyi tshogs ñams su lon par byed pa’o źes bya ba mṅon par byaṅ chub pa’i yon tan bstan te, bsod nams daṅ ye śes kyi tshogs rdzogs nas sgrib pa gñis spaṅs te, gñis su med pa’i ye śes kyi ’bras bur gyur pa ni byaṅ chub kyi sñiṅ po ste; dri ma med par grags pas bstan pa’i mdo las kyaṅ: byaṅ chub ni sbyin pa’i sñiṅ po, byaṅ chub ni tshul khrims kyi sñiṅ po, źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs pa’i phyir ro. theg pa de la źugs pas bdud daṅ bgegs kyi bar chad med par byaṅ chub kyi sñiṅ po thob par ’gyur bas na theg pa de ni thogs pa med par byaṅ chub kyi sñiṅ por ’gro ba’o. de bas na theg pa des thams cad mkhyen pa’i ye śes thob par ’gyur ba’i rgyu bsod nams daṅ ye śes kyi thsogs yoṅs su rdzogs śiṅ mthar ’byin par byed pas na tshogs gñis ñams su lon par byed pa źes bya’o.
The quotation from Vimalakīrtinirdeśa is not verbatim, but refers to Vkn p. 3611ff, Lamotte p. 200ff.6. sems can thams cad sbyin pa’i gnas kyi phyir, sems can thams cad la thogs pa med pa’i ’od zer mñam par gtoṅ ba źes bya bas mñam par phan ’dogs pa’i yon tan bstan te, sems can thams cad bla na med pa’i byaṅ chub tu mṅon par saṅs rgyas nas bsod nams kyi źiṅ sbyin pa’i gnas su ’gyur bar bya ba’i phyir mthon dman daṅ ñe riṅ med par byams pa daṅ ye śes kyi snaṅ ba’i ’od zer sñoms par gtoṅ ṅo źes bya ba’i don to.7. theg pa de ni saṅs rgyas kyi chos thams cad mṅon du gyur pa’i phyir, lam ṅan pa’i ’jigs pa thams cad las ’das pa’o źes bya bas ñan thos daṅ so so’i skye bo’i lam las rgal ba’i yon tan bstan te, saṅs rgyas kyi chos thams cad ni a) spaṅ bar bya ba daṅ, b) śes par bya ba daṅ, c) bsgrub pa bya ba daṅ, d) rdzogs par bya ba daṅ, e) thob par bya ba rnams te, de dag thams cad khoṅ du chud ciṅ rtogs pas na mṅon du gyur pa’o; de la a) spaṅ bar bya ba ni ñon moṅs pa’i sgrib pa daṅ śes bya’i sgrib pa’o, b) śes par bya ba ni gaṅ zag la bdag med pa daṅ chos la bdag med pa’o, c) bsgrub pa bya ba ni bdag daṅ gźan gyi don to, d) rdzogs par bya ba ni sa daṅ pha rol tu phyin pa’o, e) thob par bya ba ni mi gnas pa’i mya ṅan las ’das pa’o; chos de dag mṅon sum du gyur pas ñan thos kyi mya ṅan las ’das par yaṅ mi ltuṅ, ’khor bar yaṅ mi ltuṅ bas na lam ṅan pa’i ’jigs pa thams cad las ’das pa źes bya’o, yaṅ na theg pa de ni gaṅ zag la bdag med par mṅon sum du byas pas ṅan soṅ gsum du skye ba’i ’jigs pa med pas na ’jigs pa thams cad las ’das pa źes bya’o.8. theg pa de ni byaṅ chub kyi phyogs kyi chos thams cad daṅ źes bya ba la sogs pas bgegs ’joms pa’i yon tan bstan te, byaṅ chub kyi phyogs kyi chos thams cad ni dran pa ñe bar gźag pa bźi daṅ, yaṅ dag par spoṅ ba bźi daṅ, rdzu ’phrul gyi rkaṅ pa bźi la sogs pa byaṅ chub kyi phyogs sum cu rtsa bdun rnams so; rten ciṅ (175b) ’brel bar ’byuṅ ba ni chos rnams byed pa pos ma byas śiṅ rtag pa daṅ chad pa las ’das pa rgyu daṅ rkyen las skyes pas na raṅ bźin gyis ma skyes pa ste, nam mkha’ bźin no; chos de dag ñid thams cad las ’phags par gnas śiṅ mu stegs daṅ bdud la sogs pa las rgyal bar byed pas rgyal mtshan daṅ ba dan źes bya’o; chos de dag gi sgra gsaṅ mthon por bsgrags pa ni rgyal mtshan daṅ ba dan bsgreṅ ba’o; de ltar mu stegs can thams cad las rgyal ba’i rgyal mtshan daṅ ba dan bsgreṅ bas pha rol rgol ba maṅ po daṅ log pa’i tshogs maṅ po tshar gcod par byed pas na bdud daṅ, phas kyi rgol ba daṅ, ṅan pa’i tshogs can gyi tshogs rab tu ’joms pa źes bya ste, bdud ni bdud ñid do, phas kyi rgol ba ni mu stegs can rnams so, ṅan pa’i tshogs can gyi tshogs ni bdud kyi ’khor stobs daṅ bcas pa’am, mu stegs can ’khor daṅ bcas la bya’o.9. theg pa de ni saṅs rgyas kyi theg pa sgrib pa med par gyur pa ste źes bya ba la sogs pas ñon moṅs pa daṅ ñe ba’i ñon moṅs pa spoṅ ba’i yon tan bstan te, saṅs rgyas su ’gro ba’i theg pa ni saṅs rgyas kyi theg pa ste, saṅs rgyas su ’gro bar byed pa’i theg pa yaṅ yin la theg pa des ñon moṅs pa daṅ ñe ba’i ñon moṅs pa’i sgrib pa yaṅ sel bar byed pas na theg pa de ni saṅs rgyas kyi theg pa sgrib pa med par gyur pa źes bya’o, de ltar sgrib pa med par ’gyur bas mtha’ daṅ, mtha’ med par lta ba la sogs pa lta ba’i ñon moṅs pa rnams sel bar byed do źes bya bar sbyar ro, lta ba źes bya ba’i sgra mthar lta ba daṅ, mtha’ med par lta ba daṅ, rtag par lta ba daṅ, chad par lta ba daṅ, ’byuṅ bar lta ba daṅ, ’jig par lta ba źes tshig re re daṅ sbyar ro. de la mtha’ daṅ mtha’ med par lta ba ni ’di ltar ’di ni dge sbyoṅ ṅam bram ze kha cig ’jig rten pa’i bsam gtan la brten nas: ’jig rten gyi mtha’ yod par ’du śes pa daṅ, mtha’ med par ’du śes pa ste, de yaṅ ji ltar lta źe na? ’jig rten gyi mtha’ tha mar chad par ’gyur ram mi ’gyur, sñam du yaṅ dag par tshol bar byed de, gaṅ gi tshe ’jig pa’i bskal pa rjes su dran pa de’i tshe ni mtha’ yod par ’du śes ’byuṅ bas mtha’ yod par lta ba’o; gaṅ gi tshe chags pa’i bskal pa dran pa de’i tshe mtha’ med pa’i ’du śes ’byuṅ bas mtha’ med par lta’o. rtag par lta ba ni dge sbyoṅ daṅ bram ze kha cig: bdag daṅ ’jig rten ni rtag pa ste, byas pa ma yin pa daṅ, byas pas byas ma yin pa daṅ, sprul pa ma yin pa daṅ, sprul pas byas pa ma yin pa daṅ, gsad du med pa daṅ, ther zug tu gnas pa daṅ, srog śiṅ ltar brtan par gnas pa’o, sñam du ’dzin pa’o. chad par lta ba ni dge sbyoṅ ṅam bram ze kha cig ’di lta ste: bdag gzugs can rags pa ’byuṅ ba chen po bźi las byuṅ ba ji srid du ’dug ciṅ sdod la ’tsho ba, de srid du nad daṅ bcas pa, ’bras daṅ bcas pa, zug rṅu daṅ bcas pa, rims daṅ bcas pa yoṅs su gduṅ ba daṅ bcas pa yin te, nam śi ba’i ’og tu bdag chad de źig ciṅ med par gyur pa, de na bdag gtan chad par ’gyur ro, źes smra ba’o. ’byuṅ bar lta ba ni dṅos po skye bar lta ba’o. ’jig par lta ba ni dṅos po ’gag par lta ba’o; lta bar gyur pa thams cad ces smos pa ni miṅ gis smos pa las ma gtogs pa bdag tu lta ba la sogs pa kun bsdu ba’o; kun nas ldaṅ ba ni ñon moṅs pa la mṅon sum du ’byuṅ ba’o; sgrib pa ni sgrib pa lṅa rnams so; chod pa ni dge ba’i bar du gcod pa’i chos dag go; the tshom ni bden pa daṅ dkon mchog la yid mi ches pa’o; ’gyod pa ni dge ba daṅ mi dge ba byas kyaṅ ruṅ ma byas kyaṅ ruṅ phyis sems la gduṅ ba skye ba’o; sel ba ni de dag theg pa ’dis spoṅ bar byed pa’o.10. theg pa de ni lhag pa’i bsam pa daṅ sñiṅ rje chen pos phye bas na źes bya ba la sogs pas bdag daṅ gźan gyi don phun sum tshogs pa’i yon tan bstan te, lhag pa’i bsam pa daṅ sñiṅ rje chen pos phye bas źes bya ba ni lhag pa’i bsam pa chen po daṅ sñiṅ rje chen po’i rgyu las byuṅ ba źes bya ba’i tha tshig go. de la sems can rnams bde ba la gźag par sems pa ni lhag pa’i bsam pa chen po’o, sems can rnams kyi sdug bsṅal med par byed par sems pa ni sñiṅ rje chen po’o, rgyu de gñis las byuṅ bas na 1) bdag daṅ 2) gźan gyi don phun sum tshogs par ’gyur te, 1) bdag gi don phun sum tshogs pa’aṅ rnam pa bźi’o, gaṅ źe na? a) chos phun sum tshogs pa daṅ, b) theg pa phun sum tshogs pa daṅ, c) ’jig rten daṅ ’jig rten las ’das pa’i ’byor ba phun sum tshogs pa daṅ, d) mi gnas pa’i mya ṅan las ’das pa’i lam phun sum tshogs pa’o. de la chos thams cad phun sum tshogs pa źes bya bas a) chos phun sum tshogs pa bstan te, chos kyaṅ rnam pa gsum mo, gaṅ źe na? śes par bya ba’i chos daṅ, bsgrub par bya ba’i chos daṅ, thob par bya ba’i chos so; de la śes par bya ba’i chos ni gsuṅ rab yan lag bcu gñis so, bsgrub par bya ba’i chos ni byaṅ chub kyi phyogs kyi chos sum cu rtsa bdun no, thob par bya ba’i chos ni mya ṅan las ’das pa ste, de dag daṅ ldan pas na chos thams cad phun sum tshogs pa źes bya’o. rin po che thams cad daṅ ldan pa źes bya bas b) theg pa phun sum tshogs pa bstan te, theg pa der saṅs rgyas la sogs pa dkon mchog gsum daṅ ñan thos kyi theg pa la sogs pa thams cad ’dus pas na rin po che thams cad daṅ ldan pa źes bya’o. phun sum tshogs pa thams cad rñed pa źes bya bas c) ’jig rten daṅ ’jig rten las ’das pa’i ’byor pa phun sum tshogs pa bstan te, theg pa de la brten nas ’jig rten daṅ ’jig rten las ’das pa’i phun sum tshogs pa thams cad thob par ’gyur bas phun sum tshogs pa thams cad rñed pa źes bya’o. mi slu ba’i lam du ’gro ba źes bya bas d) mi gnas pa’i mya ṅan las ’das pa’i lam phun sum tshogs pa bstan te, mi slu ba’i lam ni mi gnas pa’i mya ṅan las ’das pa’i lam mo, theg pa ’dis kyaṅ lam der ’gro ba’am, lam de daṅ mthun pa’i phyir mi slu ba’i lam du ’gro ba’o. 2) sems can thams cad ñe bar ’tsho ba źes bya bas gźan gyi don phun sum tshogs pa bstan te, theg pa de la źugs na sems can thams cad phan pa daṅ bde ba thob par ’gyur ba’i phyir sems can thams cad ñe bar ’tsho ba źes bya’o.11. theg pa de ni thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med pa źes bya ba la sogs pas ’bras bu phun sum tshogs pa’i yon tan bstan te, a) rnam pa thams cad du, b) dus thams cad du, c) gnas thams cad du, d) phyogs thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med pas na theg pa de ni thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med pa źes bya ste, a) rnam pa thams cad ni sdig pa mi dge ba’i chos thams cad mi byed pa’i phyir ro, b) dus thams cad du ni dus gsum du yaṅ sdig pa mi dge ba’i chos mi byed pas so c) gnas thams cad ni lha daṅ mi’i gnas gaṅ du phyin kyaṅ sdig pa mi byed pa’i phyir ro, d) phyogs thams cad ni phyogs bcu kun tu sdig pa mi byed pas so. chos ’og nas smos pa rnams kyi rgyan gyis brgyan pa źes bya ste, de dag ni goṅ du bśad par zad do.


gaṅ ’di la mkhas pa, de ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i theg pa chen po la mkhas pa źes bya’o.

yad iha kauśalyaṃ tad bodhisattvasya mahāyānakauśalyam.

Skill in this is the bodhisattva’s skill with the great way.

goṅ du bśad pa rnams mjug bsdu ba’i phyir gaṅ ’di la mkhas pa źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs te, gaṅ ’di la mkhas pa źes bya ba ni goṅ du bśad pa rnams la’o.


de la byaṅ chub sems dpa’i chos thams cad la mkhas pa gaṅ źe na?

tatra katamad bodhisattvasya sarvadharmakauśalyam?

(p. 81) 8) What then is the bodhisattva’s skill with all moments of existence?


chos thams cad ces bya ba ni mdor na a) ’dus byas daṅ, b) ’dus ma byas so. de la byaṅ chub sems dpas ’dus byas daṅ ’dus ma byas la mkhas par bya ste;

sarvadharmā iti samāsataḥ saṃskṛtā asaṃskṛtāś ca, tatra bodhisattvena saṃskṛtāsaṃskṛtakauśalyaṃ karaṇīyam.

All moments of existence are, in short, a) conditioned, and b) unconditioned, so the bodhisattva should develop skill with the conditioned and the unconditioned.

chos thams cad la mkhas pa bstan pa’i phyir de la byaṅ chub sems dpa’i chos thams cad la mkhas pa gaṅ źe na źes dris so, dris pa’i lan gdab pa’i phyir chos thams cad ces bya ba ni mdor na ’dus byas daṅ, ’dus ma byas źes bya ba gsuṅs te, ’dus byas daṅ ’dus ma byas su chos thams cad ’dus pas, ’dus pa’i don gyis de gñis la chos thams cad ces bya’o. de la gaṅ rgyu daṅ rkyen gyis bskyed pa’i zag pa daṅ bcas pa’i chos daṅ zag pa med pa’i chos ni ’dus byas so, gaṅ rgyu daṅ rkyen gyis ma bskyed pa de bźin ñid daṅ, yaṅ dag pa’i mtha’ daṅ, stoṅ pa ñid daṅ, chos kyi dbyiṅs ni ’dus ma byas so, de la byaṅ chub sems dpas ’dus byas daṅ ’dus ma byas la mkhas par bya ste źes bya ba ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’ rnams kyis ’dus byas daṅ ’dus ma byas kyi chos rnams kyi mtshan ñid khoṅ du chud par bya ste źes bya ba’i don to.


de la byaṅ chub sems dpa’i ’dus byas la mkhas pa gaṅ źe na?

tatra katamad bodhisattvasya saṃskṛtakauśalyam?

So what then is the bodhisattva’s skill with the conditioned?


gaṅ de dag lus kyi ’du byed dge ba daṅ, ṅag gi ’du byed dge ba daṅ, yid kyi ’du byed dge ba mṅon par ’dus byas pa de dag thams cad bla na med pa yaṅ dag par rdzogs pa’i byaṅ chub tu yoṅs su bsṅo ba, ’di ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i ’dus byas la mkhas pa źes bya’o.gaṅ yaṅ dge ba’i lus daṅ, ṅag daṅ, yid kyi ’du byed mṅon par ’dus byas pa de dag thams cad byaṅ chub la rtog pas thams cad mkhyen pa ñid du yoṅs su bsṅo ba, ’di ni de’i ’dus ma byas la mkhas pa źes bya’o.

yas tān kuśalān kāyasaṃskārān kuśalān vāksaṃskārān kuśalān manaḥsaṃskārān tān sarvān abhisaṃskṛtān anuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhaye pariṇāmayatīdaṃ bodhisattvasya saṃskṛtakauśalyam.yaḥ punas tān sarvān abhisaṃskṛtān kuśalān kāyavāṅmanaḥsaṃskārān bodhipratyavekṣayā sarvajñatāyāṃ pariṇāmayatīdaṃ tasyāsaṃskṛtakauśalyam.

When he transforms into incomparable complete awakening all those conditioned things which consist in the good formative factors in the body, the good formative factors in speech, and the good formative factors in the mind, it is the bodhisattva’s skill with the conditioned.And again, when he transforms into omniscience all those conditioned things which consist in the good formative factors in body, speech and mind by understanding them as [essentially the same as] awakening, this is his skill with the unconditioned.

gaṅ de dag lus kyi ’du byed dge ba daṅ, ṅag gi ’du byed dge ba daṅ, yid kyi ’du byed dge ba źes bya ba la srog mi gcod pa daṅ, ma byin par mi len pa daṅ, ’dod pas log par mi g-yeṅ ba ni lus kyi ’du byed dge ba’o, brdzun daṅ, phra ma daṅ, ṅag rtsub po daṅ, tshig kyal pa’i tshig mi smra ba ni ṅag gi ’du byed dge ba, brnab sems daṅ, gnod sems daṅ, log par lta ba spaṅs pa ni yid kyi ’du byed dge ba źes bya’o; de dag thams cad bla na med pa yaṅ dag par rdzogs pa’i byaṅ chub tu bsṅo ba źes bya ba la, de dag ces bya ba ni goṅ du smos ma thag pa’i ’du byed rnam pa gsum mṅon par ’dus byas pa’o, bla na med pa źes bya ba ni byaṅ chub, de a) spoṅ ba daṅ, b) ye śes daṅ, c) sgrub pa daṅ, d) dus daṅ, e) thob pa daṅ, f) ldan pa daṅ, g) spyod pa la sogs pas ñan thos kyi byaṅ chub las khyad źugs pa’i phyir bla na med pa źes bya’o. de la a) spoṅ ba khyad źugs pa ni ñan thos kyi byaṅ chub kyis ñon moṅs pa’i sgrib pa tsam spoṅ bar zad kyi, ’dis ni ñon moṅs pa daṅ śes bya’i sgrib pa gñis spaṅs pas spoṅ bas khyad źugs so; b) ye śes ni gaṅ zag la bdag med pa tsam khoṅ du chud par zad kyi, ’dis ni gaṅ zag daṅ chos la bdag med pa’i ye śes khyad źugs so; c) sgrub pa ni ñan thos la sogs pas bdag gi don bsgrub pa tsam du zad kyi ’dis ni bdag daṅ gźan gyi don sgrub par byed pas na sgrub pa khyad źugs so; d) dus ni ñan thos la sogs pa tshe gsum mam1 bdun gyi bar du sbyor ba tsam du zad kyi, ’dis ni bskal pa graṅs med pa gsum gyi bar du sbyor bas na dus khyad źugs so; e) thob pa ni ñan thos kyis dgra bcom pa’i ’bras bu thob par zad kyi, ’dis ni bla na med pa’i byaṅ chub kyi ’bras bu thob pas na thob pa khyad źugs so; f) ldan pa ni ñan thos dag zad par gyi skye mched daṅ zil gyis gnon pa’i skye mched la sogs pa’i yon tan daṅ ldan par zad kyi, ’dis ni stobs daṅ mi ’jigs pa la sogs pa’i yon tan daṅ ldan pas na ldan pa khyad źugs so; g) spyod pa ni ñan thos la sogs pas daṅ pha rol tu phyin pa la mi spyod kyi, ’dis ni sa daṅ pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pas na spyod pa khyad źugs so; yaṅ dag par rdzogs pa źes bya ba ni chos thams cad phyin ci ma log par thugs su chud pa źes bya ba’i don to; byaṅ chub ni spaṅs pa daṅ ye śes phun sum tshogs pas rab tu phye ba ste, sṅar bśad pa bźin no; byaṅ chub de lta bu thob par bya ba’i phyir dge ba mṅon par ’dus byas pa rnams bsṅo ba de ni byaṅ chub tu bsṅo ba źes bya ste, de ni ’dus byas la mkhas pa’o.
gaṅ yaṅ dge ba’i lus daṅ, ṅag daṅ, yid kyi ’du byed mṅon par ’dus byas pa de dag thams cad byaṅ chub la rtog pas thams cad mkhyen pa ñid du bsṅo ba źes bya ba la, goṅ du bla na med pa’i byaṅ chub tu bsṅo ba bśad pa la byaṅ chub la rtog pa źes bya ba’i tshig ma smos pas ’dus byas su rig par bya’o, ’dir ni byaṅ chub la rtog pa źes smos pas lus daṅ ṅag daṅ yid kyi dge ba ji spyad pa thams cad kyaṅ byaṅ chub kyi mtshan ñid daṅ dbyer med par stoṅ pa ñid du brtags nas thams cad mkhyen pa thob par bya ba’i phyir bsṅo ste, byaṅ chub kyaṅ ’dus ma byas kyi mtshan ñid yin pa’i phyir ’dus ma byas la mkhas pa źes bya’o.


gźan yaṅ ’dus byas la mkhas pa ni pha rol tu phyin pa lṅa po dag yaṅ dag par sgrub pa ste.lṅa gaṅ źe na?’di lta ste: sbyin pa’i pha rol tu phyin pa daṅ, tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa daṅ, bzod pa’i pha rol tu phyin pa daṅ, brtson ’grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa daṅ, bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa ste; ’di ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i ’dus byas la mkhas pa źes bya’o.gaṅ yaṅ śes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ’dus ma byas kyi ye śes kyis pha rol tu phyin pa lṅa po dag la mi smod ciṅ, pha rol tu phyin pa thams cad kyi tshogs daṅ dge ba’i rtsa ba bsags pa’i phyir byaṅ chub sems dpa’i rnam par grol ba zag pa med pa daṅ thams cad mkhyen pa ñid du yoṅs su bsṅo ba, ’di ni de’i ’dus ma byas la mkhas pa źes bya’o.

punar aparaṃ saṃskṛtakauśalyaṃ pañca pāramitāsamudānayāḥ.katame pañca?yā imā dānapāramitā, śīlapāramitā, kṣāntipāramitā, vīryapāramitā, dhyānapāramitedaṃ bodhisattvasya saṃskṛtakauśalyam.yaḥ punaḥ prajñāpāramitāsaṃskṛtajñānena pañcapāramitā na paṃsayati, sarvapāramitāsaṃbhārakuśalamūlopacayārthaṃ bodhisattvasyānāsravavimokṣe sarvajñatāyāṃ pariṇāmayatīdaṃ tasyāsaṃskṛtakauśalyam.

Further, skill with the conditioned is the fivefold accomplishment of the perfections.Which five?The perfection of generosity, the perfection of morality, the perfection of tolerance, the perfection of vigour, the perfection of meditation. This is called the bodhisattva’s skill with the conditioned.And again, when he, through the perfection of insight – the knowledge of the unconditioned – does not depreciate the other five perfections [though inferior in causing birth in existence (saṃsāra) ], but transforms them into omniscience, and into the bodhisattva’s unsullied liberation – for the sake of accumulating all the perfections and heaping up roots of good – this is his skill with the unconditioned.

gźan yaṅ ’dus byas la mkhas pa ni źes bya bas ’dus byas daṅ ’dus ma byas la mkhas pa’i rnam graṅs gźan ston te, pha rol tu phyin pa lṅa sgrub pa ni ’dus byas la mkhas pa źes bya’o, gaṅ yaṅ śes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa źes bya ba la sogs pas śes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni ’dus ma byas la mkhas par bstan to. śes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa de yaṅ ci ’dra ba źig ce na? de’i phyir ’dus ma byas kyi ye śes kyis pha rol tu phyin pa lṅa po dag la mi smod ciṅ źes bya ba smos te, stoṅ pa ñid la dmigs pa’i ye śes ni ’dus ma byas kyi ye śes te, dṅos su na rnam par mi rtog pa’i ye śes la bya’o. pha rol tu phyin pa lṅa ni ’khor bar skye ba’i rgyu yin pas smad pa yin yaṅ, śes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pas de la sun ’byin par mi byed pa ni pha rol tu phyin pa lṅa la mi smod pa źes bya’o; pha rol tu phyin pa thams cad kyi tshogs ni sbyin pa la sogs pa pha rol tu phyin pa drug gi tshogs so; dge ba’i rtsa ba ’dod ma chags pa la sogs pa’o; phyir źes bya ba ni pha pha rol tu phyin pa’i tshogs daṅ dge ba’i rtsa ba’i tshogs bsags par bya ba’i don du’am ched du źes bya ba’i tha tshig go; byaṅ chub sems dpa’i rnam par grol ba ni ñon moṅs pa daṅ śes bya’i sgrib pa spaṅs pa’i mi gnas pa’i mya ṅan las ’das pa’o; byaṅ chub sems dpa’i thams cad mkhyen pa ni dṅos po thams cad thugs su chud pa me loṅ lta bu’i ye śes la bya’o. bsṅo ba źes bya ba ni mya ṅan las ’das pa daṅ ye śes de thob par bya ba’i don du pha rol tu phyin pa drug bsgrubs pa bsṅo ba’o; de dag gis ni ’di skad bstan pa yin te, goṅ du sbyin pa la sogs pa pha rol tu phyin pa lṅa rnams ni ’dus ma byas kyi chos rtog pa’i raṅ bźin ma yin pas ’dus byas la mkhas par bśad, śes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ’dus ma byas rtog pa’i raṅ bźin yin pas ’dus ma byas la mkhas par bśad do.


gźan yaṅ ’dus byas la mkhas pa ni gaṅ sems can thams cad la thogs pa med pa’i ’od zer mñam par gtoṅ ba’i phyir, bsdu ba’i dṅos po bźis sems can sdud pa, ’di ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i ’dus byas la mkhas pa’o.gaṅ yaṅ sems can med pa daṅ bdag med pas mi ’dzin, mi len, mchog tu ’dzin par mi byed ciṅ, bsdu ba’i dṅos po la mkhas pa de yaṅ ’dus ma byas la mos pa thams cad mkhyen pa ñid du yoṅs su bsṅo ba, ’di ni de’i ’dus ma byas la mkhas pa’o.

punar aparaṃ saṃskṛtakauśalyaṃ yaḥ sarvasattvasamāpratihataraśmipramocanārthaṃ caturbhiḥ saṃgrahavastubhiḥ sattvān saṃgṛhṇātīdaṃ bodhisattvasya saṃskṛtakauśalyam.yaḥ punar nirjīvanirātmato na gṛhṇāti nopādatte na parāmṛśati, tat saṃgrahavastukauśalyaṃ cāsaṃskṛtam adhimucyate, sarvajñatāyāṃ ca pariṇāmayatīdaṃ tasyāsaṃskṛtakauśalyam.

Further concerning skill with the conditioned: when he attracts beings with the four means of attraction so as to emit unhindered rays of light equally upon all living beings, this is the bodhisattva’s skill with the conditioned.And again, when he does not grasp, cling or adhere to things by the principle that they are without soul or self, when he relies on the skill in the ways of attracting beings as being unconditioned, when he transforms them into omniscience, this is his skill with the unconditioned.

gźan yaṅ źes bya ba la sogs pas ’dus byas daṅ ’dus ma byas la mkhas pa’i rnam graṅs gźan ston te, ye śes daṅ sñiṅ rjes sems can thams cad la bltas nas ci rigs par phan ’dogs par byed pa ni sems can thams cad la thogs pa med pa’i ’od zer mñam par gtoṅ ba źes bya’o, de ltar phan gdags par bya ba’i phyir sbyin pa daṅ, sñan par smra ba daṅ, don spyod pa daṅ, don mthun par spyod pa bźis sems can sdud par byed pa ni ’dus byas la mkhas pa źes bya’o.
mi ’dzin, mi len, mchog tu ’dzin par mi byed ces bya ba la sogs pa la de lta mod kyi, don dam par stoṅ pa yin pas phyi’i yul la dṅos por mi ’dzin, naṅ gi dṅos po la bdag tu mi len la, de ltar dṅos po daṅ bdag tu ma grub pas phan btags so źes mchog tu ’dzin par yaṅ mi byed ces bya ba’i tha tshig go; bsdu ba’i dṅos po la mkhas pa de yaṅ ’dus ma byas la mos pa źes bya ba ni bsdu ba’i dṅos po rnams kyaṅ stoṅ pa ñid kyi raṅ bźin du mos pa źes bya ba’i tha tshig go; thams cad mkhyen pa ñid du bsṅo ba źes bya ba ni de ltar stoṅ pa ñid du mos pas bsdu ba’i dṅos po la mkhas pa de de bźin ñid thugs su chud pa’i thams cad mkhyen pa’i ye śes thob par bya ba’i phyir bsṅo ba ni byaṅ chub sems dpa’i ’dus ma byas la mkhas pa yin no źes bya bar sbyar ro.


gźan yaṅ ’dus byas la mkhas pa ni gaṅ ’khor ba’i rgyun gyi ñon moṅs pa rnams gcod pa daṅ, ’khor ba’i rgyun gyi dge ba’i rtsa ba rnams mi gcod pa daṅ, byaṅ chub sgrub pa’i kun tu sbyor ba rnams kyi rgyun ’brel pa, ñi tshe ba’i kun tu sbyor ba rnams kun tu mi spyod pa, ’di ni ’dus byas la mkhas pa źes bya’o.gaṅ yaṅ stoṅ pa ñid daṅ, mtshan ma med pa daṅ, smon pa med pa’i chos rnams la ’dris par byed pa’i ye śes rtog pa la mkhas pa daṅ, byaṅ chub gźan gyi driṅ la mi ’jog ciṅ, ’dus ma byas kyaṅ mṅon sum du mi byed pa, ’di ni de’i ’dus ma byas la mkhas pa źes bya’o.

punar aparaṃ saṃskṛtakauśalyaṃ yaḥ saṃsārasrotaḥkleśān chinatti, saṃsārasrotaḥkuśalamūlāni na cchinatti, bodhipratipattisaṃyojanāni badhnāti, prādeśikasaṃyojanāni na samudācaratīdaṃ saṃskṛtakauśalyam.yat punaḥ śūnyatāyām ānimitte ’praṇihite parijayajñānapratyavekṣākauśalyam, bodhyaparapraṇeyatā cāsaṃskṛtāsākṣātkaraṇam idaṃ tasyāsaṃskṛtakauśalyam.

Further concerning skill with the conditioned: when he cuts off the vices in the stream of existence, but does not cut off the roots of good in the stream of existence, when he fastens the fetters which consist in the realization of awakening, but does not concern himself with the fetters that bind those with limited religious practice, this is skill with the conditioned.And again, skill in discerning what is knowledge acquainted with emptiness, absence of distinguishing marks and longing, (p. 82) not being taught by others concerning awakening, not realizing the unconditioned, this is his skill with the unconditioned.

’dus byas daṅ ’dus ma byas la mkhas pa rnam graṅs gźan yaṅ bstan par bźed nas gźan yaṅ ’dus byas la mkhas pa ni gaṅ ’khor ba’i rgyun gyi ñon moṅs pa rnams gcod pa daṅ źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs so, de la ’dus byas la mkhas pa rnam pa gñis te, 1) ’jig rten pa’i rgyu la mkhas pa daṅ, 2) ’jig rten las ’das pa’i rgyu la mkhas pa’o. 1) ’jig rten pa’i rgyu la mkhas pa yaṅ rnam pa gñis te, a) sdug bsṅal gyi rgyu spoṅ ba la mkhas pa daṅ, b) bde ba’i rgyu bskyed pa la mkhas pa’o; gaṅ ’khor ba’i rgyun gyi ñon moṅs pa rnams gcod pa daṅ źes bya bas a) sdug bsṅal gyi rgyu yoṅs su spoṅ ba la mkhas pa bstan te, ’khor bar rgyun du skye bar byed pa’i rgyu ’dod chags la sogs pa kun tu sbyor ba’i tshogs ni ’khor ba’i rgyun gyi ñon moṅs pa źes bya’o, de rnams spoṅ bar byed pa ni ñon moṅs pa rnams gcod pa źes bya’o; ’khor ba’i rgyun gyi dge ba’i rtsa ba rnams mi gcod pa daṅ źes bya bas b) bde ba’i rgyu bskyed pa la mkhas pa bstan te, gaṅ ’khor ba la rgyun du lha daṅ mir skye bar byed pa’i rgyu dge ba bcu daṅ, ’dod ma chags pa daṅ, źe mi sdaṅ ba la sogs pa’i dge ba’i rtsa ba rnams gcig nas gcig tu rgyun mi ’chad par byed pas na ’khor ba’i rgyun mi dge ba’i rtsa ba mi gcod pa źes bya’o. 2) ’jig rten las ’das pa’i rgyu la mkhas pa yaṅ rnam pa gñis te, a) byaṅ chub chen po’i rgyu rgyun mi gcod pa daṅ, b) źi ba phyogs gcig pa’i rgyu sgrub par mi byed pa’o; byaṅ chub sgrub pa’i kun tu sbyor ba rnams kyi rgyun ’brel pa źes bya bas a) byaṅ chub chen po’i rgyu rgyun mi gcod pa bstan te, byaṅ chub kyi don ni goṅ du smras par zad do, kun tu sbyor ba ni źi gnas daṅ lhag mthoṅ sgrub par byed pa’o, źi gnas daṅ lhag mthoṅ bsgom pa gaṅ gis byaṅ chub thob par byed pa de ni byaṅ chub sgrub pa’i kun tu sbyor ba źes bya ste, de ltar bsgom pa rgyun mi gcod pa ni kun tu sbyor ba rnams kyi rgyun ’brel pa’o; ñi tshe ba’i kun tu sbyor ba rnams mi spyad pa źes bya bas b) źi ba phyogs gcig pa’i rgyu sgrub par mi byed pa bstan te, ñi tshe ba’i kun tu sbyor ba ni źi ba phyogs gcig pa’i mya ṅan las ’das pa thob par ’gyur ba’i rgyu źi gnas daṅ lhag mthoṅ sgom par byed pa’o, mi spyad pa ni de lta bu’i rgyu la mi ’jug pa’o. yaṅ na ’khor ba’i rgyun gyi ñon moṅs pa rnams gcod kyaṅ byaṅ chub chen po thob par byed pa’i rgyu rgyun mi gcod pas na byaṅ chub sgrub pa’i kun tu sbyor ba rnams kyi rgyun ’brel pa źes bya’o; ’khor bar skye ba’i dge ba’i rtsa ba rnams rgyun mi gcod pas źi ba phyogs gcig pa’i mya ṅan las ’das par mi lhuṅ ba’i phyir ñi tshe ba’i kun tu sbyor ba rnams mi spyad pa źes bya’o.
gaṅ yaṅ stoṅ pa ñid ces bya ba la sogs pas ’dus ma byas la mkhas pa bstan te, de yaṅ tiṅ ṅe ’dzin gsum la dbaṅ thob pa daṅ, gdams ṅag daṅ rjes su bstan pa la mi brten par de bźin ñid khoṅ du chud pa daṅ, de bźin ñid khoṅ du chud kyaṅ de’i phyogs la mi gnas pa’o; gaṅ yaṅ stoṅ pa ñid daṅ, mtshan ma med pa źes bya ba la sogs pas tiṅ ṅe ’dzin gsum la dbaṅ thob pa bstan te, stoṅ pa ñid la sogs pa ni goṅ du bśad par zad do; ye śes gaṅ gis tiṅ ṅe ’dzin de gsum la dbaṅ byed par ’gyur ba de la ni ’dris par byed pa’i ye śes źes bya ste, ye śes de mṅon sum du gyur pa’am, ye śes de rtogs pa ni rtogs pa la mkhas pa’o; byaṅ chub tu gźan gyi driṅ la mi ’jog ciṅ źes bya bas gdams ṅag daṅ rjes su bstan pa la mi brten par de bźin ñid khoṅ du chud pa bstan te, de bźin gśegs pa daṅ mkhan po daṅ slob dpon gyis bstan pa’i man ṅag la mi brten par stoṅ pa gñis su med pa’i mtshan ñid khoṅ du chud pa ni byaṅ chub gźan gyi driṅ la mi ’jog pa źes bya’o; ’dus ma byas mṅon sum du mi byed ces bya bas de bźin ñid khoṅ du chud kyaṅ de’i phyogs la mi gnas pa bstan te, ’dus ma byas ni mya ṅan las ’das pa’am stoṅ pa ñid do; mṅon sum du mi byed pa ni de dag khoṅ du chud ciṅ thob kyaṅ, de’i phyogs la mi gnas pa’o.


gźan yaṅ ’dus byas la mkhas pa ni gaṅ khams gsum na yaṅ spyod la khams gsum na spyod pa’i ñon moṅs pas kyaṅ mi gos pa, ’di ni ’dus byas la mkhas pa źes bya’o.gaṅ yaṅ khams gsum nas ṅes par ’byuṅ ba’i ye śes rab tu śes kyaṅ, ṅes par ’byuṅ ba’i dbyiṅs su mi ltuṅ ba, ’di ni de’i ’dus ma byas la mkhas pa’o.

punar aparaṃ saṃskṛtakauśalyaṃ yaḥ traidhātuke carann api traidhātukacaritakleśair nopalipyata idaṃ saṃskṛtakauśalyam.yaḥ punas traidhātukaniḥsaraṇajñānam prajānann api niḥsaraṇadhātau na patatīdaṃ tasyāsaṃskṛtakauśalyam.

Further concerning skill with the conditioned: though he roams about in the three worlds, he does not get sullied by the vices connected with roaming about in the three worlds [like the lotus born from the mud does not get sullied by the mud], this is skill with the conditioned.Though he has knowledge of deliverance from the threefold world, he does not fall into the sphere of deliverance, this is his skill with the unconditioned.

’dus byas daṅ ’dus ma byas la mkhas pa’i rnam pa gźan yaṅ bstan pa’i phyir gźan yaṅ ’dus byas la mkhas pa źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs so, khams gsum na yaṅ spyod la khams gsum na spyod pa’i ñon moṅs pas kyaṅ mi gos źes bya bas ni sems can thams cad kyi don du khams gsum na yaṅ gnas la, padmo ’dam las skyes kyaṅ ’dam gyi ñes pas mi gos pa bźin du khams gsum na yod pa’i ’dod chags la sogs pas mi gos pa, ’di ni ’dus byas la mkhas pa źes bya’o.
gaṅ yaṅ khams gsum nas ṅes par ’byuṅ ba’i ye śes rab tu śes kyaṅ źes bya ba la, khams gsum nas ṅes par ’byuṅ ba’i ye śes ni ñon moṅs pa spoṅ bar byed pa daṅ, spoṅs pa mṅon du gyur pa zad la mi skye ba’i ye śes la bya’o, rab tu śes kyaṅ źes bya ba ni de mṅon sum du gyur kyaṅ źes bya ba’i tha tshig go; ṅes par ’byuṅ ba’i dbyiṅs su mi ltuṅ źes bya ba la ṅes par ’byuṅ ba’i dbyiṅs ni mya ṅan las ’das pa la bya, mi ltuṅ ba ni de ’ba’ źig gi phyogs la mi gnas pa’o.


gaṅ chos thams cad la mkhas pa źes smras pa, de ni thams cad mkhyen pa’i tshig bla dags so.de ci’i phyir źe na?rtag tu dran pa daṅ, blo gros daṅ, śes rab la mkhas pas thams cad mkhyen pa’i ye śes tshad med ciṅ mi chags pa yoṅs su rdzogs par byed pa’i phyir te, de’i phyir chos thams cad la mkhas pa źes bya’o.

yat sarvadharmakauśalyam ity uktaṃ tat sarvajñatāyā adhivacanam.tat kasya hetor?nityasmṛtimatiprajñākauśalyenāpramāṇāsaṅgasarvajñajñānaparipūritvāt; tasmād ucyate sarvadharmakauśalyam.

[To summarize, firstly, what is the explanation of the word (nirvacana):] That which is called skill with all moments of existence is another word for omniscience.[And secondly, the reason for this (hetu):] Why?One fulfils [thirdly in the summary, the fruit (phala), viz.] the immeasurable and unattached knowledge of omniscience with skill in continuous recollection, intelligence and insight; that is why it is called skill with all moments of existence.

mkhas pa brgyad po rnams rgya cher bśad pa’i ṅes pa’i tshig daṅ, rgyu daṅ, ’bras bu bsdus te bstan pa’i phyir gaṅ chos thams cad la mkhas pa źes smras pa, de ni thams cad mkhyen pa’i tshig bla dags so źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs te, chos thams cad la mkhas pa źes kyaṅ bya, thams cad mkhyen pa źes kyaṅ bya bas chos thams cad la mkhas pa źes smras pa, de ni thams cad mkhyen pa’i tshig bla dags te, ’dis ni ṅes pa’i tshig bstan to.
ci’i phyir źes bya ba ni rgyu ’dri ba ste, chos thams cad la mkhas pa de ci’i phyir thams cad mkhyen pa źes bya źe na źes bya ba’i tha tshig go; rgyu bstan pa’i phyir rtag tu dran pa daṅ, blo gros daṅ, śes rab la mkhas pa źes bya ba pa gsuṅs te, chos thams cad la mkhas pa de ni rtag tu dran pa la mkhas pa daṅ, rtag tu blo gros la mkhas pa daṅ, rtag tu śes rab la mkhas pas de la thams cad mkhyen pa źes bya’o, de gsum gyis chos thams cad la rtogs pas na mkhas pa ste, dran pa la mkhas pa ni chos rnams kyi don daṅ tshig mi brjed par byed do, blo gros la mkhas pa ni chos rnams kyi de bźin ñid rtog par byed do, śes rab la mkhas pa ni chos rnams kyi raṅ daṅ spyi’i mtshan ñid rtog par byed do.
’bras bu bstan pa’i phyir smras pa thams cad mkhyen pa’i ye śes tshad med ciṅ mi chags pa yoṅs su rdzogs par byed pa’i phyir źes bya ste, śes bya thams cad la dmigs pas na thams cad mkhyen pa’i ye śes tshad med pa źes bya ste, thams cad mkhyen pa’i ye śes ni me loṅ lta bu’i ye śes la bya bar ’dod do, ye śes de la ñon moṅs pa’i sgrib pa daṅ śes bya’i sgrib pa ma lus par spaṅs pas na mi chags pa’o, yoṅs su rdzogs par byed ces bya ba ni dran pa la sogs pa gsum gyis ye śes de ’thob ciṅ mthar phyin par byed pa’i phyir źes bya ba’i tha tshig go; de’i phyir chos thams cad la mkhas pa źes bya ba ni gaṅ gi phyir goṅ du bśad pa ltar na chos thams cad rtogs śiṅ khoṅ du chud pa de’i phyir chos thams cad la mkhas pa źes bya’o.


btsun pa śa ra dva ti’i bu, mkhas pa brgyad po de dag gis zin pa’i byaṅ chub sems dpa’ rnams kyi śes rab mi zad pa yin no.

tair aṣṭābhiḥ kauśalyair, bhadanta śāradvatīputra, parigṛhītānāṃ bodhisattvānāṃ prajñā akṣayā bhavati.

Reverend Śāradvatīputra, the insight of the bodhisattvas possessing those eight skills becomes imperishable.

mkhas pa brgyad po de dag gis zin pa źes bya ba ni mkhas pa brgyad pa ’di dag daṅ ldan pa źes bya ba’i tha tshig go.


g) gźan yaṅ dge ba daṅ mi dge ba’i chos rnams rab tu śes pa ni śes rab bo;ṅes par ’byed pa’i cha daṅ ’thun pa’i chos rnams la rtog pa ni śes rab bo;’phags pa’i chos mṅon par gyur pas na, śes rab ni tshad mar gyur pa’o;śes rab ni lta bar gyur pa daṅ, kun nas ldaṅ ba daṅ, sgrib pa daṅ, chod pa thams cad yaṅ dag pa ji lta ba bźin du rab tu rtogs pa’o;śes rab ni ’dod pa daṅ, re ba daṅ, smon pa thams cad kyi smon lam daṅ bral ba’o;śes rab ni ñon moṅs pa’i yoṅs su gduṅ ba thams cad ’jil bas na, sim par byed pa’o;śes rab ni chos kyi kun dga’ la dga’ ba’i rgyun ma chad pas na, mchog tu dga’ bar byed pa’o;śes rab ni don śes pa mṅon sum du gyur pas rton pa’o;śes rab ni byaṅ chub kyi phyogs kyi chos sum cu rtsa bdun po dag gi rten to;śes rab ni theg pa ji lta ba bźin du ’bras bu thob par gyur pas na, thob pa’i mtshan ñid do;śes rab ni raṅ bźin gyis ye śes snaṅ bas na, rab tu śes pa’i mtshan ñid do;śes rab ni chu bo thams cad las sgrol bas na, yaṅ dag par rab tu sgrol ba’o;śes rab ni yaṅ dag par skyon med par ’dren pa’o;śes rab ni dge ba’i chos thams cad rab tu sdud pa’o;śes rab ni sṅon gyi ñon moṅs pa daṅ bag la ñal thams cad daṅ bar byed pa’o;śes rab ni rtse mor gyur pa’i chos rnams kyi mchog go;śes rab ni raṅ byuṅ gi ye śes rtogs pa’i phyir, gya nom pa’o;śes rab ni khams gsum pa thams cad daṅ ma ’dres pa’i phyir, rgyu ba daṅ bral ba’o;śes rab ni thabs kun gyis zin pa’o;śes rab ni ’phags pa thams cad kyis yoṅs su bzuṅ ba’o;śes rab ni mtshan ma daṅ yoṅs su rtog pa thams cad daṅ bral ba’i phyir, tshad gzuṅ du med pa’o;śes rab ni ma rig pa daṅ gti mug gi mun pa thams cad daṅ bral bas na, bag med pa’i gñen po’o;śes rab ni rnal ’byor spyod pa’i sa la gnas pa thams cad kyi sbyor ba’o;śes rab ni theg pa thams cad la yaṅ dag par źugs pa rnams kyi ’dren pa’o;śes rab ni ma rig pa daṅ, gti mug gi mun pa daṅ, rab rib kyi liṅ tog sel bar byed pa’i phyir, snaṅ bar byed pa’o;śes rab ni mig la ji ltar mos pa rnams la mig thams cad sbyin par byed pa’o;śes rab ni mig daṅ gzugs kyi lam las yaṅ dag par ’das pa daṅ, de bźin du rna ba daṅ, sgra daṅ, sna daṅ, dri daṅ, lce daṅ, ro daṅ, lus daṅ, reg bya daṅ, yid daṅ, chos kyi lam las yaṅ dag par ’das pa’i phyir, gnas med pa’o;śes rab ni bden pa las ṅes par ’byuṅ bas na, don dam pa’o;śes rab ni śin tu dul ba rnams kyi mi ’khrugs pa’o;śes rab ni ye śes kyi sgo rnams kyi snaṅ ba’o;śes rab ni thams cad du rgyu ba ste, mi zad pa’o;śes rab ni brten pa la ’jug pa mthoṅ ba ste, mi ’gal ba’o;śes rab ni ’dzin pa daṅ ñon moṅs pa’i bciṅs thams cad gcod pa’i phyir, rnam par thar pa’i lam mo;śes rab ni ñon moṅs pa thams cad daṅ ma ’dres pa’o;śes rab ni ’grogs pa daṅ, sgrib pa daṅ, sgrib par ’gyur ba’i chos thams cad daṅ lhan cig mi gnas pa’o.

punar aparaṃ prajñā prajñānam kuśalānām akuśalānāṃ ca dharmāṇāṃ;prajñā nirīkṣaṇā nirvedhabhāgīyeṣu dharmeṣu;prajñā prāmāṇikāryadharmābhimukhībhūtatvāt;prajñā yathābhūtaprativedhaḥ sarvadṛṣṭigataparyutthānāvaraṇanīvaraṇānāṃ;prajñāpraṇidhānā sarvakāmakāṅkṣāpraṇidhīnāṃ;prajñaudbilyakariṇī sarvakleśaparidāhanirvāpakatvāt;prajñā prāmodyakāriṇī dharmārāmaprītyanucchinnatvāt;prajñā saṃprakāśakārthajñānābhimukhībhūtatvāt;prajñāśrayaḥ saptatriṃśadbodhipakṣikadharmāṇām;prajñā prāpaṇalakṣaṇā yathāyānaphalaprāpaṇatvāt;prajñā prajñānalakṣaṇā jñānasvabhāvaprabhāsatvāt;prajñā saṃpratāraṇī sarvaughottaraṇatvāt;prajñā samyagnyāmanāyikā;prajñā saṃgrahaṇī sarvakuśaladharmāṇāṃ;prajñā prasādakā sarvapūrvakleśānuśayānāṃ;prajñā varāgradharmāṇāṃ;prajñā praṇītā svayaṃbhūjñānāvabodhatayā;prajñāpracārā traidhātukānupaliptatayā;prajñā sarvathopāyagṛhītā;prajñā sarvāryaparigṛhītā;prajñā pramāṇāgrāhyā sarvanimittaparikalpavigatatayā;prajñā pramādapratipakṣāvidyāmohāndhakāravigatatvāt;prajñā yogaḥ sarvayogācārabhūmisthitānām;prajñā nāyikā sarvayānasaṃprasthitānām;prajñālokakāry avidyāmohāndhakāratimirapaṭalāpanayatayā;prajñā sarvacakṣurdātā yathācakṣuradhimuktānām;prajñāpratiṣṭhā cakṣūrūpapathasamatikrāntatayā, evaṃ śrotraśabdaghrāṇagandhajihvārasakāyaspraṣṭavyamanodharmapathasamatikrāntatayā;prajñā paramārthaḥ satyaniryāṇatvāt;prajñākṣobhaṇatā suvinītānām;prajñā prabhāso jñānamukhānām;prajñākṣayā sarvatracaritā;prajñāviruddhā pratītyāvatāradarśanī;prajñā vimuktimārgaḥ sarvagrāhakleśabandhanacchedanatayā;prajñā sarvakleśānupaliptā;prajñā na sarvasaṃvāsāvaraṇāvaraṇīyadharmaiḥ sārdhaṃ saṃvasati.

g) [The action of insight (prajñākarma):]Further, insight is knowledge of what are good and bad moments of existence;insight is discerning the moments of existence conducive to spiritual progress;insight is authoritative since the holy principles of religion [namely egolessness of the person and egolessness of moments of existence] are made manifest by it;insight is understanding all doctrinal viewpoints, manifestations of vices, hindrances and obstructions such as they are [namely, essentially empty (svabhāvaśūnya) ];insight is having no longings concerned with cupidity, hopes and wishes;insight creates pleasure since it quenches the fire of all vices;insight creates joy since it is the unbrokenness of happiness and joy concerning religion;insight throws light upon things since it makes manifest the knowledge of the meaning [namely, the limit of existence (bhūtakoṭi), the pure total reality (viśuddhadharmadhātu), etc.];insight is the basis of the thirty-seven moments of existence which are the wings of awakening;insight has the essential characteristic of attainment since it attains the fruit according to the way;insight has the essential characteristic of knowing [the special and general characteristics (svasāmānyalakṣaṇa) of moments of existence] since knowledge is essentially radiant;insight is saving since it brings you over all the floods [of cupidity (rāga), viewpoints (dṛṣṭi), ignorance (avidyā) and existence (bhava) ];insight leads to true certainty;insight embraces all good moments of existence [as they arise from it];insight (p. 83) clears up all earlier vices and bad habits;insight is the most excellent of the prominent moments of existence;insight is most sublime since it is understanding through self-originated knowledge;insight is beyond appearance since it is not stained by the threefold world;[but still] insight has grasped expedient means in every way;insight has been attained by all the holy;insight cannot be grasped by any logical standard since it is the absence of distinguishing marks and thought-constructions;insight is the adversary of indolence since it is the absence of the darkness of ignorance and delusion;insight is the practice of all those established on the stage of practising meditation;insight is the leader of the adherents of all the ways;insight makes light since it removes the obscured vision, the darkness of ignorance and delusion;insight gives sight accordingly to those wishing sight [be it the sight of insight (prajñācakṣur), the sight of the Buddhas (buddhacakṣur) or the sight of moments of existence (dharmacakṣur) ];insight has no basis since it transcends the way of eye and form, and likewise transcends the way of ears and sound, nose and smell, tongue and taste, body and tangibles, mind and moments of existence;insight is the highest meaning since it issues from truth;insight is the imperturbability of the well-trained;insight is the splendour in the gates of knowledge;insight is imperishable as it moves about everywhere;insight is unhindered as it is the vision of the entrance into dependent origination;insight is the way of liberation since it is the severing of all the bonds of grasping and the vices;insight is not stained by any vices;insight does not stay in any company [as the sixteen things mentioned above] with moments of existence making or going to make hindrances.

śes rab kyi las bstan pa’i phyir gźan yaṅ dge ba daṅ mi dge ba źes bya ba la sogs pa gsuṅs te, źar la śes rab kyi sgra’i don kyaṅ ’chad do – "To show the action of insight (prajñākarma) it is said .... etc., and consequently (prasaṅgena) the meaning (artha) of the word prajnā is decided". Cf. fol.88b1, b3; alternatively, according to the second division, this section with the exception of the last few lines is named prajñānirukti, v. ṭ. fol. 88b4, b6-7: śes rab kyi ṅes pa’i tshig, and supra p. 192 n. 1.
śes rab kyi tshig la mdo kha cig las ni rab daṅ śes pa gñis ka ’byuṅ, kha cig las gcig ’byuṅ ste, de daṅ ldan pa’i phyir śes rab ces bya’o. yaṅ na a) gźan gyis bstan pa śes pa daṅ, b) so so raṅ ñid śes pa daṅ, c) rnam par śes pa daṅ, d) rab tu źi ba śes pa daṅ, e) yon tan gyi mchog śes pas śes rab bo. de la a) gźan gyis bstan pa śes pa ni gźan gyis bstan pa’i sgra’i rjes su ’gro ba daṅ, tshul bźin yid la byed pa las yaṅ dag par lta ba skyes pa’o. b) so so raṅ ñid śes pa ni ’jig rten las ’das pa rnam par mi rtog pa’i ye śes mṅon sum du gyur pa’o. c) rnam par śes pa ni ’jig rten las ’das pa’i rjes la thob pa’i ye śes kyis chos kyi mtshan ñid rtog pa’o. d) rab tu źi ba śes pa ni bsgom pa’i lam na ñon moṅs pa’i gñen por gyur pa’i ye śes so. e) yon tan gyi mchog śes pa ni mṅon par śes pa la sogs pa yon tan khyad par can rab tu sgrub par byed pa’i śes rab bo.dge ba daṅ mi dge ba’i chos rnams rab tu śes pa ni śes rab bo źes bya ba la dge ba rnam pa gñis te, a) zag pa daṅ bcas pa daṅ b) zag pa med pa’o, de la a) zag pa daṅ bcas pa ni bsod nams su ñe bar ’gro ba’i ’du byed daṅ, mi g-yo bar ñe bar ’gro ba’i ’du byed do; b) zag pa med pa ni ’phags pa’i lam la sogs pa’o; mi dge ba ni bsod nams ma yin par ñe bar ’gro ba’i ’du byed de, srog gcod pa daṅ ma byin par len pa la sogs pa’o; chos de rnams kyi raṅ daṅ spyi’i mtshan ñid rab tu śes pa ni śes rab ces bya’o.ṅes par ’byed pa’i cha daṅ mthun pa’i chos rnams la rtog pa źes bya ba la ṅes par ’byed pa ni drod pa daṅ, spyi bo daṅ, bzod pa daṅ, ’jig rten pa’i chos kyi mchog ste, mos pas spyod pa’i sa’i tiṅ ṅe ’dzin rnams so. de’i cha daṅ mthun pa’i chos ni tiṅ ṅe ’dzin de thob pa’i rgyur gyur pa’i chos te, daṅ po dge ba’i bśes gñen las dam pa’i chos ñan pa daṅ, sems pa daṅ, de nas dran par ñe bar gźag pa bźi sgom pa daṅ, yaṅ dag par spoṅ ba bźi sgom pa la sogs pa’o. chos de rnams khoṅ du chud pa rtogs pa ste, de yaṅ śes rab kyis khoṅ du chud pas na śes rab ni ṅes par ’byed pa’i cha daṅ mthun pa’i chos la rtog pa źes bya’o.’phags pa’i chos mṅon du gyur pas na śes rab ni tshad mar gyur pa’o źes bya ba la ’phags pa ni de bźin gśegs pa daṅ byaṅ chub sems dpa’ daṅ ñan thos daṅ raṅ saṅs rgyas la sogs pa’o. de dag gi chos ni gaṅ zag la bdag med pa daṅ, chos la bdag med pa’i chos te, de yaṅ śes rab kyis mṅon sum du gyur pas śes rab ni tshad mar gyur pa ste, brtsan par gyur pa źes bya ba’i tha tshig go.śes rab ni lta bar gyur pa daṅ kun nas ldaṅ ba źes bya ba la sogs pa la lta bar gyur pa la sogs pa ni goṅ du bśad par zad do. yaṅ dag par ji lta ba bźin du rab tu rtogs pa’o źes bya ba ni miṅ gis smos pa’i chos de dag gi raṅ bźin stoṅ pa ñid du phyin ci ma log par khoṅ du chud pa ste, de yaṅ śes rab kyis khoṅ du chud pas na śes rab ni lta ba la sogs pa thams cad yaṅ dag pa ji lta ba bźin du rab tu rtogs pa’o.śes rab ni ’dod pa daṅ, re ba daṅ, smon pa thams cad kyi smon lam daṅ bral ba’o źes bya ba la ’dod pa’i khams su skye bar mos pa ni ’dod pa’o, gzugs kyi khams su skye bar mos pa ni re ba’o, gzugs med pa’i khams su skye bar mos pa ni smon pa’o; yaṅ na dṅos po yid du ’oṅ ba ’das pa rnams daṅ phrad par ’dod pa ni ’dod pa’o, de daṅ ’dra ba’i dṅos po ma ’oṅs pa rnams daṅ phrad par ’dod pa ni re ba’o, da ltar gyi ñe bar len pa’i phuṅ po rnams daṅ phrad par ’dod pa ni smon pa ste, smon lam ni dus gsum gyi dṅos po de dag la chags pa la bya’o, śes rab kyis dus gsum gyi dṅos po de dag la mi rtag pa daṅ sdug bsṅal bar mthoṅ ste, de la chags pa med pa’i phyir śes rab ni smon lam daṅ bral ba’o źes bya’o.śes rab ni ñon moṅs pa’i yoṅs su gduṅ ba thams cad ’jil bas na, sim par byed pa’o źes bya ba la ñon moṅs pa ni ’dod chags la sogs pa ste, de dag ñid lus daṅ sems la gnod pa yin pas na yoṅs su gduṅ ba źes bya’o, śes rab la ñon moṅs pa’i rgyu las byuṅ ba’i gnod pa med pa’am, śes rab kyis ñon moṅs pa’i rgyu las byuṅ ba’i gnod pa de sel bar byed pas na śes rab de ni sim par byed pa’o.śes rab ni chos kyi kun dga’ la dga’ ba’i rgyun ma bcad pas na, mchog tu dga’ bar byed pa’o źes bya ba la de kho na stoṅ pa’i mtshan ñid rtogs nas dga’ ba rgyun mi ’chad par ’byuṅ ba ni chos kyi kun dga’ la dga’ ba rgyun ma bcad pa źes bya ste, de’aṅ śes rab las byuṅ bas śes rab ni mchog tu dga’ bar byed pa’o.Read as in ṭ.: śes rab ni don śes pa mṅon sum du gyur pas na rab tu ston pa’o źes bya ba la don ni yaṅ dag pa’i mtha’ chos kyi dbyiṅs rnam par dag pa’o, don de khoṅ du chud pa’i don śes pa mṅon sum du gyur pa ste, de’aṅ śes rab kyi mṅon sum du gyur pas na śes rab de don la rtog pa’i phyir rab tu ston pa źes bya’o; yaṅ na, śes rab la don ston te, śes rab med na don mi rtogs pa’i phyir ro.śes rab ni byaṅ chub kyi phyogs kyi chos sum cu rtsa bdun po dag gi rten to źes bya ba la, byaṅ chub ni spaṅs pa daṅ ye śes kyi mtshan ñid de, de la spaṅs pa’i mtshan ñid ni ñon moṅs pa daṅ śes bya’i sgrib pa spaṅs pa’i phyir ro, ye śes ni me loṅ lta bu daṅ, mñam pa ñid daṅ, so sor kun tu rtog pa daṅ, bya ba sgrub pa’o, byaṅ chub de thob par bya ba’i rgyu’am gźi la byaṅ chub kyi phyogs źes bya ste, de’aṅ dran pa ñe bar gźag pa bźi daṅ, yaṅ dag par spoṅ ba bźi la sogs pa sum cu rtsa bdun no, śes rab la brten nas byaṅ chub kyi phyogs kyi chos sum cu rtsa bdun so so’i sems kyi rgyun la skye
